namo rudrāya haraye brahmaṇe paramātmane 
pradhānapuruṣeśāya sargasthityantakāriṇe  LiP 
nārado 'bhyarcya śaileśe śaṅkaraṃ saṅgameśvare 
hiraṇyagarbhe svarlīne hy avimukte mahālaye  LiP 
raudre goprekṣake caiva śreṣṭhe pāśupate tathā 
vighneśvare ca kedāre tathā gomāyukeśvare  LiP 
hiraṇyagarbhe candreśe īśānye ca triviṣṭape 
śukreśvare yathānyāyaṃ naimiṣaṃ prayayau muniḥ  LiP 
naimiṣeyāstadā dṛṣṭvā nāradaṃ hṛṣṭamānasāḥ 
samabhyarcyāsanaṃ tasmai tadyogyaṃ samakalpayan  LiP 
so 'pi hṛṣṭo munivarair dattaṃ bheje tadāsanam 
sampūjyamāno munibhiḥ sukhāsīno varāsane  LiP 
cakre kathāṃ vicitrārthāṃ liṅgamāhātmyamāśritām 
etasminnevakāle tu sūtaḥ paurāṇikaḥ svayam  LiP 
jagāma naimiṣaṃ dhīmān praṇāmārthaṃ tapasvinām 
tasmai sāma ca pūjāṃ ca yathāvaccakrire tadā  LiP 
naimiṣeyāstu śiṣyāya kṛṣṇadvaipāyanasya tu 
atha teṣāṃ purāṇasya śuśrūṣā samapadyata  LiP 
dṛṣṭvā tam ativiśvastaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ romaharṣaṇam 
apṛcchaṃśca tataḥ sūtam ṛṣiṃ sarve tapodhanāḥ  LiP 
purāṇasaṃhitāṃ puṇyāṃ liṅgamāhātmyasaṃyutām 
naimiṣeyā ūcuḥ
tvayā sūta mahābuddhe kṛṣṇadvaipāyano muniḥ  LiP 
upāsitaḥ purāṇārthaṃ labdhā tasmācca saṃhitā 
tasmādbhavantaṃ pṛcchāmaḥ sūta paurāṇikottamam  LiP 
purāṇasaṃhitāṃ divyāṃ liṅgamāhātmyasaṃyutām 
nārado 'pyasya devasya rudrasya paramātmanaḥ  LiP 
kṣetrāṇyāsādya cābhyarcya liṅgāni munipuṅgavaḥ 
iha saṃnihitaḥ śrīmān nārado brahmaṇaḥ sutaḥ  LiP 
bhavabhakto bhavāṃścaiva vayaṃ vai nāradastathā 
asyāgrato muneḥ puṇyaṃ purāṇaṃ vaktumarhasi  LiP 
saphalaṃ sādhitaṃ sarvaṃ bhavatā viditaṃ bhavet 
evamuktaḥ sa hṛṣṭātmā sūtaḥ paurāṇikottamaḥ  LiP 
abhivādyāgrato dhīmān nāradaṃ brahmaṇaḥ sutam 
naimiṣeyāṃśca puṇyātmā purāṇaṃ vyājahāra saḥ  LiP 
sūta uvāca
namaskṛtya mahādevaṃ brahmāṇaṃ ca janārdanam 
munīśvaraṃ tathā vyāsaṃ vaktuṃ liṅgaṃ smarāmyaham  LiP 
śabdaṃ brahmatanuṃ sākṣāc chabdabrahmaprakāśakam 
varṇāvayavam avyakta lakṣaṇaṃ bahudhā sthitam  LiP 
akārokāramakāraṃ sthūlaṃ sūkṣmaṃ parātparam 
oṅkārarūpam ṛgvaktraṃ samajihvāsamanvitam  LiP 
yajurvedamahāgrīvam atharvahṛdayaṃ vibhum 
pradhānapuruṣātītaṃ pralayotpattivarjitam  LiP 
tamasā kālarudrākhyaṃ rajasā kanakāṇḍajam 
sattvena sarvagaṃ viṣṇuṃ nirguṇatve maheśvaram  LiP 
pradhānāvayavaṃ vyāpya saptadhādhiṣṭhitaṃ kramāt 
punaḥ ṣoḍaśadhā caiva ṣaḍviṃśakam ajodbhavam  LiP 
sargapratiṣṭhāsaṃhāra līlārthaṃ liṅgarūpiṇam 
praṇamya ca yathānyāyaṃ vakṣye liṅgodbhavaṃ śubham  LiP 
iti śrīlaiṅge mahāpurāṇe prathamo 'dhyāyaḥ

sūta uvāca
īśānakalpavṛttāntam adhikṛtya mahātmanā 
brahmaṇā kalpitaṃ pūrvaṃ purāṇaṃ laiṅgam uttamam  LiP 
granthakoṭipramāṇaṃ tu śatakoṭipravistare 
caturlakṣeṇa saṃkṣipte vyāsaiḥ sarvāntareṣu vai  LiP 
vyasteṣṭā daśadhā caiva brahmādau dvāparādiṣu

asyaikādaśasāhasre granthamānamiha dvijāḥ 
tasmātsaṃkṣepato vakṣye na śrutaṃ vistareṇa yat  LiP

atraikādaśasāhasraiḥ kathito liṅgasambhavaḥ  LiP 
sargaḥ prādhānikaḥ paścāt prākṛto vaikṛtāni ca 
aṇḍasyāsya ca sambhūtir aṇḍasyāvaraṇāṣṭakam  LiP 
aṇḍodbhavatvaṃ śarvasya rajoguṇasamāśrayāt

prajāpatīnāṃ sargaś ca pṛthivyuddharaṇaṃ tathā 
brahmaṇaś ca divārātram āyuṣo gaṇanaṃ punaḥ  LiP 
savanaṃ brahmaṇaścaiva yugakalpaś ca tasya tu

punarliṅgodbhavaścaiva ṛṣimadhye pinākinaḥ  LiP

vārāṇasyāś ca māhātmyaṃ kṣetramāhātmyavarṇanam  LiP 
bhuvi rudrālayānāṃ tu saṃkhyā viṣṇorgṛhasya ca 
antarikṣe tathāṇḍe 'smin devāyatanavarṇanam  LiP 
dakṣasya patanaṃ bhūmau punaḥ svārociṣe 'ntare 
dakṣaśāpaś ca dakṣasya śāpamokṣastathaiva ca  LiP 
kailāsavarṇanaṃ caiva yogaḥ pāśupatas tathā 
caturyugapramāṇaṃ ca yugadharmaḥ suvistaraḥ  LiP 
saṃdhyāṃśakapramāṇaṃ ca saṃdhyāvṛttaṃ bhavasya ca 
śmaśānanilayaścaiva candrarekhāsamudbhavaḥ  LiP 
udvāhaḥ śaṃkarasyātha putrotpādanameva ca 
maithunātiprasaṅgena vināśo jagatāṃ bhayam  LiP 
śāpaḥ satyā kṛto devān purā viṣṇuṃ ca pālitam 
śukrotsargastu rudrasya gāṅgeyodbhava eva ca  LiP 
grahaṇādiṣu kāleṣu snāpya liṅgaṃ phalaṃ tathā 
kṣubdhadhī ca vivādaś ca dadhīcopendrayos tathā  LiP

pativratāyāścākhyānaṃ paśupāśavicāraṇā  LiP 
pravṛttilakṣaṇaṃ jñānaṃ nivṛttyadhikṛtā tathā 
vasiṣṭhatanayotpattir vāsiṣṭhānāṃ mahātmanām  LiP

sutaśoko vasiṣṭhasya arundhatyāḥ pralāpanam

parāśarasyāvatāro vyāsasya ca śukasya ca

devatāparamārthaṃ tu vijñānaṃ ca prasādataḥ 
purāṇakaraṇaṃ caiva pulastyasyājñayā guroḥ  LiP 
bhuvanānāṃ pramāṇaṃ ca grahāṇāṃ jyotiṣāṃ gatiḥ

bhojyābhojyavidhānaṃ ca sarveṣāmeva varṇinām

narakāṇāṃ svarūpaṃ ca daṇḍaḥ karmānurūpataḥ 
svarginārakiṇāṃ puṃsāṃ cihnaṃ janmāntareṣu ca  LiP

nārasya ca tathotpattiḥ kapāle vaiṣṇavāddharāt

vainyena pṛthunā bhūmeḥ purā dohapravartanam

vṛṣṇyandhakavināśāya śāpaḥ piṇḍāravāsinām

erakālābhato 'nyonyaṃ vivāde vṛṣṇivigrahaḥ 
līlayā caiva kṛṣṇena svakulasya ca saṃhṛtiḥ  LiP 
erakāstrabalenaiva gamanaṃ svecchayaiva tu

sarvapāpavinirmukto brahmalokaṃ sa gacchati  LiP

sūta uvāca
aliṅgo liṅgamūlaṃ tu avyaktaṃ liṅgamucyate 
aliṅgaḥ śiva ityukto liṅgaṃ śaivamiti smṛtam  LiP 
pradhānaṃ prakṛtiśceti yadāhurliṅgamuttamam 
gandhavarṇarasairhīnaṃ śabdasparśādivarjitam  LiP 
aguṇaṃ dhruvamakṣayyam aliṅgaṃ śivalakṣaṇam 
gandhavarṇarasairyuktaṃ śabdasparśādilakṣaṇam  LiP 
jagadyoniṃ mahābhūtaṃ sthūlaṃ sūkṣmaṃ dvijottamāḥ 
vigraho jagatāṃ liṅgam aliṅgād abhavatsvayam  LiP 
saptadhācāṣṭadhā caiva tathaikādaśadhā punaḥ 
liṅgānyaliṅgasya tathā māyayā vitatāni tu  LiP 
tebhyaḥ pradhānadevānāṃ trayamāsīcchivātmakam 
ekasmāttriṣvabhūdviśvam ekena parirakṣitam  LiP 
ekenaiva hṛtaṃ viśvaṃ vyāptaṃ tvevaṃ śivena tu 
aliṅgaṃ caiva liṅgaṃ ca liṅgāliṅgāni mūrtayaḥ  LiP 
yathāvatkathitāścaiva tasmādbrahma svayaṃ jagat 
aliṅgī bhagavān bījī sa eva parameśvaraḥ  LiP 
bījaṃ yoniś ca nirbījaṃ nirbījo bījamucyate 
bījayonipradhānānām ātmākhyā vartate tviha  LiP 
paramātmā munirbrahma nityabuddhasvabhāvataḥ 
viśuddho 'yaṃ tathā rudraḥ purāṇe śiva ucyate  LiP 
śivena dṛṣṭā prakṛtiḥ śaivī samabhavaddvijāḥ 
sargādau sā guṇairyuktā purāvyaktā svabhāvataḥ  LiP 
avyaktādiviśeṣāntaṃ viśvaṃ tasyāḥ samucchritam 
viśvadhātrī tvajākhyā ca śaivī sā prakṛtiḥ smṛtā  LiP 
tāmajāṃ lohitāṃ śuklāṃ kṛṣṇāmekāṃ bahuprajām

ajā janitrī jagatāṃ sājena samadhiṣṭhitā  LiP

ajājñayā pradhānasya sargakāle guṇais tribhiḥ  LiP 
sisṛkṣayā codyamānaḥ praviśyāvyaktamavyayam

mahatastu tathā vṛttiḥ saṃkalpādhyavasāyikā

tenaiva cāvṛtaḥ samyag ahaṃkāras tamo 'dhikaḥ 
mahato bhūtatanmātraṃ sargakṛdvai babhūva ca  LiP 
ahaṃkārācchabdamātraṃ tasmādākāśamavyayam 
saśabdamāvṛṇotpaścād ākāśaṃ śabdakāraṇam  LiP 
tanmātrādbhūtasargaś ca dvijāstvevaṃ prakīrtitaḥ 
sparśamātraṃ tathākāśāt tasmādvāyur mahānmune  LiP

rasādāpaḥ śubhāstābhyo gandhamātraṃ dharā tataḥ  LiP 
āvṛṇoddhi tathākāśaṃ sparśamātraṃ dvijottamāḥ 
āvṛṇodrūpamātraṃ tu vāyurvāti kriyātmakaḥ  LiP 
āvṛṇodrasamātraṃ vai devaḥ sākṣādvibhāvasuḥ 
āvṛṇvānā gandhamātram āpaḥ sarvarasātmikāḥ  LiP 
kṣmā sā pañcaguṇā tasmād ekonā rasasambhavāḥ 
triguṇo bhagavānvahnir dviguṇaḥ sparśasambhavaḥ  LiP

vaikārikaḥ sāttviko vai yugapatsampravartate

tasminnaṇḍe tvime lokā antarviśvamidaṃ jagat  LiP

āpo daśaguṇenaiva tadbāhyastejasā vṛtāḥ  LiP 
tejo daśaguṇenaiva bāhyato vāyunā vṛtam

mahatā śabdaheturvai pradhānenāvṛtaḥ svayam  LiP 
saptāṇḍāvaraṇānyāhus tasyātmā kamalāsanaḥ 
koṭikoṭiyutānyatra cāṇḍāni kathitāni tu  LiP

sṛṣṭāḥ pradhānena tadā labdhvā śambhostu saṃnidhim  LiP 
layaścaiva tathānyonyam āndyantam iti kīrtitam

ādikartā ca bhūtānāṃ saṃhartā paripālakaḥ

ekadaṇḍe tathā lokā ime kartā pitāmahaḥ  LiP 
prākṛtaḥ kathitastveṣa puruṣādhiṣṭhito mayā

sūta uvāca
atha prāthamikasyeha yaḥ kālastadahaḥ smṛtam 
sargasya tādṛśī rātriḥ prākṛtasya samāsataḥ  LiP 
divā sṛṣṭiṃ vikurute rajanyāṃ pralayaṃ vibhuḥ 
aupacārikamasyaitad ahorātraṃ na vidyate  LiP 
divā vikṛtayaḥ sarve vikārā viśvadevatāḥ 
prajānāṃ patayaḥ sarve tiṣṭhantyanye maharṣayaḥ  LiP 
rātrau sarve pralīyante niśānte sambhavanti ca 
ahastu tasya vaikalpo rātristādṛgvidhā smṛtā  LiP 
caturyugasahasrānte manavastu caturdaśa 
catvāri tu sahasrāṇi vatsarāṇāṃ kṛtaṃ dvijāḥ  LiP 
tāvacchatī ca vai saṃdhyā saṃdhyāṃśaś ca kṛtasya tu 
triśatī dviśatī saṃdhyā tathā caikaśatī kramāt  LiP 
aṃśakaḥ ṣaṭśataṃ tasmāt kṛtasaṃdhyāṃśakaṃ vinā 
tridvyekasāhasramito vinā saṃdhyāṃśakena tu  LiP 
tretādvāparatiṣyāṇāṃ kṛtasya kathayāmi vaḥ 
nimeṣapañcadaśakā kāṣṭhā svasthasya suvratāḥ  LiP 
martyasya cākṣṇostasyāś ca tatas triṃśatikā kalā 
kalātriṃśatiko viprā muhūrta iti kalpitaḥ  LiP 
muhūrtapañcadaśikā rajanī tādṛśaṃ tvahaḥ 
pitrye rātryahanī māsaḥ pravibhāgastayoḥ punaḥ  LiP 
kṛṣṇapakṣastvahasteṣāṃ śuklaḥ svapnāya śarvarī 
triṃśadye mānuṣā māsāḥ pitryo māsastu sa smṛtaḥ  LiP 
śatāni trīṇi māsānāṃ ṣaṣṭyā cāpyadhikāni vai 
pitryaḥ saṃvatsaro hyeṣa mānuṣeṇa vibhāvyate  LiP 
mānuṣeṇaiva mānena varṣāṇāṃ yacchataṃ bhavet 
pitṝṇāṃ trīṇi varṣāṇi saṃkhyātānīha tāni vai  LiP 
daśa vai dvyadhikā māsāḥ pitṛsaṃkhyeha saṃsmṛtā 
laukikenaiva mānena abdo yo mānuṣaḥ smṛtaḥ  LiP 
etaddivyamahorātram iti laiṅge 'tra paṭhyate 
divye rātryahanī varṣaṃ pravibhāgastayoḥ punaḥ  LiP 
ahastatrodagayanaṃ rātriḥ syāddakṣiṇāyanam 
ete rātryahanī divye prasaṃkhyāte viśeṣataḥ  LiP 
triṃśadyāni tu varṣāṇi divyo māsastu sa smṛtaḥ 
mānuṣaṃ tu śataṃ viprā divyamāsāstrayastu te  LiP 
daśa caiva tathāhāni divyo hyeṣa vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ 
trīṇi varṣaśatānyeva ṣaṣṭivarṣāṇi yāni tu  LiP 
divyaḥ saṃvatsaro hyeṣa mānuṣeṇa prakīrtitaḥ 
trīṇi varṣasahasrāṇi mānuṣāṇi pramāṇataḥ  LiP 
triṃśadanyāni varṣāṇi mataḥ saptarṣivatsaraḥ 
nava yāni sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ mānuṣāṇi tu  LiP 
anyāni navatīścaiva dhrauvaḥ saṃvatsarastu saḥ 
ṣaṭtriṃśattu sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ mānuṣāṇi tu  LiP 
varṣāṇāṃ tacchataṃ jñeyaṃ divyo hyeṣa vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ 
trīṇyeva niyutānyāhur varṣāṇāṃ mānuṣāṇi tu  LiP 
ṣaṣṭiścaiva sahasrāṇi saṃkhyātāni tu saṃkhyayā 
divyaṃ varṣasahasraṃ tu prāhuḥ saṃkhyāvido janāḥ  LiP 
divyenaiva pramāṇena yugasaṃkhyāprakalpanam 
pūrvaṃ kṛtayugaṃ nāma tatastretā vidhīyate  LiP 
dvāparaśca kaliścaiva yugānyetāni suvratāḥ 
atha saṃvatsarā dṛṣṭā mānuṣeṇa pramāṇataḥ  LiP 
kṛtasyādyasya viprendrā divyamānena kīrtitam 
sahasrāṇāṃ śatānyāsaṃś caturdaśa ca saṃkhyayā  LiP 
catvāriṃśatsahasrāṇi tathānyāni kṛtaṃ yugam 
tathā daśasahasrāṇāṃ varṣāṇāṃ śatasaṃkhyayā  LiP 
aśītiś ca sahasrāṇi kālastretāyugasya ca 
saptaiva niyutānyāhur varṣāṇāṃ mānuṣāṇi tu  LiP 
viṃśatiś ca sahasrāṇi kālastu dvāparasya ca 
tathā śatasahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ trīṇi saṃkhyayā  LiP 
ṣaṣṭiścaiva sahasrāṇi kālaḥ kaliyugasya tu 
evaṃ caturyugaḥ kāla ṛte saṃdhyāṃśakātsmṛtaḥ  LiP 
niyutānyeva ṣaṭtriṃśan niraṃśāni tu tāni vai 
catvāriṃśattathā trīṇi niyutānīha saṃkhyayā  LiP 
viṃśatiś ca sahasrāṇi saṃdhyāṃśaś ca caturyugaḥ 
evaṃ caturyugākhyānāṃ sādhikā hyekasaptatiḥ  LiP 
kṛtatretādiyuktānāṃ manorantaramucyate 
manvantarasya saṃkhyā ca varṣāgreṇa prakīrtitā  LiP 
triṃśatkoṭyastu varṣāṇāṃ mānuṣeṇa dvijottamāḥ 
saptaṣaṣṭistathānyāni niyutānyadhikāni tu  LiP 
viṃśatiś ca sahasrāṇi kālo 'yam adhikaṃ vinā 
manvantarasya saṃkhyaiṣā laiṅge 'sminkīrtitā dvijāḥ  LiP 
caturyugasya ca tathā varṣasaṃkhyā prakīrtitā 
caturyugasahasraṃ vai kalpaścaiko dvijottamāḥ  LiP 
niśānte sṛjate lokān naśyante niśi jantavaḥ 
tatra vaimānikānāṃ tu aṣṭāviṃśatikoṭayaḥ  LiP 
manvantareṣu vai saṃkhyā sāntareṣu yathātathā 
trīṇi koṭiśatānyāsan koṭyo dvinavatis tathā  LiP 
kalpe 'tīte tu vai viprāḥ sahasrāṇāṃ tu saptatiḥ 
punastathāṣṭasāhasraṃ sarvatraiva samāsataḥ  LiP 
kalpāvasānikāṃstyaktvā pralaye samupasthite 
maharlokāt prayāntyete janalokaṃ janāstataḥ  LiP 
koṭīnāṃ dve sahasre tu aṣṭau koṭiśatāni tu 
dviṣaṣṭiś ca tathā koṭyo niyutāni ca saptatiḥ  LiP 
kalpārdhasaṃkhyā divyā vai kalpamevaṃ tu kalpayet 
kalpānāṃ vai sahasraṃ tu varṣamekamajasya tu  LiP 
varṣāṇāmaṣṭasāhasraṃ brāhmaṃ vai brahmaṇo yugam 
savanaṃ yugasāhasraṃ sarvadevodbhavasya tu  LiP 
savanānāṃ sahasraṃ tu trividhaṃ triguṇaṃ tathā 
brahmaṇastu tathā proktaḥ kālaḥ kālātmanaḥ prabho  LiP 
bhavodbhavastapaścaiva bhavyo rambhaḥ kratuḥ punaḥ 
ṛturvahnirhavyavāhaḥ sāvitraḥ śuddha eva ca  LiP 
uśikaḥ kuśikaścaiva gāndhāro munisattamāḥ 
ṛṣabhaś ca tathā ṣaḍjo majjālīyaś ca madhyamaḥ  LiP 
vairājo vai niṣādaś ca mukhyo vai meghavāhanaḥ 
pañcamaścitrakaścaiva ākūtir jñāna eva ca  LiP 
manaḥ sudarśo bṛṃhaś ca tathā vai śvetalohitaḥ 
raktaś ca pītavāsāś ca asitaḥ sarvarūpakaḥ  LiP 
evaṃ kalpāstu saṃkhyātā brahmaṇo 'vyaktajanmanaḥ 
koṭikoṭisahasrāṇi kalpānāṃ munisattamāḥ  LiP 
gatāni tāvaccheṣāṇi aharniśyāni vai punaḥ 
parānte vai vikārāṇi vikāraṃ yānti viśvataḥ  LiP 
vikārasya śivasyājñā vaśenaiva tu saṃhṛtiḥ 
saṃhṛte tu vikāre ca pradhāne cātmani sthite  LiP 
sādharmyeṇāvatiṣṭhete pradhānapuruṣāvubhau 
guṇānāṃ caiva vaiṣamye viprāḥ sṛṣṭiriti smṛtā  LiP 
sāmye layo guṇānāṃ tu tayorheturmaheśvaraḥ 
līlayā devadevena sargāstvīdṛgvidhāḥ kṛtāḥ  LiP 
asaṃkhyātāś ca saṃkṣepāt pradhānād anvadhiṣṭhitāt 
asaṃkhyātāś ca kalpākhyā hy asaṃkhyātāḥ pitāmahāḥ  LiP 
harayaścāpyasaṃkhyātās tv eka eva maheśvaraḥ 
pradhānādipravṛttāni līlayā prākṛtāni tu  LiP 
guṇātmikā ca tadvṛttis tasya devasya vai tridhā 
aprākṛtasya tasyādir madhyāntaṃ nāsti cātmanaḥ  LiP 
pitāmahasyātha paraḥ parārdhadvayasaṃmitaḥ 
divā sṛṣṭaṃ tu yatsarvaṃ niśi naśyati cāsya tat  LiP 
bhūrbhuvaḥsvarmahastatra naśyate cordhvato na ca 
rātrau caikārṇave brahmā naṣṭe sthāvarajaṅgame  LiP 
suṣvāpāmbhasi yastasmān nārāyaṇa iti smṛtaḥ 
śarvaryante prabuddho vai dṛṣṭvā śūnyaṃ carācaram  LiP 
sraṣṭuṃ tadā matiṃ cakre brahmā brahmavidāṃ varaḥ 
udakairāplutāṃ kṣmāṃ tāṃ samādāya sanātanaḥ  LiP 
pūrvavatsthāpayāmāsa vārāhaṃ rūpamāsthitaḥ 
nadīnadasamudrāṃś ca pūrvavaccākarotprabhuḥ  LiP

bhūrādyāṃś caturo lokān kalpayāmāsa pūrvavat

sūta uvāca
yadā sraṣṭuṃ matiṃ cakre mohaścāsīnmahātmanaḥ 
dvijāś ca buddhipūrvaṃ tu brahmaṇo 'vyaktajanmanaḥ  LiP 
tamo moho mahāmohas tāmisraścāndhasaṃjñitaḥ 
avidyā pañcadhā hyeṣā prādurbhūtā svayambhuvaḥ  LiP 
avidyayā munergrastaḥ sargo mukhya iti smṛtaḥ 
asādhaka iti smṛtvā sargo mukhyaḥ prajāpatiḥ  LiP 
abhyamanyata so 'nyaṃ vai nagā mukhyodbhavāḥ smṛtāḥ 
tridhā kaṇṭho munestasya dhyāyato vai hyavartata  LiP 
prathamaṃ tasya vai jajñe tiryaksroto mahātmanaḥ 
ūrdhvasrotaḥ parastasya sāttvikaḥ sa iti smṛtaḥ  LiP 
arvāksroto 'nugrahaś ca tathā bhūtādikaḥ punaḥ 
brahmaṇo mahatastvādyo dvitīyo bhautikas tathā  LiP 
sargastṛtīyaścaindriyas turīyo mukhya ucyate 
tiryagyonyaḥ pañcamastu ṣaṣṭho daivika ucyate  LiP 
saptamo mānuṣo viprā aṣṭamo 'nugrahaḥ smṛtaḥ 
navamaścaiva kaumāraḥ prākṛtā vaikṛtāstvime  LiP 
purastādasṛjaddevaḥ sanandaṃ sanakaṃ tathā 
sanātanaṃ muniśreṣṭhā naiṣkarmyeṇa gatāḥ param  LiP 
marīcibhṛgvaṅgirasaḥ pulastyaṃ pulahaṃ kratum 
dakṣamatriṃ vasiṣṭhaṃ ca so 'sṛjadyogavidyayā  LiP 
navaite brahmaṇaḥ putrā brahmajñā brāhmaṇottamāḥ 
brahmavādina evaite brahmaṇaḥ sadṛśāḥ smṛtāḥ  LiP 
saṃkalpaścaiva dharmaś ca hy adharmo dharmasaṃnidhiḥ 
dvādaśaiva prajāstvetā brahmaṇo 'vyaktajanmanaḥ  LiP 
ṛbhuṃ sanatkumāraṃ ca sasarjādau sanātanaḥ 
tāvūrdhvaretasau divyau cāgrajau brahmavādinau  LiP

vakṣye bhāryākulaṃ teṣāṃ munīnāmagrajanmanām  LiP 
samāsato muniśreṣṭhāḥ prajāsambhūtimeva ca 
śatarūpāṃ tu vai rājñīṃ virājamasṛjatprabhuḥ  LiP 
svāyambhuvāttu vai rājñī śatarūpā tvayonijā 
lebhe putradvayaṃ puṇyā tathā kanyādvayaṃ ca sā  LiP 
uttānapādo hyavaro dhīmāñjyeṣṭhaḥ priyavrataḥ 
jyeṣṭhā variṣṭhā tvākūtiḥ prasūtiścānujā smṛtā  LiP 
upayeme tadākūtiṃ rucirnāma prajāpatiḥ 
prasūtiṃ bhagavāndakṣo lokadhātrīṃ ca yoginīm  LiP 
dakṣiṇāsahitaṃ yajñam ākūtiḥ suṣuve tathā 
dakṣiṇā janayāmāsa divyā dvādaśa putrikāḥ  LiP 
prasūtiḥ suṣuve dakṣāc caturviṃśatikanyakāḥ 
śraddhāṃ lakṣmīṃ dhṛtiṃ puṣṭiṃ tuṣṭiṃ medhāṃ kriyāṃ tathā  LiP 
buddhiṃ lajjāṃ vapuḥśāntiṃ siddhiṃ kīrtiṃ mahātapāḥ 
khyātiṃ śāntiṃ ca sambhūtiṃ smṛtiṃ prītiṃ kṣamāṃ tathā  LiP 
saṃnatiṃ cānasūyāṃ ca ūrjāṃ svāhāṃ surāraṇim 
svadhāṃ caiva mahābhāgāṃ pradadau ca yathākramam  LiP 
śraddhādyāścaiva kīrtyantās trayodaśa sudārikāḥ 
dharmaṃ prajāpatiṃ jagmuḥ patiṃ paramadurlabhāḥ  LiP 
upayeme bhṛgurdhīmān khyātiṃ tāṃ bhārgavāraṇim

prītiṃ pulastyaḥ puṇyātmā kṣamāṃ tāṃ pulaho muniḥ 
kratuś ca saṃnatiṃ dhīmān atristāṃ cānasūyakām  LiP 
ūrjāṃ vasiṣṭho bhagavān variṣṭho vārijekṣaṇām 
vibhāvasus tathā svāhāṃ svadhāṃ vai pitaras tathā  LiP 
putrīkṛtā satī yā sā mānasī śivasambhavā 
dakṣeṇa jagatāṃ dhātrī rudramevāsthitā patim  LiP 
ardhanārīśvaraṃ dṛṣṭvā sargādau kanakāṇḍajaḥ 
vibhajasveti cāhādau yadā jātā tadābhavat  LiP 
tasyāścaivāṃśajāḥ sarvāḥ striyastribhuvane tathā 
ekādaśāvidhā rudrās tasya cāṃśodbhavās tathā  LiP 
strīliṅgamakhilaṃ sā vai puṃliṅgaṃ nīlalohitaḥ 
taṃ dṛṣṭvā bhagavān brahmā dakṣamālokya suvratām  LiP 
bhajasva dhātrīṃ jagatāṃ mamāpi ca tavāpi ca

praśastā tava kānteyaṃ syāt putrī viśvamātṛkā

evamuktastadā dakṣo niyogādbrahmaṇo muniḥ 
labdhvā putrīṃ dadau sākṣāt satīṃ rudrāya sādaram  LiP 
dharmasya patnyaḥ śraddhādyāḥ kīrtitā vai trayodaśa 
tāsu dharmaprajāṃ vakṣye yathākramamanuttamam  LiP 
kāmo darpo 'tha niyamaḥ saṃtoṣo lobha eva ca 
śrutastu daṇḍaḥ samayo bodhaścaiva mahādyutiḥ  LiP 
apramādaś ca vinayo vyavasāyo dvijottamāḥ 
kṣemaṃ sukhaṃ yaśaścaiva dharmaputrāś ca tāsu vai  LiP 
dharmasya vai kriyāyāṃ tu daṇḍaḥ samaya eva ca 
apramādas tathā bodho buddherdharmasya tau sutau  LiP 
tasmātpañcadaśaivaite tāsu dharmātmajāstviha 
bhṛgupatnī ca suṣuve khyātirviṣṇoḥ priyāṃ śriyam  LiP 
dhātāraṃ ca vidhātāraṃ merorjāmātarau sutau 
prabhūtirnāma yā patnī marīceḥ suṣuve sutau  LiP 
pūrṇamāsaṃ tu mārīcaṃ tataḥ kanyācatuṣṭayam 
tuṣṭirjyeṣṭhā ca vai dṛṣṭiḥ kṛṣiścāpacitis tathā  LiP 
kṣamā ca suṣuve putrān putrīṃ ca pulahācchubhām 
kardamaṃ ca varīyāṃsaṃ sahiṣṇuṃ munisattamāḥ  LiP 
tathā kanakapītāṃ sa pīvarīṃ pṛthivīsamām 
prītyāṃ pulastyaś ca tathā janayāmāsa vai sutān  LiP 
dattorṇaṃ vedabāhuṃ ca putrīṃ cānyāṃ dṛṣadvatīm 
putrāṇāṃ ṣaṣṭisāhasraṃ saṃnatiḥ suṣuve śubhā  LiP 
kratostu bhāryā sarve te vālakhilyā iti śrutāḥ 
sinīvālīṃ kuhūṃ caiva rākāṃ cānumatiṃ tathā  LiP 
smṛtiś ca suṣuve patnī muneścāṅgirasas tathā 
labdhānubhāvamagniṃ ca kīrtimantaṃ ca suvratā  LiP 
atrerbhāryānasūyā vai suṣuve ṣaṭprajāstu yāḥ 
tāsvekā kanyakā nāmnā śrutiḥ sā sūnupañcakam  LiP 
satyanetro munirbhavyo mūrtirāpaḥ śanaiścaraḥ 
somaś ca vai śrutiḥ ṣaṣṭhī pañcātreyāstu sūnavaḥ  LiP 
ūrjā vasiṣṭhādvai lebhe sutāṃś ca sutavatsalā 
jyāyasī puṇḍarīkākṣān vāsiṣṭhān varalocanā  LiP 
rajaḥ suhotro bāhuś ca savanaścānaghas tathā

yaścābhimānī bhagavān bhavātmā paitāmaho vahnirasuḥ prajānām

pavamānaḥ pāvakaś ca śuciragniś ca te smṛtāḥ 
nirmathyaḥ pavamānastu vaidyutaḥ pāvakaḥ smṛtaḥ  LiP 
śuciḥ saurastu vijñeyaḥ svāhāputrāstrayastu te

ityete vahnayaḥ proktāḥ praṇīyante 'dhvareṣu ca  LiP

prajānāṃ patayaḥ sarve sarve rudrātmakāḥ smṛtāḥ  LiP 
ayajvānaś ca yajvānaḥ pitaraḥ prītimānasāḥ 
agniṣvāttāś ca yajvānaḥ śeṣā barhiṣadaḥ smṛtāḥ  LiP 
menāṃ tu mānasīṃ teṣāṃ janayāmāsa vai svadhā

dharaṇīṃ janayāmāsa mānasīṃ yajñayājinīm 
svadhā sā merurājasya patnī padmasamānanā  LiP 
pitaro 'mṛtapāḥ proktās teṣāṃ caiveha vistaraḥ 
ṛṣīṇāṃ ca kulaṃ sarvaṃ śṛṇudhvaṃ tatsuvistaram  LiP 
vadāmi pṛthagadhyāya saṃsthitaṃ vastadūrdhvataḥ

paścāddakṣaṃ vinindyaiṣā patiṃ lebhe bhavaṃ tathā

namo 'stu vo mahādevās trinetrā nīlalohitāḥ  LiP 
sarvajñāḥ sarvagā dīrghā hrasvā vāmanakāḥ śubhāḥ 
hiraṇyakeśā dṛṣṭighnā nityā buddhāś ca nirmalāḥ  LiP

evaṃ stutvā tadā rudrān rudraṃ cāha bhavaṃ śivam

namo 'stu te mahādeva prajā nārhasi śaṃkara

tatastamāha bhagavān na hi me tādṛśī sthitiḥ 
sa tvaṃ sṛja yathākāmaṃ mṛtyuyuktāḥ prajāḥ prabho  LiP 
labdhvā sasarja sakalaṃ śaṃkarāccaturānanaḥ 
jarāmaraṇasaṃyuktaṃ jagadetaccarācaram  LiP 
śaṃkaro 'pi tadā rudrair nivṛttātmā hyadhiṣṭhitaḥ 
sthāṇutvaṃ tasya vai viprāḥ śaṃkarasya mahātmanaḥ  LiP 
niṣkalasyātmanaḥ śambhoḥ svecchādhṛtaśarīriṇaḥ 
śaṃ rudraḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ karoti ghṛṇayā yataḥ  LiP 
śaṃkaraścāprayatnena tadātmā yogavidyayā 
vairāgyasthaṃ viraktasya vimuktiryacchamucyate  LiP

tasya cāsya ca saṃdhānaṃ prasādātparameṣṭhinaḥ  LiP

ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
māyāntāścaiva ghorādyā hy aṣṭaviṃśatireva ca  LiP 
koṭayo narakāṇāṃ tu pacyante tāsu pāpinaḥ 
anāśritāḥ śivaṃ rudraṃ śaṃkaraṃ nīlalohitam  LiP 
āśrayaṃ sarvabhūtānām avyayaṃ jagatāṃ patim 
puruṣaṃ paramātmānaṃ puruhūtaṃ puruṣṭutam  LiP 
tamasā kālarudrākhyaṃ rajasā kanakāṇḍajam 
sattvena sarvagaṃ viṣṇuṃ nirguṇatve maheśvaram  LiP 
kena gacchanti narakaṃ narāḥ kena mahāmate 
karmaṇākarmaṇā vāpi śrotuṃ kautūhalaṃ hi naḥ  LiP 
LiP  
sūta uvāca
rahasyaṃ vaḥ pravakṣyāmi bhavasyāmitatejasaḥ 
prabhāvaṃ śaṃkarasyādyaṃ saṃkṣepātsarvadarśinaḥ  LiP 
yoginaḥ sarvatattvajñāḥ paraṃ vairāgyamāsthitāḥ  LiP 
prāṇāyāmādibhiścāṣṭa sādhanaiḥ sahacāriṇaḥ  LiP 
karuṇādiguṇopetāḥ kṛtvāpi vividhāni te 
karmāṇi narakaṃ svargaṃ gacchantyeva svakarmaṇā  LiP 
prasādājjāyate jñānaṃ jñānādyogaḥ pravartate 
yogena jāyate muktiḥ prasādādakhilaṃ tataḥ  LiP 
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
prasādād yadi vijñānaṃ svarūpaṃ vaktumarhasi 
divyaṃ māheśvaraṃ caiva yogaṃ yogavidāṃ vara  LiP 
kathaṃ karoti bhagavān cintayā rahitaḥ śivaḥ 
prasādaṃ yogamārgeṇa kasminkāle nṛṇāṃ vibhuḥ  LiP 
romaharṣaṇa uvāca
devānāṃ ca ṛṣīṇāṃ ca pitṝṇāṃ saṃnidhau purā 
śailādinā tu kathitaṃ śṛṇvantu brahmasūnave  LiP 
vyāsāvatārāṇi tathā dvāparānte ca suvratāḥ 
yogācāryāvatārāṇi tathā tiṣye tu śūlinaḥ  LiP 
tatratatra vibhoḥ śiṣyāś catvāraḥ śamabhājanāḥ 
praśiṣyā bahavasteṣāṃ prasīdatyevamīśvaraḥ  LiP 
evaṃ kramāgataṃ jñānaṃ mukhādeva nṛṇāṃ vibhoḥ 
vaiśyāntaṃ brāhmaṇādyaṃ hi ghṛṇayā cānurūpataḥ  LiP 
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
dvāpare dvāpare vyāsāḥ ke vai kutrāntareṣu vai 
kalpeṣu kasminkalpe no vaktumarhasi cātra tān  LiP 
sūta uvāca
śṛṇvantu kalpe vārāhe dvijā vaivasvatāntare 
vyāsāṃś ca sāmprataṃ rudrāṃs tathā sarvāntareṣu vai  LiP 
vedānāṃ ca purāṇānāṃ tathā jñānapradarśakān 
yathākramaṃ pravakṣyāmi sarvāvarteṣu sāmpratam  LiP 
kratuḥ satyo bhārgavaś ca aṅgirāḥ savitā dvijāḥ 
mṛtyuḥ śatakraturdhīmān vasiṣṭho munipuṃgavaḥ  LiP 
sārasvatastridhāmā ca trivṛto munipuṃgavaḥ 
śatatejāḥ svayaṃdharmo nārāyaṇa iti śrutaḥ  LiP 
tarakṣuścāruṇirdhīmāṃs tathā devaḥ kṛtaṃjayaḥ 
ṛtaṃjayo bharadvājo gautamaḥ kavisattamaḥ  LiP 
vācaśravā muniḥ sākṣāt tathā śuṣmāyaṇiḥ śuciḥ 
tṛṇabindur munī rūkṣaḥ śaktiḥ śākteya uttaraḥ  LiP 
jātūkarṇyo hariḥ sākṣāt kṛṣṇadvaipāyano muniḥ 
vyāsāstvete ca śṛṇvantu kalau yogeśvarān kramāt  LiP 
asaṃkhyātā hi kalpeṣu vibhoḥ sarvāntareṣu ca 
kalau rudrāvatārāṇāṃ vyāsānāṃ kila gauravāt  LiP 
vaivasvatāntare kalpe vārāhe ye ca tān punaḥ 
avatārān pravakṣyāmi tathā sarvāntareṣu vai  LiP 
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
manvantarāṇi vārāhe vaktumarhasi sāmpratam 
tathaiva cordhvakalpeṣu siddhānvaivasvatāntare  LiP 
romaharṣaṇa uvāca
manuḥ svāyambhuvastvādyas tataḥ svārociṣo dvijāḥ 
uttamastāmasaścaiva raivatāścākṣuṣas tathā  LiP 
vaivasvataś ca sāvarṇir dharmaḥ sāvarṇikaḥ punaḥ 
piśaṅgaścāpiśaṅgābhaḥ śabalo varṇakas tathā  LiP 
aukārāntā akārādyā manavaḥ parikīrtitāḥ 
śvetaḥ pāṇḍus tathā raktas tāmraḥ pītaśca kāpilaḥ  LiP 
kṛṣṇaḥ śyāmas tathā dhūmraḥ sudhūmraś ca dvijottamāḥ 
apiśaṅgaḥ piśaṅgaś ca trivarṇaḥ śabalas tathā  LiP 
kālaṃdhurastu kathitā varṇato manavaḥ śubhāḥ 
nāmato varṇataścaiva varṇataḥ punareva ca  LiP 
svarātmānaḥ samākhyātāś cāntareśāḥ samāsataḥ 
vaivasvata ṛkārastu manuḥ kṛṣṇaḥ sureśvaraḥ  LiP 
saptamastasya vakṣyāmi yugāvarteṣu yoginaḥ 
samatīteṣu kalpeṣu tathā cānāgateṣu vai  LiP 
vārāhaḥ sāmprataṃ jñeyaḥ saptamāntarataḥ kramāt 
yogāvatārāṃś ca vibhoḥ śiṣyāṇāṃ saṃtatis tathā  LiP 
samprekṣya sarvakāleṣu tathāvarteṣu yoginām 
ādye śvetaḥ kalau rudraḥ sutāro madanas tathā  LiP 
suhotraḥ kaṅkaṇaścaiva lokākṣir munisattamāḥ 
jaigīṣavyo mahātejā bhagavān dadhivāhanaḥ  LiP 
ṛṣabhaś ca munirdhīmān ugraścātriḥ subālakaḥ 
gautamaścātha bhagavān sarvadevanamaskṛtaḥ  LiP 
vedaśīrṣaś ca gokarṇo guhāvāsī śikhaṇḍabhṛt 
jaṭāmālyaṭṭahāsaś ca dāruko lāṅgalī tathā  LiP 
mahākāyamuniḥ śūlī daṇḍī muṇḍīśvaraḥ svayam 
sahiṣṇuḥ somaśarmā ca nakulīśo jagadguruḥ  LiP 
vaivasvate 'ntare samyak proktā hi paramātmanaḥ 
yogācāryāvatārā ye sarvāvarteṣu suvratāḥ  LiP 
vyāsāścaivaṃ muniśreṣṭhā dvāpare dvāpare tvime 
yogeśvarāṇāṃ catvāraḥ śiṣyāḥ pratyekamavyayāḥ  LiP 
śvetaḥ śvetaśikhaṇḍī ca śvetāśvaḥ śvetalohitaḥ 
dundubhiḥ śatarūpaś ca ṛcīkaḥ ketumāṃs tathā  LiP 
viśokaśca vikeśaś ca vipāśaḥ pāpanāśanaḥ 
sumukho durmukhaścaiva durdamo duratikramaḥ  LiP 
sanakaś ca sanandaś ca prabhuryaś ca sanātanaḥ 
ṛbhuḥ sanatkumāraś ca sudhāmā virajās tathā  LiP 
śaṅkhapād vairajaścaiva meghaḥ sārasvatas tathā 
suvāhano muniśreṣṭho meghavāho mahādyutiḥ  LiP 
kapilaścāsuriścaiva tathā pañcaśikho muniḥ 
vālkalaś ca mahāyogī dharmātmāno mahaujasaḥ  LiP 
parāśaraś ca gargaś ca bhārgavaścāṅgirās tathā 
balabandhur nirāmitraḥ ketuśṛṅgastapodhanaḥ  LiP 
lambodaraś ca lambaśca lambākṣo lambakeśakaḥ 
sarvajñaḥ samabuddhiś ca sādhyaḥ sarvastathaiva ca  LiP 
sudhāmā kāśyapaścaiva vāsiṣṭho virajās tathā 
atrir devasadaścaiva śravaṇo 'tha śraviṣṭhakaḥ 
kuṇiś ca kuṇibāhuś ca kuśarīraḥ kunetrakaḥ  LiP 
kaśyapo 'pyuśanāścaiva cyavano 'tha bṛhaspatiḥ 
utathyo vāmadevaś ca mahāyogo mahābalaḥ  LiP 
vācaśravāḥ sudhīkaśca śyāvāśvaś ca yatīśvaraḥ 
hiraṇyanābhaḥ kauśalyo logākṣiḥ kuthumis tathā  LiP 
sumanturbarbarī vidvān kabandhaḥ kuśikaṃdharaḥ 
plakṣo dālbhyāyaṇiścaiva ketumān gopanas tathā  LiP 
bhallāvī madhupiṅgaśca śvetaketustaponidhiḥ 
uśiko bṛhadaśvaś ca devalaḥ kavireva ca  LiP 
śālihotro 'gniveśaśca yuvanāśvaḥ śaradvasuḥ 
chagalaḥ kuṇḍakarṇaś ca kumbhaścaiva pravāhakaḥ  LiP 
ulūko vidyutaścaiva maṇḍūko hyāśvalāyanaḥ 
akṣapādaḥ kumāraś ca ulūko vatsa eva ca  LiP 
kuśikaścaiva garbhaś ca mitraḥ kauruṣya eva ca 
śiṣyāstvete mahātmānaḥ sarvāvarteṣu yoginām  LiP 
vimalā brahmabhūyiṣṭhā jñānayogaparāyaṇāḥ 
ete pāśupatāḥ siddhā bhasmoddhūlitavigrahāḥ  LiP 
śiṣyāḥ praśiṣyāścaiteṣāṃ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ 
prāpya pāśupataṃ yogaṃ rudralokāya saṃsthitāḥ  LiP 
devādayaḥ piśācāntāḥ paśavaḥ parikīrtitāḥ 
teṣāṃ patitvātsarveśo bhavaḥ paśupatiḥ smṛtaḥ  LiP 
tena praṇīto rudreṇa paśūnāṃ patinā dvijāḥ 
yogaḥ pāśupato jñeyaḥ parāvaravibhūtaye  LiP

sūta uvāca
saṃkṣepataḥ pravakṣyāmi yogasthānāni sāmpratam 
kalpitāni śivenaiva hitāya jagatāṃ dvijāḥ  LiP 
galādadho vitastyā yan nābherupari cottamam 
yogasthānamadho nābher āvartaṃ madhyamaṃ bhruvoḥ  LiP 
sarvārthajñānaniṣpattir ātmano yoga ucyate 
ekāgratā bhaveccaiva sarvadā tatprasādataḥ  LiP 
prasādasya svarūpaṃ yat svasaṃvedyaṃ dvijottamāḥ 
vaktuṃ na śakyaṃ brahmādyaiḥ kramaśo jāyate nṛṇām  LiP 
yogaśabdena nirvāṇaṃ māheśaṃ padamucyate 
tasya heturṛṣerjñānaṃ jñānaṃ tasya prasādataḥ  LiP 
jñānena nirdahetpāpaṃ nirudhya viṣayān sadā 
niruddhendriyavṛttestu yogasiddhirbhaviṣyati  LiP 
yogo nirodho vṛtteṣu cittasya dvijasattamāḥ 
sādhanānyaṣṭadhā cāsya kathitānīha siddhaye  LiP 
yamastu prathamaḥ prokto dvitīyo niyamas tathā 
tṛtīyamāsanaṃ proktaṃ prāṇāyāmastataḥ param  LiP 
pratyāhāraṃ pañcamo vai dhāraṇā ca tataḥ parā 
dhyānaṃ saptamamityuktaṃ samādhistvaṣṭamaḥ smṛtaḥ  LiP 
tapasyuparamaścaiva yama ityabhidhīyate 
ahiṃsā prathamo hetur yamasya yamināṃ varāḥ  LiP 
satyamasteyamaparaṃ brahmacaryāparigrahau 
niyamasyāpi vai mūlaṃ yama eva na saṃśayaḥ  LiP 
ātmavat sarvabhūtānāṃ hitāyaiva pravartanam 
ahiṃsaiṣā samākhyātā yā cātmajñānasiddhidā  LiP 
dṛṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ cānumitaṃ svānubhūtaṃ yathārthataḥ 
kathanaṃ satyamityuktaṃ parapīḍāvivarjitam  LiP 
nāślīlaṃ kīrtayedevaṃ brāhmaṇānāmiti śrutiḥ 
paradoṣān parijñāya na vadediti cāparam  LiP 
anādānaṃ parasvānām āpadyapi vicārataḥ 
manasā karmaṇā vācā tadasteyaṃ samāsataḥ  LiP 
maithunasyāpravṛttirhi manovākkāyakarmaṇā 
brahmacaryamiti proktaṃ yatīnāṃ brahmacāriṇām  LiP 
iha vaikhānasānāṃ ca vidārāṇāṃ viśeṣataḥ 
sadārāṇāṃ gṛhasthānaṃ tathaiva ca vadāmi vaḥ  LiP 
svadāre vidhivatkṛtvā nivṛttiścānyataḥ sadā 
manasā karmaṇā vācā brahmacaryamiti smṛtam  LiP 
medhyā svanārī sambhogaṃ kṛtvā snānaṃ samācaret 
evaṃ gṛhastho yuktātmā brahmacārī na saṃśayaḥ  LiP 
ahiṃsāpyevamevaiṣā dvijagurvagnipūjane 
vidhinā yādṛśī hiṃsā sā tvahiṃsā iti smṛtā  LiP 
striyaḥ sadā parityājyāḥ saṅgaṃ naiva ca kārayet 
kuṇapeṣu yathā cittaṃ tathā kuryādvicakṣaṇaḥ  LiP 
viṇmūtrotsargakāleṣu bahirbhūmau yathā matiḥ 
tathā kāryā ratau cāpi svadāre cānyataḥ kutaḥ  LiP 
aṅgārasadṛśī nārī ghṛtakumbhasamaḥ pumān 
tasmānnārīṣu saṃsargaṃ dūrataḥ parivarjayet  LiP 
bhogena tṛptirnaivāsti viṣayāṇāṃ vicārataḥ 
tasmādvirāgaḥ kartavyo manasā karmaṇā girā  LiP 
na jātu kāmaḥ kāmānām upabhogena śāmyati 
haviṣā kṛṣṇavartmeva bhūya evābhivardhate  LiP 
tasmāttyāgaḥ sadā kāryas tv amṛtatvāya yoginā 
avirakto yato martyo nānāyoniṣu vartate  LiP 
tyāgenaivāmṛtatvaṃ hi śrutismṛtividāṃ varāḥ 
karmaṇā prajayā nāsti dravyeṇa dvijasattamāḥ  LiP 
tasmādvirāgaḥ kartavyo manovākkāyakarmaṇā 
ṛtau ṛtau nivṛttistu brahmacaryamiti smṛtam  LiP 
yamāḥ saṃkṣepataḥ proktā niyamāṃś ca vadāmi vaḥ 
śaucamijyā tapo dānaṃ svādhyāyopasthanigrahaḥ  LiP 
vratopavāsamaunaṃ ca snānaṃ ca niyamā daśa 
niyamaḥ syādanīhā ca śaucaṃ tuṣṭistapas tathā  LiP 
japaḥ śivapraṇīdhānaṃ padmakādyaṃ tathāsanam 
bāhyamābhyantaraṃ proktaṃ śaucamābhyantaraṃ varam  LiP 
bāhyaśaucena yuktaḥ saṃs tathā cābhyantaraṃ caret 
āgneyaṃ vāruṇaṃ brāhmaṃ kartavyaṃ śivapūjakaiḥ  LiP

ā dehāntaṃ mṛdālipya tīrthatoyeṣu sarvadā  LiP

ātmajñānāmbhasi snātvā sakṛdālipya bhāvataḥ 
suvairāgyamṛdā śuddhaḥ śaucamevaṃ prakīrtitam  LiP 
śuddhasya siddhayo dṛṣṭā naivāśuddhasya siddhayaḥ 
nyāyenāgatayā vṛttyā saṃtuṣṭo yastu suvrataḥ  LiP 
saṃtoṣastasya satatam atītārthasya cāsmṛtiḥ 
cāndrāyaṇādinipuṇas tapāṃsi suśubhāni ca  LiP

vācikaścādhamo mukhya upāṃśuścottamottamaḥ  LiP

tathā śivapraṇīdhānaṃ manovākkāyakarmaṇā  LiP 
śivajñānaṃ gurorbhaktir acalā supratiṣṭhitā 
nigraho hyapahṛtyāśu prasaktānīndriyāṇi ca  LiP 
viṣayeṣu samāsena pratyāhāraḥ prakīrtitaḥ

tasyāḥ svāsthyena dhyānaṃ ca samādhiś ca vicārataḥ 
tatraikacittatā dhyānaṃ pratyayāntaravarjitam  LiP 
cidbhāsamarthamātrasya dehaśūnyamiva sthitam 
samādhiḥ sarvahetuś ca prāṇāyāma iti smṛtaḥ  LiP 
prāṇaḥ svadehajo vāyur yamastasya nirodhanam 
tridhā dvijairyamaḥ prokto mando madhyottamas tathā  LiP 
prāṇāpānanirodhastu prāṇāyāmaḥ prakīrtitaḥ 
prāṇāyāmasya mānaṃ tu mātrādvādaśakaṃ smṛtam  LiP 
nīco dvādaśamātrastu uddhāto dvādaśaḥ smṛtaḥ 
madhyamas tu dviruddhātaś caturviṃśatimātrakaḥ  LiP 
mukhyastu yastriruddhātaḥ ṣaṭtriṃśanmātra ucyate 
prasvedakampanotthāna janakaśca yathākramam  LiP 
ānandodbhavayogārthaṃ nidrāghūrṇistathaiva ca 
romāñcadhvanisaṃviddha svāṅgamoṭanakampanam  LiP 
bhramaṇaṃ svedajanyā sā saṃvinmūrchā bhavedyadā 
tadottamottamaḥ proktaḥ prāṇāyāmaḥ suśobhanaḥ  LiP 
sagarbho 'garbha ityuktaḥ sajapo vijapaḥ kramāt 
ibho vā śarabho vāpi durādharṣo 'tha kesarī  LiP 
gṛhīto damyamānastu yathāsvasthastu jāyate 
tathā samīraṇo 'svastho durādharṣaś ca yoginām  LiP 
nyāyataḥ sevyamānastu sa evaṃ svasthatāṃ vrajet 
yathaiva mṛgarāṅnāgaḥ śarabho vāpi durmadaḥ  LiP 
kālāntaravaśādyogād damyate paramādarāt 
tathā paricayātsvāsthyaṃ samatvaṃ cādhigacchati  LiP 
yogādabhyasate yastu vyasanaṃ naiva jāyate

manovākkāyajān doṣān karturdehaṃ ca rakṣati

doṣāttasmācca naśyanti niśvāsastena jīryate

śāntiḥ praśāntirdīptiś ca prasādaś ca tathā kramāt

prakāśo dīptirityuktaḥ sarvataḥ sarvadā dvijāḥ

eteṣāṃ yaḥ prasādastu marutāmiti saṃsmṛtaḥ  LiP

apānayatyapānastu āhārādīn krameṇa ca  LiP

udvejayati marmāṇi udāno 'yaṃ prakīrtitaḥ  LiP 
samaṃ nayati gātrāṇi samānaḥ pañca vāyavaḥ 
udgāre nāga ākhyātaḥ kūrma unmīlane tu saḥ  LiP 
kṛkalaḥ kṣutakāyaiva devadatto vijṛmbhaṇe

asyā buddheḥ prasādastu prāṇāyāmena sidhyati  LiP

manute manyate yasmān matirmatimatāṃvarāḥ 
arthaṃ bodhayate yacca budhyate buddhirucyate  LiP 
asyā buddheḥ prasādastu prāṇāyāmena sidhyati 
doṣānvinirdahetsarvān prāṇāyāmādasau yamī  LiP 
pātakaṃ dhāraṇābhistu pratyāhāreṇa nirdahet 
viṣayānviṣavaddhyātvā dhyānenānīśvarān guṇān  LiP 
samādhinā yatiśreṣṭhāḥ prajñāvṛddhiṃ vivardhayet 
sthānaṃ labdhvaiva kurvīta yogāṣṭāṅgāni vai kramāt  LiP 
labdhvāsanāni vidhivad yogasiddhyartham ātmavit 
ādeśakāle yogasya darśanaṃ hi na vidyate  LiP 
agnyabhyāse jale vāpi śuṣkaparṇacaye tathā 
jantuvyāpte śmaśāne ca jīrṇagoṣṭhe catuṣpathe  LiP 
saśabde sabhaye vāpi caityavalmīkasaṃcaye 
aśubhe durjanākrānte maśakādisamanvite  LiP 
nācareddehabādhāyāṃ daurmanasyādisambhave 
sugupte tu śubhe ramye guhāyāṃ parvatasya tu  LiP 
bhavakṣetre sugupte vā bhavārāme vane 'pi vā 
gṛhe tu suśubhe deśe vijane jantuvarjite  LiP 
atyantanirmale samyak supralipte vicitrite 
darpaṇodarasaṃkāśe kṛṣṇāgarusudhūpite  LiP 
nānāpuṣpasamākīrṇe vitānopari śobhite 
phalapallavamūlāḍhye kuśapuṣpasamanvite  LiP 
samāsanastho yogāṅgāny abhyaseddhṛṣitaḥ svayam 
praṇipatya guruṃ paścād bhavaṃ devīṃ vināyakam  LiP 
yogīśvarān saśiṣyāṃś ca yogaṃ yuñjīta yogavit 
āsanaṃ svastikaṃ baddhvā padmamardhāsanaṃ tu vā  LiP 
samajānus tathā dhīmān ekajānurathāpivā 
samaṃ dṛḍhāsano bhūtvā saṃhṛtya caraṇāvubhau  LiP 
saṃvṛtāsyopabaddhākṣa uro viṣṭabhya cāgrataḥ 
pārṣṇibhyāṃ vṛṣaṇau rakṣaṃs tathā prajananaṃ punaḥ  LiP 
kiṃcidunnāmitaśira dantairdantānna saṃspṛśet 
samprekṣya nāsikāgraṃ svaṃ diśaścānavalokayan  LiP 
tamaḥ pracchādya rajasā rajaḥ sattvena chādayet 
tataḥ sattvasthito bhūtvā śivadhyānaṃ samabhyaset  LiP 
oṃkāravācyaṃ paramaṃ śuddhaṃ dīpaśikhākṛtim 
dhyāyedvai puṇḍarīkasya karṇikāyāṃ samāhitaḥ  LiP 
nābheradhastādvā vidvān dhyātvā kamalamuttamam 
tryaṅgule cāṣṭakoṇaṃ vā pañcakoṇamathāpi vā  LiP 
trikoṇaṃ ca tathāgneyaṃ saumyaṃ sauraṃ svaśaktibhiḥ 
sauraṃ saumya tathāgneyam atha vānukrameṇa tu  LiP 
āgneyaṃ ca tataḥ sauraṃ saumyamevaṃ vidhānataḥ 
agneradhaḥ prakalpyaivaṃ dharmādīnāṃ catuṣṭayam  LiP 
guṇatrayaṃ krameṇaiva maṇḍalopari bhāvayet 
sattvasthaṃ cintayedrudraṃ svaśaktyā parimaṇḍitam  LiP 
nābhau vātha gale vāpi bhrūmadhye vā yathāvidhi 
lalāṭaphalikāyāṃ vā mūrdhni dhyānaṃ samācaret  LiP 
dvidale ṣoḍaśāre vā dvādaśāre krameṇa tu 
daśāre vā ṣaḍasre vā caturasre smarecchivam  LiP 
kanakābhe tathāgāra saṃnibhe susite 'pi vā 
dvādaśādityasaṃkāśe candrabimbasame 'pi vā  LiP 
vidyutkoṭinibhe sthāne cintayetparameśvaram 
agnivarṇe 'thavā vidyud valayābhe samāhitaḥ  LiP 
vajrakoṭiprabhe sthāne padmarāganibhe 'pi vā 
nīlalohitabimbe vā yogī dhyānaṃ samabhyaset  LiP 
maheśvaraṃ hṛdi dhyāyen nābhipadme sadāśivam 
candracūḍaṃ lalāṭe tu bhrūmadhye śaṃkaraṃ svayam  LiP 
divye ca śāśvatasthāne śivadhyānaṃ samabhyaset 
nirmalaṃ niṣkalaṃ brahma suśāntaṃ jñānarūpiṇam  LiP 
alakṣaṇamanirdeśyam aṇoralpataraṃ śubham 
nirālambam atarkyaṃ ca vināśotpattivarjitam  LiP 
kaivalyaṃ caiva nirvāṇaṃ niḥśreyasam anuttamam 
amṛtaṃ cākṣaraṃ brahma hy apunarbhavam adbhutam  LiP 
mahānandaṃ parānandaṃ yogānandamanāmayam 
heyopādeyarahitaṃ sūkṣmātsūkṣmataraṃ śivam  LiP 
svayaṃvedyamavedyaṃ tac chivaṃ jñānamayaṃ param 
atīndriyam anābhāsaṃ paraṃ tattvaṃ parātparam  LiP 
sarvopādhivinirmuktaṃ dhyānagamyaṃ vicārataḥ 
advayaṃ tamasaścaiva parastātsaṃsthitaṃ param  LiP 
manasyevaṃ mahādevaṃ hṛtpadme vāpi cintayet 
nābhau sadāśivaṃ cāpi sarvadevātmakaṃ vibhum  LiP 
dehamadhye śivaṃ devaṃ śuddhajñānamayaṃ vibhum 
kanyasenaiva mārgeṇa codghātenāpi śaṃkaram  LiP 
kramaśaḥ kanyasenaiva madhyamenāpi suvrataḥ 
uttamenāpi vai vidvān kumbhakena samabhyaset  LiP 
dvātriṃśad recayeddhīmān hṛdi nābhau samāhitaḥ 
recakaṃ pūrakaṃ tyaktvā kumbhakaṃ ca dvijottamāḥ  LiP 
sākṣātsamarasenaiva dehamadhye smarecchivam 
ekībhāvaṃ sametyaivaṃ tatra yadrasasambhavam  LiP 
ānandaṃ brahmaṇo vidvān sākṣātsamarase sthitaḥ 
dhāraṇā dvādaśāyāmā dhyānaṃ dvādaśa dhāraṇam  LiP 
dhyānaṃ dvādaśakaṃ yāvat samādhir abhidhīyate 
athavā jñānināṃ viprāḥ samparkādeva jāyate  LiP 
prayatnādvā tayostulyaṃ cirādvā hyacirāddvijāḥ 
yogāntarāyās tasyātha jāyante yuñjataḥ punaḥ  LiP 
naśyanty abhyāsatas te 'pi praṇidhānena vai guroḥ  LiP

sūta uvāca
ālasyaṃ prathamaṃ paścād vyādhipīḍā prajāyate 
pramādaḥ saṃśayasthāne cittasyehānavasthitiḥ  LiP 
aśraddhādarśanaṃ bhrāntir duḥkhaṃ ca trividhaṃ tataḥ 
daurmanasyamayogyeṣu viṣayeṣu ca yogyatā  LiP 
daśadhābhiprajāyante muneryogāntarāyakāḥ 
ālasyaṃ cāpravṛttiś ca gurutvātkāyacittayoḥ  LiP 
vyādhayo dhātuvaiṣamyāt karmajā doṣajās tathā 
pramādastu samādhestu sādhanānām abhāvanam  LiP 
idaṃ vetyubhayaspṛktaṃ vijñānaṃ sthānasaṃśayaḥ 
anavasthitacittatvam apratiṣṭhā hi yoginaḥ  LiP 
labdhāyāmapi bhūmau ca cittasya bhavabandhanāt 
aśraddhābhāvarahitā vṛttirvai sādhaneṣu ca  LiP 
sādhye cittasya hi gurau jñānācāraśivādiṣu 
viparyayajñānamiti bhrāntidarśanam ucyate  LiP 
anātmanyātmavijñānam ajñānāttasya saṃnidhau 
duḥkhamādhyātmikaṃ proktaṃ tathā caivādhibhautikam  LiP 
ādhidaivikamityuktaṃ trividhaṃ sahajaṃ punaḥ 
icchāvighātātsaṃkṣobhaś cetasastadudāhṛtam  LiP 
daurmanasyaṃ niroddhavyaṃ vairāgyeṇa pareṇa tu 
tamasā rajasā caiva saṃspṛṣṭaṃ durmanaḥ smṛtam  LiP 
tadā manasi saṃjātaṃ daurmanasyamiti smṛtam 
haṭhātsvīkaraṇaṃ kṛtvā yogyāyogyavivekataḥ  LiP 
viṣayeṣu vicitreṣu jantorviṣayalolatā 
antarāyā iti khyātā yogasyaite hi yoginām  LiP 
atyantotsāhayuktasya naśyanti na ca saṃśayaḥ 
pranaṣṭeṣvantarāyeṣu dvijāḥ paścāddhi yoginaḥ  LiP 
upasargāḥ pravartante sarve te 'siddhisūcakāḥ 
pratibhā prathamā siddhir dvitīyā śravaṇā smṛtā  LiP 
vārttā tṛtīyā viprendrās turīyā ceha darśanā 
āsvādā pañcamī proktā vedanā ṣaṣṭhikā smṛtā  LiP 
svalpaṣaṭsiddhisaṃtyāgāt siddhidāḥ siddhayo muneḥ 
pratibhā pratibhāvṛtiḥ pratibhāva iti sthitiḥ  LiP 
buddhirvivecanā vedyaṃ budhyate buddhirucyate 
sūkṣme vyavahite 'tīte viprakṛṣṭe tvanāgate  LiP 
sarvatra sarvadā jñānaṃ pratibhānukrameṇa tu 
śravaṇātsarvaśabdānām aprayatnena yoginaḥ  LiP 
hrasvadīrghaplutādīnāṃ guhyānāṃ śravaṇādapi 
sparśasyādhigamo yas tu vedanā tūpapāditā  LiP 
darśanāddivyarūpāṇāṃ darśanaṃ cāprayatnataḥ 
saṃviddivyarase tasminn āsvādo hyaprayatnataḥ  LiP 
vārttā ca divyagandhānāṃ tanmātrā buddhisaṃvidā 
vindante yoginastasmād ābrahmabhuvanaṃ dvijāḥ  LiP 
jagatyasmin hi dehasthaṃ catuḥṣaṣṭiguṇaṃ samam 
aupasargikam eteṣu guṇeṣu guṇitaṃ dvijāḥ  LiP 
saṃtyājyaṃ sarvathā sarvam aupasargikamātmanaḥ 
paiśāce pārthivaṃ cāpyaṃ rākṣasānāṃ pure dvijāḥ  LiP 
yākṣe tu taijasaṃ proktaṃ gāndharve śvasanātmakam 
aindre vyomātmakaṃ sarvaṃ saumye caiva tu mānasam  LiP 
prājāpatye tvahaṅkāraṃ brāhme bodhamanuttamam 
ādye cāṣṭau dvitīye ca tathā ṣoḍaśarūpakam  LiP 
caturviṃśattṛtīye tu dvātriṃśacca caturthake 
catvāriṃśat pañcame tu bhūtamātrātmakaṃ smṛtam  LiP 
gandho rasas tathā rūpaṃ śabdaḥ sparśastathaiva ca 
pratyekamaṣṭadhā siddhaṃ pañcame tacchatakratoḥ  LiP 
tathāṣṭacatvāriṃśac ca ṣaṭpañcāśattathaiva ca 
catuḥṣaṣṭiguṇaṃ brāhmaṃ labhate dvijasattamāḥ  LiP 
aupasargikam ā brahma bhuvaneṣu parityajet 
lokeṣvālokya yogena yogavitparamaṃ sukham  LiP 
sthūlatā hrasvatā bālyaṃ vārdhakyaṃ yauvanaṃ tathā 
nānājātisvarūpaṃ ca caturbhir dehadhāraṇam  LiP 
pārthivāṃśaṃ vinā nityaṃ surabhir gandhasaṃyutaḥ 
etadaṣṭaguṇaṃ proktam aiśvaryaṃ pārthivaṃ mahat  LiP 
jale nivasanaṃ yadvad bhūmyāmiva vinirgamaḥ 
icchecchaktaḥ svayaṃ pātuṃ samudramapi nāturaḥ  LiP 
yatrecchati jagatyasmiṃs tatrāsya jaladarśanam 
yadyadvastu samādāya bhoktumicchati kāmataḥ  LiP 
tattadrasānvitaṃ tasya trayāṇāṃ dehadhāraṇam 
bhāṇḍaṃ vinātha hastena jalapiṇḍasya dhāraṇam  LiP 
avraṇatvaṃ śarīrasya pārthivena samanvitam 
etat ṣoḍaśakaṃ proktam āpyamaiśvaryamuttamam  LiP 
dehādagnivinirmāṇaṃ tattāpabhayavarjitam 
lokaṃ dagdhamapīhānyad adagdhaṃ svavidhānataḥ  LiP 
jalamadhye hutavahaṃ cādhāya parirakṣaṇam 
agninigrahaṇaṃ haste smṛtimātreṇa cāgamaḥ  LiP 
bhasmībhūtavinirmāṇaṃ yathāpūrvaṃ sakāmataḥ 
dvābhyāṃ rūpaviniṣpattir vinā taistribhir ātmanaḥ  LiP 
caturviṃśātmakaṃ hyetat taijasaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ 
manogatitvaṃ bhūtānām antarnivasanaṃ tathā  LiP 
parvatādimahābhāra skandhenodvahanaṃ punaḥ 
laghutvaṃ ca gurutvaṃ ca pāṇibhyāṃ vāyudhāraṇam  LiP 
aṅgulyagranighātena bhūmeḥ sarvatra kaṃpanam 
ekena dehaniṣpattir vātaiśvaryaṃ smṛtaṃ budhaiḥ  LiP 
chāyāvihīnaniṣpattir indriyāṇāṃ ca darśanam 
ākāśagamanaṃ nityam indriyārthaiḥ samanvitam  LiP 
dūre ca śabdagrahaṇaṃ sarvaśabdāvagāhanam 
tanmātraliṅgagrahaṇaṃ sarvaprāṇinidarśanam  LiP 
aindram aiśvaryam ityuktam etairuktaḥ purātanaḥ 
yathākāmopalabdhiś ca yathākāmavinirgamaḥ  LiP 
sarvatrābhibhavaścaiva sarvaguhyanidarśanam 
kāmānurūpanirmāṇaṃ vaśitvaṃ priyadarśanam  LiP 
saṃsāradarśanaṃ caiva mānasaṃ guṇalakṣaṇam 
chedanaṃ tāḍanaṃ bandhaṃ saṃsāraparivartanam  LiP 
sarvabhūtaprasādaś ca mṛtyukālajayas tathā 
prājāpatyamidaṃ proktam āhaṅkārikamuttamam  LiP 
akāraṇajagatsṛṣṭis tathānugraha eva ca 
pralayaścādhikāraś ca lokavṛttapravartanam  LiP 
asādṛśyamidaṃ vyaktaṃ nirmāṇaṃ ca pṛthakpṛthak 
saṃsārasya ca kartṛtvaṃ brāhmam etad anuttamam  LiP 
etāvattattvamityuktaṃ prādhānyaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ padam 
brahmaṇā tadguṇaṃ śakyaṃ vettumanyairna śakyate  LiP 
vidyate tatparaṃ śaivaṃ viṣṇunā nāvagamyate 
asaṃkhyeyaguṇaṃ śuddhaṃ ko jānīyācchivātmakam  LiP 
vyutthāne siddhayaścaitā hy upasargāś ca kīrtitāḥ 
niroddhavyāḥ prayatnena vairāgyeṇa pareṇa tu  LiP 
nāśātiśayatāṃ jñātvā viṣayeṣu bhayeṣu ca 
aśraddhayā tyajetsarvaṃ virakta iti kīrtitaḥ  LiP 
vaitṛṣṇyaṃ puruṣe khyātaṃ guṇavaitṛṣṇyamucyate 
vairāgyeṇaiva saṃtyājyāḥ siddhayaścaupasargikāḥ  LiP 
aupasargikam ā brahma bhuvaneṣu parityajet 
nirudhyaiva tyajetsarvaṃ prasīdati maheśvaraḥ  LiP 
prasanne vimalā muktir vairāgyeṇa pareṇa vai 
athavānugrahārthaṃ ca līlārthaṃ vā tadā muniḥ  LiP 
anirudhya viceṣṭedyaḥ so 'pyevaṃ hi sukhī bhavet 
kvacidbhūmiṃ parityajya hy ākāśe krīḍate śriyā  LiP 
udgirecca kvacidvedān sūkṣmānarthān samāsataḥ 
kvacicchrute tadarthena ślokabandhaṃ karoti saḥ  LiP 
kvaciddaṇḍakabandhaṃ tu kuryādbandhaṃ sahasraśaḥ 
mṛgapakṣisamūhasya rutajñānaṃ ca vindati  LiP 
brahmādyaṃ sthāvarāntaṃ ca hastāmalakavadbhavet 
bahunātra kimuktena vijñānāni sahasraśaḥ  LiP 
utpadyante muniśreṣṭhā munestasya mahātmanaḥ 
abhyāsenaiva vijñānaṃ viśuddhaṃ ca sthiraṃ bhavet  LiP 
tejorūpāṇi sarvāṇi sarvaṃ paśyati yogavit 
devabimbānyanekāni vimānāni sahasraśaḥ  LiP 
paśyati brahmaviṣṇvindra yamāgnivaruṇādikān 
grahanakṣatratārāś ca bhuvanāni sahasraśaḥ  LiP 
pātālatalasaṃsthāś ca samādhisthaḥ sa paśyati 
ātmavidyāpradīpena svasthenācalanena tu  LiP 
prasādāmṛtapūrṇena sattvapātrasthitena tu 
tamo nihatya puruṣaḥ paśyati hyātmanīśvaram  LiP 
tasya prasādāddharmaś ca aiśvaryaṃ jñānameva ca

na śakyo vistaro vaktuṃ varṣāṇāmayutairapi

sūta uvāca
satāṃ jitātmanāṃ sākṣād dvijātīnāṃ dvijottamāḥ 
dharmajñānāṃ ca sādhūnām ācāryāṇāṃ śivātmanām  LiP 
dayāvatāṃ dvijaśreṣṭhās tathā caiva tapasvinām 
saṃnyāsināṃ viraktānāṃ jñānināṃ vaśagātmanām  LiP 
dānināṃ caiva dāntānāṃ trayāṇāṃ satyavādinām 
alubdhānāṃ sayogānāṃ śrutismṛtividāṃ dvijāḥ  LiP 
śrautasmārtāviruddhānāṃ prasīdati maheśvaraḥ 
saditi brahmaṇaḥ śabdas tadante ye labhantyuta  LiP 
sāyujyaṃ brahmaṇo yāti tena santaḥ pracakṣate 
daśātmake ye viṣaye sādhane cāṣṭalakṣaṇe  LiP 
na krudhyanti na hṛṣyanti jitātmānastu te smṛtāḥ 
sāmānyeṣu ca dravyeṣu tathā vaiśeṣikeṣu ca  LiP 
brahmakṣatraviśo yasmād yuktāstasmāddvijātayaḥ 
varṇāśrameṣu yuktasya svargādisukhakāriṇaḥ  LiP 
śrautasmārtasya dharmasya jñānāddharmajña ucyate 
vidyāyāḥ sādhanātsādhu brahmacārī gurorhitaḥ  LiP 
kriyāṇāṃ sādhanāccaiva gṛhasthaḥ sādhurucyate 
sādhanāttapaso 'raṇye sādhurvaikhānasaḥ smṛtaḥ  LiP 
yatamāno yatiḥ sādhuḥ smṛto yogasya sādhanāt 
evamāśramadharmāṇāṃ sādhanātsādhavaḥ smṛtāḥ  LiP 
gṛhastho brahmacārī ca vānaprastho yatis tathā 
dharmādharmāviha proktau śabdāvetau kriyātmakau  LiP 
kuśalākuśalaṃ karma dharmādharmāviti smṛtau 
dhāraṇārthe mahān hy eṣa dharmaśabdaḥ prakīrtitaḥ  LiP 
adhāraṇe mahattve ca adharma iti cocyate 
atreṣṭaprāpako dharma ācāryairupadiśyate  LiP 
adharmaścāniṣṭaphalo hy ācāryairupadiśyate 
vṛddhāścālolupāścaiva ātmavanto hyadāmbhikāḥ  LiP 
samyagvinītā ṛjavas tānācāryān pracakṣate 
svayamācarate yasmād ācāre sthāpayatyapi  LiP 
ācinoti ca śāstrārthān ācāryastena cocyate 
vijñeyaṃ śravaṇācchrautaṃ smaraṇātsmārtamucyate  LiP 
ijyā vedātmakaṃ śrautaṃ smārtaṃ varṇāśramātmakam 
dṛṣṭvānurūpamarthaṃ yaḥ pṛṣṭo naivāpi gūhati  LiP 
yathādṛṣṭapravādastu satyaṃ laiṅge 'tra paṭhyate 
brahmacaryaṃ tathā maunaṃ nirāhāratvameva ca  LiP 
ahiṃsā sarvataḥ śāntis tapa ityabhidhīyate 
ātmavat sarvabhūteṣu yo hitāyāhitāya ca  LiP 
vartate tvasakṛdvṛttiḥ kṛtsnā hyeṣā dayā smṛtā 
yadyadiṣṭatamaṃ dravyaṃ nyāyenaivāgataṃ kramāt  LiP 
tattadguṇavate deyaṃ dātustaddānalakṣaṇam 
dānaṃ trividhamityetat kaniṣṭhajyeṣṭhamadhyamam  LiP 
kāruṇyātsarvabhūtebhyaḥ saṃvibhāgastu madhyamaḥ 
śrutismṛtibhyāṃ vihito dharmo varṇāśramātmakaḥ  LiP 
śiṣṭācārāviruddhaś ca sa dharmaḥ sādhurucyate 
māyākarmaphalatyāgī śivātmā parikīrtitaḥ  LiP 
nivṛttaḥ sarvasaṅgebhyo yukto yogī prakīrtitaḥ 
asakto bhayato yastu viṣayeṣu vicārya ca  LiP 
alubdhaḥ saṃyamī proktaḥ prārthito 'pi samantataḥ 
ātmārthaṃ vā parārthaṃ vā indriyāṇīha yasya vai  LiP 
na mithyā sampravartante śamasyaiva tu lakṣaṇam 
anudvigno hyaniṣṭeṣu tatheṣṭānnābhinandati  LiP 
prītitāpaviṣādebhyo vinivṛttirviraktatā 
saṃnyāsaḥ karmaṇāṃ nyāsaḥ kṛtānāmakṛtaiḥ saha  LiP 
kuśalākuśalānāṃ tu prahāṇaṃ nyāsa ucyate 
avyaktādyaviśeṣānte vikāre 'sminnacetane  LiP 
cetanācetanānyatva vijñānaṃ jñānamucyate 
evaṃ tu jñānayuktasya śraddhāyuktasya śaṅkaraḥ  LiP 
prasīdati na saṃdeho dharmaścāyaṃ dvijottamāḥ 
kiṃ tu guhyatamaṃ vakṣye sarvatra parameśvare  LiP 
bhave bhaktirna saṃdehas tayā yukto vimucyate 
ayogyasyāpi bhagavān bhaktasya parameśvaraḥ  LiP 
prasīdati na saṃdeho nigṛhya vividhaṃ tamaḥ 
jñānamadhyāpanaṃ homo dhyānaṃ yajñastapaḥ śrutam  LiP 
dānamadhyayanaṃ sarvaṃ bhavabhaktyai na saṃśayaḥ 
cāndrāyaṇasahasraiś ca prājāpatyaśatais tathā  LiP 
māsopavāsaiścānyairvā bhaktirmunivarottamāḥ 
abhaktā bhagavatyasmiṃl loke giriguhāśaye  LiP 
patanti cātmabhogārthaṃ bhakto bhāvena mucyate 
bhaktānāṃ darśanādeva nṛṇāṃ svargādayo dvijāḥ  LiP 
na durlabhā na sandeho bhaktānāṃ kiṃ punas tathā 
brahmaviṣṇusurendrāṇāṃ tathānyeṣāmapi sthitiḥ  LiP 
bhaktyā eva munīnāṃ ca balasaubhāgyameva ca 
bhavena ca tathā proktaṃ samprekṣyomāṃ pinākinā  LiP 
devyai devena madhuraṃ vārāṇasyāṃ purā dvijāḥ 
avimukte samāsīnā rudreṇa paramātmanā  LiP 
rudrāṇī rudramāhedaṃ labdhvā vārāṇasīṃ purīm 
śrīdevyuvāca
kena vaśyo mahādeva pūjyo dṛśyastvamīśvaraḥ  LiP 
tapasā vidyayā vāpi yogeneha vada prabho 
sūta uvāca
niśamya vacanaṃ tasyās tathā hyālokya pārvatīm  LiP 
āha bālendutilakaḥ pūrṇenduvadanāṃ hasan 
smṛtvātha menayā patnyā girergāṃ kathitāṃ purā  LiP 
cirakālasthitiṃ prekṣya girau devyā mahātmanaḥ 
devi labdhā purī ramyā tvayā yatpraṣṭumarhasi  LiP 
sthānārthaṃ kathitaṃ mātrā vismṛteha vilāsini 
purā pitāmahenāpi pṛṣṭaḥ praśnavatāṃ vare  LiP 
yathā tvayādya vai pṛṣṭo draṣṭuṃ brahmātmakaṃ tvaham 
śvete śvetena varṇena dṛṣṭvā kalpe tu māṃ śubhe  LiP 
sadyojātaṃ tathā rakte raktaṃ vāmaṃ pitāmahaḥ 
pīte tatpuruṣaṃ pītam aghore kṛṣṇamīśvaram  LiP 
īśānaṃ viśvarūpākhyo viśvarūpaṃ tadāha mām  LiP 
pitāmaha uvāca
vāma tatpuruṣāghora sadyojāta maheśvara 
dṛṣṭo mayā tvaṃ gāyatryā devadeva maheśvara 
kena vaśyo mahādeva dhyeyaḥ kutra ghṛṇānidhe  LiP 
dṛśyaḥ pūjyas tathā devyā vaktumarhasi śaṅkara 
śrībhagavānuvāca
avocaṃ śraddhayaiveti vaśyo vārijasaṃbhava  LiP 
dhyeyo liṅge tvayā dṛṣṭe viṣṇunā payasāṃ nidhau 
pūjyaḥ pañcāsyarūpeṇa pavitraiḥ pañcabhirdvijaiḥ  LiP 
bhava bhaktyādya dṛṣṭo 'haṃ tvayāṇḍaja jagadguro 
so 'pi māmāha bhāvārthaṃ dattaṃ tasmai mayā purā  LiP 
bhāvaṃ bhāvena deveśi dṛṣṭavānmāṃ hṛdīśvaram 
tasmāttu śraddhayā vaśyo dṛśyaḥ śreṣṭhagireḥ sute  LiP 
pūjyo liṅge na saṃdehaḥ sarvadā śraddhayā dvijaiḥ 
śraddhā dharmaḥ paraḥ sūkṣmaḥ śraddhā jñānaṃ hutaṃ tapaḥ  LiP 
śraddhā svargaś ca mokṣaś ca dṛśyo 'haṃ śraddhayā sadā  LiP

ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
kathaṃ vai dṛṣṭavānbrahmā sadyojātaṃ maheśvaram 
vāmadevaṃ mahātmānaṃ purāṇapuruṣottamam  LiP 
aghoraṃ ca tatheśānaṃ yathāvadvaktumarhasi 
sūta uvāca
ekonatriṃśakaḥ kalpo vijñeyaḥ śvetalohitaḥ  LiP 
tasmiṃstatparamaṃ dhyānaṃ dhyāyato brahmaṇastadā 
utpannastu śikhāyuktaḥ kumāraḥ śvetalohitaḥ  LiP 
taṃ dṛṣṭvā puruṣaṃ śrīmān brahmā vai viśvatomukhaḥ 
hṛdi kṛtvā mahātmānaṃ brahmarūpiṇamīśvaram  LiP 
sadyojātaṃ tato brahmā dhyānayogaparo 'bhavat 
dhyānayogātparaṃ jñātvā vavande devamīśvaram  LiP 
sadyojātaṃ tato brahma brahma vai samacintayat 
tato 'sya pārśvataḥ śvetāḥ prādurbhūtā mahāyaśāḥ  LiP 
sunando nandanaścaiva viśvanandopanandanau 
śiṣyāste vai mahātmāno yaistadbrahma sadāvṛtam  LiP 
tasyāgre śvetavarṇābhaḥ śveto nāma mahāmuniḥ 
vijajñe 'tha mahātejās tasmājjajñe harastvasau  LiP 
tatra te munayaḥ sarve sadyojātaṃ maheśvaram 
prapannāḥ parayā bhaktyā gṛṇanto brahma śāśvatam  LiP

prāṇāyāmaparā bhūtvā brahmatatparamānasāḥ  LiP 
te sarve pāpanirmuktā vimalā brahmavarcasaḥ 
viṣṇulokamatikramya rudralokaṃ vrajanti te  LiP

sūta uvāca
tatastriṃśattamaḥ kalpo rakto nāma prakīrtitaḥ 
brahmā yatra mahātejā raktavarṇamadhārayat  LiP 
dhyāyataḥ putrakāmasya brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ 
prādurbhūto mahātejāḥ kumāro raktabhūṣaṇaḥ  LiP 
raktamālyāmbaradharo raktanetraḥ pratāpavān 
sa taṃ dṛṣṭvā mahātmānaṃ kumāraṃ raktavāsasam  LiP 
paraṃ dhyānaṃ samāśritya bubudhe devamīśvaram 
sa taṃ praṇamya bhagavān brahmā paramayantritaḥ  LiP 
vāmadevaṃ tato brahmā brahma vai samacintayat 
tathā stuto mahādevo brahmaṇā parameśvaraḥ  LiP 
pratītahṛdayaḥ sarva idamāha pitāmaham 
dhyāyatā putrakāmena yasmātte 'haṃ pitāmaha  LiP 
dṛṣṭaḥ paramayā bhaktyā stutaś ca brahmapūrvakam 
tasmāddhyānabalaṃ prāpya kalpe kalpe prayatnataḥ  LiP

tatastasya mahātmānaś catvāraste kumārakāḥ  LiP 
saṃbabhūvurmahātmāno viśuddhā brahmavarcasaḥ 
virajāś ca vibāhuś ca viśoko viśvabhāvanaḥ  LiP 
brahmaṇyā brahmaṇastulyā vīrā adhyavasāyinaḥ 
raktāṃbaradharāḥ sarve raktamālyānulepanāḥ  LiP 
raktakuṅkumaliptāṅgā raktabhasmānulepanāḥ 
tato varṣasahasrānte brahmatve 'dhyavasāyinaḥ  LiP 
gṛṇantaś ca mahātmāno brahma tadvāmadaivikam

te sarve pāpanirmuktā vimalā brahmacāriṇaḥ

sūta uvāca
ekatriṃśattamaḥ kalpaḥ pītavāsā iti smṛtaḥ 
brahmā yatra mahābhāgaḥ pītavāsā babhūva ha  LiP 
dhyāyataḥ putrakāmasya brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ 
prādurbhūto mahātejāḥ kumāraḥ pītavastradhṛk  LiP 
pītagandhānuliptāṅgaḥ pītamālyāṃbaro yuvā 
hemayajñopavītaś ca pītoṣṇīṣo mahābhujaḥ  LiP

tato dhyānagatastatra brahmā māheśvarīṃ varām

matiḥ smṛtirbuddhiriti gāyamānaḥ punaḥ punaḥ  LiP

viśvamāvṛtya yogena jagatsarvaṃ vaśīkuru  LiP

pradadau devadeveśaḥ catuṣpādāṃ jagadguruḥ  LiP 
tatastāṃ dhyānayogena viditvā parameśvarīm 
brahmā lokaguroḥ so 'tha pratipede maheśvarīm  LiP 
gāyatrīṃ tu tato raudrīṃ dhyātvā brahmānuyantritaḥ 
ityetāṃ vaidikīṃ vidyāṃ raudrīṃ gāyatrīmīritām  LiP

aiśvaryaṃ jñānasaṃpattiṃ vairāgyaṃ ca dadau prabhuḥ  LiP 
tato 'sya pārśvato divyāḥ prādurbhūtāḥ kumārakāḥ 
pītamālyāṃbaradharāḥ pītasraganulepanāḥ  LiP

tato varṣasahasrānta uṣitvā vimalaujasaḥ  LiP

dharmayogabalopetā munīnāṃ dīrghasattriṇām  LiP

praviśanti mahādevaṃ rudraṃ te tvapunarbhavāḥ  LiP

sūta uvāca
tatastasmingate kalpe pītavarṇe svayaṃbhuvaḥ

sūta uvāca
tatastasmin gate kalpe kṛṣṇavarṇe bhayānake 
tuṣṭāva devadeveśaṃ brahmā taṃ brahmarūpiṇam  LiP 
anugṛhya tatastuṣṭo brahmāṇamavadaddharaḥ 
anenaiva tu rūpeṇa saṃharāmi na saṃśayaḥ  LiP 
brahmahatyādikān ghorāṃs tathānyānapi pātakān 
hīnāṃścaiva mahābhāga tathaiva vividhānyapi  LiP 
upapātakamapyevaṃ tathā pāpāni suvrata 
mānasāni sutīkṣṇāni vācikāni pitāmaha  LiP 
kāyikāni sumiśrāṇi tathā prāsaṃgikāni ca 
buddhipūrvaṃ kṛtānyeva sahajāgantukāni ca  LiP 
mātṛdehotthitānyevaṃ pitṛdehe ca pātakam 
saṃharāmi na saṃdehaḥ sarvaṃ pātakajaṃ vibho  LiP 
lakṣaṃ japtvā hyaghorebhyo brahmahā mucyate prabho 
tadardhaṃ vācike vatsa tadardhaṃ mānase punaḥ  LiP 
caturguṇaṃ buddhipūrve krodhādaṣṭaguṇaṃ smṛtam 
vīrahā lakṣamātreṇa bhrūṇahā koṭimabhyaset  LiP 
mātṛhā niyutaṃ japtvā śudhyate nātra saṃśayaḥ 
goghnaścaiva kṛtaghnaś ca strīghnaḥ pāpayuto naraḥ  LiP 
ayutāghoramabhyasya mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ 
surāpo lakṣamātreṇa buddhyābuddhyāpi vai prabho  LiP 
mucyate nātra saṃdehas tadardhena ca vāruṇīm 
asnātāśī sahasreṇa ajapī ca tathā dvijaḥ  LiP 
ahutāśī sahasreṇa adātā ca viśudhyati 
brāhmaṇasvāpahartā ca svarṇasteyī narādhamaḥ  LiP 
niyutaṃ mānasaṃ japtvā mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ 
gurutalparato vāpi mātṛghno vā narādhamaḥ  LiP 
brahmaghnaś ca japedevaṃ mānasaṃ vai pitāmaha 
saṃparkātpāpināṃ pāpaṃ tatsamaṃ paribhāṣitam  LiP 
tathāpyayutamātreṇa pātakādvai pramucyate 
saṃsargātpātakī lakṣaṃ japedvai mānasaṃ dhiyā  LiP 
upāṃśu yaccaturdhā vai vācikaṃ cāṣṭadhā japet 
pātakādardhameva syād upapātakināṃ smṛtam  LiP 
tadardhaṃ kevale pāpe nātra kāryā vicāraṇā 
brahmahatyā surāpānaṃ suvarṇasteyameva ca  LiP 
kṛtvā ca gurutalpaṃ ca pāpakṛdbrāhmaṇo yadi 
rudragāyatriyā grāhyaṃ gomūtraṃ kāpilaṃ dvijāḥ  LiP 
gandhadvāreti tasyā vai gomayaṃ svastham āharet 
tejo 'si śuktam ityājyaṃ kāpilaṃ saṃharedbudhaḥ  LiP 
āpyāyasveti ca kṣīraṃ dadhikrāvṇeti cāharet 
gavyaṃ dadhi navaṃ sākṣāt kāpilaṃ vai pitāmaha  LiP 
devasya tveti mantreṇa saṃgrahedvai kuśodakam 
ekasthaṃ hemapātre vā kṛtvāghoreṇa rājate  LiP 
tāmre vā padmapātre vā pālāśe vā dale śubhe 
sakūrcaṃ sarvaratnāḍhyaṃ kṣiptvā tatraiva kāñcanam  LiP 
japellakṣamaghorākhyaṃ hutvā caiva ghṛtādibhiḥ 
ghṛtena caruṇā caiva samidbhiś ca tilais tathā  LiP 
yavaiś ca vrīhibhiścaiva juhuyādvai pṛthakpṛthak 
pratyekaṃ saptavāraṃ tu dravyālābhe ghṛtena tu  LiP 
hutvāghoreṇa deveśaṃ snātvāghoreṇa vai dvijāḥ 
aṣṭadroṇaghṛtenaiva snāpya paścādviśodhya ca  LiP 
ahorātroṣitaḥ snātaḥ pibetkūrcaṃ śivāgrataḥ 
brāhmaṃ brahmajapaṃ kuryād ācamya ca yathāvidhi  LiP 
evaṃ kṛtvā kṛtaghno 'pi brahmahā bhrūṇahā tathā 
vīrahā gurughātī ca mitraviśvāsaghātakaḥ  LiP 
steyī suvarṇasteyī ca gurutalparataḥ sadā 
madyapo vṛṣalīsaktaḥ paradāravidharṣakaḥ  LiP

sūta uvāca
athānyo brahmaṇaḥ kalpo vartate munipuṅgavāḥ 
viśvarūpa iti khyāto nāmataḥ paramādbhutaḥ  LiP 
vinivṛtte tu saṃhāre punaḥ sṛṣṭe carācare 
brahmaṇaḥ putrakāmasya dhyāyataḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ  LiP 
prādurbhūtā mahānādā viśvarūpā sarasvatī 
viśvamālyāṃbaradharā viśvayajñopavītinī  LiP 
viśvoṣṇīṣā viśvagandhā viśvamātā mahoṣṭhikā 
tathāvidhaṃ sa bhagavān īśānaṃ parameśvaram  LiP 
śuddhasphaṭikasaṃkāśaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam 
atha taṃ manasā dhyātvā yuktātmā vai pitāmahaḥ  LiP 
vavande devamīśānaṃ sarveśaṃ sarvagaṃ prabhum 
omīśāna namaste 'stu mahādeva namo 'stu te  LiP 
namo 'stu sarvavidyānām īśāna parameśvara 
namo 'stu sarvabhūtānām īśāna vṛṣavāhana  LiP 
brahmaṇo 'dhipate tubhyaṃ brahmaṇe brahmarūpiṇe 
namo brahmādhipataye śivaṃ me 'stu sadāśiva  LiP 
oṅkāramūrte deveśa sadyojāta namonamaḥ 
prapadye tvāṃ prapanno 'smi sadyojātāya vai namaḥ  LiP 
abhave ca bhave tubhyaṃ tathā nātibhave namaḥ 
bhavodbhava bhaveśāna māṃ bhajasva mahādyute  LiP 
vāmadeva namastubhyaṃ jyeṣṭhāya varadāya ca 
namo rudrāya kālāya kalanāya namo namaḥ  LiP 
namo vikaraṇāyaiva kālavarṇāya varṇine 
balāya balināṃ nityaṃ sadā vikaraṇāya te  LiP 
balapramathanāyaiva baline brahmarūpiṇe 
sarvabhūteśvareśāya bhūtānāṃ damanāya ca  LiP 
manonmanāya devāya namastubhyaṃ mahādyute 
vāmadevāya vāmāya namastubhyaṃ mahātmane  LiP 
jyeṣṭhāya caiva śreṣṭhāya rudrāya varadāya ca 
kālahantre namastubhyaṃ namastubhyaṃ mahātmane  LiP 
iti stavena deveśaṃ nanāma vṛṣabhadhvajam 
yaḥ paṭhet sakṛdeveha brahmalokaṃ gamiṣyati  LiP 
śrāvayedvā dvijān śrāddhe sa yāti paramāṃ gatim 
evaṃ dhyānagataṃ tatra praṇamantaṃ pitāmaham  LiP 
uvāca bhagavānīśaḥ prīto 'haṃ te kimicchasi 
tatastu praṇato bhūtvā vāgviśuddhaṃ maheśvaram  LiP 
uvāca bhagavān rudraṃ prītaṃ prītena cetasā 
yadidaṃ viśvarūpaṃ te viśvagauḥ śreyasīśvarī  LiP 
etadveditumicchāmi yatheyaṃ parameśvara 
kaiṣā bhagavatī devī catuṣpādā caturmukhī  LiP 
catuḥśṛṅgī caturvaktrā caturdaṃṣṭrā catuḥstanī 
caturhastā caturnetrā viśvarūpā kathaṃ smṛtā  LiP 
kiṃnāmagotrā kasyeyaṃ kiṃvīryā cāpi karmataḥ 
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā devadevo vṛṣadhvajaḥ  LiP 
prāha devavṛṣaṃ brahmā brahmāṇaṃ cātmasaṃbhavam 
rahasyaṃ sarvamantrāṇāṃ pāvanaṃ puṣṭivardhanam  LiP 
śṛṇuṣvaitatparaṃ guhyam ādisarge yathā tathā 
evaṃ yo vartate kalpo viśvarūpastvasau mataḥ  LiP 
brahmasthānamidaṃ cāpi yatra prāptaṃ tvayā prabho 
tvattaḥ parataraṃ deva viṣṇunā tatpadaṃ śubham  LiP 
vaikuṇṭhena viśuddhena mama vāmāṅgajena vā 
tadāprabhṛti kalpaś ca trayastriṃśattamo hyayam  LiP 
śataṃ śatasahasrāṇām atītā ye svayaṃbhuvaḥ 
purastāttava deveśa tacchṛṇuṣva mahāmate  LiP 
ānandastu sa vijñeya ānandatve vyavasthitaḥ 
māṇḍavyagotrastapasā mama putratvamāgataḥ  LiP 
tvayi yogaṃ ca sāṃkhyaṃ ca tapovidyāvidhikriyāḥ 
ṛtaṃ satyaṃ dayā brahma ahiṃsā sanmatiḥ kṣamā  LiP 
dhyānaṃ dhyeyaṃ damaḥ śāntir vidyāvidyā matirdhṛtiḥ 
kāntirnītiḥ prathā medhā lajjā dṛṣṭiḥ sarasvatī  LiP 
tuṣṭiḥ puṣṭiḥ kriyā caiva prasādaś ca pratiṣṭhitāḥ 
dvātriṃśatsuguṇā hyeṣā dvātriṃśākṣarasaṃjñayā  LiP 
prakṛtirvihitā brahmaṃs tvatprasūtirmaheśvarī 
viṣṇorbhagavataścāpi tathānyeṣāmapi prabho  LiP 
saiṣā bhagavatī devī matprasūtiḥ pratiṣṭhitā 
caturmukhī jagadyoniḥ prakṛtir gauḥ pratiṣṭhitā  LiP 
gaurī māyā ca vidyā ca kṛṣṇā haimavatīti ca 
pradhānaṃ prakṛtiścaiva yāmāhustattvacintakāḥ  LiP 
ajāmekāṃ lohitāṃ śuklakṛṣṇāṃ viśvaprajāṃ sṛjamānāṃ sarūpām 
ajo 'haṃ māṃ viddhi tāṃ viśvarūpaṃ gāyatrīṃ gāṃ viśvarūpāṃ hi buddhyā  LiP 
evamuktvā mahādevaḥ sasarja parameśvaraḥ 
tataś ca pārśvagā devyāḥ sarvarūpakumārakāḥ  LiP 
jaṭī muṇḍī śikhaṇḍī ca ardhamuṇḍaś ca jajñire 
tatastena yathoktena yogena sumahaujasaḥ  LiP 
divyavarṣasahasrānte upāsitvā maheśvaram 
dharmopadeśamakhilaṃ kṛtvā yogamayaṃ dṛḍham  LiP 
śiṣṭāś ca niyatātmānaḥ praviṣṭā rudramīśvaram  LiP

sūta uvāca
evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ proktaḥ sahyādīnāṃ samudbhavaḥ 
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi śrāvayedvā dvijottamān  LiP 
sa yāti brahmasāyujyaṃ prasādātparameṣṭhinaḥ 
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
kathaṃ liṅgamabhūlliṅge samabhyarcyaḥ sa śaṅkaraḥ  LiP 
kiṃ liṅgaṃ kas tathā liṅgī sūta vaktumihārhasi 
romaharṣaṇa uvāca
evaṃ devāś ca ṛṣayaḥ praṇipatya pitāmaham  LiP 
apṛcchan bhagavaṃlliṅgaṃ kathamāsīditi svayam 
liṅge maheśvaro rudraḥ samabhyarcyaḥ kathaṃ tviti  LiP 
kiṃ liṅgaṃ kas tathā liṅgī so 'pyāha ca pitāmahaḥ 
pitāmaha uvāca
pradhānaṃ liṅgamākhyātaṃ liṅgī ca parameśvaraḥ  LiP 
rakṣārthamaṃbudhau mahyaṃ viṣṇostvāsīt surottamāḥ 
vaimānike gate sarge janalokaṃ saharṣibhiḥ  LiP 
sthitikāle tadā pūrṇe tataḥ pratyāhṛte tathā 
caturyugasahasrānte satyalokaṃ gate surāḥ  LiP 
vinādhipatyaṃ samatāṃ gate 'nte brahmaṇo mama 
śuṣke ca sthāvare sarve tv anāvṛṣṭyā ca sarvaśaḥ  LiP 
paśavo mānuṣā vṛkṣāḥ piśācāḥ piśitāśanāḥ 
gandharvādyāḥ krameṇaiva nirdagdhā bhānubhānubhiḥ  LiP

nārāyaṇo mahābāhuḥ sarvātmā sadasanmayaḥ  LiP 
tathābhūtamahaṃ dṛṣṭvā śayānaṃ paṅkajekṣaṇam 
māyayā mohitastasya tamavocamamarṣitaḥ  LiP 
kastvaṃ vadeti hastena samutthāpya sanātanam 
tadā hastaprahāreṇa tīvreṇa sa dṛḍhena tu  LiP 
prabuddho 'hīyaśayanāt samāsīnaḥ kṣaṇaṃ vaśī 
dadarśa nidrāviklinna nīrajāmalalocanaḥ  LiP 
māmagre saṃsthitaṃ bhāsā dhyāsito bhagavān hariḥ 
āha cotthāya bhagavān hasanmāṃ madhuraṃ sakṛt  LiP 
svāgataṃsvāgataṃ vatsa pitāmaha mahādyute 
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā smitapūrvaṃ surarṣabhāḥ  LiP 
rajasā baddhavairaś ca tamavocaṃ janārdanam 
bhāṣase vatsa vatseti sargasaṃhārakāraṇam  LiP 
mām ihāntaḥsmitaṃ kṛtvā guruḥ śiṣyamivānagha 
kartāraṃ jagatāṃ sākṣāt prakṛteś ca pravartakam  LiP 
sanātanamajaṃ viṣṇuṃ viriñciṃ viśvasaṃbhavam 
viśvātmānaṃ vidhātāraṃ dhātāraṃ paṅkajekṣaṇam  LiP 
kimarthaṃ bhāṣase mohād vaktumarhasi satvaram 
so 'pi māmāha jagatāṃ kartāhamiti lokaya  LiP 
bhartā hartā bhavān aṅgād avatīrṇo mamāvyayāt 
vismṛto 'si jagannāthaṃ nārāyaṇamanāmayam  LiP 
puruṣaṃ paramātmānaṃ puruhūtaṃ puruṣṭutam 
viṣṇumacyutamīśānaṃ viśvasya prabhavodbhavam  LiP 
tavāparādho nāstyatra mama māyākṛtaṃ tvidam 
śṛṇu satyaṃ caturvaktra sarvadeveśvaro hyayam  LiP 
kartā netā ca hartā ca na mayāsti samo vibhuḥ 
ahameva paraṃ brahma paraṃ tattvaṃ pitāmaha  LiP 
ahameva paraṃ jyotiḥ paramātmā tvahaṃ vibhuḥ 
yadyaddṛṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ sarvaṃ jagatyasmiṃścarācaram  LiP 
tattadviddhi caturvaktra sarvaṃ manmayamityatha 
mayā sṛṣṭaṃ purāvyaktaṃ caturviṃśatikaṃ svayam  LiP 
nityāntā hyaṇavo baddhāḥ sṛṣṭāḥ krodhodbhavādayaḥ 
prasādāddhi bhavānaṇḍāny anekānīha līlayā  LiP 
sṛṣṭā buddhirmayā tasyām ahaṅkārastridhā tataḥ 
tanmātrāpañcakaṃ tasmān manaḥ ṣaṣṭhendriyāṇi ca  LiP

āvayoścābhavadyuddhaṃ sughoraṃ romaharṣaṇam 
pralayārṇavamadhye tu rajasā baddhavairayoḥ  LiP 
etasminnantare liṅgam abhavaccāvayoḥ puraḥ

nārāyaṇo 'pi viśvātmā nīlāñjanacayopamam  LiP

evaṃ varṣasahasraṃ tu tvaranviṣṇuradhogataḥ  LiP

tāvatkālaṃ gato hyūrdhvam ahamapyarisūdanaḥ  LiP

praṇipatya mayā sārdhaṃ sasmāra kimidaṃ tviti  LiP 
tadā samabhavattatra nādo vai śabdalakṣaṇaḥ 
omomiti suraśreṣṭhāḥ suvyaktaḥ plutalakṣaṇaḥ  LiP

liṅgasya dakṣiṇe bhāge tadāpaśyatsanātanam  LiP 
ādyavarṇamakāraṃ tu ukāraṃ cottare tataḥ 
makāraṃ madhyataścaiva nādāntaṃ tasya caumiti  LiP

deva uvāca
cintayā rahito rudro vāco yanmanasā saha  LiP 
aprāpya taṃ nivartante vācyastvekākṣareṇa saḥ 
ekākṣareṇa tadvācyam ṛtaṃ paramakāraṇam  LiP 
satyamānandamamṛtaṃ paraṃ brahma parātparam 
ekākṣarādakārākhyo bhagavānkanakāṇḍajaḥ  LiP 
ekākṣarādukārākhyo hariḥ paramakāraṇam 
ekākṣarānmakārākhyo bhagavānnīlalohitaḥ  LiP 
sargakartā tvakārākhyo hy ukārākhyastu mohakaḥ 
makārākhyas tayor nityam anugrahakaro 'bhavat  LiP 
makārākhyo vibhurbījī hy akāro bījamucyate 
ukārākhyo hariryoniḥ pradhānapuruṣeśvaraḥ  LiP 
bījī ca bījaṃ tadyonir nādākhyaś ca maheśvaraḥ 
bījī vibhajya cātmānaṃ svecchayā tu vyavasthitaḥ  LiP 
asya liṅgādabhūdbījam akāro bījinaḥ prabhoḥ 
ukārayonau nikṣiptam avardhata samantataḥ  LiP 
sauvarṇamabhavaccāṇḍam āveṣṭyādyaṃ tadakṣaram 
anekābdaṃ tathā cāpsu divyamaṇḍaṃ vyavasthitam  LiP 
tato varṣasahasrānte dvidhā kṛtamajodbhavam 
aṇḍam apsu sthitaṃ sākṣād ādyākhyeneśvareṇa tu  LiP

sa sraṣṭā sarvalokānāṃ sa eva trividhaḥ prabhuḥ  LiP

divyaṃ śabdamayaṃ rūpam āsthāya prahasan sthitaḥ 
akārastasya mūrdhā tu lalāṭaṃ dīrghamucyate  LiP 
ikāro dakṣiṇaṃ netram īkāro vāmalocanam

vāmaṃ kapolam ṝkāro ḷ ḹ nāsāpuṭe ubhe  LiP 
ekāram oṣṭhamūrddhvaś ca aikārastvadharo vibhoḥ 
okāraś ca tathaukāro dantapaṅktidvayaṃ kramāt  LiP

kādipañcākṣarāṇyasya pañca hastāni dakṣiṇe  LiP 
cādipañcākṣarāṇyevaṃ pañca hastāni vāmataḥ 
ṭādipañcākṣaraṃ pādas tādipañcākṣaraṃ tathā  LiP 
pakāramudaraṃ tasya phakāraḥ pārśvamucyate 
bakāro vāmapārśvaṃ vai bhakāraṃ skandhamasya tat  LiP 
makāraṃ hṛdayaṃ śaṃbhor mahādevasya yoginaḥ 
yakārādisakārāntaṃ vibhorvai sapta dhātavaḥ  LiP 
hakāra ātmarūpaṃ vai kṣakāraḥ krodha ucyate 
taṃ dṛṣṭvā umayā sārdhaṃ bhagavantaṃ maheśvaram  LiP 
praṇamya bhagavān viṣṇuḥ punaścāpaśyadūrddhvataḥ

śuddhasphaṭikasaṃkāśaṃ subhāṣṭatriṃśadakṣaram

abhicārikamatyarthaṃ trayastriṃśacchubhākṣaram  LiP 
yajurvedasamāyuktaṃ pañcatriṃśacchubhākṣaram

viṣṇur uvāca
ekākṣarāya rudrāya akārāyātmarūpiṇe 
ukārāyādidevāya vidyādehāya vai namaḥ  LiP 
tṛtīyāya makārāya śivāya paramātmane 
sūryāgnisomavarṇāya yajamānāya vai namaḥ  LiP 
agnaye rudrarūpāya rudrāṇāṃ pataye namaḥ 
śivāya śivamantrāya sadyojātāya vedhase  LiP 
vāmāya vāmadevāya varadāyāmṛtāya te 
aghorāyātighorāya sadyojātāya raṃhase  LiP 
īśānāya śmaśānāya ativegāya vegine 
namo 'stu śrutipādāya ūrdhvaliṅgāya liṅgine  LiP

vāyave vāyuvegāya namaste vāyuvyāpine 
tejase tejasāṃ bhartre namastejo 'dhivyāpine  LiP 
jalāya jalabhūtāya namaste jalavyāpine

śabdasparśasvarūpāya rasagandhāya gandhine

anantāya virūpāya anantānāmayāya ca 
śāśvatāya variṣṭhāya vārigarbhāya yogine  LiP 
saṃsthitāyāmbhasāṃ madhye āvayormadhyavarcase 
goptre hartre sadā kartre nidhanāyeśvarāya ca  LiP 
acetanāya cintyāya cetanāyāsahāriṇe 
arūpāya surūpāya anaṅgāyāṅgahāriṇe  LiP 
bhasmadigdhaśarīrāya bhānusomāgnihetave 
śvetāya śvetavarṇāya tuhinādricarāya ca  LiP 
suśvetāya suvaktrāya namaḥ śvetaśikhāya ca 
śvetāsyāya mahāsyāya namaste śvetalohita  LiP 
sutārāya viśiṣṭāya namo dundubhine hara 
śatarūpavirūpāya namaḥ ketumate sadā  LiP 
ṛddhiśokaviśokāya pinākāya kapardine 
vipāśāya supāśāya namaste pāśanāśine  LiP 
suhotrāya haviṣyāya subrahmaṇyāya sūriṇe 
sumukhāya suvaktrāya durdamāya damāya ca  LiP 
kaṅkāya kaṅkarūpāya kaṅkaṇīkṛtapannaga 
sanakāya namastubhyaṃ sanātana sanandana  LiP 
sanatkumārasāraṅgam āraṇāya mahātmane 
lokākṣiṇe tridhāmāya namo virajase sadā  LiP 
śaṅkhapālāya śaṅkhāya rajase tamase namaḥ 
sārasvatāya meghāya meghavāhana te namaḥ  LiP 
suvāhāya vivāhāya vivādavaradāya ca 
namaḥ śivāya rudrāya pradhānāya namonamaḥ  LiP 
triguṇāya namastubhyaṃ caturvyūhātmane namaḥ 
saṃsārāya namastubhyaṃ namaḥ saṃsārahetave  LiP 
mokṣāya mokṣarūpāya mokṣakartre namonamaḥ 
ātmane ṛṣaye tubhyaṃ svāmine viṣṇave namaḥ  LiP 
namo bhagavate tubhyaṃ nāgānāṃ pataye namaḥ 
oṅkārāya namastubhyaṃ sarvajñāya namo namaḥ  LiP 
sarvāya ca namastubhyaṃ namo nārāyaṇāya ca 
namo hiraṇyagarbhāya ādidevāya te namaḥ  LiP 
namo 'stvajāya pataye prajānāṃ vyūhahetave 
mahādevāya devānām īśvarāya namo namaḥ  LiP 
śarvāya ca namastubhyaṃ satyāya śamanāya ca 
brahmaṇe caiva bhūtānāṃ sarvajñāya namo namaḥ  LiP 
mahātmane namastubhyaṃ prajñārūpāya vai namaḥ 
citaye citirūpāya smṛtirūpāya vai namaḥ  LiP 
jñānāya jñānagamyāya namaste saṃvide sadā 
śikharāya namastubhyaṃ nīlakaṇṭhāya vai namaḥ  LiP 
ardhanārīśarīrāya avyaktāya namonamaḥ 
ekādaśavibhedāya sthāṇave te namaḥ sadā  LiP 
namaḥ somāya sūryāya bhavāya bhavahāriṇe 
yaśaskarāya devāya śaṅkarāyeśvarāya ca  LiP 
namo 'ṃbikādhipataye umāyāḥ pataye namaḥ 
hiraṇyabāhave tubhyaṃ namaste hemaretase  LiP 
nīlakeśāya vittāya śitikaṇṭhāya vai namaḥ 
kapardine namastubhyaṃ nāgāṅgābharaṇāya ca  LiP 
vṛṣārūḍhāya sarvasya hartre kartre namonamaḥ 
vīrarāmātirāmāya rāmanāthāya te vibho  LiP 
namo rājādhirājāya rājñāmadhigatāya te 
namaḥ pālādhipataye pālāśākṛntate namaḥ  LiP 
namaḥ keyūrabhūṣāya gopate te namonamaḥ 
namaḥ śrīkaṇṭhanāthāya namo likucapāṇaye  LiP 
bhuvaneśāya devāya vedaśāstra namo 'stu te 
sāraṅgāya namastubhyaṃ rājahaṃsāya te namaḥ  LiP 
kanakāṅgadahārāya namaḥ sarpopavītine 
sarpakuṇḍalamālāya kaṭisūtrīkṛtāhine  LiP 
vedagarbhāya garbhāya viśvagarbhāya te śiva 
brahmovāca
virarāmeti saṃstutvā brahmaṇā sahito hariḥ  LiP 
etatstotravaraṃ puṇyaṃ sarvapāpapraṇāśanam 
yaḥ paṭhecchrāvayedvāpi brāhmaṇān vedapāragān  LiP 
sa yāti brahmaṇo loke pāpakarmarato 'pi vai 
tasmājjapetpaṭhennityaṃ śrāvayedbrāhmaṇāñchubhān  LiP 
sarvapāpaviśuddhyarthaṃ viṣṇunā paribhāṣitam  LiP

sūta uvāca
athovāca mahādevaḥ prīto 'haṃ surasattamau 
paśyatāṃ māṃ mahādevaṃ bhayaṃ sarvaṃ vimucyatām  LiP 
yuvāṃ prasūtau gātrābhyāṃ mama pūrvaṃ mahābalau 
ayaṃ me dakṣiṇe pārśve brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ  LiP 
vāme pārśve ca me viṣṇur viśvātmā hṛdayodbhavaḥ 
prīto 'haṃ yuvayoḥ samyag varaṃ dadmi yathepsitam  LiP 
evamuktvā tu taṃ viṣṇuṃ karābhyāṃ parameśvaraḥ 
pasparśa subhagābhyāṃ tu kṛpayā tu kṛpānidhiḥ  LiP 
tataḥ prahṛṣṭamanasā praṇipatya maheśvaram 
prāha nārāyaṇo nāthaṃ liṅgasthaṃ liṅgavarjitam  LiP 
yadi prītiḥ samutpannā yadi deyo varaś ca nau 
bhaktirbhavatu nau nityaṃ tvayi cāvyabhicāriṇī  LiP 
devaḥ pradattavān devāḥ svātmanyavyabhicāriṇīm 
brahmaṇe viṣṇave caiva śraddhāṃ śītāṃśubhūṣaṇaḥ  LiP 
jānubhyāmavanīṃ gatvā punarnārāyaṇaḥ svayam 
praṇipatya ca viśveśaṃ prāha mandataraṃ vaśī  LiP 
āvayordevadeveśa vivādamatiśobhanam 
ihāgato bhavān yasmād vivādaśamanāya nau  LiP 
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā punaḥ prāha haro harim 
praṇipatya sthitaṃ mūrdhnā kṛtāñjalipuṭaṃ smayan  LiP 
śrīmahādeva uvāca
pralayasthitisargāṇāṃ kartā tvaṃ dharaṇīpate 
vatsa vatsa hare viṣṇo pālayaitaccarācaram  LiP 
tridhā bhinno hyahaṃ viṣṇo brahmaviṣṇubhavākhyayā 
sargarakṣālayaguṇair niṣkalaḥ parameśvaraḥ  LiP 
saṃmohaṃ tyaja bho viṣṇo pālayainaṃ pitāmaham 
pādme bhaviṣyati sutaḥ kalpe tava pitāmahaḥ  LiP 
tadā drakṣyasi māṃ caivaṃ so 'pi drakṣyati padmajaḥ 
evamuktvā sa bhagavāṃs tatraivāntaradhīyata  LiP 
tadāprabhṛti lokeṣu liṅgārcā supratiṣṭhitā 
liṅgavedī mahādevī liṅgaṃ sākṣānmaheśvaraḥ  LiP

sūta uvāca
āsīdekārṇavaṃ ghoram avibhāgaṃ tamomayam  LiP 
madhye caikārṇave tasmin śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ 
jīmūtābho 'mbujākṣaś ca kirīṭī śrīpatirhariḥ  LiP 
nārāyaṇamukhodgīrṇa sarvātmā puruṣottamaḥ 
aṣṭabāhurmahāvakṣā lokānāṃ yonirucyate  LiP 
kimapyacintyaṃ yogātmā yogamāsthāya yogavit 
phaṇāsahasrakalitaṃ tamapratimavarcasam  LiP 
mahābhogapaterbhogaṃ sādhvāstīrya mahocchrayam 
tasminmahati paryaṅke śete caikārṇave prabhuḥ  LiP 
evaṃ tatra śayānena viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā 
ātmārāmeṇa krīḍārthaṃ līlayākliṣṭakarmaṇā  LiP 
śatayojanavistīrṇaṃ taruṇādityasannibham 
vajradaṇḍaṃ mahotsedhaṃ nābhyāṃ sṛṣṭaṃ tu puṣkaram  LiP 
tasyaivaṃ krīḍamānasya samīpaṃ devamīḍhuṣaḥ 
hemagarbhāṇḍajo brahmā rukmavarṇo hyatīndriyaḥ  LiP 
caturvaktro viśālākṣaḥ samāgamya yadṛcchayā 
śriyā yuktena divyena suśubhena sugandhinā  LiP 
krīḍamānaṃ ca padmena dṛṣṭvā brahmā śubhekṣaṇam 
savismayamathāgamya saumyasampannayā girā  LiP 
provāca ko bhavāñchete hy āśrito madhyamambhasām 
atha tasyācyutaḥ śrutvā brahmaṇastu śubhaṃ vacaḥ  LiP 
udatiṣṭhata paryaṅkād vismayotphullalocanaḥ 
pratyuvācottaraṃ caiva kalpe kalpe pratiśrayaḥ  LiP

ko bhavān viśvamūrtirvai kartavyaṃ kiṃ ca te mayā  LiP 
evaṃ bruvantaṃ vaikuṇṭhaṃ pratyuvāca pitāmahaḥ 
māyayā mohitaḥ śaṃbhor avijñāya janārdanam  LiP 
māyayā mohitaṃ devam avijñātaṃ mahātmanaḥ 
yathā bhavāṃstathaivāham ādikartā prajāpatiḥ  LiP 
savismayaṃ vacaḥ śrutvā brahmaṇo lokatantriṇaḥ 
anujñātaś ca te nātha vaikuṇṭho viśvasaṃbhavaḥ  LiP 
kautūhalānmahāyogī praviṣṭo brahmaṇo mukham 
imānaṣṭādaśa dvīpān sasamudrān saparvatān  LiP 
praviśya sumahātejāś cāturvarṇyasamākulān 
brahmaṇastambhaparyantaṃ saptalokān sanātanān  LiP 
brahmaṇastūdare dṛṣṭvā sarvānviṣṇurmahābhujaḥ 
aho 'sya tapaso vīryam ityuktvā ca punaḥ punaḥ  LiP 
aṭitvā vividhāṃllokān viṣṇurnānāvidhāśrayān 
tato varṣasahasrānte nāntaṃ hi dadṛśe yadā  LiP 
tadāsya vaktrānniṣkramya pannagendraniketanaḥ 
nārāyaṇo jagaddhātā pitāmahamathābravīt  LiP

nāhamantaṃ prapaśyāmi udarasya tavānagha  LiP

praviśya lokān paśyaitān anaupamyānsurottama 
tataḥ prāhlādinīṃ vāṇīṃ śrutvā tasyābhinandya ca  LiP 
śrīpaterudaraṃ bhūyaḥ praviveśa pitāmahaḥ 
tāneva lokān garbhasthān apaśyat satyavikramaḥ  LiP 
paryaṭitvā tu devasya dadṛśe 'ntaṃ na vai hareḥ 
jñātvā gatiṃ tasya pitāmahasya dvārāṇi sarvāṇi pidhāya viṣṇuḥ 
vibhurmanaḥ kartumiyeṣa cāśu sukhaṃ prasupto 'hamiti pracintya  LiP

padmasūtrānusāreṇa cānvapaśyatpitāmahaḥ 
ujjahārātmano rūpaṃ puṣkarāccaturānanaḥ  LiP

śūlapāṇirmahādevo hemavīrāṃbaracchadaḥ  LiP

ityevaṃ manasā dhyātvā pratyuvācedamuttaram  LiP

kiṃ mayā ca kṛtaṃ deva yanmāṃ priyamanuttamam  LiP

evaṃ bruvāṇaṃ deveśaṃ lokayātrānugaṃ tataḥ  LiP 
pratyuvācāmbujābhākṣaṃ brahmā vedanidhiḥ prabhuḥ 
yo 'sau tavodaraṃ pūrvaṃ praviṣṭo 'haṃ tvadicchayā  LiP

tvayā matsarabhāvena māṃ vaśīkartumicchatā  LiP 
āśu dvārāṇi sarvāṇi pihitāni samantataḥ 
tato mayā mahābhāga saṃcintya svena tejasā  LiP

mā bhūtte manaso 'lpo 'pi vyāghāto 'yaṃ kathaṃcana  LiP 
ityeṣānugatirviṣṇo kāryāṇām aupasarpiṇī 
yanmayānantaraṃ kāryaṃ brūhi kiṃ karavāṇyaham  LiP 
tataḥ paramameyātmā hiraṇyakaśipo ripuḥ 
anavadyāṃ priyāmiṣṭāṃ śivāṃ vāṇīṃ pitāmahāt  LiP

putro bhava mamārighna mudaṃ prāpsyasi śobhanām  LiP 
sadbhāvavacanaṃ brūhi padmādavatara prabho

adyaprabhṛti sarveśaḥ śvetoṣṇīṣavibhūṣitaḥ 
padmayoniriti hyevaṃ khyāto nāmnā bhaviṣyasi  LiP 
putro me tvaṃ bhava brahman saptalokādhipaḥ prabho 
tataḥ sa bhagavāndevo varaṃ dattvā kirīṭine  LiP 
evaṃ bhavatu cetyuktvā prītātmā gatamatsaraḥ 
pratyāsannam athāyāntaṃ bālārkābhaṃ mahānanam  LiP

tadāpyahaṃ tvayā jñātaḥ parameṇa samādhinā 
viśvarūpā ca saṃvṛttā gāyatrī lokadhāriṇī  LiP 
tasmin viśvatvam āpannaṃ ye māṃ vetsyanti bhūtale 
teṣāṃ śivaś ca saumyaś ca bhaviṣyāmi sadaiva hi  LiP 
yasmācca viśvarūpo vai kalpo 'yaṃ samudāhṛtaḥ 
viśvarūpā tathā ceyaṃ sāvitrī samudāhṛtā  LiP 
sarvarūpā tathā ceme saṃvṛttā mama putrakāḥ 
catvāraste mayā khyātāḥ putra vai lokasaṃmatāḥ  LiP 
yasmācca sarvavarṇatvaṃ prajānāṃ ca bhaviṣyati 
sarvabhakṣā ca medhyā ca varṇataś ca bhaviṣyati  LiP 
mokṣo dharmastathārthaś ca kāmaśceti catuṣṭayam 
yasmādvedāś ca vedyaṃ ca caturdhā vai bhaviṣyati  LiP 
bhūtagrāmāś ca catvāra āśramāś ca tathaiva ca 
dharmasya pādāścatvāraś catvāro mama putrakāḥ  LiP 
tasmāccaturyugāvasthaṃ jagadvai sacarācaram 
caturdhāvasthitaścaiva catuṣpādo bhaviṣyati  LiP 
bhūrloko 'tha bhuvarlokaḥ svarlokaś ca mahas tathā 
janastapaś ca satyaṃ ca viṣṇulokastataḥ param  LiP 
aṣṭākṣarasthito lokaḥ sthāne sthāne tadakṣaram 
bhūrbhuvaḥ svarmahaścaiva pādāścatvāra eva ca  LiP 
bhūrlokaḥ prathamaḥ pādo bhuvarlokastataḥ param 
svarloko vai tṛtīyaś ca caturthastu mahas tathā  LiP 
pañcamastu janastatra ṣaṣṭhaś ca tapa ucyate 
satyaṃ tu saptamo loko hy apunarbhavagāminām  LiP 
viṣṇulokaḥ smṛtaṃ sthānaṃ punarāvṛttidurlabham 
skāndamaumaṃ tathā sthānaṃ sarvasiddhisamanvitam  LiP 
rudralokaḥ smṛtastasmāt padaṃ tadyogināṃ śubham 
nirmamā nirahaṅkārāḥ kāmakrodhavivarjitāḥ  LiP 
drakṣyanti taddvijā yuktā dhyānatatparamānasāḥ 
yasmāccatuṣpadā hyeṣā tvayā dṛṣṭā sarasvatī  LiP 
pādāntaṃ viṣṇulokaṃ vai kaumāraṃ śāntamuttamam 
aumaṃ māheśvaraṃ caiva tasmāddṛṣṭā catuṣpadā  LiP 
tasmāttu paśavaḥ sarve bhaviṣyanti catuṣpadāḥ 
tataścaiṣāṃ bhaviṣyanti catvāraste payodharāḥ  LiP 
somaś ca mantrasaṃyukto yasmānmama mukhāccyutaḥ 
jīvaḥ prāṇabhṛtāṃ brahman punaḥ pītastanāḥ smṛtāḥ  LiP 
tasmātsomamayaṃ caiva amṛtaṃ jīvasaṃjñitam 
catuṣpādā bhaviṣyanti śvetatvaṃ cāsya tena tat  LiP 
yasmāccaiva kriyā bhūtvā dvipadā ca maheśvarī 
dṛṣṭā punastathaivaiṣā sāvitrī lokabhāvinī  LiP 
tasmācca dvipadāḥ sarve dvistanāś ca narāḥ śubhāḥ 
tasmācceyamajā bhūtvā sarvavarṇā maheśvarī  LiP 
yā vai dṛṣṭā mahāsattvā sarvabhūtadharā tvayā 
tasmācca viśvarūpatvaṃ prajānāṃ vai bhaviṣyati  LiP 
ajaścaiva mahātejā viśvarūpo bhaviṣyati 
amogharetāḥ sarvatra mukhe cāsya hutāśanaḥ  LiP 
tasmātsarvagato medhyaḥ paśurūpī hutāśanaḥ 
tapasā bhāvitātmāno ye māṃ drakṣyanti vai dvijāḥ  LiP 
īśitve ca vaśitve ca sarvagaṃ sarvataḥ sthitam 
rajastamobhyāṃ nirmuktās tyaktvā mānuṣyakaṃ vapuḥ  LiP 
matsamīpamupeṣyanti punarāvṛttidurlabham 
ityevamukto bhagavān brahmā rudreṇa vai dvijāḥ  LiP 
praṇamya prayato bhūtvā punarāha pitāmahaḥ 
ya evaṃ bhagavān vidvān gāyatryā vai maheśvaram  LiP 
viśvātmānaṃ hi sarvaṃ tvāṃ gāyatryāstava ceśvara 
tasya dehi paraṃ sthānaṃ tathāstviti ca so 'bravīt  LiP 
tasmādvidvān hi viśvatvam asyāścāsya mahātmanaḥ 
sa yāti brahmasāyujyaṃ vacanād brahmaṇaḥ prabhoḥ  LiP 
LiP  
sūta uvāca
śrutvaivamakhilaṃ brahmā rudreṇa paribhāṣitam 
punaḥ praṇamya deveśaṃ rudramāha prajāpatiḥ  LiP 
bhagavandevadeveśa viśvarūpaṃ maheśvara 
umādhava mahādeva namo lokābhivandita  LiP 
viśvarūpa mahābhāga kasminkāle maheśvara 
yā imāste mahādeva tanavo lokavanditāḥ  LiP 
kasyāṃ vā yugasaṃbhūtyāṃ drakṣyantīha dvijātayaḥ 
kena vā tapasā deva dhyānayogena kena vā  LiP 
namaste vai mahādeva śakyo draṣṭuṃ dvijātibhiḥ 
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā śarvaḥ samprekṣya taṃ puraḥ  LiP 
smayanprāha mahādeva ṛgyajuḥsāmasaṃbhavaḥ 
śrībhagavānuvāca
tapasā naiva vṛttena dānadharmaphalena ca  LiP 
na tīrthaphalayogena kratubhir vāptadakṣiṇaiḥ 
na vedādhyayanairvāpi na vittena na vedanaiḥ  LiP 
na śakyaṃ mānavairdraṣṭum ṛte dhyānādahaṃ tviha 
saptame caiva vārāhe tatastasminpitāmaha  LiP 
kalpeśvaro 'tha bhagavān sarvalokaprakāśanaḥ 
manurvaivasvataścaiva tava pautro bhaviṣyati  LiP 
tadā caturyugāvasthe tasminkalpe yugāntike 
anugrahārthaṃ lokānāṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ hitāya ca  LiP 
utpatsyāmi tadā brahman punar asmin yugāntike 
yugapravṛttyā ca tadā tasmiṃś ca prathame yuge  LiP 
dvāpare prathame brahman yadā vyāsaḥ svayaṃ prabhuḥ 
tadāhaṃ brāhmaṇārthāya kalau tasmin yugāntike  LiP 
bhaviṣyāmi śikhāyuktaḥ śveto nāma mahāmuniḥ 
himavacchikhare ramye chāgale parvatottame  LiP 
tatra śiṣyāḥ śikhāyuktā bhaviṣyanti tadā mama 
śvetaḥ śvetaśikhaścaiva śvetāsyaḥ śvetalohitaḥ  LiP 
catvārastu mahātmāno brāhmaṇā vedapāragāḥ 
tataste brahmabhūyiṣṭhā dṛṣṭvā brahmagatiṃ parām  LiP 
matsamīpaṃ gamiṣyanti dhyānayogaparāyaṇāḥ 
tataḥ punaryadā brahman dvitīye dvāpare prabhuḥ  LiP 
prajāpatiryadā vyāsaḥ sadyo nāma bhaviṣyati 
tadā lokahitārthāya sutāro nāma nāmataḥ  LiP 
bhaviṣyāmi kalau tasmin śiṣyānugrahakāmyayā 
tatrāpi mama te śiṣyā nāmataḥ parikīrtitāḥ  LiP 
dundubhiḥ śatarūpaś ca ṛcīkaḥ ketumāṃstadā 
prāpya yogaṃ tathā dhyānaṃ sthāpya brahma ca bhūtale  LiP 
rudralokaṃ gamiṣyanti sahacāritvameva ca 
tṛtīye dvāpare caiva yadā vyāsastu bhārgavaḥ  LiP 
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi damanastu yugāntike 
tatrāpi ca bhaviṣyanti catvāro mama putrakāḥ  LiP 
vikośaś ca vikeśaś ca vipāśaḥ śāpanāśanaḥ 
te 'pi tenaiva mārgeṇa yogoktena mahaujasaḥ  LiP 
rudralokaṃ gamiṣyanti punarāvṛttidurlabham 
caturthe dvāpare caiva yadā vyāso 'ṅgirāḥ smṛtaḥ  LiP 
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi suhotro nāma nāmataḥ 
tatrāpi mama te putrāś catvāro 'pi tapodhanāḥ  LiP 
dvijaśreṣṭhā bhaviṣyanti yogātmāno dṛḍhavratāḥ 
sumukho durmukhaścaiva durdaro duratikramaḥ  LiP 
prāpya yogagatiṃ sūkṣmāṃ vimalā dagdhakilbiṣāḥ 
te 'pi tenaiva mārgeṇa yogayuktā mahaujasaḥ  LiP 
rudralokaṃ gamiṣyanti punarāvṛttidurlabham 
pañcame dvāpare caiva vyāsastu savitā yadā  LiP 
tadā cāpi bhaviṣyāmi kaṅko nāma mahātapāḥ 
anugrahārthaṃ lokānāṃ yogātmaikakalāgatiḥ  LiP 
catvārastu mahābhāgā vimalāḥ śuddhayonayaḥ 
śiṣyā mama bhaviṣyanti yogātmāno dṛḍhavratāḥ  LiP 
sanakaḥ sanandanaś caiva prabhuryaś ca sanātanaḥ 
vibhuḥ sanatkumāraś ca nirmamā nirahaṃkṛtāḥ  LiP 
matsamīpamupeṣyanti punarāvṛttidurlabham 
parīvarte punaḥ ṣaṣṭhe mṛtyurvyāso yadā vibhuḥ  LiP 
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi logākṣīr nāma nāmataḥ 
tatrāpi mama te śiṣyā yogātmāno dṛḍhavratāḥ  LiP 
bhaviṣyanti mahābhāgāś catvāro lokasaṃmatāḥ 
sudhāmā virajāścaiva śaṅkhapādraja eva ca  LiP 
yogātmāno mahātmānaḥ sarve vai dagdhakilbiṣāḥ 
te 'pi tenaiva mārgeṇa dhyānayogasamanvitāḥ  LiP 
matsamīpaṃ gamiṣyanti punarāvṛttidurlabham 
saptame parivarte tu yadā vyāsaḥ śatakratuḥ  LiP 
vibhunāmā mahātejāḥ prathitaḥ pūrvajanmani 
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi kalau tasmin yugāntike  LiP 
jaigīṣavyo vibhuḥ khyātaḥ sarveṣāṃ yogināṃ varaḥ 
tatrāpi mama te putrā bhaviṣyanti yuge tathā  LiP 
sārasvataś ca meghaś ca meghḥḥaṃ yogaṃ rudralokaṃ gatā hi te  LiP 
trayodaśe punaḥ prāpte parivarte krameṇa tu 
dharmo nārāyaṇo nāma vyāsastu bhavitā yadā  LiP 
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi vālirnāma mahāmuniḥ 
vālakhilyāśrame puṇye parvate gandhamādane  LiP 
tatrāpi mama te putrā bhaviṣyanti tapodhanāḥ 
sudhāmā kāśyapaścaiva vāsiṣṭho virajāstathā  LiP 
mahāyogabalopetā vimalā ūrdhvaretasaḥ 
prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ rudralokaṃ gatā hi te  LiP 
yadā vyāsastarakṣustu paryāye tu caturdaśe 
tatrāpi punarevāhaṃ bhaviṣyāmi yugāntike  LiP 
vaṃśe tvaṅgirasāṃ śreṣṭhe gautamo nāma nāmataḥ 
bhaviṣyati mahāpuṇyaṃ gautamaṃ nāma tadvanam  LiP 
tatrāpi mama te putrā bhaviṣyanti kalau tadā 
atrirdevasadaścaiva śravaṇo 'tha śraviṣṭhakaḥ  LiP 
yogātmāno mahātmānaḥ sarve yogasamanvitāḥ 
prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ rudralokāya te gatāḥ  LiP 
tataḥ pañcadaśe prāpte parivarte kramāgate 
traiyyāruṇiryadā vyāso dvāpare samapadyata  LiP 
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi nāmnā vedaśirā dvijaḥ 
tatra vedaśiro nāma astraṃ tatpārameśvaram  LiP 
bhaviṣyati mahāvīryaṃ vedaśīrṣaś ca parvataḥ 
himavatpṛṣṭhamāsādya sarasvatyāṃ nagottame  LiP 
tatrāpi mama te putrā bhaviṣyanti tapodhanāḥ 
kuṇiś ca kuṇibāhuś ca kuśarīraḥ kunetrakaḥ  LiP 
yogātmāno mahātmānaḥ sarve te hyūrdhvaretasaḥ 
prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ rudralokāya te gatāḥ  LiP 
vyāso yuge ṣoḍaśe tu yadā devo bhaviṣyati 
tatra yogapradānāya bhaktānāṃ ca yatātmanām  LiP 
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi gokarṇo nāma nāmataḥ 
bhaviṣyati supuṇyaṃ ca gokarṇaṃ nāma tadvanam  LiP 
tatrāpi mama te putrā bhaviṣyanti ca yoginaḥ 
kāśyapo hyuśanāścaiva cyavano 'tha bṛhaspatiḥ  LiP 
te 'pi tenaiva mārgeṇa dhyānayogasamanvitāḥ 
prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ gantāro rudrameva hi  LiP 
tataḥ saptadaśe caiva parivarte kramāgate 
yadā bhaviṣyati vyāso nāmnā devakṛtañjayaḥ  LiP 
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi guhāvāsīti nāmataḥ 
himavacchikhare ramye mahottuṅge mahālaye  LiP 
siddhakṣetraṃ mahāpuṇyaṃ bhaviṣyati mahālayam 
tatrāpi mama te putrā yogajñā brahmavādinaḥ  LiP 
bhaviṣyanti mahātmāno nirmamā nirahaṃkṛtāḥ 
utathyo vāmadevaś ca mahāyogo mahābalaḥ  LiP 
teṣāṃ śatasahasraṃ tu śiṣyāṇāṃ dhyānayoginām 
bhaviṣyanti tadā kāle sarve te dhyānayuñjakāḥ  LiP 
yogābhyāsaratāścaiva hṛdi kṛtvā maheśvaram 
mahālaye padaṃ nyastaṃ dṛṣṭvā yānti śivaṃ padam  LiP 
ye cānye 'pi mahātmānaḥ kalau tasmin yugāntike 
dhyāne manaḥ samādhāya vimalāḥ śuddhabuddhayaḥ  LiP 
mama prasādādyāsyanti rudralokaṃ gatajvarāḥ 
gatvā mahālayaṃ puṇyaṃ dṛṣṭvā māheśvaraṃ padam  LiP 
tīrṇastārayate jantur daśa pūrvāndaśottarān 
ātmānamekaviṃśaṃ tu tārayitvā mahālaye  LiP 
mama prasādādyāsyanti rudralokaṃ gatajvarāḥ 
tato 'ṣṭādaśame caiva parivarte yadā vibho  LiP 
tadā ṛtañjayo nāma vyāsastu bhavitā muniḥ 
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi śikhaṇḍī nāma nāmataḥ  LiP 
siddhakṣetre mahāpuṇye devadānavapūjite 
himavacchikhare ramye śikhaṇḍī nāma parvataḥ  LiP 
śikhaṇḍino vanaṃ cāpi yatra siddhaniṣevitam 
tatrāpi mama te putrā bhaviṣyanti tapodhanāḥ  LiP 
vācaśravā ṛcīkaś ca śyāvāśvaś ca yatīśvaraḥ 
yogātmāno mahātmānaḥ sarve te vedapāragāḥ  LiP 
prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ rudralokāya saṃvṛtāḥ 
atha ekonaviṃśe tu parivarte kramāgate  LiP 
vyāsastu bhavitā nāmnā bharadvājo mahāmuniḥ 
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi jaṭāmālī ca nāmataḥ  LiP 
himavacchikhare ramye jaṭāyuryatra parvataḥ 
tatrāpi mama te putrā bhaviṣyanti mahaujasaḥ  LiP 
hiraṇyanābhaḥ kauśalyo lokākṣī kuthumis tathā 
īśvarā yogadharmāṇaḥ sarve te hyūrdhvaretasaḥ  LiP 
prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ rudralokāya saṃsthitāḥ 
tato viṃśatimaścaiva parivarto yadā tadā  LiP 
gautamastu tadā vyāso bhaviṣyati mahāmuniḥ 
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi aṭṭahāsastu nāmataḥ  LiP
