tatraiva himavatpṛṣṭhe aṭṭahāso mahāgiriḥ  LiP 
devadānavayakṣendra siddhacāraṇasevitaḥ 
tatrāpi mama te putrā bhaviṣyanti mahaujasaḥ  LiP 
yogātmāno mahātmāno dhyāyino niyatavratāḥ 
sumanturbarbarī vidvān kabandhaḥ kuśikaṃdharaḥ  LiP 
prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ rudralokāya te gatāḥ 
ekaviṃśe punaḥ prāpte parivarte kramāgate  LiP 
vācaśravāḥ smṛto vyāso yadā sa ṛṣisattamaḥ 
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi dāruko nāma nāmataḥ  LiP 
tasmādbhaviṣyate puṇyaṃ devadāruvanaṃ śubham 
tatrāpi mama te putrā bhaviṣyanti mahaujasaḥ  LiP 
plakṣo dārbhāyaṇiścaiva ketumān gautamas tathā 
yogātmāno mahātmāno niyatā ūrdhvaretasaḥ  LiP 
naiṣṭhikaṃ vratamāsthāya rudralokāya te gatāḥ 
dvāviṃśe parivarte tu vyāsaḥ śuṣmāyaṇo yadā  LiP 
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi vārāṇasyāṃ mahāmuniḥ 
nāmnā vai lāṅgalī bhīmo yatra devāḥ savāsavāḥ  LiP 
drakṣyanti māṃ kalau tasmin bhavaṃ caiva halāyudham 
tatrāpi mama te putrā bhaviṣyanti sudhārmikāḥ  LiP 
bhallavī madhupiṅgaś ca śvetaketuḥ kuśas tathā 
prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ te 'pi dhyānaparāyaṇāḥ  LiP 
vimalā brahmabhūyiṣṭhā rudralokāya saṃsthitāḥ 
parivarte trayoviṃśe tṛṇabinduryadā muniḥ  LiP 
vyāso hi bhavitā brahmaṃs tadāhaṃ bhavitā punaḥ 
śveto nāma mahākāyo muniputrastu dhārmikaḥ  LiP 
tatra kālaṃ jariṣyāmi tadā girivarottame 
tena kālañjaro nāma bhaviṣyati sa parvataḥ  LiP

uśiko bṛhadaśvaś ca devalaḥ kavireva ca  LiP

chagalaḥ kuṇḍakarṇaś ca kubhāṇḍaś ca pravāhakaḥ  LiP

akṣapādaḥ kumāraś ca ulūko vatsa eva ca

aṣṭāviṃśe punaḥ prāpte parivarte kramāgate  LiP

yadā bhaviṣyati vyāso nāmnā dvaipāyanaḥ prabhuḥ  LiP

vasudevādyaduśreṣṭho vāsudevo bhaviṣyati  LiP

lokavismayanārthāya brahmacāriśarīrakaḥ  LiP

kuśikaś caiva gargaś ca mitraḥ kauruṣya eva ca  LiP

prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ vimalā hyūrdhvaretasaḥ  LiP 
rudralokaṃ gamiṣyanti punarāvṛttidurlabham 
ete pāśupatāḥ siddhā bhasmoddhūlitavigrahāḥ  LiP 
liṅgārcanaratā nityaṃ bāhyābhyantarataḥ sthitāḥ 
bhaktyā mayi ca yogena dhyānaniṣṭhā jitendriyāḥ  LiP 
saṃsārabandhacchedārthaṃ jñānamārgaprakāśakam 
svarūpajñānasiddhyarthaṃ yogaṃ pāśupataṃ mahat  LiP 
yogamārgā anekāś ca jñānamārgās tv anekaśaḥ 
na nivṛttimupāyānti vinā pañcākṣarīṃ kvacit  LiP 
yadācarettapaścāyaṃ sarvadvandvavivarjitam 
tadā sa mukto mantavyaḥ pakvaṃ phalamiva sthitaḥ  LiP 
ekāhaṃ yaḥ pumānsamyak caretpāśupatavratam 
na sāṃkhye pañcarātre vā na prāpnoti gatiṃ kadā  LiP 
ityetadvai mayā proktam avatāreṣu lakṣaṇam 
manvādikṛṣṇaparyantam aṣṭāviṃśad yugakramāt  LiP 
tatra śrutisamūhānāṃ vibhāgo dharmalakṣaṇaḥ 
bhaviṣyati tadā kalpe kṛṣṇadvaipāyano yadā  LiP 
sūta uvāca
niśamyaivaṃ mahātejā mahādevena kīrtitam 
rudrāvatāraṃ bhagavān praṇipatya maheśvaram  LiP 
tuṣṭāva vāgbhir iṣṭābhiḥ punaḥ prāha ca śaṅkaram 
pitāmaha uvāca
sarve viṣṇumayā devāḥ sarve viṣṇumayā gaṇāḥ  LiP 
na hi viṣṇusamā kācid gatiranyā vidhīyate 
ityevaṃ satataṃ vedā gāyanti nātra saṃśayaḥ  LiP 
sa devadevo bhagavāṃs tava liṅgārcane rataḥ 
tava praṇāmaparamaḥ kathaṃ devo hyabhūtprabhuḥ  LiP 
sūta uvāca
niśamya vacanaṃ tasya brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ 
prapibanniva cakṣurbhyāṃ prītastatpraśnagauravāt  LiP 
pūjāprakaraṇaṃ tasmai tamālokyāha śaṅkaraḥ 
bhavānnārāyaṇaścaiva śakraḥ sākṣātsurottamaḥ  LiP 
munayaś ca sadā liṅgaṃ sampūjya vidhipūrvakam 
svaṃsvaṃ padaṃ vibho prāptās tasmāt sampūjayanti te  LiP 
liṅgārcanaṃ vinā niṣṭhā nāsti tasmājjanārdanaḥ 
ātmano yajate nityaṃ śraddhayā bhagavānprabhuḥ  LiP 
ityevamuktvā brahmāṇam anugṛhya maheśvaraḥ 
punaḥ samprekṣya deveśaṃ tatraivāntaradhīyata  LiP 
tamuddiśya tadā brahmā namaskṛtya kṛtāñjaliḥ 
sraṣṭuṃ tvaśeṣaṃ bhagavāṃl labdhasaṃjñastu śaṅkarāt  LiP 
LiP  
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
kathaṃ pūjyo mahādevo liṅgamūrtirmaheśvaraḥ 
vaktumarhasi cāsmākaṃ romaharṣaṇa sāṃpratam  LiP 
sūta uvāca
devyā pṛṣṭo mahādevaḥ kailāse tāṃ nagātmajām 
aṅkasthāmāha deveśo liṅgārcanavidhiṃ kramāt  LiP 
tadā pārśve sthito nandī śālaṅkāyanakātmajaḥ 
śrutvākhilaṃ purā prāha brahmaputrāya suvratāḥ  LiP 
sanatkumārāya śubhaṃ liṅgārcanavidhiṃ param 
tasmādvyāso mahātejāḥ śrutavāñchrutisaṃmitam  LiP 
snānayogopacāraṃ ca yathā śailādino mukhāt 
śrutavān tatpravakṣyāmi snānādyaṃ cārcanāvidhim  LiP 
śailādiruvāca
atha snānavidhiṃ vakṣye brāhmaṇānāṃ hitāya ca 
sarvapāpaharaṃ sākṣāc chivena kathitaṃ purā  LiP 
anena vidhinā snātvā sakṛtpūjya ca śaṅkaram 
brahmakūrcaṃ ca pītvā tu sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate  LiP 
trividhaṃ snānamākhyātaṃ devadevena śaṃbhunā 
hitāya brāhmaṇādyānāṃ caturmukhasutottama  LiP 
vāruṇaṃ purataḥ kṛtvā tataścāgneyamuttamam 
mantrasnānaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā pūjayetparameśvaram  LiP 
bhāvaduṣṭo 'mbhasi snātvā bhasmanā ca na śudhyati 
bhāvaśuddhaścarecchaucam anyathā na samācaret  LiP 
saritsarastaḍāgeṣu sarveṣv ā pralayaṃ naraḥ 
snātvāpi bhāvaduṣṭaścen na śudhyati na saṃśayaḥ  LiP 
nṛṇāṃ hi cittakamalaṃ prabuddhamabhavadyadā 
prasuptaṃ tamasā jñāna bhānorbhāsā tadā śuciḥ  LiP 
mṛcchakṛttilapuṣpaṃ ca snānārthaṃ bhasitaṃ tathā 
ādāya tīre niḥkṣipya snānatīrthe kuśāni ca  LiP 
prakṣālyācamya pādau ca malaṃ dehādviśodhya ca 
dravyaistu tīradeśasthais tataḥ snānaṃ samācaret  LiP 
uddhṛtāsītimantreṇa punardehaṃ viśodhayet 
mṛdādāya tataścānyad vastraṃ snātvā hyanulbaṇam  LiP 
gandhadvārāṃ durādharṣām iti mantreṇa mantravit 
kapilāgomayenaiva khasthenaiva tu lepayet  LiP 
punaḥ snātvā parityajya tadvastraṃ malinaṃ tataḥ 
śuklavastraparīdhāno bhūtvā snānaṃ samācaret  LiP 
sarvapāpaviśuddhyartham āvāhya varuṇaṃ tathā 
sampūjya manasā devaṃ dhyānayajñena vai bhavam  LiP 
ācamya tristadā tīrthe hy avagāhya bhavaṃ smaran 
punarācamya vidhivad abhimantrya mahājalam  LiP 
avagāhya punastasmin japedvai cāghamarṣaṇam 
tattoye bhānusomāgni maṇḍalaṃ ca smaredvaśī  LiP 
ācamya ca punastasmāj jalāduttīrya mantravit 
praviśya tīrthamadhye tu punaḥ puṇyavivṛddhaye  LiP 
śṛṅgeṇa parṇapuṭakaiḥ pālāśaiḥ kṣālitais tathā 
sakuśena sapuṣpeṇa jalenaivābhiṣecayet  LiP 
rudreṇa pavamānena tvaritākhyena mantravit 
taratsamandīvargādyais tathā śāntidvayena ca  LiP 
śāntidharmeṇa caikena pañcabrahmapavitrakaiḥ 
tattanmantrādhidevānāṃ svarūpaṃ ca ṛṣīn smaran  LiP 
evaṃ hi cābhiṣicyātha svamūrdhni payasā dvijāḥ 
dhyāyecca tryambakaṃ devaṃ hṛdi pañcāsyam īśvaram  LiP 
ācamyācamanaṃ kuryāt svasūtroktaṃ samīkṣya ca 
pavitrahastaḥ svāsīnaḥ śucau deśe yathāvidhi  LiP 
abhyukṣya sakuśaṃ cāpi dakṣiṇena kareṇa tu 
pibetprakṣipya tristoyaṃ cakrī bhūtvā hyatandritaḥ  LiP 
pradakṣiṇaṃ tataḥ kuryād dhiṃsāpāpapraśāntaye 
evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ proktaṃ snānācamanamuttamam  LiP 
sarveṣāṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ tu hitārthe dvijasattamāḥ  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge snānavidhirnāma pañcaviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
LiP  
nandyuvāca
āvāhayettato devīṃ gāyatrīṃ vedamātaram 
āyātu varadā devīty anenaiva maheśvarīm  LiP 
pādyamācamanīyaṃ ca tasyāścārghyaṃ pradāpayet 
prāṇāyāmatrayaṃ kṛtvā samāsīnaḥ sthito 'pi vā  LiP 
sahasraṃ vā tadardhaṃ vā śatamaṣṭottaraṃ tu vā 
gāyatrīṃ praṇavenaiva trividheṣvekamācaret  LiP 
arghyaṃ dattvā samabhyarcya praṇamya śirasā svayam 
uttame śikhare devīty uktvodvāsya ca mātaram  LiP 
prācyālokyābhivandyeśāṃ gāyatrīṃ vedamātaram 
kṛtāñjalipuṭo bhūtvā prārthayedbhāskaraṃ tathā  LiP 
udutyaṃ ca tathā citraṃ jātavedasameva ca 
abhivandya punaḥ sūryaṃ brahmāṇaṃ ca vidhānataḥ  LiP 
tathā saurāṇi sūktāni ṛgyajuḥsāmajāni ca 
japtvā pradakṣiṇaṃ paścāt triḥ kṛtvā ca vibhāvasoḥ  LiP 
ātmānaṃ cāntarātmānaṃ paramātmānameva ca 
abhivandya punaḥ sūryaṃ brahmāṇaṃ ca vibhāvasum  LiP 
munīn pitṝn yathānyāyaṃ svanāmnāvāhayettataḥ 
sarvānāvāhayāmīti devānāvāhya sarvataḥ  LiP 
tarpayedvidhinā paścāt prāṅmukho vā hyudaṅmukhaḥ 
dhyātvā svarūpaṃ tattattvam abhivandya yathākramam  LiP 
devānāṃ puṣpatoyena ṛṣīṇāṃ tu kuśāṃbhasā 
pitṝṇāṃ tilatoyena gandhayuktena sarvataḥ  LiP 
yajñopavītī devānāṃ nivītī ṛṣitarpaṇam 
prācīnāvītī viprendra pitṝṇāṃ tarpayet kramāt  LiP 
aṅgulyagreṇa vai dhīmāṃs tarpayeddevatarpaṇam 
ṛṣīn kaniṣṭhāṅgulinā śrotriyaḥ sarvasiddhaye  LiP 
pitṝṃstu tarpayed vidvān dakṣiṇāṅguṣṭhakena tu 
tathaivaṃ muniśārdūla brahmayajñaṃ yajed dvijaḥ  LiP 
devayajñaṃ ca mānuṣyaṃ bhūtayajñaṃ tathaiva ca 
pitṛyajñaṃ ca pūtātmā yajñakarmaparāyaṇaḥ  LiP 
svaśākhādhyayanaṃ vipra brahmayajña iti smṛtaḥ 
agnau juhoti yaccānnaṃ devayajña iti smṛtaḥ  LiP 
sarveṣāmeva bhūtānāṃ balidānaṃ vidhānataḥ 
bhūtayajña iti prokto bhūtidaḥ sarvadehinām  LiP 
sadārān sarvatattvajñān brāhmaṇān vedapāragān 
praṇamya tebhyo yaddattam annaṃ mānuṣa ucyate  LiP 
pitṝn uddiśya yaddattaṃ pitṛyajñaḥ sa ucyate 
evaṃ pañca mahāyajñān kuryāt sarvārthasiddhaye  LiP 
sarveṣāṃ śṛṇu yajñānāṃ brahmayajñaḥ paraḥ smṛtaḥ 
brahmayajñarato martyo brahmaloke mahīyate  LiP 
brahmayajñena tuṣyanti sarve devāḥ savāsavāḥ 
brahmā ca bhagavānviṣṇuḥ śaṅkaro nīlalohitaḥ  LiP 
vedāś ca pitaraḥ sarve nātra kāryā vicāraṇā 
grāmādbahirgato bhūtvā brāhmaṇo brahmayajñavit  LiP 
yāvat tvadṛṣṭam abhavad uṭajānāṃ chadaṃ naraḥ 
prācyāmudīcyāṃ ca tathā prāgudīcyāmathāpi vā  LiP 
puṇyamācamanaṃ kuryād brahmayajñārthameva tat 
prītyarthaṃ ca ṛcāṃ viprāḥ triḥ pītvā plāvya plāvya ca  LiP 
yajuṣāṃ parimṛjyaivaṃ dviḥ prakṣālya ca vāriṇā 
prītyarthaṃ sāmavedānām upaspṛśya ca mūrdhani  LiP 
spṛśedatharvavedānāṃ netre cāṅgirasāṃ tathā 
nāsike brāhmaṇo 'ṅgānāṃ kṣālya kṣālya ca vāriṇā  LiP 
aṣṭādaśapurāṇānāṃ brahmādyānāṃ tathaiva ca 
tathā copapurāṇānāṃ saurādīnāṃ yathākramam  LiP 
puṇyānāmitihāsānāṃ śaivādīnāṃ tathaiva ca 
śrotre spṛśeddhi tuṣṭyarthaṃ hṛddeśaṃ tu tataḥ spṛśet  LiP 
kalpādīnāṃ tu sarveṣāṃ kalpavitkalpavittamāḥ 
evamācamya cāstīrya darbhapiñjūlam ātmanaḥ  LiP 
kṛtvā pāṇitale dhīmān ātmano dakṣiṇottaram 
hemāṅgulīyasaṃyukto brahmabandhayuto 'pi vā  LiP 
vidhivadbrahmayajñaṃ ca kuryātsūtrī samāhitaḥ 
akṛtvā ca muniḥ pañca mahāyajñāndvijottamaḥ  LiP 
bhuktvā ca sūkarāṇāṃ tu yonau vai jāyate naraḥ 
tasmātsarvaprayatnena kartavyāḥ śubhamicchatā  LiP 
brahmayajñādatha snānaṃ kṛtvādau sarvathātmanaḥ 
tīrthaṃ saṃgṛhya vidhivat praviśecchibiraṃ vaśī  LiP 
bahireva gṛhātpādau hastau prakṣālya vāriṇā 
bhasmasnānaṃ tataḥ kuryād vidhivad dehaśuddhaye  LiP 
śodhya bhasma yathānyāyaṃ praṇavenāgnihotrajam 
jyotiḥ sūrya iti prātar juhuyādudite yataḥ  LiP 
jyotiragnis tathā sāyaṃ samyak cānudite mṛṣā 
tasmāduditahomasthaṃ bhasitaṃ pāvanaṃ śubham  LiP 
nāsti satyasamaṃ yasmād asatyaṃ pātakaṃ ca yat 
īśānena śirodeśaṃ mukhaṃ tatpuruṣeṇa ca  LiP 
urodeśamaghoreṇa guhyaṃ vāmena suvratāḥ 
sadyena pādau sarvāṅgaṃ praṇavenābhiṣecayet  LiP 
tataḥ prakṣālayetpādaṃ hastaṃ brahmavidāṃ varaḥ 
vyapohya bhasma cādāya devadevamanusmaran  LiP 
mantrasnānaṃ tataḥ kuryād āpohiṣṭhādibhiḥ kramāt 
puṇyaiścaiva tathā mantrair ṛgyajuḥsāmasaṃbhavaiḥ  LiP 
dvijānāṃ tu hitāyaivaṃ kathitaṃ snānamadya te 
saṃkṣipya yaḥ sakṛtkuryāt sa yāti paramaṃ padam  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge pañcayajñavidhānaṃ nāma ṣaḍviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ

śailādiruvāca
vakṣyāmi śṛṇu saṃkṣepāl liṅgārcanāvidhikramam 
vaktuṃ varṣaśatenāpi na śakyaṃ vistareṇa yat  LiP 
evaṃ snātvā yathānyāyaṃ pūjāsthānaṃ praviśya ca 
prāṇāyāmatrayaṃ kṛtvā dhyāyeddevaṃ triyaṃbakam  LiP 
pañcavaktraṃ daśabhujaṃ śuddhasphaṭikasannibham 
sarvābharaṇasaṃyuktaṃ citrāṃbaravibhūṣitam  LiP 
tasya rūpaṃ samāśritya dāhanaplāvanādibhiḥ 
śaivīṃ tanuṃ samāsthāya pūjayetparameśvaram  LiP 
dehaśuddhiṃ ca kṛtvaiva mūlamantraṃ nyaset kramāt 
sarvatra praṇavenaiva brahmāṇi ca yathākramam  LiP 
sūtre namaḥ śivāyeti chandāṃsi parame śubhe 
mantrāṇi sūkṣmarūpeṇa saṃsthitāni yatastataḥ  LiP 
nyagrodhabīje nyagrodhas tathā sūtre tu śobhane 
mahatyapi mahadbrahma saṃsthitaṃ sūkṣmavatsvayam  LiP 
secayedarcanasthānaṃ gandhacandanavāriṇā 
dravyāṇi śodhayetpaścāt kṣālanaprokṣaṇādibhiḥ  LiP 
kṣālanaṃ prokṣaṇaṃ caiva praṇavena vidhīyate 
prokṣaṇī cārghyapātraṃ ca pādyapātram anukramāt  LiP 
tathā hyācamanīyārthaṃ kalpitaṃ pātrameva ca 
sthāpayed vidhinā dhīmān avaguṇṭhya yathāvidhi  LiP 
darbhair ācchādayeccaiva prokṣayecchuddhavāriṇā 
teṣu teṣvatha sarveṣu kṣipettoyaṃ suśītalam  LiP 
praṇavena kṣipetteṣu dravyāṇyālokya buddhimān 
uśīraṃ candanaṃ caiva pādye tu parikalpayet  LiP 
jātikaṅkolakarpūra bahumūlatamālakam 
cūrṇayitvā yathānyāyaṃ kṣipedācamanīyake  LiP 
evaṃ sarveṣu pātreṣu dāpayeccandanaṃ tathā 
karpūraṃ ca yathānyāyaṃ puṣpāṇi vividhāni ca  LiP 
kuśāgramakṣatāṃścaiva yavavrīhitilāni ca 
ājyasiddhārthapuṣpāṇi bhasitaṃ cārghyapātrake  LiP 
kuśapuṣpayavavrīhi bahumūlatamālakam 
dāpayetprokṣaṇīpātre bhasitaṃ praṇavena ca  LiP 
nyasetpañcākṣaraṃ caiva gāyatrīṃ rudradevatām 
kevalaṃ praṇavaṃ vāpi vedasāramanuttamam  LiP 
atha saṃprokṣayetpaścād dravyāṇi praṇavena tu 
prokṣaṇīpātrasaṃsthena īśānādyaiś ca pañcabhiḥ  LiP 
pārśvato devadevasya nandinaṃ māṃsamarcayet 
dīptānalāyutaprakhyaṃ trinetraṃ tridaśeśvaram  LiP 
bālendumukuṭaṃ caiva harivaktraṃ caturbhujam 
puṣpamālādharaṃ saumyaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam  LiP 
uttare cātmanaḥ puṇyāṃ bhāryāṃ ca marutāṃ śubhām 
suyaśāṃ suvratāṃ cāmbāṃ pādamaṇḍanatatparām  LiP 
evaṃ pūjya praviśyāntar bhavanaṃ parameṣṭhinaḥ 
dattvā puṣpāñjaliṃ bhaktyā pañcamūrdhasu pañcabhiḥ  LiP 
gandhapuṣpais tathā dhūpair vividhaiḥ pūjya śaṅkaram 
skandaṃ vināyakaṃ devīṃ liṅgaśuddhiṃ ca kārayet  LiP 
japtvā sarvāṇi mantrāṇi praṇavādinamo 'ntakam 
kalpayedāsanaṃ paścāt padmākhyaṃ praṇavena tat  LiP 
tasya pūrvadalaṃ sākṣād aṇimāmayam akṣaram 
laghimā dakṣiṇaṃ caiva mahimā paścimaṃ tathā  LiP 
prāptistathottaraṃ patraṃ prākāmyaṃ pāvakasya tu 
īśitvaṃ nairṛtaṃ patraṃ vaśitvaṃ vāyugocare  LiP 
sarvajñatvaṃ tathaiśānyaṃ karṇikā soma ucyate 
somasyādhas tathā sūryas tasyādhaḥ pāvakaḥ svayam  LiP 
dharmādayo vidikṣvete tv anantaṃ kalpayetkramāt 
avyaktādicaturdikṣu somasyānte guṇatrayam  LiP 
ātmatrayaṃ tataścordhvaṃ tasyānte śivapīṭhikā 
sadyojātaṃ prapadyāmīty āvāhya parameśvaram  LiP 
vāmadevena mantreṇa sthāpayedāsanopari 
sānnidhyaṃ rudragāyatryā aghoreṇa nirudhya ca  LiP 
īśānaḥ sarvavidyānām iti mantreṇa pūjayet 
pādyamācamanīyaṃ ca vibhoścārghyaṃ pradāpayet  LiP 
snāpayedvidhinā rudraṃ gandhacandanavāriṇā 
pañcagavyavidhānena gṛhya pātre 'bhimantrya ca  LiP 
praṇavenaiva gavyaistu snāpayecca yathāvidhi 
ājyena madhunā caiva tathā cekṣurasena ca  LiP 
puṇyairdravyairmahādevaṃ praṇavenābhiṣecayet 
jalabhāṇḍaiḥ pavitraistu mantraistoyaṃ kṣipettataḥ  LiP 
śuddhiṃ kṛtvā yathānyāyaṃ sitavastreṇa sādhakaḥ 
kuśāpāmārgakarpūra jātipuṣpakacampakaiḥ  LiP 
karavīraiḥ sitaiścaiva mallikākamalotpalaiḥ 
āpūrya puṣpaiḥ suśubhaiḥ candanādyaiś ca tajjalam  LiP 
nyasenmantrāṇi tattoye sadyojātādikāni tu 
suvarṇakalaśenātha tathā vai rājatena vā  LiP 
tāmreṇa padmapatreṇa pālāśena dalena vā 
śaṃkhena mṛnmayenātha śodhitena śubhena vā  LiP 
sakūrcena sapuṣpeṇa snāpayenmantrapūrvakam 
mantrāṇi te pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu sarvārthasiddhaye  LiP 
yairliṅgaṃ sakṛdapyevaṃ snāpya mucyeta mānavaḥ 
pavamānena mantrajñāḥ tathā vāmīyakena ca  LiP 
rudreṇa nīlarudreṇa śrīsūktena śubhena ca 
rajanīsūktakenaiva camakena śubhena ca  LiP 
hotāreṇātha śirasā atharveṇa śubhena ca 
śāntyā cātha punaḥ śāntyā bhāruṇḍenāruṇena ca  LiP 
vāruṇena ca jyeṣṭhena tathā vedavratena ca 
tathāntareṇa puṇyena sūktena puruṣeṇa ca  LiP 
tvaritenaiva rudreṇa kapinā ca kapardinā 
āvosajeti sāmnā tu bṛhaccandreṇa viṣṇunā  LiP 
virūpākṣeṇa skandena śataṛgbhiḥ śivais tathā

Dāruvana
munayo dārugahane tapastepuḥ sudāruṇam 
tuṣṭyarthaṃ devadevasya sadāratanayāgnayaḥ  LiP 
tuṣṭo rudro jagannāthaś cekitāno vṛṣadhvajaḥ 
dhūrjaṭiḥ parameśāno bhagavānnīlalohitaḥ  LiP 
pravṛttilakṣaṇaṃ jñānaṃ jñātuṃ dāruvanaukasām 
parīkṣārthaṃ jagannāthaḥ śraddhayā krīḍayā ca saḥ  LiP 
nivṛttilakṣaṇajñāna pratiṣṭhārthaṃ ca śaṅkaraḥ 
devadāruvanasthānāṃ pravṛttijñānacetasām  LiP 
vikṛtaṃ rūpamāsthāya digvāsā viṣamekṣaṇaḥ 
mugdho dvihastaḥ kṛṣṇāṅgo divyaṃ dāruvanaṃ yayau  LiP 
mandasmitaṃ ca bhagavān strīṇāṃ manasijodbhavam 
bhrūvilāsaṃ ca gānaṃ ca cakārātīva suṃdaraḥ  LiP 
saṃprokṣya nārīvṛndaṃ vai muhurmuhuranaṅgahā 
anaṅgavṛddhim akarod atīva madhurākṛtiḥ  LiP 
vane taṃ puruṣaṃ dṛṣṭvā vikṛtaṃ nīlalohitam 
striyaḥ pativratāścāpi tamevānvayurādarāt  LiP 
vanoṭajadvāragatāś ca nāryo visrastavastrābharaṇā viceṣṭāḥ 
labdhvā smitaṃ tasya mukhāravindād drumālayasthās tam athānvayustāḥ  LiP 
dṛṣṭvā kāścidbhavaṃ nāryo madaghūrṇitalocanāḥ 
vilāsabāhyāstāścāpi bhrūvilāsaṃ pracakrire  LiP 
atha dṛṣṭvāparā nāryaḥ kiṃcit prahasitānanāḥ 
kiṃcid visrastavasanāḥ srastakāñcīguṇā jaguḥ  LiP

svānsvānvicitrān valayānpravidhya madānvitā bandhujanāṃś ca jagmuḥ  LiP 
kācittadā taṃ na viveda dṛṣṭvā vivāsanā srastamahāṃśukā ca 
śākhāvicitrān viṭapānprasiddhān madānvitā bandhujanāṃstathānyāḥ  LiP 
kāścijjagustaṃ nanṛtur nipetuś ca dharātale

kutretyatha prasīdeti jajalpuḥ prītamānasāḥ  LiP 
viparītā nipeturvai visrastāṃśukamūrdhajāḥ 
pativratāḥ patīnāṃ tu saṃnidhau bhavamāyayā  LiP 
dṛṣṭvā śrutvā bhavastāsāṃ ceṣṭāvākyāni cāvyayaḥ 
śubhaṃ vāpyaśubhaṃ vāpi noktavānparameśvaraḥ  LiP 
dṛṣṭvā nārīkulaṃ viprās tathābhūtaṃ ca śaṅkaram

tapāṃsi teṣāṃ sarveṣāṃ pratyāhanyanta śaṅkare 
yathādityaprakāśena tārakā nabhasi sthitāḥ  LiP

samṛddhaśreyasāṃ yonir yajñā vai nāśamāptavān  LiP 
bhṛgor api ca śāpena viṣṇuḥ paramavīryavān

ṛṣiṇā gautamenorvyāṃ kruddhena vinipātitam  LiP

dvitīyaścāmṛtādhāro hy apeyo brāhmaṇaiḥ kṛtaḥ  LiP

story of Sudarśana
sudarśanena muninā kālamṛtyurapi svayam 
purā bhūmau dvijāgryeṇa jito hyatithipūjayā  LiP 
anyathā nāsti saṃtartuṃ gṛhasthaiś ca dvijottamaiḥ 
tyaktvā cātithipūjāṃ tām ātmano bhuvi śodhanam  LiP 
gṛhastho 'pi purā jetuṃ sudarśana iti śrutaḥ 
pratijñāmakarojjāyāṃ bhāryāmāha pativratām  LiP 
suvrate subhru subhage śṛṇu sarvaṃ prayatnataḥ 
tvayā vai nāvamantavyā gṛhe hyatithayaḥ sadā  LiP 
sarva eva svayaṃ sākṣād atithiryatpinākadhṛk 
tasmādatithaye dattvā ātmānamapi pūjaya  LiP 
evamuktvātha saṃtaptā vivaśā sā pativratā 
patimāha rudantī ca kimuktaṃ bhavatā prabho  LiP 
tasyāstadvacanaṃ śrutvā punaḥ prāha sudarśanaḥ 
deyaṃ sarvaṃ śivāyārye śiva evātithiḥ svayam  LiP 
tasmātsarve pūjanīyāḥ sarve 'pyatithayaḥ sadā 
evamuktā tadā bhartrā bhāryā tasya pativratā  LiP 
śeṣāmivājñāmādāya mūrdhnā sā prācarattadā 
parīkṣituṃ tathā śraddhāṃ tayoḥ sākṣād dvijottamāḥ  LiP 
dharmo dvijottamo bhūtvā jagāmātha munergṛham 
taṃ dṛṣṭvā cārcayāmāsa sārghyādyairanaghā dvijam  LiP 
sampūjitastayā tāṃ tu prāha dharmo dvijaḥ svayam 
bhadre kutaḥ patirdhīmāṃs tava bhartā sudarśanaḥ  LiP 
annādyairalamadyārye svaṃ dātumiha cārhasi 
sā ca lajjāvṛtā nārī smarantī kathitaṃ purā  LiP 
bhartrā nyamīlayannetre cacāla ca pativratā 
kiṃcetyāha punastaṃ vai dharme cakre ca sā matim  LiP 
nivedituṃ kilātmānaṃ tasmai patyurihājñayā 
etasminnantare bhartā tasyā nāryāḥ sudarśanaḥ  LiP 
gṛhadvāraṃ gato dhīmāṃs tāmuvāca mahāmuniḥ 
ehyehi kva gatā bhadre tamuvācātithiḥ svayam  LiP 
bhāryayā tvanayā sārdhaṃ maithunastho 'hamadya vai 
sudarśana mahābhāga kiṃ kartavyamihocyatām  LiP 
suratāntastu viprendra saṃtuṣṭo 'haṃ dvijottama 
sudarśanastataḥ prāha suprahṛṣṭo dvijottamaḥ  LiP 
bhuṅkṣva caināṃ yathākāmaṃ gamiṣye 'haṃ dvijottama 
hṛṣṭo 'tha darśayāmāsa svātmānaṃ dharmarāṭ svayam  LiP 
pradadau cepsitaṃ sarvaṃ tamāha ca mahādyutiḥ 
eṣā na bhuktā viprendra manasāpi suśobhanā  LiP 
mayā caiṣā na saṃdehaḥ śraddhāṃ jñātumihāgataḥ 
jito vai yastvayā mṛtyur dharmeṇaikena suvrata  LiP 
aho 'sya tapaso vīryam ityuktvā prayayau ca saḥ 
tasmāttathā pūjanīyāḥ sarve hyatithayaḥ sadā  LiP 
bahunātra kimuktena bhāgyahīnā dvijottamāḥ 
tameva śaraṇaṃ tūrṇaṃ gantumarhatha śaṅkaram  LiP 
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā brahmaṇo brāhmaṇarṣabhāḥ 
brahmāṇamabhivandyārtāḥ procurākulitekṣaṇāḥ  LiP 
brāhmaṇā ūcuḥ
nāpekṣitaṃ mahābhāga jīvitaṃ vikṛtāḥ striyaḥ 
dṛṣṭo 'smābhir mahādevo nindito yastvaninditaḥ  LiP

pitāmaha uvāca
ādau vedānadhītyaiva śraddhayā ca guroḥ sadā 
vicāryārthaṃ munerdharmān pratijñāya dvijottamāḥ  LiP 
grahaṇāntaṃ hi vā vidvān atha dvādaśavārṣikam 
snātvāhṛtya ca dārānvai putrānutpādya suvratān  LiP 
vṛttibhiścānurūpābhis tān vibhajya sutānmuniḥ 
agniṣṭomādibhiśceṣṭvā yajñairyajñeśvaraṃ vibhum  LiP 
pūjayet paramātmānaṃ prāpyāraṇyaṃ vibhāvasau 
munirdvādaśavarṣaṃ vā varṣamātram athāpi vā  LiP 
pakṣadvādaśakaṃ vāpi dinadvādaśakaṃ tu vā 
kṣīrabhuk saṃyutaḥ śāntaḥ sarvān sampūjayetsurān  LiP 
iṣṭvaivaṃ juhuyādagnau yajñapātrāṇi mantrataḥ 
apsu vai pārthivaṃ nyasya gurave taijasāni tu  LiP

praṇipatya guruṃ bhūmau viraktaḥ saṃnyasedyatiḥ  LiP

vratenānaśanenāpi toyavṛttyāpi vā punaḥ  LiP

evaṃ jīvanmṛto no cet ṣaṇmāsādvatsarāttu vā  LiP 
prasthānādikamāyāsaṃ svadehasya caredyatiḥ 
śivasāyujyamāpnoti karmaṇāpyevamācaran  LiP 
sadyo 'pi labhate muktiṃ bhaktiyukto dṛḍhavratāḥ  LiP 
tyāgena vā kiṃ vidhināpy anena bhaktasya rudrasya śubhairvrataiśca 
yajñaiś ca dānairvividhaiś ca homair labdhaiścaśāstrairvividhaiś ca vedaiḥ  LiP 
śvetenaivaṃ jito mṛtyur bhavabhaktyā mahātmanā 
vo 'stu bhaktirmahādeve śaṅkare paramātmani  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge ekonatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ

śailādiruvāca
evamuktāstadā tena brahmaṇā brāhmaṇarṣabhāḥ 
śvetasya ca kathāṃ puṇyām apṛcchan paramarṣayaḥ  LiP 
pitāmaha uvāca
śveto nāma muniḥ śrīmān gatāyurgirigahvare 
sakto hyabhyarcya yadbhaktyā tuṣṭāva ca maheśvaram  LiP 
rudrādhyāyena puṇyena namastetyādinā dvijāḥ 
tataḥ kālo mahātejāḥ kālaprāptaṃ dvijottamam  LiP 
netuṃ saṃcintya viprendrāḥ sānnidhyamakaronmuneḥ 
śveto 'pi dṛṣṭvā taṃ kālaṃ kālaprāpto 'pi śaṅkaram  LiP 
pūjayāmāsa puṇyātmā triyaṃbakamanusmaran 
triyaṃbakaṃ yajedevaṃ sugandhiṃ puṣṭivardhanam  LiP 
kiṃ kariṣyati me mṛtyur mṛtyormṛtyurahaṃ yataḥ

etadvaḥ sampravakṣyāmi kathā sarvasvamadya vai

tulyau mānāvamānau ca tadāvaraṇamuttamam  LiP 
bhasmasnānena digdhāṅgo dhyāyate manasā bhavam 
yadyakāryasahasrāṇi kṛtvā yaḥ snāti bhasmanā  LiP 
tatsarvaṃ dahate bhasma yathāgnistejasā vanam 
tasmād yatnaparo bhūtvā trikālamapi yaḥ sadā  LiP 
bhasmanā kurute snānaṃ gāṇapatyaṃ sa gacchati 
samāhṛtya kratūn sarvān gṛhītvā vratamuttamam  LiP 
dhyāyanti ye mahādevaṃ līlāsadbhāvabhāvitāḥ 
uttareṇāryapanthānaṃ te 'mṛtatvamavāpnuyuḥ  LiP 
dakṣiṇena ca panthānaṃ ye śmaśānāni bhejire 
aṇimā garimā caiva laghimā prāptireva ca  LiP 
icchā kāmāvasāyitvaṃ tathā prākāmyameva ca 
īkṣaṇena ca panthānaṃ ye śmaśānāni bhejire 
aṇimā garimā caiva laghimā prāptireva ca  LiP 
indrādayas tathā devāḥ kāmikavratamāsthitāḥ 
aiśvaryaṃ paramaṃ prāpya sarve prathitatejasaḥ  LiP 
vyapagatamadamohamuktarāgas tamorajodoṣavivarjitasvabhāvaḥ 
paribhavamidamuttamaṃ viditvā paśupatiyogaparo bhavetsadaiva  LiP 
imaṃ pāśupataṃ dhyāyan sarvapāpapraṇāśanam 
yaḥ paṭhecca śucirbhūtvā śraddadhāno jitendriyaḥ  LiP 
sarvapāpaviśuddhātmā rudralokaṃ sa gacchati 
te sarve munayaḥ śrutvā vasiṣṭhādyā dvijottamāḥ  LiP 
bhasmapāṇḍuradigdhāṅgā babhūvurvigataspṛhāḥ 
rudralokāya kalpānte saṃsthitāḥ śivatejasā  LiP 
tasmānna nindyāḥ pūjyāśca vikṛtā malinā api 
rūpānvitāś ca viprendrāḥ sadā yogīndraśaṅkayā  LiP 
bahunā kiṃ pralāpena bhavabhaktā dvijottamāḥ 
saṃpūjyāḥ sarvayatnena śivavannātra saṃśayaḥ  LiP 
malināścaiva viprendrā bhavabhaktā dṛḍhavratāḥ 
dadhīcastu yathā deva devaṃ jitvā vyavasthitaḥ  LiP 
nārāyaṇaṃ tathā loke rudrabhaktyā na saṃśayaḥ 
tasmātsarvaprayatnena bhasmadigdhatanūruhāḥ  LiP 
jaṭino muṇḍinaścaiva nagnā nānāprakāriṇaḥ 
saṃpūjyāḥ śivavannityaṃ manasā karmaṇā girā  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge yogipraśaṃsā nāma catustriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
LiP  
sanatkumāra uvāca
kathaṃ jaghāna rājānaṃ kṣupaṃ pādena suvrata 
dadhīcaḥ samare jitvā devadevaṃ janārdanam  LiP 
vajrāsthitvaṃ kathaṃ lebhe mahādevānmahātapāḥ 
vaktumarhasi śailāde jito mṛtyustvayā yathā  LiP 
śailādiruvāca
brahmaputro mahātejā rājā kṣupa iti smṛtaḥ 
abhūnmitro dadhīcasya munīndrasya janeśvaraḥ  LiP 
cirāttayoḥ prasaṃgādvai vādaḥ kṣupadadhīcayoḥ 
abhavat kṣatriyaśreṣṭho vipra eveti viśrutaḥ  LiP 
aṣṭānāṃ lokapālānāṃ vapurdhārayate nṛpaḥ 
tasmādindro hyayaṃ vahnir yamaś ca nirṛtis tathā  LiP 
varuṇaścaiva vāyuś ca somo dhanada eva ca 
īśvaro 'haṃ na saṃdeho nāvamantavya eva ca  LiP 
mahatī devatā yā sā mahataścāpi suvrata 
tasmāttvayā mahābhāga cyāvaneya sadā hyaham  LiP 
nāvamantavya eveha pūjanīyaś ca sarvathā 
śrutvā tathā mataṃ tasya kṣupasya munisattamaḥ  LiP 
dadhīcaś cyāvaniś cogro gauravādātmano dvijaḥ 
atāḍayatkṣupaṃ mūrdhni dadhīco vāmamuṣṭinā 
cicheda vajreṇa ca taṃ dadhīcaṃ balavān kṣupaḥ  LiP 
brahmaloke purāsau hi brahmaṇaḥ kṣutasaṃbhavaḥ 
labdhaṃ vajraṃ ca kāryārthaṃ vajriṇā coditaḥ prabhuḥ  LiP 
svecchayaiva naro bhūtvā narapālo babhūva saḥ 
tasmādrājā sa viprendram ajayadvai mahābalaḥ  LiP 
yathā vajradharaḥ śrīmān balavāṃstamasānvitaḥ 
papāta bhūmau nihato vajreṇa dvijapuṅgavaḥ  LiP 
sasmāra ca tadā tatra duḥkhādvai bhārgavaṃ munim 
śukro 'pi saṃdhayāmāsa tāḍitaṃ kuliśena tam  LiP 
yogādetya dadhīcasya dehaṃ dehabhṛtāṃvaraḥ 
saṃdhāya pūrvavaddehaṃ dadhīcasyāha bhārgavaḥ  LiP 
bho dadhīca mahābhāga devadevamumāpatim 
sampūjya pūjyaṃ brahmādyair devadevaṃ nirañjanam  LiP 
avadhyo bhava viprarṣe prasādāttryambakasya tu 
mṛtasaṃjīvanaṃ tasmāl labdhametanmayā dvija  LiP 
nāsti mṛtyubhayaṃ śaṃbhor bhaktānāmiha sarvataḥ 
mṛtasaṃjīvanaṃ cāpi śaivamadya vadāmi te  LiP 
triyaṃbakaṃ yajāmahe trailokyapitaraṃ prabhum 
trimaṇḍalasya pitaraṃ triguṇasya maheśvaram  LiP 
tritattvasya trivahneś ca tridhābhūtasya sarvataḥ 
trivedasya mahādevaṃ sugandhiṃ puṣṭivardhanam  LiP 
sarvabhūteṣu sarvatra triguṇe prakṛtau tathā 
indriyeṣu tathānyeṣu deveṣu ca gaṇeṣu ca  LiP 
puṣpeṣu gandhavatsūkṣmaḥ sugandhiḥ parameśvaraḥ 
puṣṭiś ca prakṛtiryasmāt puruṣasya dvijottama  LiP 
mahadādiviśeṣānta vikalpasyāpi suvrata 
viṣṇoḥ pitāmahasyāpi munīnāṃ ca mahāmune  LiP 
indrasyāpi ca devānāṃ tasmādvai puṣṭivardhanaḥ 
taṃ devamamṛtaṃ rudraṃ karmaṇā tapasā tathā  LiP 
svādhyāyena ca yogena dhyānena ca yajāmahe 
satyenānena mukṣīyān mṛtyupāśād bhavaḥ svayam  LiP 
bandhamokṣakaro yasmād urvārukamiva prabhuḥ 
mṛtasaṃjīvano mantro mayā labdhastu śaṅkarāt  LiP 
japtvā hutvābhimantryaivaṃ jalaṃ pītvā divāniśam 
liṅgasya saṃnidhau dhyātvā nāsti mṛtyubhayaṃ dvija  LiP 
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā tapasārādhya śaṅkaram 
vajrāsthitvam avadhyatvam adīnatvaṃ ca labdhavān  LiP 
evamārādhya deveśaṃ dadhīco munisattamaḥ 
prāpyāvadhyatvamanyaiś ca vajrāsthitvaṃ prayatnataḥ  LiP 
atāḍayacca rājendraṃ pādamūlena mūrdhani 
kṣupo dadhīcaṃ vajreṇa jaghānorasi ca prabhuḥ  LiP 
nābhūnnāśāya tadvajraṃ dadhīcasya mahātmanaḥ 
prabhāvātparameśasya vajrabaddhaśarīriṇaḥ  LiP 
dṛṣṭvāpyavadhyatvamadīnatāṃ ca kṣupo dadhīcasya tadā prabhāvam 
ārādhayāmāsa hariṃ mukundam indrānujaṃ prekṣya tadāṃbujākṣam  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge kṣupābidhanṛpaparābhavavarṇanaṃ nāma pañcatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
LiP  
nandyuvāca
pūjayā tasya saṃtuṣṭo bhagavānpuruṣottamaḥ 
śrībhūmisahitaḥ śrīmāñ śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ  LiP 
kirīṭī padmahastaś ca sarvābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ 
pītāṃbaraś ca bhagavān devairdaityaiś ca saṃvṛtaḥ  LiP 
pradadau darśanaṃ tasmai divyaṃ vai garuḍadhvajaḥ 
divyena darśanenaiva dṛṣṭvā devaṃ janārdanam  LiP 
tuṣṭāva vāgbhir iṣṭābhiḥ praṇamya garuḍadhvajam 
tvamādistvamanādiś ca prakṛtistvaṃ janārdanaḥ  LiP 
puruṣastvaṃ jagannātho viṣṇurviśveśvaro bhavān 
yo 'yaṃ brahmāsi puruṣo viśvamūrtiḥ pitāmahaḥ  LiP 
tattvamādyaṃ bhavāneva paraṃ jyotirjanārdana 
paramātmā paraṃ dhāma śrīpate bhūpate prabho  LiP 
tvatkrodhasaṃbhavo rudras tamasā ca samāvṛtaḥ 
tvatprasādājjagaddhātā rajasā ca pitāmahaḥ  LiP 
tvatprasādātsvayaṃ viṣṇuḥ sattvena puruṣottamaḥ 
kālamūrte hare viṣṇo nārāyaṇa jaganmaya  LiP 
mahāṃs tathā ca bhūtādis tanmātrāṇīndriyāṇi ca 
tvayaivādhiṣṭhitānyeva viśvamūrte maheśvara  LiP 
mahādeva jagannātha pitāmaha jagadguro 
prasīda devadeveśa prasīda parameśvara  LiP 
prasīda tvaṃ jagannātha śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ 
vaikuṇṭha śaure sarvajña vāsudeva mahābhuja  LiP 
saṃkarṣaṇa mahābhāga pradyumna puruṣottama 
aniruddha mahāviṣṇo sadā viṣṇo namo 'stu te  LiP 
viṣṇo tavāsanaṃ divyam avyaktaṃ madhyato vibhuḥ 
sahasraphaṇasaṃyuktas tamomūrtirdharādharaḥ  LiP 
adhaś ca dharmo deveśa jñānaṃ vairāgyameva ca 
aiśvaryamāsanasyāsya pādarūpeṇa suvrata  LiP 
saptapātālapādastvaṃ dharājaghanameva ca 
vāsāṃsi sāgarāḥ sapta diśaścaiva mahābhujāḥ  LiP 
dyaurmūrdhā te vibho nābhiḥ khaṃ vāyurnāsikāṃ gataḥ 
netre somaś ca sūryaś ca keśā vai puṣkarādayaḥ  LiP 
nakṣatratārakā dyauś ca graiveyakavibhūṣaṇam 
kathaṃ stoṣyāmi deveśaṃ pūjyaś ca puruṣottamaḥ  LiP 
śraddhayā ca kṛtaṃ divyaṃ yac chrutaṃ yacca kīrtitam 
yadiṣṭaṃ tatkṣamasveśa nārāyaṇa namo 'stu te  LiP 
śailādiruvāca
idaṃ tu vaiṣṇavaṃ stotraṃ sarvapāpapraṇāśanam 
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi kṣupeṇa parikīrtitam  LiP 
śrāvayedvā dvijān bhaktyā viṣṇulokaṃ sa gacchati  LiP 
sampūjya caivaṃ tridaśeśvarādyaiḥ stutvā stutaṃ devamajeyamīśam 
vijñāpayāmāsa nirīkṣya bhaktyā janārdanāya praṇipatya mūrdhnā  LiP 
rājovāca
bhagavanbrāhmaṇaḥ kaścid dadhīca iti viśrutaḥ 
dharmavettā vinītātmā sakhā mama purābhavat  LiP 
avadhyaḥ sarvadā sarvaiḥ śaṅkarārcanatatparaḥ 
sāvajñaṃ vāmapādena sa māṃ mūrdhni sadasyatha  LiP 
tāḍayāmāsa deveśa viṣṇo viśvajagatpate 
uvāca ca madāviṣṭo na bibhemīti sarvataḥ  LiP 
jetumicchāmi taṃ vipraṃ dadhīcaṃ jagadīśvara 
yathā hitaṃ tathā kartuṃ tvamarhasi janārdana  LiP 
śailādiruvāca
jñātvā so 'pi dadhīcasya hy avadhyatvaṃ mahātmanaḥ 
sasmāra ca maheśasya prabhāvamatulaṃ hariḥ  LiP 
evaṃ smṛtvā hariḥ prāha brahmaṇaḥ kṣutasaṃbhavam 
viprāṇāṃ nāsti rājendra bhayametya maheśvaram  LiP 
viśeṣādrudrabhaktānām abhayaṃ sarvadā nṛpa 
nīcānāmapi sarvatra dadhīcasyāsya kiṃ punaḥ  LiP 
tasmāttava mahābhāga vijayo nāsti bhūpate 
duḥkhaṃ karomi viprasya śāpārthaṃ sasurasya me  LiP 
bhavitā tasya śāpena dakṣayajñe suraiḥ samam 
vināśo mama rājendra punarutthānameva ca  LiP 
tasmātsametya viprendraṃ sarvayatnena bhūpate 
karomi yatnaṃ rājendra dadhīcavijayāya te  LiP 
śailādiruvāca
śrutvā vākyaṃ kṣupaḥ prāha tathāstviti janārdanam 
bhagavānapi viprasya dadhīcasyāśramaṃ yayau  LiP 
āsthāya rūpaṃ viprasya bhagavān bhaktavatsalaḥ 
dadhīcamāha brahmarṣim abhivandya jagadguruḥ  LiP 
śrībhagavānuvāca
bhobho dadhīca brahmarṣe bhavārcanaratāvyaya 
varamekaṃ vṛṇe tvattas taṃ bhavāndātumarhati  LiP 
yācito devadevena dadhīcaḥ prāha viṣṇunā 
jñātaṃ tavepsitaṃ sarvaṃ na bibhemi tavāpyaham  LiP 
bhavān viprasya rūpeṇa āgato 'si janārdana 
bhūtaṃ bhaviṣyaṃ deveśa vartamānaṃ janārdana  LiP 
jñātaṃ prasādādrudrasya dvijatvaṃ tyaja suvrata 
ārādhito 'si deveśa kṣupeṇa madhusūdana  LiP 
jāne tavaināṃ bhagavan bhaktavatsalatāṃ hare 
sthāne tavaiṣā bhagavan bhaktavātsalyatā hare  LiP 
asti cedbhagavan bhītir bhavārcanaratasya me 
vaktumarhasi yatnena varadāṃbujalocana  LiP 
vadāmi na mṛṣā tasmān na bibhemi janārdana 
na bibhemi jagatyasmin devadaityadvijādapi  LiP 
nandyuvāca
śrutvā vākyaṃ dadhīcasya tadāsthāya janārdanaḥ 
svarūpaṃ sasmitaṃ prāha saṃtyajya dvijatāṃ kṣaṇāt  LiP 
śrībhagavānuvāca
bhayaṃ dadhīca sarvatra nāstyeva tava suvrata 
bhavārcanarato yasmād bhavān sarvajña eva ca  LiP 
bibhemīti sakṛdvaktuṃ tvamarhasi namastava 
niyogānmama viprendra kṣupaṃ prati sadasyatha  LiP 
evaṃ śrutvāpi tadvākyaṃ sāntvaṃ viṣṇormahāmuniḥ 
na bibhemīti taṃ prāha dadhīco devasattamam  LiP 
prabhāvāddevadevasya śaṃbhoḥ sākṣātpinākinaḥ 
śarvasya śaṅkarasyāsya sarvajñasya mahāmuniḥ  LiP 
tatastasya muneḥ śrutvā vacanaṃ kupito hariḥ 
cakramudyamya bhagavān didhakṣurmunisattamam  LiP 
abhavatkuṇṭhitāgraṃ hi viṣṇoścakraṃ sudarśanam 
prabhāvāddhi dadhīcasya kṣupasyaiva hi saṃnidhau  LiP 
dṛṣṭvā tatkuṇṭhitāgraṃ hi cakraṃ cakriṇamāha saḥ 
dadhīcaḥ sasmitaṃ sākṣāt sadasadvyaktikāraṇam  LiP 
bhagavan bhavatā labdhaṃ purātīva sudāruṇam 
sudarśanamiti khyātaṃ cakraṃ viṣṇo prayatnataḥ  LiP 
bhavasyaitacchubhaṃ cakraṃ na jighāṃsati māmiha 
brahmāstrādyaistathānyairhi prayatnaṃ kartumarhasi  LiP 
śailādiruvāca
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā dṛṣṭvā nirvīryamāyudham 
sasarja ca punastasmai sarvāstrāṇi samantataḥ  LiP 
cakrurdevāstatastasya viṣṇoḥ sāhāyyamavyayāḥ 
dvijenaikena yoddhuṃ hi pravṛttasya mahābalāḥ  LiP 
kuśamuṣṭiṃ tadādāya dadhīcaḥ saṃsmaranbhavam 
sasarja sarvadevebhyo vajrāsthiḥ sarvato vaśī  LiP 
divyaṃ triśūlam abhavat kālāgnisadṛśaprabham 
dagdhuṃ devānmatiṃ cakre yugāntāgnirivāparaḥ  LiP 
indranārāyaṇādyaiś ca devaistyaktāni yāni tu 
āyudhāni samastāni praṇemus triśikhaṃ mune  LiP 
devāś ca dudruvuḥ sarve dhvastavīryā dvijottama 
sasarja bhagavān viṣṇuḥ svadehātpuruṣottamaḥ  LiP 
ātmanaḥ sadṛśān divyāṃl lakṣalakṣāyutān gaṇān 
tāni sarvāṇi sahasā dadāha munisattamaḥ  LiP 
tato vismayanārthāya viśvamūrtirabhūddhariḥ 
tasya dehe hareḥ sākṣād apaśyaddvijasattamaḥ  LiP 
dadhīco bhagavānvipraḥ devatānāṃ gaṇān pṛthak 
rudrāṇāṃ koṭayaścaiva gaṇānāṃ koṭayastadā  LiP 
aṇḍānāṃ koṭayaścaiva viśvamūrtestanau tadā 
dṛṣṭvaitadakhilaṃ tatra cyāvanir vismitaṃ tadā  LiP 
viṣṇumāha jagannāthaṃ jaganmayamajaṃ vibhum 
aṃbhasābhyukṣya taṃ viṣṇuṃ viśvarūpaṃ mahāmuniḥ  LiP 
māyāṃ tyaja mahābāho pratibhāsā vicārataḥ 
vijñānānāṃ sahasrāṇi durvijñeyāni mādhava  LiP 
mayi paśya jagat sarvaṃ tvayā sārdham anindita 
brahmāṇaṃ ca tathā rudraṃ divyāṃ dṛṣṭiṃ dadāmi te  LiP 
ityuktvā darśayāmāsa svatanau nikhilaṃ muniḥ 
taṃ prāha ca hariṃ devaṃ sarvadevabhavodbhavam  LiP 
māyayā hyanayā kiṃ vā mantraśaktyātha vā prabho 
vastuśaktyātha vā viṣṇo dhyānaśaktyātha vā punaḥ  LiP 
tyaktvā māyāmimāṃ tasmād yoddhumarhasi yatnataḥ 
evaṃ tasya vacaḥ śrutvā dṛṣṭvā māhātmyamadbhutam  LiP 
devāś ca dudruvurbhūyo devaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ ca tam 
vārayāmāsa niśceṣṭaṃ padmayonirjagadguruḥ  LiP 
niśamya vacanaṃ tasya brahmaṇastena nirjitaḥ 
jagāma bhagavān viṣṇuḥ praṇipatya mahāmunim  LiP 
kṣupo duḥkhāturo bhūtvā sampūjya ca munīśvaram 
dadhīcamabhivandyāśu prārthayāmāsa viklavaḥ  LiP 
dadhīca kṣamyatāṃ deva mayājñānātkṛtaṃ sakhe 
viṣṇunā hi surairvāpi rudrabhaktasya kiṃ tava  LiP 
prasīda parameśāna durlabhā durjanairdvija 
bhaktirbhaktimatāṃ śreṣṭha madvidhaiḥ kṣatriyādhamaiḥ  LiP 
śrutvānugṛhya taṃ vipro dadhīcastapatāṃ varaḥ 
rājānaṃ muniśārdūlaḥ śaśāpa ca surottamān  LiP 
rudrakopāgninā devāḥ sadevendrā munīśvaraiḥ 
dhvastā bhavantu devena viṣṇunā ca samanvitāḥ  LiP 
prajāpater makhe puṇye dakṣasya sumahātmanaḥ 
evaṃ śaptvā kṣupaṃ prekṣya punarāha dvijottamaḥ  LiP 
devaiś ca pūjyā rājendra nṛpaiś ca vividhairgaṇaiḥ 
brāhmaṇā eva rājendra balinaḥ prabhaviṣṇavaḥ  LiP 
ityuktvā svoṭajaṃ vipraḥ praviveśa mahādyutiḥ 
dadhīcamabhivandyaiva jagāma svaṃ nṛpaḥ kṣayam  LiP 
tadeva tīrthamabhavat sthāneśvaramiti smṛtam 
sthāneśvaram anuprāpya śivasāyujyam āpnuyāt  LiP 
kathitastava saṃkṣepād vivādaḥ kṣubdadhīcayoḥ 
prabhāvaś ca dadhīcasya bhavasya ca mahāmune  LiP 
ya idaṃ kīrtayeddivyaṃ vivādaṃ kṣubdadhīcayoḥ 
jitvāpamṛtyuṃ dehānte brahmalokaṃ prayāti saḥ  LiP 
ya idaṃ kīrtya saṃgrāmaṃ praviśettasya sarvadā 
nāsti mṛtyubhayaṃ caiva vijayī ca bhaviṣyati  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge kṣupadadhīcisaṃvādo nāma ṣaṭtriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ

bhavānkathamanuprāpto mahādevamumāpatim 
śrotumicchāmi tatsarvaṃ vaktumarhasi me prabho  LiP 
śailādiruvāca
prajākāmaḥ śilādo 'bhūt pitā mama mahāmune 
so 'pyandhaḥ suciraṃ kalaṃ tapastepe suduścaram  LiP 
tapatastasya tapasā saṃtuṣṭo vajradhṛk prabhuḥ 
śilādamāha tuṣṭo 'smi varayasva varāniti  LiP 
tataḥ praṇamya deveśaṃ sahasrākṣaṃ sahāmaraiḥ 
provāca muniśārdūla kṛtāñjalipuṭo harim  LiP 
śilāda uvāca
bhagavandevatārighna sahasrākṣa varaprada 
ayonijaṃ mṛtyuhīnaṃ putramicchāmi suvrata  LiP 
śakra uvāca
putraṃ dāsyāmi viprarṣe yonijaṃ mṛtyusaṃyutam 
anyathā te na dāsyāmi mṛtyuhīnā na santi vai  LiP 
na dāsyati sutaṃ te 'tra mṛtyuhīnamayonijam 
pitāmaho 'pi bhagavān kimutānye mahāmune  LiP 
so 'pi devaḥ svayaṃ brahmā mṛtyuhīno na ceśvaraḥ 
yonijaś ca mahātejāś cāṇḍajaḥ padmasaṃbhavaḥ  LiP 
maheśvarāṅgajaścaiva bhavānyāstanayaḥ prabhuḥ 
tasyāpyāyuḥ samākhyātaṃ parārdhadvayasaṃmitam  LiP 
koṭikoṭisahasrāṇi aharbhūtāni yāni vai 
samatītāni kalpānāṃ tāvaccheṣāparatraye  LiP 
tasmādayonije putre mṛtyuhīne prayatnataḥ 
parityajāśāṃ viprendra gṛhāṇātmasamaṃ sutam  LiP 
śailādiruvāca
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā pitā me lokaviśrutaḥ 
śilāda iti puṇyātmā punaḥ prāha śacīpatim  LiP 
śilāda uvāca
bhagavannaṇḍayonitvaṃ padmayonitvameva ca 
maheśvarāṅgayonitvaṃ śrutaṃ vai brahmaṇo mayā  LiP 
purā mahendradāyādād gadataścāsya pūrvajāt 
nāradādvai mahābāho kathamatrāśu no vada  LiP 
dākṣāyaṇī sā dakṣo 'pi devaḥ padmodbhavātmajaḥ 
pautrīkanakagarbhasya kathaṃ tasyāḥ suto vibhuḥ  LiP 
śakra uvāca
sthāne saṃśayituṃ vipra tava vakṣyāmi kāraṇam 
kalpe tatpuruṣe vṛttaṃ brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ  LiP 
sasarja sakalaṃ dhyātvā brahmāṇaṃ parameśvaraḥ 
janārdano jagannāthaḥ kalpe vai meghavāhane  LiP 
divyaṃ varṣasahasraṃ tu megho bhūtvāvahaddharam 
nārāyaṇo mahādevaṃ bahumānena sādaram  LiP 
dṛṣṭvā bhāvaṃ mahādevo hareḥ svātmani śaṅkaraḥ 
pradadau tasya sakalaṃ sraṣṭuṃ vai brahmaṇā saha  LiP 
tadā taṃ kalpamāhurvai meghavāhanasaṃjñayā 
hiraṇyagarbhastaṃ dṛṣṭvā tasya dehodbhavastadā  LiP 
janārdanasutaḥ prāha tapasā prāpya śaṅkaram 
tava vāmāṅgajo viṣṇur dakṣiṇāṅgabhavo hyaham  LiP 
mayā saha jagatsarvaṃ tathāpyasṛjadacyutaḥ 
jaganmayo 'vahadyasmān megho bhūtvā divāniśam  LiP 
bhavantamavahadviṣṇur devadevaṃ jagadgurum 
nārāyaṇādapi vibho bhakto 'haṃ tava śaṅkara  LiP 
prasīda dehi me sarvaṃ sarvātmatvaṃ tava prabho 
tadātha labdhvā bhagavān bhavātsarvātmatāṃ kṣaṇāt  LiP 
tvaramāṇo 'tha saṃgamya dadarśa puruṣottamam 
ekārṇavālaye śubhre tv andhakāre sudāruṇe  LiP 
hemaratnacite divye manasā ca vinirmite 
duṣprāpye durjanaiḥ puṇyaiḥ sanakādyairagocare  LiP 
jagadāvāsahṛdayaṃ dadarśa puruṣaṃ tvajaḥ 
anantabhogaśayyāyāṃ śāyinaṃ paṅkajekṣaṇam  LiP 
śaṅkhacakragadāpadmaṃ dhārayantaṃ caturbhujam 
sarvābharaṇasaṃyuktaṃ śaśimaṇḍalasannibham  LiP 
śrīvatsalakṣaṇaṃ devaṃ prasannāsyaṃ janārdanam 
ramāmṛdukarāmbhoja sparśaraktapadāmbujam  LiP 
paramātmānamīśānaṃ tamasā kālarūpiṇam 
rajasā sarvalokānāṃ sargalīlāpravartakam  LiP 
sattvena sarvabhūtānāṃ sthāpakaṃ parameśvaram 
sarvātmānaṃ mahātmānaṃ paramātmānamīśvaram  LiP 
kṣīrārṇave 'mṛtamaye śāyinaṃ yoganidrayā 
taṃ dṛṣṭvā prāha vai brahmā bhagavantaṃ janārdanam  LiP 
grasāmi tvāṃ prasādena yathāpūrvaṃ bhavānaham 
smayamānastu bhagavān pratibudhya pitāmaham  LiP 
udaikṣata mahābāhuḥ smitamīṣaccakāra saḥ 
viveśa cāṇḍajaṃ taṃ tu grastastena mahātmanā  LiP 
tatastaṃ cāsṛjadbrahmā bhruvormadhyena cācyutam 
sṛṣṭastena hariḥ prekṣya sthitastasyātha saṃnidhau  LiP 
etasminnantare rudraḥ sarvadevabhavodbhavaḥ 
vikṛtaṃ rūpamāsthāya purā dattavarastayoḥ  LiP 
āgacchadyatra vai viṣṇur viśvātmā parameśvaraḥ 
prasādamatulaṃ kartuṃ brahmaṇaś ca hareḥ prabhuḥ  LiP 
tataḥ sametya tau devau sarvadevabhavodbhavam 
apaśyatāṃ bhavaṃ devaṃ kālāgnisadṛśaṃ prabhum  LiP 
tau taṃ tuṣṭuvatuścaiva śarvamugraṃ kapardinam 
praṇematuś ca varadaṃ bahumānena dūrataḥ  LiP 
bhavo 'pi bhagavān devam anugṛhya pitāmaham 
janārdanaṃ jagannāthas tatraivāntaradhīyata  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge brahmaṇo varapradānaṃ nāma saptatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
LiP  
śailādiruvāca
gate maheśvare deve tamuddiśya janārdanaḥ 
praṇamya bhagavānprāha padmayonimajodbhavaḥ  LiP 
śrīviṣṇuruvāca
parameśo jagannāthaḥ śaṅkarastveṣa sarvagaḥ 
āvayorakhilasyeśaḥ śaraṇaṃ ca maheśvaraḥ  LiP 
ahaṃ vāmāṅgajo brahman śaṅkarasya mahātmanaḥ 
bhavān bhavasya devasya dakṣiṇāṅgabhavaḥ svayam  LiP 
māmāhur ṛṣayaḥ prekṣya pradhānaṃ prakṛtiṃ tathā 
avyaktamajamityevaṃ bhavantaṃ puruṣastviti  LiP 
evamāhurmahādevam āvayorapi kāraṇam 
īśaṃ sarvasya jagataḥ prabhumavyayamīśvaram  LiP 
so 'pi tasyāmareśasya vacanādvārijodbhavaḥ 
vareṇyaṃ varadaṃ rudram astuvatpraṇanāma ca  LiP 
athāmbhasā plutāṃ bhūmīṃ samādhāya janārdanaḥ 
pūrvavatsthāpayāmāsa vārāhaṃ rūpamāsthitaḥ  LiP 
nadīnadasamudrāṃś ca pūrvavaccākarotprabhuḥ 
kṛtvā corvīṃ prayatnena nimnonnatavivarjitām  LiP 
dharāyāṃ so 'cinotsarvān bhūdharān bhūdharākṛtiḥ 
bhūrādyāṃścaturo lokān kalpayāmāsa pūrvavat  LiP 
sraṣṭuṃ ca bhagavāṃścakre matiṃ matimatāṃ varaḥ 
mukhyaṃ ca tairyagyonyaṃ ca daivikaṃ mānuṣaṃ tathā  LiP 
vibhuścānugrahaṃ tatra kaumārakam adīnadhīḥ 
purastādasṛjaddevaḥ sanandaṃ sanakaṃ tathā  LiP 
sanātanaṃ satāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ naiṣkarmyeṇa gatāḥ param 
marīcibhṛgvaṅgirasaṃ pulastyaṃ pulahaṃ kratum  LiP 
dakṣamatriṃ vasiṣṭhaṃ ca so 'sṛjad yogavidyayā 
saṃkalpaṃ caiva dharmaṃ ca hy adharmaṃ bhagavānprabhuḥ  LiP 
dvādaśaiva prajāstvetā brahmaṇo 'vyaktajanmanaḥ 
ṛbhuṃ sanatkumāraṃ ca sasarjādau sanātanaḥ  LiP 
tau cordhvaretasau divyau cāgrajau brahmavādinau 
kumārau brahmaṇastulyau sarvajñau sarvabhāvinau  LiP 
evaṃ mukhyādikān sṛṣṭvā padmayoniḥ śilāśana 
yugadharmānaśeṣāṃś ca kalpayāmāsa viśvasṛk  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge vaiṣṇavakathanaṃ nāmāṣṭatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
LiP  
śailādiruvāca
śrutvā śakreṇa kathitaṃ pitā mama mahāmuniḥ 
punaḥ papraccha deveśaṃ praṇamya racitāñjaliḥ  LiP 
śilāda uvāca
bhagavan śakra sarvajña devadevanamaskṛta 
śacīpate jagannātha sahasrākṣa maheśvara  LiP 
yugadharmānkathaṃ cakre bhagavānpadmasaṃbhavaḥ 
vaktumarhasi me sarvaṃ sāṃprataṃ praṇatāya me  LiP 
śailādiruvāca
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā śilādasya mahātmanaḥ 
vyājahāra yathādṛṣṭaṃ yugadharmaṃ suvistaram  LiP 
śakra uvāca
caturyuga
ādyaṃ kṛtayugaṃ viddhi tatastretāyugaṃ mune 
dvāparaṃ tiṣyamityete catvārastu samāsataḥ  LiP 
sattvaṃ kṛtaṃ rajastretā dvāparaṃ ca rajastamaḥ 
kalistamaś ca vijñeyaṃ yugavṛttiryugeṣu ca  LiP 
dhyānaṃ paraṃ kṛtayuge tretāyāṃ yajña ucyate 
bhajanaṃ dvāpare śuddhaṃ dānameva kalau yuge  LiP 
catvāri ca sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ tatkṛtaṃ yugam 
tasya tāvacchatī saṃdhyā saṃdhyāṃśaś ca tathāvidhaḥ  LiP 
catvāri ca sahasrāṇi mānuṣāṇi śilāśana 
āyuḥ kṛtayuge viddhi prajānāmiha suvrata  LiP 
tataḥ kṛtayuge tasmin saṃdhyāṃśe ca gate tu vai 
pādāvaśiṣṭo bhavati yugadharmastu sarvataḥ  LiP 
caturbhāgaikahīnaṃ tu tretāyugamanuttamam 
kṛtārdhaṃ dvāparaṃ viddhi tadardhaṃ tiṣyamucyate  LiP 
triśatī dviśatī saṃdhyā tathā caikaśatī mune 
saṃdhyāṃśakaṃ tathāpyevaṃ kalpeṣvevaṃ yuge yuge  LiP 
ādye kṛtayuge dharmaś catuṣpādaḥ sanātanaḥ 
tretāyuge tripādastu dvipādo dvāpare sthitaḥ  LiP 
tripādahīnastiṣye tu sattāmātreṇa dhiṣṭhitaḥ 
kṛtayuga
kṛte tu mithunotpattir vṛttiḥ sākṣādrasollasā  LiP 
prajāstṛptāḥ sadā sarvāḥ sarvānandāś ca bhoginaḥ 
adhamottamatā tāsāṃ na viśeṣāḥ prajāḥ śubhāḥ  LiP 
tulyamāyuḥ sukhaṃ rūpaṃ tāsāṃ tasminkṛte yuge 
tāsāṃ prītirna ca dvandvaṃ na dveṣo nāsti ca klamaḥ  LiP 
parvatodadhivāsinyo hy aniketāśrayāstu tāḥ 
viśokāḥ sattvabahulā ekāntabahulās tathā  LiP 
tā vai niṣkāmacāriṇyo nityaṃ muditamānasāḥ 
apravṛttiḥ kṛtayuge karmaṇoḥ śubhapāpayoḥ  LiP 
varṇāśramavyavasthā ca tadāsīnna ca saṃkaraḥ 
rasollāsaḥ kālayogāt tretākhye naśyate dvija  LiP 
tasyāṃ siddhau pranaṣṭāyām anyā siddhiḥ prajāyate 
apāṃ saukṣmye pratigate tadā meghātmanā tu vai  LiP 
meghebhyastanayitnubhyaḥ pravṛttaṃ vṛṣṭisarjanam 
sakṛd eva tathā vṛṣṭyā saṃyukte pṛthivītale  LiP 
prādurāsaṃstadā tāsāṃ vṛkṣāste gṛhasaṃjñitāḥ 
sarvavṛttyupabhogastu tāsāṃ tebhyaḥ prajāyate  LiP 
vartayanti sma tebhyastās tretāyugamukhe prajāḥ 
tataḥ kālena mahatā tāsāmeva viparyayāt  LiP 
rāgalobhātmako bhāvas tadā hyākasmiko 'bhavat 
viparyayeṇa tāsāṃ tu tena tatkālabhāvinā  LiP 
praṇaśyanti tataḥ sarve vṛkṣāste gṛhasaṃjñitāḥ 
tatasteṣu pranaṣṭeṣu vibhrāntā maithunodbhavāḥ  LiP 
api dhyāyanti tāṃ siddhiṃ satyābhidhyāyinastadā 
prādurbabhūvustāsāṃ tu vṛkṣāste gṛhasaṃjñitāḥ  LiP 
vastrāṇi te prasūyante phalānyābharaṇāni ca 
teṣveva jāyate tāsāṃ gandhavarṇarasānvitam  LiP 
amākṣikaṃ mahīvīryaṃ puṭake puṭake madhu 
tena tā vartayanti sma sukhamāyuḥ sadaiva hi  LiP 
hṛṣṭapuṣṭāstayā siddhyā prajā vai vigatajvarāḥ 
tataḥ kālāntareṇaiva punarlobhāvṛtāstu tāḥ  LiP 
vṛkṣāṃstānparyagṛhṇanti madhu vā mākṣikaṃ balāt 
tāsāṃ tenopacāreṇa punarlobhakṛtena vai  LiP 
pranaṣṭā madhunā sārdhaṃ kalpavṛkṣāḥ kvacitkvacit 
tasyāmevālpaśiṣṭāyāṃ siddhyāṃ kālavaśāttadā  LiP 
āvartanāttu tretāyāṃ dvandvānyabhyutthitāni vai 
śītavarṣātapaistīvrais tatastā duḥkhitā bhṛśam  LiP 
dvandvaiḥ sampīḍyamānāś ca cakrur āvaraṇāni tu 
kṛtadvandvapratīghātāḥ ketanāni girau tataḥ  LiP 
pūrvaṃ nikāmacārāstā hy aniketā athāvasan 
yathāyogaṃ yathāprīti niketeṣvavasanpunaḥ  LiP 
kṛtvā dvandvopaghātāṃstān vṛttyupāyamacintayan 
naṣṭeṣu madhunā sārdhaṃ kalpavṛkṣeṣu vai tadā  LiP 
vivādavyākulāstā vai prajāstṛṣṇākṣudhārditāḥ 
tataḥ prādurbabhau tāsāṃ siddhistretāyuge punaḥ  LiP 
vārtāyāḥ sādhikāpyanyā vṛṣṭistāsāṃ nikāmataḥ 
tāsāṃ vṛṣṭyudakādīni hy abhavannimnagāni tu  LiP 
abhavanvṛṣṭisaṃtatyā srotasthānāni nimnagāḥ 
evaṃ nadyaḥ pravṛttāstu dvitīye vṛṣṭisarjane  LiP 
ye punastadapāṃ stokāḥ patitāḥ pṛthivītale 
apāṃ bhūmeś ca saṃyogād oṣadhyastāstadābhavan  LiP 
athālpakṛṣṭāścānuptā grāmyāraṇyāścaturdaśa 
ṛtupuṣpaphalāścaiva vṛkṣagulmāś ca jajñire  LiP 
prādurbhūtāni caitāni vṛkṣajātyauṣadhāni ca 
tenauṣadhena vartante prajāstretāyuge tadā  LiP 
tataḥ punarabhūttāsāṃ rāgo lobhaś ca sarvaśaḥ 
avaśyaṃ bhāvinārthena tretāyugavaśena ca  LiP 
tatastāḥ paryagṛhṇanta nadīkṣetrāṇi parvatān 
vṛkṣagulmauṣadhīścaiva prasahya tu yathābalam  LiP 
viparyayeṇa cauṣadhyaḥ pranaṣṭāstāścaturdaśa 
matvā dharāṃ praviṣṭāstā ityauṣadhyaḥ pitāmahaḥ  LiP 
dudoha gāṃ prayatnena sarvabhūtahitāya vai 
tadāprabhṛti cauṣadhyaḥ phālakṛṣṭāstvitastataḥ  LiP 
vārtāṃ kṛṣiṃ samāyātā vartukāmāḥ prayatnataḥ 
vārtā vṛttiḥ samākhyātā kṛṣikāmaprayatnataḥ  LiP 
anyathā jīvitaṃ tāsāṃ nāsti tretāyugātyaye 
hastodbhavā hyapaścaiva bhavanti bahuśastadā  LiP 
tatrāpi jagṛhuḥ sarve cānyonyaṃ krodhamūrchitāḥ 
sutadāradhanādyāṃstu balādyugabalena tu  LiP 
maryādāyāḥ pratiṣṭhārthaṃ jñātvā tadakhilaṃ vibhuḥ 
sasarja kṣatriyāṃstrātuṃ kṣatātkamalasaṃbhavaḥ  LiP 
varṇāśramapratiṣṭhāṃ ca cakāra svena tejasā 
vṛttena vṛttinā vṛttaṃ viśvātmā nirmame svayam  LiP 
yajñapravartanaṃ caiva tretāyāmabhavatkramāt 
paśuyajñaṃ na sevante kecittatrāpi suvratāḥ  LiP 
balādviṣṇustadā yajñam akarotsarvadṛk kramāt 
dvijāstadā praśaṃsanti tatastvāhiṃsakaṃ mune  LiP 
dvāpareṣvapi vartante matibhedāstadā nṛṇām 
manasā karmaṇā vācā kṛcchrādvārtā prasidhyati  LiP 
tadā tu sarvabhūtānāṃ kāyakleśavaśātkramāt 
lobho bhṛtirvaṇigyuddhaṃ tattvānāmaviniścayaḥ  LiP 
vedaśākhāpraṇayanaṃ dharmāṇāṃ saṃkaras tathā 
varṇāśramaparidhvaṃsaḥ kāmadveṣau tathaiva ca  LiP 
dvāpare tu pravartante rāgo lobho madas tathā 
vedo vyāsaiścaturdhā tu vyasyate dvāparādiṣu  LiP 
eko vedaścatuṣpādas tretāsviha vidhīyate 
saṃkṣayādāyuṣaścaiva vyasyate dvāpareṣu saḥ  LiP 
ṛṣiputraiḥ punarbhedā bhidyante dṛṣṭivibhramaiḥ 
mantrabrāhmaṇavinyāsaiḥ svaravarṇaviparyayaiḥ  LiP 
saṃhitā ṛgyajuḥsāmnāṃ saṃhanyante manīṣibhiḥ 
sāmānyā vaikṛtāścaiva draṣṭṛbhistaiḥ pṛthakpṛthak  LiP 
brāhmaṇaṃ kalpasūtrāṇi mantrapravacanāni ca 
anye tu prasthitāstānvai kecittānpratyavasthitāḥ  LiP 
itihāsapurāṇāni bhidyante kālagauravāt 
brāhmaṃ pādmaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ ca śaivaṃ bhāgavataṃ tathā  LiP 
bhaviṣyaṃ nāradīyaṃ ca mārkaṇḍeyamataḥ param 
āgneyaṃ brahmavaivartaṃ laiṅgaṃ vārāhameva ca  LiP 
vāmanākhyaṃ tataḥ kūrmaṃ mātsyaṃ gāruḍameva ca 
skāndaṃ tathā ca brahmāṇḍaṃ teṣāṃ bhedaḥ prakathyate  LiP 
laiṅgam ekādaśavidhaṃ prabhinnaṃ dvāpare śubham 
manvatriviṣṇuhārīta yājñavalkyośano 'ṅgirāḥ  LiP 
yamāpastambasaṃvartāḥ kātyāyanabṛhaspatī 
parāśaravyāsaśaṅkha likhitā dakṣagautamau  LiP 
śātātapo vasiṣṭhaś ca evamādyaiḥ sahasraśaḥ 
avṛṣṭirmaraṇaṃ caiva tathā vyādhyādyupadravāḥ  LiP 
vāṅmanaḥkarmajair duḥkhair nirvedo jāyate tataḥ 
nirvedājjāyate teṣāṃ duḥkhamokṣavicāraṇā  LiP 
vicāraṇācca vairāgyaṃ vairāgyāddoṣadarśanam 
doṣāṇāṃ darśanāccaiva dvāpare jñānasaṃbhavaḥ  LiP 
eṣā rajastamoyuktā vṛttir vai dvāpare smṛtā 
ādye kṛte tu dharmo 'sti sa tretāyāṃ pravartate  LiP 
dvāpare vyākulībhūtvā praṇaśyati kalau yuge  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge ekonacatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ

śakra uvāca
tiṣye māyāmasūyāṃ ca vadhaṃ caiva tapasvinām 
sādhayanti narāstatra tamasā vyākulendriyāḥ  LiP 
kalau pramādako rogaḥ satataṃ kṣudbhayāni ca 
anāvṛṣṭibhayaṃ ghoraṃ deśānāṃ ca viparyayaḥ  LiP 
na prāmāṇyaṃ śruterasti nṛṇāṃ cādharmasevanam 
adhārmikāstvanācārā mahākopālpacetasaḥ  LiP 
anṛtaṃ bruvate lubdhās tiṣye jātāś ca duṣprajāḥ 
duriṣṭairduradhītaiś ca durācārairdurāgamaiḥ  LiP 
viprāṇāṃ karma doṣeṇa prajānāṃ jāyate bhayam 
nādhīyante tadā vedān na yajanti dvijātayaḥ  LiP 
utsīdanti narāścaiva kṣatriyāś ca viśaḥ kramāt 
śūdrāṇāṃ mantrayogena saṃbandho brāhmaṇaiḥ saha  LiP 
bhavatīha kalau tasmiñ śayanāsanabhojanaiḥ 
rājānaḥ śūdrabhūyiṣṭhā brāhmaṇān bādhayanti te  LiP 
bhrūṇahatyā vīrahatyā prajāyante prajāsu vai 
śūdrāś ca brāhmaṇācārāḥ śūdrācārāś ca brāhmaṇāḥ  LiP 
rājavṛttisthitāś caurāś caurācārāś ca pārthivāḥ 
ekapatnyo na śiṣyanti vardhiṣyantyabhisārikāḥ  LiP

saṃdhyāṃśa
eṣā kaliyugāvasthā saṃdhyāṃśaṃ tu nibodha me 
yuge yuge ca hīyante trīṃstrīnpādāṃstu siddhayaḥ  LiP

Pramiti
evaṃ saṃdhyāṃśake kāle samprāpte tu yugāntike 
teṣāṃ śāstā hyasādhūnāṃ bhūtānāṃ nidhanotthitaḥ  LiP

kṛtvā bījāvaśeṣāṃ tu pṛthivīṃ krūrakarmaṇaḥ  LiP 
parasparanimittena kopenākasmikena tu

behaviour of people during yugānta

indra uvāca

tadaikādaśadhātmānaṃ pravibhajya vyavasthitaḥ  LiP

sā cāsṛjattadā lakṣmīṃ durgāṃ śreṣṭhāṃ sarasvatīm  LiP 
vāmāṃ raudrīṃ mahāmāyāṃ vaiṣṇavīṃ vārijekṣaṇām 
kalāṃ vikiriṇīṃ caiva kālīṃ kamalavāsinīm  LiP 
balavikariṇīṃ devīṃ balapramathinīṃ tathā 
sarvabhūtasya damanīṃ sasṛje ca manonmanīm  LiP 
tathānyā bahavaḥ sṛṣṭās tayā nāryaḥ sahasraśaḥ 
rudraiścaiva mahādevas tābhistribhuvaneśvaraḥ  LiP 
sarvātmanaś ca tasyāgre hy atiṣṭhatparameśvaraḥ 
mṛtasya tasya devasya brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ  LiP 
ghṛṇī dadau punaḥ prāṇān brahmaputro maheśvaraḥ 
brahmaṇaḥ pradadau prāṇān ātmasthāṃstu tadā prabhuḥ  LiP 
prahṛṣṭo 'bhūttato rudraḥ kiṃcitpratyāgatāsavam 
abhyabhāṣata deveśo brahmāṇaṃ paramaṃ vacaḥ  LiP 
mā bhairdeva mahābhāga viriñca jagatāṃ guro 
mayeha sthāpitāḥ prāṇās tasmāduttiṣṭha vai prabho  LiP 
śrutvā vacastatastasya svapnabhūtaṃ manogatam 
pitāmahaḥ prasannātmā netraiḥ phullāmbujaprabhaiḥ  LiP 
tataḥ pratyāgataprāṇaḥ samudaikṣan maheśvaram 
sa udvīkṣya ciraṃ kālaṃ snigdhagaṃbhīrayā girā  LiP 
uvāca bhagavān brahmā samutthāya kṛtāñjaliḥ 
bho bho vada mahābhāga ānandayasi me manaḥ  LiP 
ko bhavān aṣṭamūrtir vai sthita ekādaśātmakaḥ 
indra uvāca
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā vyājahāra maheśvaraḥ  LiP 
spṛśankarābhyāṃ brahmāṇaṃ sukhābhyāṃ sa surārihā 
śrīśaṅkara uvāca
māṃ viddhi paramātmānam enāṃ māyāmajāmiti  LiP 
ete vai saṃsthitā rudrās tvāṃ rakṣitumihāgatāḥ 
tataḥ praṇamya taṃ brahmā devadevamuvāca ha  LiP 
kṛtāñjalipuṭo bhūtvā harṣagadgadayā girā 
bhagavandevadeveśa duḥkhairākulito hyaham  LiP 
saṃsārānmoktumīśāna māmihārhasi śaṅkara 
tataḥ prahasya bhagavān pitāmahamumāpatiḥ  LiP 
tadā rudrairjagannāthas tayā cāntardadhe vibhuḥ 
indra uvāca
tasmācchilāda lokeṣu durlabho vai tvayonijaḥ  LiP 
mṛtyuhīnaḥ pumānviddhi samṛtyuḥ padmajo 'pi saḥ 
kiṃtu deveśvaro rudraḥ prasīdati yadīśvaraḥ  LiP 
na durlabho mṛtyuhīnas tava putro hyayonijaḥ 
mayā ca viṣṇunā caiva brahmaṇā ca mahātmanā  LiP 
ayonijaṃ mṛtyuhīnam asamarthaṃ niveditum 
śailādiruvāca
evaṃ vyāhṛtya viprendram anugṛhya ca taṃ ghṛṇī  LiP 
devairvṛto yayau devaḥ sitenebhena vai prabhuḥ  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge indravākyaṃ nāmaikacatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
LiP  
sūta uvāca
gate puṇye ca varade sahasrākṣe śilāśanaḥ 
ārādhayanmahādevaṃ tapasātoṣayadbhavam  LiP 
atha tasyaivamaniśaṃ tatparasya dvijasya tu 
divyaṃ varṣasahasraṃ tu gataṃ kṣaṇamivādbhutam  LiP 
valmīkenāvṛtāṅgaś ca lakṣyaḥ kīṭagaṇairmuniḥ 
vajrasūcīmukhaiścānyai raktakīṭaiś ca sarvataḥ  LiP 
nirmāṃsarudhiratvag vai nirlepaḥ kuḍyavat sthitaḥ 
asthiśeṣo 'bhavatpaścāt tamamanyata śaṅkaraḥ  LiP 
yadā spṛṣṭo munistena kareṇa ca smarāriṇā 
tadaiva muniśārdūlaś cotsasarja klamaṃ dvijaḥ  LiP 
tapatastasya tapasā prabhustuṣṭātha śaṅkaraḥ 
tuṣṭastavetyathovāca sagaṇaścomayā saha  LiP 
tapasānena kiṃ kāryaṃ bhavataste mahāmate 
dadāmi putraṃ sarvajñaṃ sarvaśāstrārthapāragam  LiP 
tataḥ praṇamya deveśaṃ stutvovāca śilāśanaḥ 
harṣagadgadayā vācā somaṃ somavibhūṣaṇam  LiP 
śilāda uvāca
bhagavandevadeveśa tripurārdana śaṅkara 
ayonijaṃ mṛtyuhīnaṃ putramicchāmi sattama  LiP 
sūta uvāca
pūrvamārādhitaḥ prāha tapasā parameśvaraḥ 
śilādaṃ brahmaṇā rudraḥ prītyā paramayā punaḥ  LiP 
śrīdevadeva uvāca
pūrvamārādhito vipra brahmaṇāhaṃ tapodhana 
tapasā cāvatārārthaṃ munibhiś ca surottamaiḥ  LiP 
tava putro bhaviṣyāmi nandināmnā tvayonijaḥ 
pitā bhaviṣyasi mama piturvai jagatāṃ mune  LiP 
evamuktvā muniṃ prekṣya praṇipatya sthitaṃ ghṛṇī 
somaḥ somopamaḥ prītas tatraivāntaradhīyata  LiP 
labdhaputraḥ pitā rudrāt prīto mama mahāmune 
yajñāṅgaṇaṃ mahatprāpya yajñārthaṃ yajñavittamaḥ  LiP 
tadaṅgaṇādahaṃ śaṃbhos tanujastasya cājñayā 
saṃjātaḥ pūrvamevāhaṃ yugāntāgnisamaprabhaḥ  LiP 
vavarṣustadā puṣkarāvartakādyā jaguḥ khecarāḥ kinnarāḥ siddhasādhyāḥ 
śilādātmajatvaṃ gate mayyupendraḥ sasarjātha vṛṣṭiṃ supuṣpaughamiśrām  LiP 
māṃ dṛṣṭvā kālasūryābhaṃ jaṭāmukuṭadhāriṇam 
tryakṣaṃ caturbhujaṃ bālaṃ śūlaṭaṅkagadādharam  LiP 
vajriṇaṃ vajradaṃṣṭraṃ ca vajriṇārādhitaṃ śiśum 
vajrakuṇḍalinaṃ ghoraṃ nīradopamaniḥsvanam  LiP 
brahmādyāstuṣṭuvuḥ sarve surendraś ca munīśvarāḥ 
neduḥ samantataḥ sarve nanṛtuścāpsarogaṇāḥ  LiP 
ṛṣayo muniśārdūla ṛgyajuḥsāmasaṃbhavaiḥ 
mantrairmāheśvaraiḥ stutvā sampraṇemurmudānvitāḥ  LiP 
brahmā hariś ca rudraś ca śakraḥ sākṣācchivāṃbikā 
jīvaścendurmahātejā bhāskaraḥ pavano 'nalaḥ  LiP 
īśāno nirṛtiryakṣo yamo varuṇa eva ca 
viśvedevās tathā rudrā vasavaś ca mahābalāḥ  LiP 
lakṣmīḥ sākṣācchacī jyeṣṭhā devī caiva sarasvatī 
aditiś ca ditiścaiva śraddhā lajjā dhṛtis tathā  LiP 
nandā bhadrā ca surabhī suśīlā sumanās tathā 
vṛṣendraś ca mahātejā dharmo dharmātmajas tathā  LiP 
āvṛtya māṃ tathāliṅgya tuṣṭuvurmunisattama 
śilādo 'pi munirdṛṣṭvā pitā me tādṛśaṃ tadā  LiP 
prītyā praṇamya puṇyātmā tuṣṭāveṣṭapradaṃ sutam 
śilāda uvāca
bhagavandevadeveśa triyaṃbaka mamāvyaya  LiP 
putro 'si jagatāṃ yasmāt trātā duḥkhāddhi kiṃ punaḥ 
rakṣako jagatāṃ yasmāt pitā me putra sarvaga  LiP 
ayonija namastubhyaṃ jagadyone pitāmaha 
pitā putra maheśāna jagatāṃ ca jagadguro  LiP 
vatsa vatsa mahābhāga pāhi māṃ parameśvara 
tvayāhaṃ nandito yasmān nandī nāmnā sureśvara  LiP 
tasmānnandaya māṃ nandin namāmi jagadīśvaram 
prasīda pitarau me 'dya rudralokaṃ gatau vibho  LiP 
pitāmahaś ca bho nandin navatīrṇe maheśvare 
mamaiva saphalaṃ loke janma vai jagatāṃ prabho  LiP 
avatīrṇe sute nandin rakṣārthaṃ mahyamīśvara 
tubhyaṃ namaḥ sureśāna nandīśvara namo 'stu te  LiP 
putra pāhi mahābāho devadeva jagadguro 
putratvameva nandīśa matvā yatkīrtitaṃ mayā  LiP 
tvayā tatkṣamyatāṃ vatsa stavastavya surāsuraiḥ 
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi mama putraprabhāṣitam  LiP 
śrāvayedvā dvijān bhaktyā mayā sārdhaṃ sa modate 
evaṃ stutvā sutaṃ bālaṃ praṇamya bahumānataḥ  LiP 
munīśvarāṃś ca samprekṣya śilāda uvāca suvrataḥ 
paśyadhvaṃ munayaḥ sarve mahābhāgyaṃ mamāvyayaḥ  LiP 
nandī yajñāṅgaṇe devaś cāvatīrṇo yataḥ prabhuḥ 
matsamaḥ kaḥ pumāṃlloke devo vā dānavo 'pi vā  LiP 
eṣa nandī yato jāto yajñabhūmau hitāya me  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge nandikeśvarotpattir nāma dvicatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
LiP  
nandikeśvara uvāca
mayā saha pitā hṛṣṭaḥ praṇamya ca maheśvaram 
uṭajaṃ svaṃ jagāmāśu nidhiṃ labdhveva nirdhanaḥ  LiP 
yadāgato 'hamuṭajaṃ śilādasya mahāmune 
tadā vai daivikaṃ rūpaṃ tyaktvā mānuṣyam āsthitaḥ  LiP 
naṣṭā caiva smṛtirdivyā yena kenāpi kāraṇāt 
mānuṣyamāsthitaṃ dṛṣṭvā pitā me lokapūjitaḥ  LiP 
vilalāpātiduḥkhārtaḥ svajanaiś ca samāvṛtaḥ 
jātakarmādikāścaiva cakāra mama sarvavit  LiP 
śālaṅkāyanaputro vai śilādaḥ putravatsalaḥ 
upadiṣṭā hi tenaiva ṛkśākhā yajuṣas tathā  LiP 
sāmaśākhāsahasraṃ ca sāṅgopāṅgaṃ mahāmune 
āyurvedaṃ dhanurvedaṃ gāndharvaṃ cāśvalakṣaṇam  LiP 
hastināṃ caritaṃ caiva narāṇāṃ caiva lakṣaṇam 
sampūrṇe saptame varṣe tato 'tha munisattamau  LiP 
mitrāvaruṇanāmānau tapoyogabalānvitau 
tasyāśramaṃ gatau divyau draṣṭuṃ māṃ cājñayā vibhoḥ  LiP 
ūcatuś ca mahātmānau māṃ nirīkṣya muhurmuhuḥ 
tāta nandyayamalpāyuḥ sarvaśāstrārthapāragaḥ  LiP 
na dṛṣṭamevamāścaryam āyurvarṣādataḥ param 
ityuktavati viprendraḥ śilādaḥ putravatsalaḥ  LiP 
samāliṅgya ca duḥkhārto rurodātīva visvaram 
hā putra putra putreti papāta ca samantataḥ  LiP 
aho balaṃ daivavidher vidhātuśceti duḥkhitaḥ 
tasya cārtasvaraṃ śrutvā tadāśramanivāsinaḥ  LiP 
nipeturvihvalātyarthaṃ rakṣāścakruś ca maṅgalam 
tuṣṭuvuś ca mahādevaṃ triyaṃbakamumāpatim  LiP 
hutvā triyaṃbakenaiva madhunaiva ca saṃplutām 
dūrvāmayutasaṃkhyātāṃ sarvadravyasamanvitām  LiP 
pitā vigatasaṃjñaś ca tathā caiva pitāmahaḥ 
viceṣṭaś ca lalāpāsau mṛtavannipapāta ca  LiP 
mṛtyor bhīto 'ham acirāc chirasā cābhivandya tam 
mṛtavatpatitaṃ sākṣāt pitaraṃ ca pitāmaham  LiP 
pradakṣiṇīkṛtya ca taṃ rudrajāpyarato 'bhavam 
hṛtpuṇḍarīke suṣire dhyātvā devaṃ triyaṃbakam  LiP 
tryakṣaṃ daśabhujaṃ śāntaṃ pañcavaktraṃ sadāśivam 
saritaścāntare puṇye sthitaṃ māṃ parameśvaraḥ  LiP 
tuṣṭo 'bravīnmahādevaḥ somaḥ somārdhabhūṣaṇaḥ 
vatsa nandinmahābāho mṛtyorbhītiḥ kutastava  LiP 
mayaiva preṣitau viprau matsamastvaṃ na saṃśayaḥ 
vatsainattava dehaṃ ca laukikaṃ paramārthataḥ  LiP 
nāstyeva daivikaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ śilādena purā tava 
devaiś ca munibhiḥ siddhair gandharvairdānavottamaiḥ  LiP 
pūjitaṃ yatpurā vatsa daivikaṃ nandikeśvara 
saṃsārasya svabhāvo 'yaṃ sukhaṃ duḥkhaṃ punaḥ punaḥ  LiP 
nṛṇāṃ yoniparityāgaḥ sarvathaiva vivekinaḥ 
evamuktvā tu māṃ sākṣāt sarvadevamaheśvaraḥ  LiP 
karābhyāṃ suśubhābhyāṃ ca ubhābhyāṃ parameśvaraḥ 
pasparśa bhagavān rudraḥ paramārtiharo haraḥ  LiP 
uvāca ca mahādevas tuṣṭātmā vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ 
nirīkṣya gaṇapāṃścaiva devīṃ himavataḥ sutām  LiP 
samālokya ca tuṣṭātmā mahādevaḥ sureśvaraḥ 
ajaro jarayā tyakto nityaṃ duḥkhavivarjitaḥ  LiP 
akṣayaścāvyayaścaiva sapitā sasuhṛjjanaḥ 
mameṣṭo gaṇapaścaiva madvīryo matparākramaḥ  LiP 
iṣṭo mama sadā caiva mama pārśvagataḥ sadā 
madbalaścaiva bhavitā mahāyogabalānvitaḥ  LiP 
evamuktvā ca māṃ devo bhagavān sagaṇastadā 
kuśeśayamayīṃ mālāṃ samunmucyātmanastadā  LiP 
ābabandha mahātejā mama devo vṛṣadhvajaḥ 
tayāhaṃ mālayā jātaḥ śubhayā kaṇṭhasaktayā  LiP 
tryakṣo daśabhujaścaiva dvitīya iva śaṅkaraḥ 
tata eva samādāya hastena parameśvaraḥ  LiP 
uvāca brūhi kiṃ te 'dya dadāmi varamuttamam 
tato jaṭāśritaṃ vāri gṛhītvā cātinirmalam  LiP 
uktā nadī bhavasveti utsasarja vṛṣadhvajaḥ 
tataḥ sā divyatoyā ca pūrṇāsitajalā śubhā  LiP 
padmotpalavanopetā prāvartata mahānadī 
tāmāha ca mahādevo nadīṃ paramaśobhanām  LiP 
yasmājjaṭodakādeva pravṛttā tvaṃ mahānadī 
tasmājjaṭodakā puṇyā bhaviṣyasi saridvarā  LiP 
tvayi snātvā naraḥ kaścit sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate 
tato devyā mahādevaḥ śilādatanayaṃ prabhuḥ  LiP 
putraste 'yamiti procya pādayoḥ saṃnyapātayat 
sā māmāghrāya śirasi pāṇibhyāṃ parimārjatī  LiP 
putrapremṇābhyaṣiñcacca srotobhistanayaistribhiḥ 
payasā śaṅkhagaureṇa devadevaṃ nirīkṣya sā  LiP 
tāni srotāṃsi trīṇyasyāḥ srotasvinyo 'bhavaṃstadā 
nadīṃ trisrotasaṃ devo bhagavānavadadbhavaḥ  LiP 
trisrotasaṃ nadīṃ dṛṣṭvā vṛṣaḥ paramaharṣitaḥ 
nanāda nādāttasmācca saridanyā tato 'bhavat  LiP 
vṛṣadhvaniriti khyātā devadevena sā nadī 
jāṃbūnadamayaṃ citraṃ sarvaratnamayaṃ śubham  LiP 
svaṃ devaścādbhutaṃ divyaṃ nirmitaṃ viśvakarmaṇā 
mukuṭaṃ cābabandheśo mama mūrdhni vṛṣadhvajaḥ  LiP 
kuṇḍale ca śubhe divye vajravaiḍūryabhūṣite 
ābabandha mahādevaḥ svayameva maheśvaraḥ  LiP 
māṃ tathābhyarcitaṃ vyomni dṛṣṭvā meghaiḥ prabhākaraḥ 
meghāṃbhasā cābhyaṣiñcac chilādanam atho mune  LiP 
tasyābhiṣiktasya tadā pravṛttā srotasā bhṛśam 
yasmāt suvarṇānniḥsṛtya nadyeṣā sampravartate  LiP 
svarṇodaketi tāmāha devadevastriyaṃbakaḥ 
jāmbūnadamayādyasmād dvitīyā mukuṭācchubhā  LiP 
prāvartata nadī puṇyā ūcur jambūnadīti tām 
etatpañcanadaṃ nāma japyeśvarasamīpagam  LiP 
yaḥ pañcanadamāsādya snātvā japyeśvareśvaram 
pūjayecchivasāyujyaṃ prayātyeva na saṃśayaḥ  LiP 
Devī adopts Nandin
atha devo mahādevaḥ sarvabhūtapatirbhavaḥ 
devīmuvāca śarvāṇīm umāṃ girisutāmajām  LiP 
devī nandīśvaraṃ devam abhiṣiñcāmi bhūtapam 
gaṇendraṃ vyāhariṣyāmi kiṃ vā tvaṃ manyase 'vyaye  LiP 
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā bhavānī harṣitānanā 
smayantī varadaṃ prāha bhavaṃ bhūtapatiṃ patim  LiP 
sarvalokādhipatyaṃ ca gaṇeśatvaṃ tathaiva ca 
dātumarhasi deveśa śailādistanayo mama  LiP 
tataḥ sa bhagavāñśarvaḥ sarvalokeśvareśvaraḥ 
sasmāra gaṇapān divyān devadevo vṛṣadhvajaḥ  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge nandikeśvaraprādurbhāvanandikeśvarābhiṣekamantro nāma tricatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ

śailādiruvāca
smaraṇādeva rudrasya samprāptāś ca gaṇeśvarāḥ 
sarve sahasrahastāś ca sahasrāyudhapāṇayaḥ  LiP 
trinetrāś ca mahātmānas tridaśairapi vanditāḥ 
koṭikālāgnisaṃkāśā jaṭāmukuṭadhāriṇaḥ  LiP 
daṃṣṭrākarālavadanā nityā buddhāś ca nirmalāḥ 
koṭikoṭigaṇaistulyair ātmanā ca gaṇeśvarāḥ 
asaṃkhyātā mahātmānas tatrājagmurmudā yutāḥ  LiP 
gāyantaś ca dravantaś ca nṛtyantaś ca mahābalāḥ 
mukhāḍambaravādyāni vādayantastathaiva ca  LiP 
rathairnāgairhayaiścaiva siṃhamarkaṭavāhanāḥ 
vimāneṣu tathārūḍhā hemacitreṣu vai gaṇāḥ  LiP 
bherīmṛdaṅgakādyaiś ca paṇavānakagomukhaiḥ 
vāditrairvividhaiścānyaiḥ paṭahairekapuṣkaraiḥ  LiP 
bherīmurajasaṃnādair āḍambarakaḍiṇḍimaiḥ 
mardalairveṇuvīṇābhir vividhaistālaniḥsvanaiḥ  LiP 
darduraistalaghātaiś ca kacchapaiḥ paṇavairapi 
vādyamānairmahāyogā ājagmurdevasaṃsadam  LiP 
te gaṇeśā mahāsattvāḥ sarvadeveśvareśvarāḥ 
praṇamya devaṃ devīṃ ca idaṃ vacanam abruvan  LiP 
bhagavandevadeveśa triyaṃbaka vṛṣadhvaja 
kimarthaṃ ca smṛtā deva ājñāpaya mahādyute  LiP 
kiṃ sāgarāñśoṣayāmo yamaṃ vā saha kiṅkaraiḥ 
hanmo mṛtyusutāṃ mṛtyuṃ paśuvaddhanma padmajam  LiP 
baddhvendraṃ saha devaiś ca saha viṣṇuṃ ca vāyunā 
ānayāmaḥ susaṃkruddhā daityānvā saha dānavaiḥ  LiP 
kasyādya vyasanaṃ ghoraṃ kariṣyāmastavājñayā 
kasya vādyotsavo deva sarvakāmasamṛddhaye  LiP 
tāṃstathāvādinaḥ sarvān gaṇeśān sarvasaṃmatān 
uvāca devaḥ sampūjya koṭikoṭiśatānprabhuḥ  LiP 
śṛṇudhvaṃ yatkṛte yūyam ihāhūtā jagaddhitāḥ 
śrutvā ca prayatātmānaḥ kurudhvaṃ tadaśaṅkitāḥ  LiP 
nandīśvaro 'yaṃ putro naḥ sarveṣāmīśvareśvaraḥ 
vipro 'yaṃ nāyakaścaiva senānīr vaḥ samṛddhimān  LiP 
tamimaṃ mama saṃdeśād yūyaṃ sarve 'pi saṃmatāḥ 
senānyam abhiṣiñcadhvaṃ mahāyogapatiṃ patim  LiP 
evamuktā bhagavatā gaṇapāḥ sarva eva te 
evamastviti saṃmantrya saṃbhārānāharaṃstataḥ  LiP 
tasya sarvāśrayaṃ divyaṃ jāṃbūnadamayaṃ śubham 
āsanaṃ merusaṃkāśaṃ manoharam upāharan  LiP 
naikastaṃbhamayaṃ cāpi cāmīkaravaraprabham 
muktādāmāvalambaṃ ca maṇiratnāvabhāsitam  LiP 
staṃbhaiś ca vaiḍūryamayaiḥ kiṅkiṇījālasaṃvṛtam 
cāruratnakasaṃyuktaṃ maṇḍapaṃ viśvatomukham  LiP 
kṛtvā vinyasya tanmadhye tadāsanavaraṃ śubham 
tasyāgrataḥ pādapīṭhaṃ nīlavajrāvabhāsitam  LiP 
cakruḥ pādapratiṣṭhārthaṃ kalaśau cāsya pārśvagau 
sampūrṇau paramāmbhobhir aravindāvṛtānanau  LiP 
kalaśānāṃ sahasraṃ tu sauvarṇaṃ rājataṃ tathā 
tāmrajaṃ mṛnmayaṃ caiva sarvatīrthāmbupūritam  LiP 
vāsoyugaṃ tathā divyaṃ gandhaṃ divyaṃ tathaiva ca 
keyūre kuṇḍale caiva mukuṭaṃ hārameva ca  LiP 
chatraṃ śataśalākaṃ ca vālavyajanameva ca 
dattaṃ mahātmanā tena brahmaṇā parameṣṭhinā  LiP 
śaṅkhahārāṅgagaureṇa pṛṣṭhenāpi virājitam 
vyajanaṃ candraśubhraṃ ca hemadaṇḍaṃ sucāmaram  LiP 
airāvataḥ supratīko gajāvetau supūjitau 
mukuṭaṃ kāñcanaṃ caiva nirmitaṃ viśvakarmaṇā  LiP 
kuṇḍale cāmale divye vajraṃ caiva varāyudham 
jāṃbūnadamayaṃ sūtraṃ keyūradvayameva ca  LiP 
sambhārāṇi tathānyāni vividhāni bahūnyapi 
samantān ninyur avyagrā gaṇapā devasaṃmatāḥ  LiP 
tato devāś ca sendrāś ca nārāyaṇamukhās tathā 
munayo bhagavānbrahmā navabrahmāṇa eva ca  LiP 
devaiś ca lokāḥ sarve te tato jagmurmudā yutāḥ 
teṣvāgateṣu sarveṣu bhagavānparameśvaraḥ  LiP 
sarvakāryavidhiṃ kartum ādideśa pitāmaham 
pitāmaho 'pi bhagavān niyogādeva tasya tu  LiP 
cakāra sarvaṃ bhagavān abhiṣekaṃ samāhitaḥ 
arcayitvā tato brahmā svayamevābhyaṣecayat  LiP 
tato viṣṇustataḥ śakro lokapālāstathaiva ca 
abhyaṣiñcanta vidhivad gaṇendraṃ śivaśāsanāt  LiP 
ṛṣayastuṣṭuvuścaiva pitā mahapurogamāḥ 
stutavatsu tatasteṣu viṣṇuḥ sarvajagatpatiḥ  LiP 
śirasyañjalimādāya tuṣṭāva ca samāhitaḥ 
prāñjaliḥ praṇato bhūtvā jayaśabdaṃ cakāra ca  LiP 
tato gaṇādhipāḥ sarve tato devāstato 'surāḥ 
evaṃ stutaścābhiṣikto devaiḥ sabrahmakaistadā  LiP 
udvāhaś ca kṛtastatra niyogātparameṣṭhinaḥ 
marutāṃ ca sutā devī suyaśākhyā babhūva yā  LiP 
labdhaṃ śaśiprabhaṃ chatraṃ tayā tatra vibhūṣitam 
cāmare cāmarāsakta hastāgraiḥ strīgaṇairyutā  LiP 
siṃhāsanaṃ ca paramaṃ tayā cādhiṣṭhitaṃ mayā 
alaṃkṛtā mahālakṣmyā mukuṭādyaiḥ subhūṣaṇaiḥ  LiP 
labdho hāraś ca paramo devyāḥ kaṇṭhagatas tathā 
vṛṣendraś ca sito nāgaḥ siṃhaḥ siṃhadhvajas tathā  LiP 
rathaś ca hemacchatraṃ ca candrabiṃbasamaprabham 
adyāpi sadṛśaḥ kaścin mayā nāsti vibhuḥ kvacit  LiP 
sānvayaṃ ca gṛhītveśas tathā saṃbandhibāndhavaiḥ 
āruhya vṛṣamīśāno mayā devyā gataḥ śivaḥ  LiP 
tadā devīṃ bhavaṃ dṛṣṭvā mayā ca prārthayan gaṇaiḥ 
munidevarṣayaḥ siddhā ājñāṃ pāśupatīṃ dvijāḥ  LiP 
athājñāṃ pradadau teṣām arhāṇām ājñayā vibhoḥ 
nandiko nagajābhartus teṣāṃ pāśupatīṃ śubhām  LiP 
tasmāddhi munayo labdhvā tadājñāṃ munipuṅgavāt 
bhavabhaktāstadā cāsaṃs tasmādevaṃ samarcayet  LiP 
namaskāravihīnastu nāma udgirayedbhave 
brahmaghnadaśasaṃtulyaṃ tasya pāpaṃ garīyasam  LiP 
tasmātsarvaprakāreṇa namaskārādimuccaret 
ādau kuryānnamaskāraṃ tadante śivatāṃ vrajet  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge nandikeśvarābhiṣeko nāma catuścatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ

ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
sūta suvyaktamakhilaṃ kathitaṃ śaṅkarasya tu 
sarvātmabhāvaṃ rudrasya svarūpaṃ vaktumarhasi  LiP 
sūta uvāca
bhūrbhuvaḥ svarmahaścaiva janaḥ sākṣāttapas tathā 
satyalokaś ca pātālaṃ narakārṇavakoṭayaḥ  LiP 
tārakāgrahasomārkā dhruvaḥ saptarṣayas tathā 
vaimānikāstathānye ca tiṣṭhantyasya prasādataḥ  LiP 
anena nirmitāstvevaṃ tadātmāno dvijarṣabhāḥ 
samaṣṭirūpaḥ sarvātmā saṃsthitaḥ sarvadā śivaḥ  LiP 
sarvātmānaṃ mahātmānaṃ mahādevaṃ maheśvaram 
na vijānanti saṃmūḍhā māyayā tasya mohitāḥ  LiP 
tasya devasya rudrasya śarīraṃ vai jagattrayam 
tasmātpraṇamya taṃ vakṣye jagatāṃ nirṇayaṃ śubham  LiP 
purā vaḥ kathitaṃ sarvaṃ mayāṇḍasya yathā kṛtiḥ 
bhuvanānāṃ svarūpaṃ ca brahmāṇḍe kathayāmyaham  LiP 
pṛthivī cāntarikṣaṃ ca svarmaharjana eva ca 
tapaḥ satyaṃ ca saptaite lokāstvaṇḍodbhavāḥ śubhāḥ  LiP 
adhastādatra caiteṣāṃ dvijāḥ sapta talāni tu 
mahātalādayasteṣāṃ adhastānnarakāḥ kramāt  LiP 
mahātalaṃ hematalaṃ sarvaratnopaśobhitam 
prāsādaiś ca vicitraiś ca bhavasyāyatanais tathā  LiP 
anantena ca saṃyuktaṃ mucukundena dhīmatā 
nṛpeṇa balinā caiva pātālasvargavāsinā  LiP 
śailaṃ rasātalaṃ viprāḥ śārkaraṃ hi talātalam 
pītaṃ sutalamityuktaṃ vitalaṃ vidrumaprabham  LiP 
sitaṃ hi atalaṃ tacca talaṃ yacca sitetaram 
kṣmāyāstu yāvadvistāro hy adhasteṣāṃ ca suvratāḥ  LiP 
talānāṃ caiva sarveṣāṃ tāvatsaṃkhyā samāhitā 
sahasrayojanaṃ vyoma daśasāhasrameva ca  LiP 
lakṣaṃ saptasahasraṃ hi talānāṃ saghanasya tu 
vyomnaḥ pramāṇaṃ mūlaṃ tu triṃśatsāhasrakeṇa tu  LiP 
suvarṇena muniśreṣṭhās tathā vāsukinā śubham 
rasātalamiti khyātaṃ tathānyaiś ca niṣevitam  LiP 
virocanahiraṇyākṣa narakādyaiś ca sevitam 
talātalamiti khyātaṃ sarvaśobhāsamanvitam  LiP 
vaināyakādibhiścaiva kālanemipurogamaiḥ 
pūrvadevaiḥ samākīrṇaṃ sutalaṃ ca tathāparaiḥ  LiP 
vitalaṃ dānavādyaiś ca tārakāgnimukhais tathā 
mahāntakādyair nāgaiś ca prahlādenāsureṇa ca  LiP 
vitalaṃ cātra vikhyātaṃ kambalāśvaniṣevitam 
mahākumbhena vīreṇa hayagrīveṇa dhīmatā  LiP 
śaṅkukarṇena saṃbhinnaṃ tathā namucipūrvakaiḥ 
tathānyair vividhair vīrais talaṃ caiva suśobhitam  LiP 
taleṣu teṣu sarveṣu cāmbayā parameśvaraḥ 
skandena nandinā sārdhaṃ gaṇapaiḥ sarvato vṛtaḥ  LiP 
talānāṃ caiva sarveṣām ūrdhvataḥ saptasaptamāḥ 
kṣmātalāni dharā cāpi saptadhā kathayāmi vaḥ  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge pātālavarṇanaṃ nāma pañcacatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
LiP  
sūta uvāca
saptadvīpā tathā pṛthvī nadīparvatasaṃkulā 
samudraiḥ saptabhiścaiva sarvataḥ samalaṃkṛtā  LiP 
jambūḥ plakṣaḥ śālmaliś ca kuśaḥ krauñcastathaiva ca 
śākaḥ puṣkaranāmā ca dvīpāstvabhyantare kramāt  LiP 
saptadvīpeṣu sarveṣu sāmbaḥ sarvagaṇairvṛtaḥ 
nānāveṣadharo bhūtvā sānnidhyaṃ kurute haraḥ  LiP 
kṣārodekṣurasodaś ca surodaś ca ghṛtodadhiḥ 
dadhyarṇavaś ca kṣīrodaḥ svādūdaścāpyanukramāt  LiP 
samudreṣviha sarveṣu sarvadā sagaṇaḥ śivaḥ 
jalarūpī bhavaḥ śrīmān krīḍate cormibāhubhiḥ  LiP 
kṣīrārṇavāmṛtamiva sadā kṣīrārṇave hariḥ 
śete śivajñānadhiyā sākṣādvai yoganidrayā  LiP 
yadā prabuddho bhagavān prabuddhamakhilaṃ jagat 
yadā suptastadā suptaṃ tanmayaṃ ca carācaram  LiP 
tenaiva sṛṣṭamakhilaṃ dhṛtaṃ rakṣitameva ca 
saṃhṛtaṃ devadevasya prasādātparameṣṭhinaḥ  LiP 
suṣeṇā iti vikhyātā yajante puruṣarṣabham 
aniruddhaṃ muniśreṣṭhāḥ śaṅkhacakragadādharam  LiP 
ye cāniruddhaṃ puruṣaṃ dhyāyantyātmavidāṃ varāḥ 
nārāyaṇasamāḥ sarve sarvasaṃpatsamanvitāḥ  LiP 
sanandanaś ca bhagavān sanakaś ca sanātanaḥ 
vālakhilyāś ca siddhāś ca mitrāvaruṇakau tathā  LiP 
yajanti satataṃ tatra viśvasya prabhavaṃ harim 
saptadvīpeṣu tiṣṭhanti nānāśṛṅgā mahodayāḥ  LiP 
āsamudrāyatāḥ kecid girayo gahvarais tathā 
dharāyāḥ patayaścāsan bahavaḥ kālagauravāt  LiP 
sāmarthyātparameśānāḥ krauñcārerjanakātprabhoḥ 
manvantareṣu sarveṣu atītānāgateṣviha  LiP 
pravakṣyāmi dhareśān vo vakṣye svāyaṃbhuve 'ntare 
manvantareṣu sarveṣu atītānāgateṣu ca  LiP 
tulyābhimāninaścaiva sarve tulyaprayojanāḥ 
svāyaṃbhuvasya ca manoḥ pautrāstvāsanmahābalāḥ  LiP 
priyavratātmajā vīrās te daśeha prakīrtitāḥ 
āgnīdhraścāgnibāhuś ca medhā medhātithirvasuḥ  LiP 
jyotiṣmāndyutimān havyaḥ savanaḥ putra eva ca 
priyavrato 'bhyaṣiñcattān sapta saptasu pārthivān  LiP 
jambūdvīpeśvaraṃ cakre āgnīdhraṃ sumahābalam 
plakṣadvīpeśvaraścāpi tena medhātithiḥ kṛtaḥ  LiP 
śālmaleś ca vapuṣmantaṃ rājānamabhiṣiktavān 
jyotiṣmantaṃ kuśadvīpe rājānaṃ kṛtavānnṛpaḥ  LiP 
dyutimantaṃ ca rājānaṃ krauñcadvīpe samādiśat 
śākadvīpeśvaraṃ cāpi havyaṃ cakre priyavrataḥ  LiP 
puṣkarādhipatiṃ cakre savanaṃ cāpi suvratāḥ 
puṣkare savanasyāpi mahāvītaḥ suto 'bhavat  LiP 
dhātakī caiva dvāvetau putrau putravatāṃ varau 
mahāvītaṃ smṛtaṃ varṣaṃ tasya nāmnā mahātmanaḥ  LiP 
nāmnā tu dhātakeścaiva dhātakīkhaṇḍamucyate 
havyo 'pyajanayat putrāñ chākadvīpeśvaraḥ prabhuḥ  LiP 
jaladaṃ ca kumāraṃ ca sukumāraṃ maṇīcakam 
kusumottaramodākī saptamastu mahādrumaḥ  LiP 
aladaṃ jaladasyātha varṣaṃ prathamamucyate 
kumārasya tu kaumāraṃ dvitīyaṃ parikīrtitam  LiP 
sukumāraṃ tṛtīyaṃ tu sukumārasya kīrtyate 
maṇīcakaṃ caturthaṃ tu māṇīcakamihocyate  LiP 
kusumottarasya vai varṣaṃ pañcamaṃ kusumottaram 
modakaṃ cāpi modāker varṣaṃ ṣaṣṭhaṃ prakīrtitam  LiP 
mahādrumasya nāmnā tu saptamaṃ tanmahādrumam 
teṣāṃ tu nāmabhistāni sapta varṣāṇi tatra vai  LiP 
krauñcadvīpeśvarasyāpi putrā dyutimatastu vai 
kuśalo manugaścoṣṇaḥ pīvaraścāndhakārakaḥ  LiP 
muniśca dundubhiścaiva sutā dyutimatastu vai 
teṣāṃ svanāmabhir deśāḥ krauñcadvīpāśrayāḥ śubhāḥ  LiP 
kuśaladeśaḥ kuśale manugasya manonugaḥ 
uṣṇasyoṣṇaḥ smṛto deśaḥ pīvaraḥ pīvarasya ca  LiP 
andhakārasya kathito deśo nāmnāndhakārakaḥ 
munerdeśo muniḥ prokto dundubher dundubhiḥ smṛtaḥ  LiP 
ete janapadāḥ sapta krauñcadvīpeṣu bhāsvarāḥ 
jyotiṣmantaḥ kuśadvīpe sapta cāsanmahaujasaḥ  LiP 
udbhido veṇumāṃścaiva dvairatho lavaṇo dhṛtiḥ 
ṣaṣṭhaḥ prabhākaraścāpi saptamaḥ kapilaḥ smṛtaḥ  LiP 
udbhidaṃ prathamaṃ varṣaṃ dvitīyaṃ veṇumaṇḍalam 
tṛtīyaṃ dvairathaṃ caiva caturthaṃ lavaṇaṃ smṛtam  LiP 
pañcamaṃ dhṛtimat ṣaṣṭhaṃ prabhākaram anuttamam 
saptamaṃ kapilaṃ nāma kapilasya prakīrtitam  LiP 
śālmalasyeśvarāḥ sapta sutāste vai vapuṣmataḥ 
śvetaś ca haritaścaiva jīmūto rohitas tathā  LiP 
vaidyuto mānasaścaiva suprabhaḥ saptamas tathā 
śvetasya deśaḥ śvetastu haritasya ca hāritaḥ  LiP 
jīmūtasya ca jīmūto rohitasya ca rohitaḥ 
vaidyuto vaidyutasyāpi mānasasya ca mānasaḥ  LiP 
suprabhaḥ suprabhasyāpi sapta vai deśalāñchakāḥ 
plakṣadvīpe tu vakṣyāmi jambūdvīpādanantaram  LiP 
sapta medhātitheḥ putrāḥ plakṣadvīpeśvarā nṛpāḥ 
jyeṣṭhaḥ śāntabhayasteṣāṃ saptavarṣāṇi tāni vai  LiP 
tasmācchāntabhayāccaiva śiśirastu sukhodayaḥ 
ānandaś ca śivaścaiva kṣemakaś ca dhruvas tathā  LiP 
tāni teṣāṃ tu nāmāni saptavarṣāṇi bhāgaśaḥ 
niveśitāni taistāni pūrvaṃ svāyaṃbhuve 'ntare  LiP 
medhātithestu putraistaiḥ plakṣadvīpanivāsibhiḥ 
varṇāśramācārayutāḥ prajāstatra niveśitāḥ  LiP 
plakṣadvīpādivarṣeṣu śākadvīpāntikeṣu vai 
jñeyaḥ pañcasu dharmo vai varṇāśramavibhāgaśaḥ  LiP 
sukhamāyuḥ svarūpaṃ ca balaṃ dharmo dvijottamāḥ 
pañcasveteṣu dvīpeṣu sarvasādhāraṇaṃ smṛtam  LiP 
rudrārcanaratā nityaṃ maheśvaraparāyaṇāḥ 
anye ca puṣkaradvīpe prajātāś ca prajeśvarāḥ  LiP 
prajāpateś ca rudrasya bhāvāmṛtasukhotkaṭāḥ  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge bhuvanakośe dvīpadvīpeśvarakathanaṃ nāma ṣaṭcatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ

sūta uvāca
āgnīdhraṃ jyeṣṭhadāyādaṃ kāmyaputraṃ mahābalam 
priyavrato 'bhyaṣiñcadvai jaṃbūdvīpeśvaraṃ nṛpaḥ  LiP 
so 'tīva bhavabhaktaś ca tapasvī taruṇaḥ sadā 
bhavārcanarataḥ śrīmān gomāndhīmāndvijarṣabhāḥ  LiP 
tasya putrā babhūvuste prajāpatisamā nava 
sarve māheśvarāścaiva mahādevaparāyaṇāḥ  LiP 
jyeṣṭho nābhir iti khyātas tasya kiṃpuruṣo 'nujaḥ 
harivarṣastṛtīyastu caturtho vai tvilāvṛtaḥ  LiP 
ramyastu pañcamas tatra hiraṇmān ṣaṣṭha ucyate 
kurustu saptamasteṣāṃ bhadrāśvastvaṣṭamaḥ smṛtaḥ  LiP 
navamaḥ ketumālastu teṣāṃ deśānnibodhata 
nābhestu dakṣiṇaṃ varṣaṃ hemākhyaṃ tu pitā dadau  LiP 
hemakūṭaṃ tu yadvarṣaṃ dadau kiṃpuruṣāya saḥ 
naiṣadhaṃ yatsmṛtaṃ varṣaṃ haraye tatpitā dadau  LiP 
ilāvṛtāya pradadau meruryatra tu madhyamaḥ 
nīlācalāśritaṃ varṣaṃ ramyāya pradadau pitā  LiP 
śvetaṃ yaduttaraṃ tasmāt pitrā dattaṃ hiraṇmate 
yaduttaraṃ śṛṅgavarṣaṃ pitā tatkurave dadau  LiP 
varṣaṃ mālyavataṃ cāpi bhadrāśvasya nyavedayat 
gandhamādanavarṣaṃ tu ketumālāya dattavān  LiP 
ityetāni mahāntīha nava varṣāṇi bhāgaśaḥ 
āgnīdhrasteṣu varṣeṣu putrāṃstānabhiṣicya vai  LiP 
yathākramaṃ sa dharmātmā tatastu tapasi sthitaḥ 
tapasā bhāvitaścaiva svādhyāyaniratastvabhūt  LiP 
svādhyāyanirataḥ paścāc chivadhyānaratas tvabhūt 
yāni kiṃpuruṣādyāni varṣāṇyaṣṭau śubhāni ca  LiP 
teṣāṃ svabhāvataḥ siddhiḥ sukhaprāyā hyayatnataḥ 
viparyayo na teṣvasti jarāmṛtyubhayaṃ na ca  LiP 
dharmādharmau na teṣvāstāṃ nottamādhamamadhyamāḥ 
na teṣvasti yugāvasthā kṣetreṣvaṣṭasu sarvataḥ  LiP 
rudrakṣetre mṛtāścaiva jaṅgamāḥ sthāvarās tathā 
bhaktāḥ prāsaṃgikāścāpi teṣu kṣetreṣu yānti te  LiP 
teṣāṃ hitāya rudreṇa cāṣṭakṣetraṃ vinirmitam 
tatra teṣāṃ mahādevaḥ sānnidhyaṃ kurute sadā  LiP 
dṛṣṭvā hṛdi mahādevam aṣṭakṣetranivāsinaḥ 
sukhinaḥ sarvadā teṣāṃ sa eveha parā gatiḥ  LiP 
nābhernisargaṃ vakṣyāmi himāṅke 'sminnibodhata 
nābhistvajanayatputraṃ merudevyāṃ mahāmatiḥ  LiP 
ṛṣabhaṃ pārthivaśreṣṭhaṃ sarvakṣatrasya pūjitam 
ṛṣabhādbharato jajñe vīraḥ putraśatāgrajaḥ  LiP 
so 'bhiṣicyātha ṛṣabho bharataṃ putravatsalaḥ 
jñānavairāgyamāśritya jitvendriyamahoragān  LiP 
sarvātmanātmani sthāpya paramātmānamīśvaram 
nagno jaṭī nirāhāraś cīrī dhvāntagato hi saḥ  LiP 
nirāśastyaktasaṃdehaḥ śaivamāpa paraṃ padam 
himādrerdakṣiṇaṃ varṣaṃ bharatāya nyavedayat  LiP 
tasmāttu bhārataṃ varṣaṃ tasya nāmnā vidurbudhāḥ 
bharatasyātmajo vidvān sumatirnāma dhārmikaḥ  LiP 
babhūva tasmiṃstadrājyaṃ bharataḥ saṃnyaveśayat 
putrasaṃkrāmitaśrīko vanaṃ rājā viveśa saḥ  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge bharatavarṣakathanaṃ nāma saptacatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
LiP  
suta uvāca
Meru
asya dvīpasya madhye tu merur nāma mahāgiriḥ 
nānāratnamayaiḥ śṛṅgaiḥ sthitaḥ sthitimatāṃ varaḥ  LiP 
caturaśītisāhasram utsedhena prakīrtitaḥ 
praviṣṭaḥ ṣoḍaśādhastād vistṛtaḥ ṣoḍaśaiva tu  LiP 
śarāvavat saṃsthitatvād dvātriṃśanmūrdhni vistṛtaḥ 
vistārāt triguṇaś cāsya pariṇāho 'numaṇḍalaḥ  LiP 
haimīkṛto maheśasya śubhāṅgasparśanena ca 
dhattūrapuṣpasaṃkāśaḥ sarvadevaniketanaḥ  LiP 
krīḍābhūmiś ca devānām anekāścaryasaṃyutaḥ 
lakṣayojana āyāmas tasyaivaṃ tu mahāgireḥ  LiP 
tataḥ ṣoḍaśasāhasraṃ yojanāni kṣiteradhaḥ

paścime nīlasaṃkāśa uttare vidrumaprabhaḥ  LiP 
Amarāvatī
amarāvatī pūrvabhāge nānāprāsādasaṃkulā 
nānādevagaṇaiḥ kīrṇā maṇijālasamāvṛtā  LiP 
gopurairvividhākārair hemaratnavibhūṣitaiḥ 
toraṇair hemacitraistu maṇikḷptaiḥ pathi sthitaiḥ  LiP 
saṃlāpālāpakuśalaiḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitaiḥ 
stanabhāravinamraiś ca madaghūrṇitalocanaiḥ  LiP 
strīsahasraiḥ samākīrṇā cāpsarobhiḥ samantataḥ 
dīrghikābhirvicitrābhiḥ phullāmbhoruhasaṃkulaiḥ  LiP 
hemasopānasaṃyuktair hemasaikatarāśibhiḥ 
nīlotpalaiścotpalaiś ca haimaiścāpi sugandhibhiḥ  LiP 
evaṃvidhaistaṭākaiś ca nadībhiś ca nadairyutā 
virājate purī śubhrā tayāsau parvataḥ śubhaḥ  LiP 
other cities at Mt Meru
tejasvinī nāma purī āgneyyāṃ pāvakasya tu 
amarāvatīsamā divyā sarvabhogasamanvitā  LiP 
vaivasvatī dakṣiṇe tu yamasya yamināṃ varāḥ

mahodayā cottare ca aiśānyāṃ tu yaśovatī

girerupari viprendrāḥ śuddhasphaṭikasannibham 
sahasrabhaumaṃ vistīrṇaṃ vimānaṃ vāmataḥ sthitam  LiP 
tasminmahābhujaḥ śarvaḥ somasūryāgnilocanaḥ 
siṃhāsane maṇimaye devyāste ṣaṇmukhena ca  LiP

somasya varuṇasyātha nirṛteḥ pāvakasya ca  LiP 
vāyoścaiva tu rudrasya śarvālayasamantataḥ 
teṣāṃ teṣāṃ vimāneṣu divyeṣu vividheṣu ca  LiP 
īśānyāmīśvarakṣetre nityārcā ca vyavasthitā 
siddheśvaraiś ca bhagavāñ chailādiḥ śiṣyasaṃmataḥ  LiP 
sanatkumāraḥ siddhaistu sukhāsīnaḥ sureśvaraḥ 
sanakaś ca sanandaś ca sadṛśāś ca sahasraśaḥ  LiP

bālasūryapratīkāśaṃ vimānaṃ tatra śobhanam  LiP 
śailādinaḥ śubhaṃ cāsti tasminnāste gaṇeśvaraḥ 
ṣaṇmukhasya gaṇeśasya gaṇānāṃ tu sahasraśaḥ  LiP 
suyaśāyāḥ sunetrāyāḥ mātṝṇāṃ madanasya ca 
tasya jambūnadī nāma mūlamāveṣṭya saṃsthitā  LiP 
tasya dakṣiṇapārśve tu jambūvṛkṣaḥ suśobhanaḥ 
atyucchritaḥ suvistīrṇaḥ sarvakālaphalapradaḥ  LiP 
Ilāvṛta
meroḥ samantādvistīrṇaṃ śubhaṃ varṣamilāvṛtam 
tatra jambūphalāhārāḥ keciccāmṛtabhojanāḥ  LiP 
jāṃbūnadasamaprakhyā nānāvarṇāś ca bhoginaḥ 
merupādāśrito viprā dvīpo 'yaṃ madhyamaḥ śubhaḥ  LiP
