tata utkṣipya tāṃ devo jagataḥ sthāpanecchayā  LiP 
pṛthivyāḥ pravibhāgāya manaścakre 'mbujekṣaṇaḥ 
pṛthivīṃ ca samāṃ kṛtvā pṛthivyāṃ so 'cinod girīn  LiP 
prāksarge dahyamāne tu tadā saṃvartakāgninā 
tenāgninā viśīrṇāste parvatā bhūrivistarāḥ  LiP 
śaityādekārṇave tasmin vāyunā tena saṃhatāḥ 
niṣiktā yatra yatrāsaṃs tatra tatrācalābhavan  LiP 
tadācalatvād acalāḥ parvabhiḥ parvatāḥ smṛtāḥ 
girayo hi nigīrṇatvāc chayānatvācchiloccayāḥ  LiP 
tatasteṣu vikīrṇeṣu koṭiśo hi giriṣvatha 
viśvakarmā vibhajate kalpādiṣu punaḥ punaḥ  LiP 
sasamudrāmimāṃ pṛthvīṃ saptadvīpāṃ saparvatām 
bhūrādyāṃś caturo lokān punaḥ so 'tha vyakalpayat  LiP 
Brahmā creates animals etc
lokān prakalpayitvātha prajāsargaṃ sasarja ha 
brahmā svayaṃbhūrbhagavān sisṛkṣurvividhāḥ prajāḥ  LiP 
sasarja sṛṣṭiṃ tadrūpāṃ kalpādiṣu yathāpurā 
tasyābhidhyāyataḥ sargaṃ tathā vai buddhipūrvakam  LiP 
buddhyāś ca samakāle vai prādurbhūtas tamomayaḥ 
tamomoho mahāmohas tāmisraścāndhasaṃjñitaḥ  LiP 
avidyā pañcaparvaiṣā prādurbhūtā mahātmanaḥ 
pañcadhāvasthitaḥ sargo dhyāyataḥ so 'bhimāninaḥ  LiP 
saṃvṛtastamasā caiva bījāṅkuravadāvṛtaḥ 
bahirantaścāprakāśas tabdho niḥsaṃjña eva ca  LiP 
yasmātteṣāṃ vṛtā buddhir duḥkhāni karaṇāni ca 
tasmātte saṃvṛtātmāno nagā mukhyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ  LiP 
mukhyasargaṃ tathābhūtaṃ dṛṣṭvā brahmā hyasādhakam 
aprasannamanāḥ so 'tha tato 'nyaṃ so hyamanyata  LiP 
tasyābhidhyāyataścaiva tiryaksrotā hyavartata 
tasmāt tiryakpravṛttaḥ sa tiryaksrotās tataḥ smṛtaḥ  LiP 
paśvādayaste vikhyātā utpathagrāhiṇo dvijāḥ 
tasyābhidhyāyato 'nyaṃ vai sāttvikaḥ samavartata  LiP 
ūrdhvasrotāstṛtīyastu sa vai cordhvaṃ vyavasthitaḥ 
yasmātpravartate cordhvam ūrdhvasrotāstataḥ smṛtaḥ  LiP 
te sukhaprītibahulā bahirantaś ca saṃvṛtāḥ 
prakāśā bahirantaś ca ūrdhvasrotobhavāḥ smṛtāḥ  LiP 
te sattvasya ca yogena sṛṣṭāḥ sattvodbhavāḥ smṛtāḥ 
ūrdhvasrotāstṛtīyo vai devasargastu sa smṛtaḥ  LiP 
prakāśād bahirantaś ca ūrdhvasrotodbhavāḥ smṛtāḥ 
te ūrdhvasrotaso jñeyās tuṣṭātmāno budhaiḥ smṛtāḥ  LiP 
ūrdhvasrotaḥsu sṛṣṭeṣu deveṣu varadaḥ prabhuḥ 
prītimānabhavadbrahmā tato 'nyaṃ so 'bhyamanyata  LiP 
sasarja sargamanyaṃ hi sādhakaṃ prabhurīśvaraḥ 
tato 'bhidhyāyatastasya satyābhidhyāyinastadā  LiP 
prādurāsīttadā vyaktād arvāksrotāstu sādhakaḥ 
yasmād arvāṅnyavartanta tato 'rvāksrotasas tu te  LiP 
te ca prakāśabahulās tamaḥpṛktā rajo 'dhikāḥ 
tasmātte duḥkhabahulā bhūyobhūyaś ca kāriṇaḥ  LiP 
saṃvṛtā bahirantaś ca manuṣyāḥ sādhakāś ca te  LiP 
lakṣaṇaistārakādyaiste hy aṣṭadhā tu vyavasthitāḥ  LiP 
siddhātmāno manuṣyāste gandharvasahadharmiṇaḥ 
ityeṣa taijasaḥ sargo hy arvāksrotaḥprakīrtitaḥ  LiP 
pañcamo 'nugrahaḥ sargaś caturdhā tu vyavasthitaḥ 
viparyayeṇa śaktyā ca siddhyā tuṣṭyā tathaiva ca  LiP 
sthāvareṣu viparyāsas tiryagyoniṣu śaktitaḥ 
siddhātmāno manuṣyāstu ṛṣideveṣu kṛtsnaśaḥ  LiP 
ityeṣa prākṛtaḥ sargo vaikṛto navamaḥ smṛtaḥ 
bhūtādikānāṃ bhūtānāṃ ṣaṣṭhaḥ sargaḥ sa ucyate  LiP 
nivṛttaṃ vartamānaṃ ca teṣāṃ jānanti vai punaḥ 
bhūtādikānāṃ bhūtānāṃ saptamaḥ sarga eva ca  LiP 
te parigrāhiṇaḥ sarve saṃvibhāgaratāḥ punaḥ 
svādanāś cāpyaśīlāś ca jñeyā bhūtādikāś ca te  LiP 
viparyayeṇa bhūtādir aśaktyā ca vyavasthitaḥ 
prathamo mahataḥ sargo vijñeyo brahmaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ  LiP 
tanmātrāṇāṃ dvitīyastu bhūtasargaḥ sa ucyate 
vaikārikastṛtīyastu sarga aindriyakaḥ smṛtaḥ  LiP 
ityeṣa prākṛtaḥ sargaḥ sambhūto buddhipūrvakaḥ 
mukhyasargaścaturthaś ca mukhyā vai sthāvarāḥ smṛtāḥ  LiP 
tato 'rvāksrotasāṃ sargaḥ saptamaḥ sa tu mānuṣaḥ 
aṣṭamo 'nugrahaḥ sargaḥ sāttvikastāmasaś ca saḥ  LiP 
pañcaite vaikṛtāḥ sargāḥ prākṛtāstu trayaḥ smṛtāḥ 
prākṛto vaikṛtaścaiva kaumāro navamaḥ smṛtaḥ  LiP 
abuddhipūrvakāḥ sargāḥ prākṛtāstu trayaḥ smṛtāḥ 
buddhipūrvaṃ pravartante ṣaṭ punarbrahmaṇastu te  LiP 
vistarānugrahaḥ sargaḥ kīrtyamāno nibodhata 
caturdhāvasthitaḥ so 'tha sarvabhūteṣu kṛtsnaśaḥ  LiP 
ityete prākṛtāścaiva vaikṛtāś ca nava smṛtāḥ 
parasparānuraktāś ca kāraṇaiś ca budhaiḥ smṛtāḥ  LiP 
Brahmā's sons
agre sasarja vai brahmā mānasānātmanaḥ samān 
ṛbhuḥ sanatkumāraś ca dvāvetāvūrdhvaretasau  LiP 
pūrvotpannau purā tebhyaḥ sarveṣāmapi pūrvajau 
vyatīte tvaṣṭame kalpe purāṇau lokasākṣiṇau  LiP 
tau vārāhe tu bhūrloke tejaḥ saṃkṣipya dhiṣṭhitau 
tāvubhau mokṣakarmāṇāv āropyātmānamātmani  LiP 
prajāṃ dharmaṃ ca kāmaṃ ca tyaktvā vairāgyamāsthitau 
yathotpannastathaiveha kumāraḥ sa ihocyate  LiP 
tasmāt sanatkumāreti nāmāsyeha prakīrtitam 
sanandaṃ sanakaṃ caiva vidvāṃsaṃ ca sanātanam  LiP 
vijñānena nivṛttāste vyavartanta mahaujasaḥ 
saṃbuddhāścaiva nānātve apravṛttāś ca yoginaḥ  LiP 
asṛṣṭvaiva prajāsargaṃ pratisargaṃ gatāḥ punaḥ 
tatasteṣu vyatīteṣu tato 'nyān sādhakān sutān  LiP 
mānasānasṛjadbrahmā punaḥ sthānābhimāninaḥ 
ā bhūtasamplavāvasthā yairiyaṃ vidhṛtā mahī  LiP 
āpo 'gniṃ pṛthivīṃ vāyum antarikṣaṃ divaṃ tathā 
samudrāṃś ca nadīścaiva tathā śailavanaspatīn  LiP 
oṣadhīnāṃ tathātmāno vallīnāṃ vṛkṣavīrudhām 
latāḥ kāṣṭhāḥ kalāścaiva muhūrtāḥ saṃdhirātryahān  LiP 
ardhamāsāṃś ca māsāṃś ca ayanābdayugāni ca 
sthānābhimāninaḥ sarve sthānākhyāścaiva te smṛtāḥ  LiP 
Brahma's eleven sons
devānṛṣīṃś ca mahato gadatastān nibodhata 
marīcibhṛgvaṅgirasaṃ pulastyaṃ pulahaṃ kratum  LiP 
dakṣamatriṃ vasiṣṭhaṃ ca so 'sṛjanmānasān nava 
nava brahmāṇa ityete purāṇe niścayaṃ gatāḥ  LiP 
teṣāṃ brahmātmakānāṃ vai sarveṣāṃ brahmavādinām 
sthānāni kalpayāmāsa pūrvavatpadmasaṃbhavaḥ  LiP 
tato 'sṛjacca saṃkalpaṃ dharmaṃ caiva sukhāvaham 
so 'sṛjad vyavasāyāttu dharmaṃ devo maheśvaraḥ  LiP 
saṃkalpaṃ caiva saṃkalpāt sarvalokapitāmahaḥ 
mānasaś ca rucirnāma vijajñe brahmaṇaḥ prabhoḥ  LiP 
prāṇādbrahmāsṛjaddakṣaṃ cakṣurbhyāṃ ca marīcinam 
bhṛgustu hṛdayājjajñe ṛṣiḥ salilajanmanaḥ  LiP 
śiraso 'ṅgirasaścaiva śrotrādatriṃ tathāsṛjat 
pulastyaṃ ca tathodānād vyānācca pulahaṃ punaḥ  LiP 
samānajo vasiṣṭhaś ca apānānnirmame kratum 
ityete brahmaṇaḥ putrā divyā ekādaśā smṛtāḥ  LiP 
dharmādayaḥ prathamajāḥ sarve te brahmaṇaḥ sutāḥ 
bhṛgvādayastu te sṛṣṭā navaite brahmavādinaḥ  LiP 
gṛhamedhinaḥ purāṇās te dharmas taiḥ sampravartitaḥ 
teṣāṃ dvādaśa te vaṃśā divyā devaguṇānvitāḥ  LiP 
kriyāvantaḥ prajāvanto maharṣibhir alaṃkṛtāḥ 
Ṛbhu Sanatkumāra
ṛbhuḥ sanatkumāraś ca dvāvetāvūrdhvaretasau  LiP 
pūrvotpannau paraṃ tebhyaḥ sarveṣāmapi pūrvajau 
vyatīte tvaṣṭame kalpe purāṇau lokasākṣiṇau  LiP 
virājetāmubhau loke tejaḥ saṃkṣipya dhiṣṭhitau 
tāvubhau yogakarmāṇāv āropyātmānam ātmani  LiP 
prajāṃ dharmaṃ ca kāmaṃ ca tyaktvā vairāgyamāsthitau 
yathotpannaḥ sa eveha kumāraḥ sa ihocyate  LiP 
tasmātsanatkumāreti nāmāsyeha pratiṣṭhitam 
tato 'bhidhyāyatastasya jajñire mānasāḥ prajāḥ  LiP 
taccharīrasamutpannaiḥ kāryaistaiḥ kāraṇaiḥ saha 
kṣetrajñāḥ samavartanta gātrebhyastasya dhīmataḥ  LiP 
tato devāsurapitṝn mānuṣāṃś ca catuṣṭayam 
sisṛkṣur ambhāṃsyetāni svam ātmānam ayūyujat  LiP 
tatastu yuñjatastasya tamomātrasamudbhavam 
samabhidhyāyataḥ sargaṃ prayatnena prajāpateḥ  LiP 
tato 'sya jaghanātpūrvam asurā jajñire sutāḥ 
asura nirukti
asuḥ prāṇaḥ smṛto viprās tajjanmānas tato 'surāḥ  LiP 
yayā sṛṣṭāsurāḥ sarve tāṃ tanuṃ sa vyapohata 
origin of time units night etc  
sāpaviddhā tanus tena sadyo rātrir ajāyata  LiP 
sā tamobahulā yasmāt tato rātrirniyāmikā 
āvṛtāstamasā rātrau prajāstasmātsvapantyuta  LiP 
sṛṣṭvāsurāṃstataḥ so vai tanumanyāmagṛhṇata 
avyaktāṃ sattvabahulāṃ tatastāṃ so 'bhyapūjayat  LiP 
tatastāṃ yuñjatas tasya priyam āsīt prajāpateḥ 
deva nirukti
tato mukhātsamutpannā dīvyatastasya devatāḥ  LiP 
yato 'sya dīvyato jātās tena devāḥ prakīrtitāḥ 
dhāturdiviti yaḥ proktaḥ krīḍāyāṃ sa vibhāvyate  LiP 
yasmāttasya tu dīvyanto jajñire tena devatāḥ 
devānsṛṣṭvātha deveśas tanumanyāmapadyata  LiP 
utsṛṣṭā sā tanustena sadyo 'haḥ samajāyata 
tasmādaho dharmayuktaṃ devatāḥ samupāsate  LiP 
sattvamātrātmikāmeva tato 'nyāṃ so 'bhyamanyata 
pitṛvanmanyamānasya putrāṃstāndhyāyataḥ prabhoḥ  LiP 
pitaro hyupapakṣābhyāṃ rātryahṇor antare 'bhavan 
tasmātte pitaro devāḥ pitṛtvaṃ tena teṣu tat  LiP 
yayā sṛṣṭāstu pitaras tanuṃ tāṃ sa vyapohata 
sāpaviddhā tanustena sadyaḥ saṃdhyā vyajāyata  LiP 
yasmādahardevatānāṃ rātriryā sāsurī smṛtā 
tayormadhye tu paitrī yā tanuḥ sā tu garīyasī  LiP 
tasmāddevā surāḥ sarve ṛṣayo mānavās tathā 
upāsante mudāyuktā rātryahṇor madhyamāṃ tanum  LiP 
tato hyanyāṃ punarbrahmā tanuṃ vai samagṛhṇata 
rajomātrātmikāyāṃ tu manasā so 'sṛjatprabhuḥ  LiP 
rajaḥpriyāṃstataḥ so 'tha mānasānasṛjatsutān 
manasvinastatastasya mānavā jajñire sutāḥ  LiP 
sṛṣṭvā punaḥ prajāścāpi svāṃ tanuṃ tām apohata 
sāpaviddhā tanustena jyotsnā sadyastvajāyata  LiP 
yasmādbhavanti saṃhṛṣṭā jyotsnāyā udbhave prajāḥ 
ityetāstanavastena hy apaviddhā mahātmanā  LiP 
sadyo rātryahanī caiva saṃdhyā jyotsnā ca jajñire 
jyotsnā saṃdhyā ahaścaiva sattvamātrātmakaṃ trayam  LiP 
tamomātrātmikā rātriḥ sā vai tasmānniśātmikā 
tasmāddevā divātanvā tuṣṭyā sṛṣṭā mukhāttu vai  LiP 
yasmātteṣāṃ divā janma balinastena vai divā 
tanvā yayāsurān rātrau jaghanādasṛjatprabhuḥ  LiP 
prāṇebhyo niśijanmāno balino niśi tena te 
etānyeva bhaviṣyāṇāṃ devānāmasuraiḥ saha  LiP 
pitṝṇāṃ mānavānāṃ ca atītānāgateṣu vai 
manvantareṣu sarveṣu nimittāni bhavanti hi  LiP 
jyotsnā rātryahanī saṃdhyā catvāryaṃbhāṃsi tāni vai 
bhānti yasmāt tato 'ṃbhāṃsi śabdo 'yaṃ sumanīṣibhiḥ  LiP 
bhātirdīptau nigaditaḥ punaścātha prajāpatiḥ 
so 'mbhāṃsyetāni sṛṣṭvā tu devamānuṣadānavān  LiP 
pitṝṃścaiva sṛjattanvā ātmanā vividhānpunaḥ 
origin of Rākṣasas
tāmutsṛjya tanuṃ jyotsnāṃ tato 'nyāṃ prāpya sa prabhuḥ  LiP 
mūrtiṃ tamorajaḥprāyāṃ punarevābhyapūjayat 
andhakāre kṣudhāviṣṭāṃs tato 'nyān so 'sṛjat prabhuḥ  LiP 
tena sṛṣṭāḥ kṣudhātmāno aṃbhāṃsyādātum udyatāḥ 
ambhāṃsyetāni rakṣāma uktavantastu teṣu ye  LiP 
rākṣasā nāma te yasmāt kṣudhāviṣṭā niśācarāḥ 
ye 'bruvan yakṣamo 'mbhāṃsi teṣāṃ hṛṣṭāḥ parasparam  LiP 
tena te karmaṇā yakṣā guhyakā gūḍhakarmaṇā 
rakṣeti pālane cāpi dhātureṣa vibhāṣyate  LiP 
evaṃ ca yakṣatir dhātur bhakṣaṇe sa nirucyate 
originnirukti of snakes
taṃ dṛṣṭvā hyapriyeṇāsya keśāḥ śīrṇāstu dhīmataḥ  LiP 
te śīrṇāścotthitā hyūrdhvaṃ te caivārurudhuḥ prabhum 
hīnāstacchiraso vālā yasmāccaivāvasarpiṇaḥ  LiP 
vyālātmānaḥ smṛtā vālā hīnatvādahayaḥ smṛtāḥ 
patatvātpannagāścaiva sarpāścaivāvasarpaṇāt  LiP 
tasya krodhodbhavo yo 'sau agnigarbhaḥ sudāruṇaḥ 
sa tu sarpān sahotpannān āviveśa viṣātmakaḥ  LiP 
sarpānsṛṣṭvā tataḥ kruddhaḥ krodhātmāno vinirmame 
varṇena kapiśenogrās te bhūtāḥ piśitāśanāḥ  LiP 
bhūtatvātte smṛtā bhūtāḥ piśācāḥ piśitāśanāt 
originnirukti of Gandharvas
prasannaṃ gāyatastasya gandharvā jajñire yadā  LiP 
dhayatītyeṣa vai dhātuḥ pānatve paripaṭhyate 
dhayanto jajñire vācaṃ gandharvāstena te smṛtāḥ  LiP 
aṣṭasvetāsu sṛṣṭāsu devayoniṣu sa prabhuḥ 
creation of animals
tataḥ svacchandato 'nyāni vayāṃsi vayasāsṛjat  LiP 
svacchandataḥ svacchandāṃsi vayasā ca vayāṃsi ca 
paśūnsṛṣṭvā sa deveśo 'sṛjatpakṣigaṇānapi  LiP 
mukhato 'jāḥ sasarjātha vakṣasaś cāvayo 'sṛjat 
gāścaivāthodarādbrahmā pārśvābhyāṃ ca vinirmame  LiP 
padbhyāṃ cāśvān samātaṅgān rāsabhān āvayān mṛgān 
uṣṭrānaśvatarāṃścaiva tathānyāścaiva jātayaḥ  LiP 
oṣadhyaḥ phalamūlinyo romabhyastasya jajñire 
evaṃ paśvoṣadhīḥ sṛṣṭvā yūyujat so 'dhvare prabhuḥ  LiP 
gaurajaḥ pūruṣo meṣo hy aśvo 'śvataragardabhau 
etāngrāmyānpaśūnāhur āraṇyānvai nibodhata  LiP 
śvāpado dvikhuro hastī vānarāḥ pakṣipañcamāḥ 
audakāḥ paśavaḥ ṣaṣṭhāḥ saptamāstu sarīsṛpāḥ  LiP 
mahiṣā gavayākṣāś ca plavaṃgāḥ śarabhā vṛkāḥ 
siṃhastu saptamasteṣām āraṇyāḥ paśavaḥ smṛtāḥ  LiP 
creation of sacrifice
gāyatraṃ ca ṛcaṃ caiva trivṛtsāmarathaṃtaram 
agniṣṭomaṃ ca yajñānāṃ nirmame prathamān mukhāt  LiP 
yajūṃṣi traiṣṭubhaṃ chanda stomaṃ pañcadaśaṃ tathā 
bṛhatsāma tathokthyaṃ ca dakṣiṇādasṛjanmukhāt  LiP 
sāmāni jagatīchanda stomaṃ saptadaśaṃ tathā 
vairūpamatirātraṃ ca paścimādasṛjanmukhāt  LiP 
ekaviṃśamatharvāṇam āptoryāmāṇam eva ca 
anuṣṭubhaṃ savairājam uttarādasṛjanmukhāt  LiP 
vidyuto 'śanimeghāṃś ca rohitendradhanūṃṣi ca 
tejāṃsi ca sasarjādau kalpasya bhagavānprabhuḥ  LiP 
uccāvacāni bhūtāni gātrebhyastasya jajñire 
brahmaṇastu prajāsargaṃ sṛjato hi prajāpateḥ  LiP 
sṛṣṭvā catuṣṭayaṃ pūrvaṃ devāsuranarānpitṝn 
tato 'sṛjat sa bhūtāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca  LiP 
yakṣānpiśācān gandharvāṃs tv athaivāpsarasāṃ gaṇān 
narakinnararakṣāṃsi vayaḥpaśumṛgoragān  LiP 
avyayaṃ ca vyayaṃ cāpi yadidaṃ sthāṇujaṅgamam 
teṣāṃ vai yāni karmāṇi prāksṛṣṭyāṃ pratipedire  LiP 
tānyeva pratipadyante sṛjyamānāḥ punaḥ punaḥ 
hiṃsrāhiṃsre mṛdukrūre dharmādharme nṛtānṛte  LiP 
tadbhāvitāḥ prapadyante tasmāttattasya rocate 
mahābhūteṣu sṛṣṭeṣu indriyārtheṣu mūrtiṣu  LiP 
viniyogaṃ ca bhūtānāṃ dhātaiva vyadadhāt svayam 
kecitpuruṣakāraṃ tu prāhuḥ karma sumānavāḥ  LiP 
daivamityapare viprāḥ svabhāvaṃ bhūtacintakāḥ 
pauruṣaṃ karma daivaṃ ca phalavṛttisvabhāvataḥ  LiP 
na caikaṃ na pṛthagbhāvam adhikaṃ na tato viduḥ 
etadevaṃ ca naikaṃ ca nāmabhedena nāpyubhe  LiP 
karmasthā viṣamaṃ brūyuḥ sattvasthāḥ samadarśanāḥ 
nāma rūpaṃ ca bhūtānāṃ kṛtānāṃ ca prapañcanam  LiP 
vedaśabdebhya evādau nirmame sa maheśvaraḥ 
ṛṣīṇāṃ nāmadheyāni yāś ca vedeṣu vṛttayaḥ  LiP 
śarvaryante prasūtānāṃ tānyevaibhyo dadātyajaḥ 
evaṃvidhāḥ sṛṣṭayastu brahmaṇo 'vyaktajanmanaḥ  LiP 
śarvaryante pradṛśyante siddhimāśritya mānasīm 
evaṃbhūtāni sṛṣṭāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca  LiP 
yadāsya tāḥ prajāḥ sṛṣṭā na vyavardhanta sattamāḥ 
tamomātrāvṛto brahmā tadā śokena duḥkhitaḥ  LiP 
tataḥ sa vidadhe buddhim arthaniścayagāminīm 
athātmani samadrākṣīt tamomātrāṃ niyāmikām  LiP 
rajaḥsattvaṃ parityajya vartamānāṃ svadharmataḥ 
tataḥ sa tena duḥkhena duḥkhaṃ cakre jagatpatiḥ  LiP 
tamaś ca vyanudatpaścād rajaḥ sattvaṃ tamāvṛṇot 
origin of adharma and hiṃsā
tattamaḥ pratinunnaṃ vai mithunaṃ samajāyata  LiP 
adharmastamaso jajñe hiṃsā śokādajāyata 
tatastasminsamudbhūte mithune dāruṇātmike  LiP 
Śatarūpā
gatāsur bhagavān āsīt prītiś cainam aśiśriyat 
svāṃ tanuṃ sa tato brahmā tāmapohata bhāsvarām  LiP 
dvidhā kṛtvā svakaṃ deham ardhena puruṣo 'bhavat 
ardhena nārī sā tasya śatarūpā vyajāyata  LiP 
prakṛtiṃ bhūtadhātrīṃ tāṃ kāmādvai sṛṣṭavānprabhuḥ 
sā divaṃ pṛthivīṃ caiva mahimnā vyāpyadhiṣṭhitā  LiP 
brahmaṇaḥ sā tanuḥ pūrvā divamāvṛtya tiṣṭhati 
yā tvardhātsṛjato nārī śatarūpā vyajāyata  LiP 
sā devī niyutaṃ taptvā tapaḥ paramaduścaram 
bhartāraṃ dīptayaśasaṃ puruṣaṃ pratyapadyata  LiP 
sa vai svāyaṃbhuvaḥ pūrvaṃ puruṣo manurucyate 
tasyaiva saptatiyugaṃ manvantaramihocyate  LiP 
lebhe sa puruṣaḥ patnīṃ śatarūpām ayonijām 
tayā sārdhaṃ sa ramate tasmātsā ratirucyate  LiP 
prathamaḥ saṃprayogātmā kalpādau samapadyata 
Manu creates the creatures
virājam asṛjad brahmā so 'bhavat puruṣo virāṭ  LiP 
samrāṭ ca śatarūpā vai vairājaḥ sa manuḥ smṛtaḥ 
sa vairājaḥ prajāsargaṃ sasarja puruṣo manuḥ  LiP 
vairājātpuruṣād vīrāc chatarūpā vyajāyata 
priyavratottānapādau putrau dvau lokasaṃmatau  LiP 
kanye dve ca mahābhāge yābhyāṃ jātā imāḥ prajāḥ 
devī nāma tathākūtiḥ prasūtiścaiva te ubhe  LiP 
svāyaṃbhuvaḥ prasūtiṃ tu dakṣāya pradadau prabhuḥ 
prāṇo dakṣa iti jñeyaḥ saṃkalpo manurucyate  LiP 
ruceḥ prajāpateḥ so 'tha ākūtiṃ pratyapādayat 
ākūtyāṃ mithunaṃ jajñe mānasasya ruceḥ śubham  LiP 
yajñaś ca dakṣiṇā caiva yamalau saṃbabhūvatuḥ 
yajñasya dakṣiṇāyāṃ tu putrā dvādaśa jajñire  LiP 
yāmā iti samākhyātā devāḥ svāyaṃbhuve 'ntare 
etasya putrā yajñasya tasmādyāmāś ca te smṛtāḥ  LiP 
ajitaścaiva śukraś ca gaṇau dvau brahmaṇā kṛtau 
yāmāḥ pūrvaṃ prajātā ye te 'bhavaṃstu divaukasaḥ  LiP 
svāyaṃbhuvasutāyāṃ tu prasūtyāṃ lokamātaraḥ 
tasyāṃ kanyāścaturviṃśad dakṣas tvajanayat prabhuḥ  LiP 
sarvāstāś ca mahābhāgāḥ sarvāḥ kamalalocanāḥ 
bhogavatyaś ca tāḥ sarvāḥ sarvāstā yogamātaraḥ  LiP 
sarvāś ca brahmavādinyaḥ sarvā viśvasya mātaraḥ 
śraddhā lakṣmīrdhṛtistuṣṭiḥ puṣṭirmedhā kriyā tathā  LiP 
buddhirlajjā vapuḥ śāntiḥ siddhiḥ kīrtistrayodaśa 
patnyarthaṃ pratijagrāha dharmo dākṣāyaṇīḥ prabhuḥ  LiP 
dārāṇyetāni vai tasya vihitāni svayaṃbhuvā 
tābhyaḥ śiṣṭāyavīyasya ekādaśa sulocanāḥ  LiP 
daughters and grandchildren of Dakṣa
satī khyātyatha saṃbhūtiḥ smṛtiḥ prītiḥ kṣamā tathā 
saṃnatiścānasūyā ca ūrjā svāhā svadhā tathā  LiP 
tās tathā pratyapadyanta punaranye maharṣayaḥ 
rudro bhṛgur marīciś ca aṅgirāḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ  LiP 
pulastyo 'trir vasiṣṭhaś ca pitaro 'gnistathaiva ca 
satīṃ bhavāya prāyacchat khyātiṃ ca bhṛgave tataḥ  LiP 
marīcaye ca saṃbhūtiṃ smṛtimaṅgirase dadau 
prītiṃ caiva pulastyāya kṣamāṃ vai pulahāya ca  LiP 
kratave saṃnatiṃ nāma anasūyāṃ tathātraye 
ūrjāṃ dadau vasiṣṭhāya svāhāmapyagnaye dadau  LiP 
svadhāṃ caiva pitṛbhyastu tāsvapatyā nibodhata 
etāḥ sarvā mahābhāgāḥ prajāsvanusṛtāḥ sthitāḥ  LiP 
manvantareṣu sarveṣu yāvadābhūtasaṃplavam 
śraddhā kāmaṃ vijajñe vai darpo lakṣmīsutaḥ smṛtaḥ  LiP 
dhṛtyāstu niyamaḥ putras tuṣṭyāḥ saṃtoṣa eva ca 
puṣṭyā lobhaḥ sutaścāpi medhāputraḥ śrutas tathā  LiP 
kriyāyāmabhavatputro daṇḍaḥ samaya eva ca 
buddhyāṃ bodhaḥ sutas tadvat pramādo 'pyupajāyata  LiP 
lajjāyāṃ vinayaḥ putro vyavasāyo vasoḥ sutaḥ 
kṣemaḥ śāntisutaścāpi sukhaṃ siddhervyajāyata  LiP 
yaśaḥ kīrtisutaścāpi ityete dharmasūnavaḥ 
kāmasya harṣaḥ putro vai devyāṃ prītyāṃ vyajāyata  LiP 
ityeṣa vai sutodarkaḥ sargo dharmasya kīrtitaḥ 
jajñe hiṃsā tvadharmādvai nikṛtiṃ cānṛtaṃ sutam  LiP 
nikṛtyāṃ tu dvayaṃ jajñe bhayaṃ naraka eva ca 
māyā ca vedanā cāpi mithunadvayametayoḥ  LiP 
bhūyo jajñe 'tha vai māyā mṛtyuṃ bhūtāpahāriṇam 
vedanāyāḥ sutaścāpi duḥkhaṃ jajñe ca rauravaḥ  LiP 
mṛtyor vyādhijarāśoka krodhāsūyāś ca jajñire 
duḥkhottarāḥ sutā hyete sarve cādharmalakṣaṇāḥ  LiP 
naiṣāṃ bhāryāstu putrāś ca sarve hyete parigrahāḥ 
ityeṣa tāmasaḥ sargo jajñe dharmaniyāmakaḥ  LiP 
Śiva creates mental  immortal sons  Rudras
prajāḥ sṛjeti vyādiṣṭo brahmaṇā nīlalohitaḥ 
so 'bhidhyāya satīṃ bhāryāṃ nirmame hyātmasaṃbhavān  LiP 
nādhikānna ca hīnāṃstān mānasānātmanaḥ samān 
sahasraṃ hi sahasrāṇāṃ so 'sṛjat kṛttivāsasaḥ  LiP 
tulyānevātmanaḥ sarvān rūpatejobalaśrutaiḥ 
piṅgalānsaniṣaṅgāṃś ca sakapardānsalohitān  LiP 
viśiṣṭān harikeśāṃś ca dṛṣṭighnāṃś ca kapālinaḥ 
mahārūpānvirūpāṃś ca viśvarūpān svarūpiṇaḥ  LiP 
rathinaścarmiṇaścaiva varmiṇaś ca varūthinaḥ 
sahasraśatabāhūṃś ca divyān bhaumāntarikṣagān  LiP 
sthūlaśīrṣān aṣṭadaṃṣṭrān dvijihvāṃs tāṃs trilocanān 
annādān piśitāśāṃś ca ājyapānsomapānapi  LiP 
mīḍhuṣo 'tikapālāṃś ca śitikaṇṭhordhvaretasaḥ 
havyādāñchrutadharmāṃś ca dharmiṇo hyatha barhiṇaḥ  LiP 
āsīnāndhāvataścaiva pañcabhūtānsahasraśaḥ 
adhyāpino 'dhyāyinaś ca japato yuñjatas tathā  LiP 
dhūmavanto jvalantaś ca nadīmanto 'tidīptinaḥ 
vṛddhānbuddhimataścaiva brahmiṣṭhāñśubhadarśanān  LiP 
nīlagrīvān sahasrākṣān sarvāṃścātha kṣamākarān 
adṛśyānsarvabhūtānāṃ mahāyogānmahaujasaḥ  LiP 
bhramanto 'bhidravantaś ca plavantaś ca sahasraśaḥ 
ayātayāmān asṛjad rudrānetān surottamān  LiP 
brahmā dṛṣṭvābravīdenaṃ māsrākṣīrīdṛśīḥ prajāḥ 
sraṣṭavyā nātmanastulyāḥ prajā deva namo 'stu te  LiP 
anyāḥ sṛja tvaṃ bhadraṃ te prajā vai mṛtyusaṃyutāḥ 
nārapsyante hi karmāṇi prajāvagatamṛtyavaḥ  LiP 
evamukto 'bravīdenaṃ nāhaṃ mṛtyujarānvitāḥ 
prajāḥ srakṣyāmi bhadraṃ te sthito 'haṃ tvaṃ sṛja prajāḥ  LiP 
ete ye vai mayā sṛṣṭā virūpā nīlalohitāḥ 
sahasrāṇāṃ sahasraṃ tu ātmano niḥsṛtāḥ prajāḥ  LiP 
ete devā bhaviṣyanti rudrā nāma mahābalāḥ 
pṛthivyāmantarikṣe ca dikṣu caiva pariśritāḥ  LiP 
śatarudrāḥ samātmāno bhaviṣyantīti yājñikāḥ 
yajñabhājo bhaviṣyanti sarvadevagaṇaiḥ saha  LiP 
manvantareṣu ye devā bhaviṣyantīha bhedataḥ 
sārdhaṃ tair ījyamānās te sthāsyantīha ā yugakṣayāt  LiP 
evamuktastadā brahmā mahādevena dhīmatā 
pratyuvāca namaskṛtya hṛṣyamāṇaḥ prajāpatiḥ  LiP 
evaṃ bhavatu bhadraṃ te yathā te vyāhṛtaṃ vibho 
brahmaṇā samanujñāte tathā sarvamabhūtkila  LiP 
tataḥ prabhṛti deveśo na cāsūyata vai prajāḥ 
ūrdhvaretāḥ sthitaḥ sthāṇur yāvadābhūtasaṃplavam  LiP 
yasmāduktaḥ sthito 'smīti tasmātsthāṇuriti smṛtaḥ 
Śiva transforms into Ardhanārīśvara
eṣa devo mahādevaḥ puruṣo 'rkasamadyutiḥ  LiP 
ardhanārīnaravapus tejasā jvalanopamaḥ 
svecchayāsau dvidhābhūtaḥ pṛthak strī puruṣaḥ pṛthak  LiP 
sa evaikādaśārdhena sthito 'sau parameśvaraḥ 
tatra yā sā mahābhāgā śaṅkarasyārdhakāyinī  LiP 
prāguktā tu mahādevī strī saiveha satī hyabhūt 
hitāya jagatāṃ devī dakṣeṇārādhitā purā  LiP 
forms of DevīDurgā
kāryārthaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ tasyāḥ śuklaṃ vāmaṃ tathāsitam 
ātmānaṃ vibhajasveti proktā devena śaṃbhunā  LiP 
sā tathoktā dvidhābhūtā śuklā kṛṣṇā ca vai dvijāḥ 
tasyā nāmāni vakṣyāmi śṛṇvantu ca samāhitāḥ  LiP 
svāhā svadhā mahāvidyā medhā lakṣmīḥ sarasvatī 
satī dākṣāyaṇī vidyā icchāśaktiḥ kriyātmikā  LiP 
aparṇā caikaparṇā ca tathā caivaikapāṭalā 
umā haimavatī caiva kalyāṇī caikamātṛkā  LiP 
khyātiḥ prajñā mahābhāgā loke gaurīti viśrutā 
gaṇāṃbikā mahādevī nandinī jātavedasī  LiP 
ekarūpamathaitasyāḥ pṛthagdehavibhāvanāt 
sāvitrī varadā puṇyā pāvanī lokaviśrutā  LiP 
ājñā āveśanī kṛṣṇā tāmasī sāttvikī śivā 
prakṛtirvikṛtā raudrī durgā bhadrā pramāthinī  LiP 
kālarātrirmahāmāyā revatī bhūtanāyikā 
dvāparāntavibhāge ca nāmānīmāni suvratāḥ  LiP 
gautamī kauśikī cāryā caṇḍī kātyāyanī satī 
kumārī yādavī devī varadā kṛṣṇapiṅgalā  LiP 
barhidhvajā śūladharā paramā brahmacāriṇī 
mahendropendrabhaginī dṛṣadvaty ekaśūladhṛk  LiP 
aparājitā bahubhujā pragalbhā siṃhavāhinī 
śumbhādidaityahantrī ca mahāmahiṣamardinī  LiP 
amoghā vindhyanilayā vikrāntā gaṇanāyikā 
devyā nāmavikārāṇi ityetāni yathākramam  LiP 
bhadrakālyā mayoktāni samyakphalapradāni ca 
ye paṭhanti narāsteṣāṃ vidyate na ca pātakam  LiP 
araṇye parvate vāpi pure vāpyathavā gṛhe 
rakṣāmetāṃ prayuñjīta jale vātha sthale 'pi vā  LiP 
vyāghrakumbhīnacorebhyo bhayasthāne viśeṣataḥ 
āpatsvapi ca sarvāsu devyā nāmāni kīrtayet  LiP 
āryakagrahabhūtaiś ca pūtanāmātṛbhis tathā 
abhyarditānāṃ bālānāṃ rakṣāmetāṃ prayojayet  LiP 
mahādevīkale dve tu prajñā śrīś ca prakīrtite 
ābhyāṃ devīsahasrāṇi yairvyāptamakhilaṃ jagat  LiP 
anayā devadevo 'sau satyā rudro maheśvaraḥ 
ātiṣṭhatsarvalokānāṃ hitāya parameśvaraḥ  LiP 
rudraḥ paśupatiścāsīt purā dagdhaṃ puratrayam 
devāś ca paśavaḥ sarve babhūvustasya tejasā  LiP 
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi ādisargakramaṃ śubham 
sa yāti brahmaṇo lokaṃ śrāvayedvā dvijottamān  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge sṛṣṭivistāro nāma saptatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
LiP  
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
samāsād vistarāccaiva sargaḥ proktastvayā śubhaḥ 
kathaṃ paśupatiścāsīt puraṃ dagdhuṃ maheśvaraḥ  LiP 
kathaṃ ca paśavaścāsan devāḥ sabrahmakāḥ prabhoḥ 
mayasya tapasā pūrvaṃ sudurgaṃ nirmitaṃ puram  LiP 
haimaṃ ca rājataṃ divyam ayasmayam anuttamam 
sudurgaṃ devadevena dagdhamityeva naḥ śrutam  LiP 
kathaṃ dadāha bhagavān bhaganetranipātanaḥ 
ekeneṣunipātena divyenāpi tadā katham  LiP 
viṣṇunotpāditairbhūtair na dagdhaṃ tatpuratrayam 
purasya saṃbhavaḥ sarvo varalābhaḥ purā śrutaḥ  LiP 
idānīṃ dahanaṃ sarvaṃ vaktumarhasi suvrata 
teṣāṃ tadvacanaṃ śrutvā sūtaḥ paurāṇikottamaḥ  LiP 
yathā śrutaṃ tathā prāha vyāsād viśvārthasūcakāt 
sūta uvāca
trailokyasyāsya śāpāddhi manovākkāyasaṃbhavāt  LiP 
nihate tārake daitye tāraputre sabāndhave 
skandena vā prayatnena tasya putrā mahābalāḥ  LiP 
vidyunmālī tārakākṣaḥ kamalākṣaś ca vīryavān 
tapastepurmahātmāno mahābalaparākramāḥ  LiP 
tapa ugraṃ samāsthāya niyame parame sthitāḥ 
tapasā karśayāmāsur dehān svāndānavottamāḥ  LiP 
teṣāṃ pitāmahaḥ prīto varadaḥ pradadau varam 
daityā ūcuḥ
avadhyatvaṃ ca sarveṣāṃ sarvabhūteṣu sarvadā  LiP 
sahitā varayāmāsuḥ sarvalokapitāmaham 
tān abravīt tadā devo lokānāṃ prabhur avyayaḥ  LiP 
nāsti sarvāmaratvaṃ vai nivartadhvam ato 'surāḥ 
anyaṃ varaṃ vṛṇīdhvaṃ vai yādṛśaṃ samprarocate  LiP 
tataste sahitā daityāḥ sampradhārya parasparam 
brahmāṇamabruvandaityāḥ praṇipatya jagadgurum  LiP 
vayaṃ purāṇi trīṇyeva samāsthāya mahīmimām 
vicariṣyāma lokeśa tvatprasādājjagadguro  LiP 
tathā varṣasahasreṣu sameṣyāmaḥ parasparam 
ekībhāvaṃ gamiṣyanti purāṇyetāni cānagha  LiP 
samāgatāni caitāni yo hanyādbhagavaṃstadā 
ekenaiveṣuṇā devaḥ sa no mṛtyurbhaviṣyati  LiP 
evamastviti tāndevaḥ pratyuktvā prāviśaddivam 
tato mayaḥ svatapasā cakre vīraḥ purāṇyatha  LiP 
kāñcanaṃ divi tatrāsīd antarikṣe ca rājatam 
āyasaṃ cābhavad bhūmau puraṃ teṣāṃ mahātmanām  LiP 
ekaikaṃ yojanaśataṃ vistārāyāmataḥ samam 
kāñcanaṃ tārakākṣasya kamalākṣasya rājatam  LiP 
vidyunmāleścāyasaṃ vai trividhaṃ durgamuttamam 
mayaś ca balavāṃstatra daityadānavapūjitaḥ  LiP 
hairaṇye rājate caiva kṛṣṇāyasamaye tathā 
ālayaṃ cātmanaḥ kṛtvā tatrāste balavāṃstadā  LiP 
evaṃ babhūvurdaityānām atidurgāṇi suvratāḥ 
purāṇi trīṇi viprendrās trailokyamiva cāparam  LiP 
puratraye tadā jāte sarve daityā jagattraye 
puratrayaṃ praviśyaiva babhūvuste balādhikāḥ  LiP 
kalpadrumasamākīrṇaṃ gajavājisamākulam 
nānāprasādasaṃkīrṇaṃ maṇijālaiḥ samāvṛtam  LiP 
sūryamaṇḍalasaṃkāśair vimānairviśvatomukhaiḥ 
padmarāgamayaiḥ śubhraiḥ śobhitaṃ candrasaṃnibhaiḥ  LiP 
prāsādairgopurairdivyaiḥ kailāsaśikharopamaiḥ 
śobhitaṃ tripuraṃ teṣāṃ pṛthakpṛthaganuttamaiḥ  LiP 
divyastrībhiḥ susampūrṇaṃ gandharvaiḥ siddhacāraṇaiḥ 
rudrālayaiḥ pratigṛhaṃ sāgnihotrair dvijottamāḥ  LiP 
vāpīkūpataḍāgaiś ca dīrghikābhistu sarvataḥ 
mattamātaṅgayūthaiś ca turaṅgaiś ca suśobhanaiḥ  LiP 
rathaiś ca vividhākārair vicitrairviśvatomukhaiḥ 
sabhāprapādibhiś caiva krīḍāsthānaiḥ pṛthak pṛthak  LiP 
vedādhyayanaśālābhir vividhābhiḥ samantataḥ 
adhṛṣyaṃ manasāpyanyair mayasyaiva ca māyayā  LiP 
piety of Tripura's inhabitants
pativratābhiḥ sarvatra sevitaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ 
kṛtvāpi sumahat pāpam apāpaiḥ śaṅkarārcanāt  LiP 
daityeśvarairmahābhāgaiḥ sadāraiḥ sasutairdvijāḥ 
śrautasmārtārthadharmajñais taddharmanirataiḥ sadā  LiP 
mahādevetaraṃ tyaktvā devaṃ tasyārcane sthitaiḥ 
vyūḍhoraskair vṛṣaskandhaiḥ sarvāyudhadharaiḥ sadā  LiP 
sarvadā kṣudhitaiścaiva dāvāgnisadṛśekṣaṇaiḥ 
praśāntaiḥ kupitaiścaiva kubjair vāmanakais tathā  LiP 
nīlotpaladalaprakhyair nīlakuñcitamūrdhajaiḥ 
nīlādrimerusaṃkāśair nīradopamaniḥsvanaiḥ 
mayena rakṣitaiḥ sarvaiḥ śikṣitairyuddhalālasaiḥ  LiP 
atha samararataiḥ sadā samantāc chivapadapūjanayā sulabdhavīryaiḥ 
ravimarudamarendrasaṃnikāśaiḥ suramathanaiḥ sudṛḍhaiḥ susevitaṃ tat  LiP 
sendrā devā dvijaśreṣṭhā drumā dāvāgninā yathā 
puratrayāgninā dagdhā hy abhavan daityavaibhavāt  LiP 
athaivaṃ te tadā dagdhā devā deveśvaraṃ harim 
abhivandya tadā prāhus tamapratimavarcasam  LiP 
so 'pi nārāyaṇaḥ śrīmān cintayāmāsa cetasā 
kiṃ kāryaṃ devakāryeṣu bhagavāniti sa prabhuḥ  LiP 
tadā sasmāra vai yajñaṃ yajñamūrtirjanārdanaḥ 
yajvā yajñabhugīśāno yajvanāṃ phaladaḥ prabhuḥ  LiP 
tato yajñaḥ smṛtastena devakāryārthasiddhaye 
devaṃ te puruṣaṃ caiva praṇemustuṣṭuvustadā  LiP 
bhagavānapi taṃ dṛṣṭvā yajñaṃ prāha sanātanam 
sanātanastadā sendrān devān ālokya cācyutaḥ  LiP 
śrīviṣṇuruvāca
anenopasadā devā yajadhvaṃ parameśvaram 
puratrayavināśāya jagattrayavibhūtaye  LiP 
sūta uvāca
atha tasya vacaḥ śrutvā devadevasya dhīmataḥ 
siṃhanādaṃ mahatkṛtvā yajñeśaṃ tuṣṭuvuḥ surāḥ  LiP

sūta uvāca

Śivas chariot for destruction of Tripura
atha rudrasya devasya nirmito viśvakarmaṇā 
sarvalokamayo divyo ratho yatnena sādaram  LiP 
sarvabhūtamayaścaiva sarvadevanamaskṛtaḥ 
sarvadevamayaścaiva sauvarṇaḥ sarvasaṃmataḥ  LiP 
rathāṅgaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ sūryo vāmāṅgaṃ soma eva ca 
dakṣiṇaṃ dvādaśāraṃ hi ṣoḍaśāraṃ tathottaram  LiP 
areṣu teṣu viprendrāś cādityā dvādaśaiva tu 
śaśinaḥ ṣoḍaśāreṣu kalā vāmasya suvratāḥ  LiP 
ṛkṣāṇi ca tadā tasya vāmasyaiva tu bhūṣaṇam 
nemyaḥ ṣaḍṛtavaścaiva tayorvai viprapuṅgavāḥ  LiP 
puṣkaraṃ cāntarikṣaṃ vai rathanīḍaś ca mandaraḥ 
astādrirudayādriś ca ubhau tau kūbarau smṛtau  LiP 
adhiṣṭhānaṃ mahāmerur āśrayāḥ kesarācalāḥ 
vegaḥ saṃvatsarastasya ayane cakrasaṃgamau  LiP 
muhūrtā bandhurāstasya śamyāścaiva kalāḥ smṛtāḥ 
tasya kāṣṭhāḥ smṛtā ghoṇā cākṣadaṇḍāḥ kṣaṇāś ca vai  LiP 
nimeṣāścānukarṣāś ca īṣā cāsya lavāḥ smṛtāḥ

tatpuruṣāya namo 'stu īśānāya namonamaḥ  LiP

anantāsanasaṃsthāya anantāyāntakāriṇe 
vimalāya viśālāya vimalāṅgāya te namaḥ  LiP 
vimalāsanasaṃsthāya vimalārthārtharūpiṇe 
yogapīṭhāntarasthāya yogine yogadāyine  LiP 
yogināṃ hṛdi saṃsthāya sadā nīvāraśūkavat

pratyāhāraratānāṃ ca pratisthānasthitāya ca

dhyānāya dhyānarūpāya dhyānagamyāya te namaḥ  LiP 
dhyeyāya dhyeyagamyāya dhyeyadhyānāya te namaḥ 
dhyeyānāmapi dhyeyāya namo dhyeyatamāya te  LiP 
samādhānābhigamyāya samādhānāya te namaḥ 
samādhānaratānāṃ tu nirvikalpārtharūpiṇe  LiP

nāsti vijñānināṃ śaucaṃ prāyaścittādi codanā 
viśuddhā vidyayā sarve brahmavidyāvido janāḥ  LiP 
nāsti kriyā ca lokeṣu sukhaṃ duḥkhaṃ vicārataḥ 
dharmādharmau japo homo dhyānināṃ saṃnidhiḥ sadā  LiP 
parānandātmakaṃ liṅgaṃ viśuddhaṃ śivamakṣaram 
niṣkalaṃ sarvagaṃ jñeyaṃ yogināṃ hṛdi saṃsthitam  LiP 
liṅgaṃ tu dvividhaṃ prāhur bāhyamābhyantaraṃ dvijāḥ 
bāhyaṃ sthūlaṃ muniśreṣṭhāḥ sūkṣmamābhyantaraṃ dvijāḥ  LiP 
karmayajñaratāḥ sthūlāḥ sthūlaliṅgārcane ratāḥ 
asatāṃ bhāvanārthāya nānyathā sthūlavigrahaḥ  LiP 
ādhyātmikaṃ ca yalliṅgaṃ pratyakṣaṃ yasya no bhavet 
asau mūḍho bahiḥ sarvaṃ kalpayitvaiva nānyathā  LiP 
jñānināṃ sūkṣmamamalaṃ bhavetpratyakṣamavyayam 
yathā sthūlamayuktānāṃ mṛtkāṣṭhādyaiḥ prakalpitam  LiP 
artho vicārato nāstīty anye tattvārthavedinaḥ 
niṣkalaḥ sakalaśceti sarvaṃ śivamayaṃ tataḥ  LiP 
vyomaikamapi dṛṣṭaṃ hi śarāvaṃ prati suvratāḥ 
pṛthaktvaṃ cāpṛthaktvaṃ ca śaṅkarasyeti cāpare  LiP 
pratyayārthaṃ hi jagatām ekastho 'pi divākaraḥ 
eko 'pi bahudhā dṛṣṭo jalādhāreṣu suvratāḥ  LiP 
jantavo divi bhūmau ca sarve vai pāñcabhautikāḥ 
tathāpi bahulā dṛṣṭā jātivyaktivibhedataḥ  LiP 
dṛśyate śrūyate yadyat tattadviddhi śivātmakam 
bhedo janānāṃ loke 'smin pratibhāso vicārataḥ  LiP 
svapne ca vipulān bhogān bhuktvā martyaḥ sukhī bhavet 
duḥkhī ca bhogaṃ duḥkhaṃ ca nānubhūtaṃ vicārataḥ  LiP 
evamāhustathānye ca sarve vedārthatattvagāḥ 
hṛdi saṃsāriṇāṃ sākṣāt sakalaḥ parameśvaraḥ  LiP 
yogināṃ niṣkalo devo jñānināṃ ca jaganmayaḥ 
trividhaṃ parameśasya vapurloke praśasyate  LiP 
niṣkalaṃ prathamaṃ caikaṃ tataḥ sakalaniṣkalam 
tṛtīyaṃ sakalaṃ caiva nānyatheti dvijottamāḥ  LiP 
arcayanti muhuḥ kecit sadā sakalaniṣkalam 
sarvajñaṃ hṛdaye kecic chivaliṅge vibhāvasau  LiP 
sakalaṃ munayaḥ kecit sadā saṃsāravartinaḥ 
evamabhyarcayantyeva sadārāḥ sasutā narāḥ  LiP 
yathā śivas tathā devī yathā devī tathā śivaḥ 
tasmādabhedabuddhyaiva saptaviṃśatprabhedataḥ  LiP 
yajanti dehe bāhye ca catuṣkoṇe ṣaḍasrake 
daśāre dvādaśāre ca ṣoḍaśāre trirasrake  LiP 
sa svecchayā śivaḥ sākṣād devyā sārdhaṃ sthitaḥ prabhuḥ 
saṃtāraṇārthaṃ ca śivaḥ sadasadvyaktivarjitaḥ  LiP 
tamekamāhurdviguṇaṃ ca kecit kecittamāhustriguṇātmakaṃ ca 
ūcus tathā taṃ ca śivaṃ tathānye saṃsāriṇaṃ vedavido vadanti  LiP 
bhaktyā ca yogena śubhena yuktā viprāḥ sadā dharmaratā viśiṣṭāḥ 
yajanti yogeśam aśeṣamūrtiṃ ṣaḍasramadhye bhagavantameva  LiP 
ye tatra paśyanti śivaṃ trirasre tritattvamadhye triguṇaṃ triyakṣam 
te yānti cainaṃ na ca yogino 'nye tayā ca devyā puruṣaṃ purāṇam  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge śivādvaitakathanaṃ nāma pañcasaptatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
LiP  
sūta uvāca
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi svecchāvigrahasaṃbhavam 
pratiṣṭhāyāḥ phalaṃ sarvaṃ sarvalokahitāya vai  LiP 
skandomāsahitaṃ devam āsīnaṃ paramāsane 
kṛtvā bhaktyā pratiṣṭhāpya sarvānkāmānavāpnuyāt  LiP 
skandomāsahitaṃ devaṃ sampūjya vidhinā sakṛt 
yatphalaṃ labhate martyas tadvadāmi yathāśrutam  LiP 
sūryakoṭipratikāśair vimānaiḥ sārvakāmikaiḥ 
rudrakanyāsamākīrṇair geyanāṭyasamanvitaiḥ  LiP 
śivavatkrīḍate yogī yāvadābhūtasaṃplavam 
tatra bhuktvā mahābhogān vimānaiḥ sārvakāmikaiḥ  LiP 
aumaṃ kaumāramaiśānaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ brāhmameva ca 
prājāpatyaṃ mahātejā janalokaṃ mahas tathā  LiP 
aindram āsādya caindratvaṃ kṛtvā varṣāyutaṃ punaḥ 
bhuktvā caiva bhuvarloke bhogān divyān suśobhanān  LiP 
merumāsādya devānāṃ bhavaneṣu pramodate 
ekapādaṃ caturbāhuṃ trinetraṃ śūlasaṃyutam  LiP 
sṛṣṭvā sthitaṃ hariṃ vāme dakṣiṇe caturānanam 
aṣṭāviṃśatirudrāṇāṃ koṭiḥ sarvāṅgasuprabham  LiP 
pañcaviṃśatikaṃ sākṣāt puruṣaṃ hṛdayāttathā 
prakṛtiṃ vāmataścaiva buddhiṃ vai buddhideśataḥ  LiP 
ahaṅkāramahaṅkārāt tanmātrāṇi tu tatra vai 
indriyāṇīndriyādeva līlayā parameśvaram  LiP 
pṛthivīṃ pādamūlāttu guhyadeśājjalaṃ tathā 
nābhideśāt tathā vahniṃ hṛdayādbhāskaraṃ tathā  LiP 
kaṇṭhātsomaṃ tathātmānaṃ bhrūmadhyānmastakāddivam 
sṛṣṭaivaṃ saṃsthitaṃ sākṣāj jagatsarvaṃ carācaram  LiP 
sarvajñaṃ sarvagaṃ devaṃ kṛtvā vidyāvidhānataḥ 
pratiṣṭhāpya yathānyāyaṃ śivasāyujyamāpnuyāt  LiP 
tripādaṃ saptahastaṃ ca catuḥśṛṅgaṃ dviśīrṣakam 
kṛtvā yajñeśamīśānaṃ viṣṇuloke mahīyate  LiP 
tatra bhuktvā mahābhogān kalpalakṣaṃ sukhī naraḥ 
kramādāgatya loke 'smin sarvayajñāntago bhavet  LiP 
vṛṣārūḍhaṃ tu yaḥ kuryāt somaṃ somārdhabhūṣaṇam 
hayamedhāyutaṃ kṛtvā yatpuṇyaṃ tad avāpya saḥ  LiP 
kāñcanena vimānena kiṅkiṇījālamālinā 
gatvā śivapuraṃ divyaṃ tatraiva sa vimucyate  LiP 
nandinā sahitaṃ devaṃ sāmbaṃ sarvagaṇairvṛtam 
kṛtvā yatphalamāpnoti vakṣye tadvai yathāśrutam  LiP 
sūryamaṇḍalasaṃkāśair vimānair vṛṣasaṃyutaiḥ 
apsarogaṇasaṃkīrṇair devadānavadurlabhaiḥ  LiP 
nṛtyadbhir apsaraḥsaṃghaiḥ sarvataḥ sarvaśobhitaiḥ 
gatvā śivapuraṃ divyaṃ gāṇapatyamavāpnuyāt  LiP 
nṛtyantaṃ devadeveśaṃ śailajāsahitaṃ prabhum 
sahasrabāhuṃ sarvajñaṃ caturbāhum athāpi vā  LiP 
bhṛgvādyairbhūtasaṃghaiś ca saṃvṛtaṃ parameśvaram 
śailajāsahitaṃ sākṣād vṛṣabhadhvajamīśvaram  LiP 
brahmendraviṣṇusomādyaiḥ sadā sarvairnamaskṛtam 
mātṛbhir munibhiścaiva saṃvṛtaṃ parameśvaram  LiP 
kṛtvā bhaktyā pratiṣṭhāpya yatphalaṃ tadvadāmyaham 
sarvayajñatapodāna tīrthadeveṣu yat phalam  LiP 
tatphalaṃ koṭiguṇitaṃ labdhvā yāti śivaṃ padam 
tatra bhuktvā mahābhogān yāvad ābhūtasaṃplavam  LiP 
sṛṣṭyantare punaḥ prāpte mānavaṃ padamāpnuyāt 
nagnaṃ caturbhujaṃ śvetaṃ trinetraṃ sarpamekhalam  LiP 
kapālahastaṃ deveśaṃ kṛṣṇakuñcitamūrdhajam 
kṛtvā bhaktyā pratiṣṭhāpya śivasāyujyamāpnuyāt  LiP 
ibhendradārakaṃ devaṃ sāṃbaṃ siddhārthadaṃ prabhum 
sudhūmravarṇaṃ raktākṣaṃ trinetraṃ candrabhūṣaṇam  LiP 
kākapakṣadharaṃ mūrdhnā nāgaṭaṅkadharaṃ haram 
siṃhājinottarīyaṃ ca mṛgacarmāṃbaraṃ prabhum  LiP 
tīkṣṇadaṃṣṭraṃ gadāhastaṃ kapālodyatapāṇinam 
huṃphaṭkāre mahāśabda śabditākhiladiṅmukham  LiP 
puṇḍarīkājinaṃ dorbhyāṃ bibhrantaṃ kambukaṃ tathā 
hasantaṃ ca nadantaṃ ca pibantaṃ kṛṣṇasāgaram  LiP 
nṛtyantaṃ bhūtasaṃghaiś ca gaṇasaṃghais tvalaṃkṛtam 
kṛtvā bhaktyā pratiṣṭhāpya yathāvibhavavistaram  LiP 
sarvavighnān atikramya śivaloke mahīyate 
tatra bhuktvā mahābhogān yāvadābhūtasaṃplavam  LiP 
jñānaṃ vicārato labdhvā rudrebhyastatra mucyate 
ardhanārīśvaraṃ devaṃ caturbhujamanuttamam  LiP 
varadābhayahastaṃ ca śūlapadmadharaṃ prabhum 
strīpuṃbhāvena saṃsthānaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam  LiP 
kṛtvā bhaktyā pratiṣṭhāpya śivaloke mahīyate 
tatra bhuktvā mahābhogān aṇimādiguṇairyutaḥ  LiP 
ācandratārakaṃ jñānaṃ tato labdhvā vimucyate 
yaḥ kuryāddevadeveśaṃ sarvajñaṃ lakulīśvaram  LiP 
vṛtaṃ śiṣyapraśiṣyaiś ca vyākhyānodyatapāṇinam 
kṛtvā bhaktyā pratiṣṭhāpya śivalokaṃ sa gacchati  LiP 
bhuktvā tu vipulāṃstatra bhogān yugaśataṃ naraḥ 
jñānayogaṃ samāsādya tatraiva ca vimucyate  LiP 
pūrvadevāmarāṇāṃ ca yatsthānaṃ sakalepsitam 
kṛtamudrasya devasya citābhasmānulepinaḥ  LiP 
tripuṇḍradhāriṇasteṣāṃ śiromālādharasya ca 
brahmaṇaḥ keśakenaikam upavītaṃ ca bibhrataḥ  LiP 
bibhrato vāmahastena kapālaṃ brahmaṇo varam 
viṣṇoḥ kalevaraṃ caiva bibhrataḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ  LiP 
kṛtvā bhaktyā pratiṣṭhāpya mucyate bhavasāgarāt 
oṃnamo nīlakaṇṭhāya iti puṇyākṣarāṣṭakam  LiP 
mantramāha sakṛdvā yaḥ pātakaiḥ sa vimucyate 
mantreṇānena gandhādyair bhaktyā vittānusārataḥ  LiP 
sampūjya devadeveśaṃ śivaloke mahīyate 
jālandharāntakaṃ devaṃ sudarśanadharaṃ prabhum  LiP 
kṛtvā bhaktyā pratiṣṭhāpya dvidhābhūtaṃ jalaṃdharam 
prayāti śivasāyujyaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā  LiP 
sudarśanapradaṃ devaṃ sākṣātpūrvoktalakṣaṇam 
arcamānena devena cārcitaṃ netrapūjayā  LiP 
kṛtvā bhaktyā pratiṣṭhāpya śivaloke mahīyate 
tiṣṭhato 'tha nikumbhasya pṛṣṭhataścaraṇāṃbujam  LiP 
vāmetaraṃ suvinyasya vāme cāliṅgya cādrijām 
śūlāgre kūrparaṃ sthāpya kiṅkiṇīkṛtapannagam  LiP 
samprekṣya cāndhakaṃ pārśve kṛtāñjalipuṭaṃ sthitam 
rūpaṃ kṛtvā yathānyāyaṃ śivasāyujyamāpnuyāt  LiP 
yaḥ kuryāddevadeveśaṃ tripurāntakamīśvaram 
dhanurbāṇasamāyuktaṃ somaṃ somārdhabhūṣaṇam  LiP 
rathe susaṃsthitaṃ devaṃ caturānanasārathim 
tadākāratayā so 'pi gatvā śivapuraṃ sukhī  LiP 
krīḍate nātra saṃdeho dvitīya iva śaṅkaraḥ 
tatra bhuktvā mahābhogān yāvad icchā dvijottamāḥ  LiP 
jñānaṃ vicāritaṃ labdhvā tatraiva sa vimucyate  LiP 
gaṅgādharaṃ sukhāsīnaṃ candraśekharameva ca  LiP 
gaṅgayā sahitaṃ caiva vāmotsaṅge 'ṃbikānvitam 
vināyakaṃ tathā skandaṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ durgāṃ suśobhanām  LiP 
bhāskaraṃ ca tathā somaṃ brahmāṇīṃ ca maheśvarīm 
kaumārīṃ vaiṣṇavīṃ devīṃ vārāhīṃ varadāṃ tathā  LiP 
indrāṇīṃ caiva cāmuṇḍāṃ vīrabhadrasamanvitām 
vighneśena ca yo dhīmān śivasāyujyamāpnuyāt  LiP 
liṅgamūrtiṃ mahājvālām ālāsaṃvṛtam avyayam 
liṅgasya madhye vai kṛtvā candraśekharamīśvaram  LiP 
vyomni kuryāt tathā liṅgaṃ brahmāṇaṃ haṃsarūpiṇam 
viṣṇuṃ varāharūpeṇa liṅgasyādhastvadhomukham  LiP 
brahmāṇaṃ dakṣiṇe tasya kṛtāñjalipuṭaṃ sthitam 
madhye liṅgaṃ mahāghoraṃ mahāmbhasi ca saṃsthitam  LiP 
kṛtvā bhaktyā pratiṣṭhāpya śivasāyujyamāpnuyāt 
kṣetrasaṃrakṣakaṃ devaṃ tathā pāśupataṃ prabhum  LiP 
kṛtvā bhaktyā yathānyāyaṃ śivaloke mahīyate  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge śivamūrtipratiṣṭhāphalakathanaṃ nāma ṣaṭsaptatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
LiP  
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
liṅgapratiṣṭhāpuṇyaṃ ca liṅgasthāpanameva ca 
liṅgānāṃ caiva bhedāś ca śrutaṃ tava mukhādiha  LiP 
mṛdādiratnaparyantair dravyaiḥ kṛtvā śivālayam 
yatphalaṃ labhate martyas tatphalaṃ vaktumarhasi  LiP 
sūta uvāca
yasya bhakto 'pi loke 'smin putradāragṛhādibhiḥ 
bādhyate jñānayuktaścen na ca tasya gṛhaistu kim  LiP 
tathāpi bhaktāḥ parameśvarasya kṛtveṣṭaloṣṭairapi rudralokam 
prayānti divyaṃ hi vimānavaryaṃ surendrapadmodbhavavanditasya  LiP 
bālyāttu loṣṭena ca kṛtvā mṛdāpi vā pāṃsubhir ādidevam 
gṛhaṃ ca tādṛgvidhamasya śaṃbhoḥ sampūjya rudratvamavāpnuvanti  LiP 
tasmātsarvaprayatnena bhaktyā bhaktaiḥ śivālayam 
kartavyaṃ sarvayatnena dharmakāmārthasiddhaye  LiP 
kesaraṃ nāgaraṃ vāpi drāviḍaṃ vā tathāparam 
kṛtvā rudrālayaṃ bhaktyā śivaloke mahīyate  LiP 
kailāsākhyaṃ ca yaḥ kuryāt prāsādaṃ parameṣṭhinaḥ 
kailāsaśikharākārair vimānair modate sukhī  LiP 
mandaraṃ vā prakurvīta śivāya vidhipūrvakam 
bhaktyā vittānusāreṇa uttamādhamamadhyamam  LiP 
mandarādripratīkāśair vimānairviśvatomukhaiḥ 
apsarogaṇasaṃkīrṇair devadānavadurlabhaiḥ  LiP 
gatvā śivapuraṃ ramyaṃ bhuktvā bhogān yathepsitān 
jñānayogaṃ samāsādya gāṇapatyaṃ labhennaraḥ  LiP 
yaḥ kuryānmerunāmānaṃ prāsādaṃ parameṣṭhinaḥ 
sa yatphalamavāpnoti na tat sarvair mahāmakhaiḥ  LiP 
sarvayajñatapodāna tīrthavedeṣu yatphalam 
tatphalaṃ sakalaṃ labdhvā śivavanmodate ciram  LiP 
niṣadhaṃ nāma yaḥ kuryāt prāsādaṃ bhaktitaḥ sudhīḥ 
śivalokamanuprāpya śivavanmodate ciram  LiP 
kuryādvā yaḥ śubhaṃ viprā himaśailamanuttamam 
himaśailopamair yānair gatvā śivapuraṃ śubham  LiP 
jñānayogaṃ samāsādya gāṇapatyamavāpnuyāt 
nīlādriśikharākhyaṃ vā prāsādaṃ yaḥ suśobhanam  LiP 
kṛtvā vittānusāreṇa bhaktyā rudrāya śaṃbhave 
yatphalaṃ labhate martyas tatphalaṃ pravadāmyaham  LiP 
himaśaile kṛte bhaktyā yatphalaṃ prāk tavoditam 
tatphalaṃ sakalaṃ labdhvā sarvadevanamaskṛtaḥ  LiP 
rudralokamanuprāpya rudraiḥ sārdhaṃ pramodate 
mahendraśailanāmānaṃ prāsādaṃ rudrasaṃmatam  LiP 
kṛtvā yatphalamāpnoti tatphalaṃ pravadāmyaham 
mahendraparvatākārair vimānairvṛṣasaṃyutaiḥ  LiP 
gatvā śivapuraṃ divyaṃ bhuktvā bhogānyathepsitān 
jñānaṃ vicāritaṃ rudraiḥ samprāpya munipuṅgavāḥ  LiP 
viṣayān viṣavat tyaktvā śivasāyujyamāpnuyāt 
hemnā yastu prakurvīta prāsādaṃ ratnaśobhitam  LiP 
drāviḍaṃ nāgaraṃ vāpi kesaraṃ vā vidhānataḥ 
kūṭaṃ vā maṇḍapaṃ vāpi samaṃ vā dīrgham eva ca  LiP 
na tasya śakyate vaktuṃ puṇyaṃ śatayugairapi 
jīrṇaṃ vā patitaṃ vāpi khaṇḍitaṃ sphuṭitaṃ tathā  LiP 
pūrvavatkārayedyastu dvārādyaiḥ suśubhaṃ dvijāḥ 
prāsādaṃ maṇḍapaṃ vāpi prākāraṃ gopuraṃ tu vā  LiP 
karturapyadhikaṃ puṇyaṃ labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ 
vṛttyarthaṃ vā prakurvīta naraḥ karma śivālaye  LiP 
yaḥ sa yāti na saṃdehaḥ svargalokaṃ sabāndhavaḥ 
yaścātmabhogasiddhyartham api rudrālaye sakṛt  LiP 
karma kuryādyadi sukhaṃ labdhvā cāpi pramodate 
tasmād āyatanaṃ bhaktyā yaḥ kuryān munisattamāḥ  LiP 
kāṣṭheṣṭakādibhir martyaḥ śivaloke mahīyate 
prasādārthaṃ maheśasya prāsāde munipuṅgavāḥ  LiP 
kartavyaḥ sarvayatnena dharmakāmārthamuktaye 
aśaktaścenmuniśreṣṭhāḥ prāsādaṃ kartumuttamam  LiP 
saṃmārjanādibhir vāpi sarvānkāmānavāpnuyāt 
saṃmārjanaṃ tu yaḥ kuryān mārjanyā mṛdusūkṣmayā  LiP 
cāndrāyaṇasahasrasya phalaṃ māsena labhyate 
yaḥ kuryādvastrapūtena gandhagomayavāriṇā  LiP 
ālepanaṃ yathānyāyaṃ varṣacāndrāyaṇaṃ labhet 
ardhakrośaṃ śivakṣetraṃ śivaliṅgātsamantataḥ  LiP 
yas tyajed dustyajān prāṇāñ śivasāyujyam āpnuyāt 
svāyaṃbhuvasya mānaṃ hi tathā bāṇasya suvratāḥ  LiP 
svāyaṃbhuve tadardhaṃ syāt syād ārṣe ca tadardhakam 
mānuṣe ca tadardhaṃ syāt kṣetramānaṃ dvijottamāḥ  LiP 
evaṃ yatīnāmāvāse kṣetramānaṃ dvijottamāḥ 
rudrāvatāre cādyaṃ yac chiṣye caiva praśiṣyake  LiP 
narāvatāre tacchiṣye tacchiṣye ca praśiṣyake 
śrīparvate mahāpuṇye tasya prānte ca vā dvijāḥ  LiP 
tasminvā yastyajetprāṇāñ chivasāyujyamāpnuyāt 
vārāṇasyāṃ tathāpyevam avimukte viśeṣataḥ  LiP 
kedāre ca mahākṣetre prayāge ca viśeṣataḥ 
kurukṣetre ca yaḥ prāṇān saṃtyajedyāti nirvṛtim  LiP 
prabhāse puṣkare 'vantyāṃ tathā caivāmareśvare 
vaṇīśailākule caiva mṛto yāti śivātmatām  LiP 
vārāṇasyāṃ mṛto jantur na jātu jantutāṃ vrajet 
triviṣṭape vimukte ca kedāre saṃgameśvare  LiP 
śālaṅke vā tyajetprāṇāṃs tathā vai jambukeśvare 
śukreśvare vā gokarṇe bhāskareśe guheśvare  LiP 
hiraṇyagarbhe nandīśe sa yāti paramāṃ gatim 
niyamaiḥ śoṣya yo dehaṃ tyajetkṣetre śivasya tu  LiP 
sa yāti śivatāṃ yogī mānuṣe daivike 'pi vā 
ārṣe vāpi muniśreṣṭhās tathā svāyaṃbhuve 'pi vā  LiP 
svayaṃbhūte tathā deve nātra kāryā vicāraṇā 
ādhāyāgniṃ śivakṣetre sampūjya parameśvaram  LiP 
svadehapiṇḍaṃ juhuyād yaḥ sa yāti parāṃ gatim 
yāvattāvannirāhāro bhūtvā prāṇān parityajet  LiP 
śivakṣetre muniśreṣṭhāḥ śivasāyujyamāpnuyāt 
chittvā pādadvayaṃ cāpi śivakṣetre vasettu yaḥ  LiP 
sa yāti śivatāṃ caiva nātra kāryā vicāraṇā 
kṣetrasya darśanaṃ puṇyaṃ praveśastacchatādhikaḥ  LiP 
tasmācchataguṇaṃ puṇyaṃ sparśanaṃ ca pradakṣiṇam 
tasmācchataguṇaṃ puṇyaṃ jalasnānamataḥ param  LiP 
kṣīrasnānaṃ tato viprāḥ śatādhikamanuttamam 
dadhnā sahasramākhyātaṃ madhunā tacchatādhikam  LiP 
ghṛtasnānena cānantaṃ śārkare tacchatādhikam 
śivakṣetrasamīpasthāṃ nadīṃ prāpyāvagāhya ca  LiP 
tyajeddehaṃ vihāyānnaṃ śivaloke mahīyate 
śivakṣetrasamīpasthā nadyaḥ sarvāḥ suśobhanāḥ  LiP 
vāpīkūpataḍāgāś ca śivatīrthā iti smṛtāḥ 
snātvā teṣu naro bhaktyā tīrtheṣu dvijasattamāḥ  LiP 
brahmahatyādibhiḥ pāpair mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ 
prātaḥ snātvā muniśreṣṭhāḥ śivatīrtheṣu mānavaḥ  LiP 
aśvamedhaphalaṃ prāpya rudralokaṃ sa gacchati 
madhyāhne śivatīrtheṣu snātvā bhaktyā sakṛnnaraḥ  LiP 
gaṅgāsnānasamaṃ puṇyaṃ labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ 
astaṃ gate tathā cārke snātvā gacchecchivaṃ padam  LiP 
pāpakañcukamutsṛjya śivatīrtheṣu mānavaḥ 
dvijās triṣavaṇaṃ snātvā śivatīrthe sakṛnnaraḥ  LiP 
śivasāyujyamāpnoti nātra kāryā vicāraṇā 
purātha sūkaraḥ kaścit śvānaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhayātpathi  LiP 
prasaṃgādvāramekaṃ tu śivatīrthe 'vagāhya ca 
mṛtaḥ svayaṃ dvijaśreṣṭhā gāṇapatyamavāptavān  LiP 
yaḥ prātardevadeveśaṃ śivaṃ liṅgasvarūpiṇam 
paśyetsa yāti sarvasmād adhikāṃ gatimeva ca  LiP 
madhyāhne ca mahādevaṃ dṛṣṭvā yajñaphalaṃ labhet 
sāyāhne sarvayajñānāṃ phalaṃ prāpya vimucyate  LiP 
mānasairvācikaiḥ pāpaiḥ kāyikaiś ca mahattaraiḥ 
tathopapātakaiścaiva pāpaiścaivānupātakaiḥ  LiP 
saṃkrame devamīśānaṃ dṛṣṭvā liṅgākṛtiṃ prabhum 
māsena yatkṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tyaktvā yāti śivaṃ padam  LiP 
ayane cārdhamāsena dakṣiṇe cottarāyaṇe 
viṣuve caiva sampūjya prayāti paramāṃ gatim  LiP 
pradakṣiṇatrayaṃ kuryād yaḥ prāsādaṃ samantataḥ 
savyāpasavyanyāyena mṛdugatyā śucirnaraḥ  LiP 
pade pade 'śvamedhasya yajñasya phalamāpnuyāt 
vācā yastu śivaṃ nityaṃ saṃrauti parameśvaram  LiP 
so 'pi yāti śivaṃ sthānaṃ prāpya kiṃ punareva ca 
kṛtvā maṇḍalakaṃ kṣetraṃ gandhagomayavāriṇā  LiP 
muktāphalamayaiścūrṇair indranīlamayais tathā 
padmarāgamayaiścaiva sphāṭikaiś ca suśobhanaiḥ  LiP 
tathā mārakataiścaiva sauvarṇai rājatais tathā 
tadvarṇair laukikaiścaiva cūrṇairvittavivarjitaiḥ  LiP 
ālikhya kamalaṃ bhadraṃ daśahastapramāṇataḥ 
sakarṇikaṃ mahābhāgā mahādevasamīpataḥ  LiP 
tatrāvāhya mahādevaṃ navaśaktisamanvitam 
pañcabhiśca tathā ṣaḍbhir aṣṭābhiśceṣṭadaṃ param  LiP 
punaraṣṭābhir īśānaṃ daśāre daśabhis tathā 
punarbāhye ca daśabhiḥ sampūjya praṇipatya ca  LiP 
nivedya devadevāya kṣitidānaphalaṃ labhet 
śālipiṣṭādibhir vāpi padmamālikhya nirdhanaḥ  LiP 
pūrvoktamakhilaṃ puṇyaṃ labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ 
dvādaśāraṃ tathālikhya maṇḍalaṃ padam uttamam  LiP 
ratnacūrṇādibhiścūrṇais tathā dvādaśamūrtibhiḥ 
maṇḍalasya ca madhye tu bhāskaraṃ sthāpya pūjayet  LiP 
grahaiś ca saṃvṛtaṃ vāpi sūryasāyujyamuttamam 
evaṃ prākṛtam apyārthyāṃ ṣaḍasraṃ parikalpya ca  LiP 
madhyadeśe ca deveśīṃ prakṛtiṃ brahmarūpiṇīm 
dakṣiṇe sattvamūrtiṃ ca vāmataś ca rajoguṇam  LiP 
agratastu tamomūrtiṃ madhye devīṃ tathāṃbikām 
pañcabhūtāni tanmātrā pañcakaṃ caiva dakṣiṇe  LiP 
karmendriyāṇi pañcaiva tathā buddhīndriyāṇi ca 
uttare vidhivatpūjya ṣaḍasre caiva pūjayet  LiP 
ātmānaṃ cāntarātmānaṃ yugalaṃ buddhimeva ca 
ahaṅkāraṃ ca mahatā sarvayajñaphalaṃ labhet  LiP 
evaṃ vaḥ kathitaṃ sarvaṃ prākṛtaṃ maṇḍalaṃ param 
ato vakṣyāmi viprendrāḥ sarvakāmārthasādhanam  LiP 
gocarmamātramālikhya maṇḍalaṃ gomayena tu 
caturaśraṃ vidhānena cādbhir abhyukṣya mantravit  LiP 
alaṃkṛtya vitānādyaiś chatrair vāpi manoramaiḥ 
budbudairardhacandraiś ca haimairaśvatthapatrakaiḥ  LiP 
sitairvikasitaiḥ padmai raktair nīlotpalais tathā 
muktādāmair vitānānte lambitastu sitairdhvajaiḥ  LiP 
sitamṛtpātrakaiścaiva suślakṣṇaiḥ pūrṇakumbhakaiḥ 
phalapallavamālābhir vaijayantībhir aṃśukaiḥ  LiP 
pañcāśaddīpamālābhir dhūpaiḥ pañcavidhais tathā 
pañcāśaddalasaṃyuktam ālikhetpadmamuttamam  LiP 
tattadvarṇais tathā cūrṇaiḥ śvetacūrṇairathāpi vā 
ekahastapramāṇena kṛtvā padmaṃ vidhānataḥ  LiP 
karṇikāyāṃ nyased devaṃ devyā deveśvaraṃ bhavam 
varṇāni ca nyasetpatre rudraiḥ prāgādyanukramāt  LiP 
praṇavādinamo 'ntāni sarvavarṇāni suvratāḥ 
sampūjyaivaṃ muniśreṣṭhā gandhapuṣpādibhiḥ kramāt  LiP 
brāhmaṇān bhojayettatra pañcāśadvidhipūrvakam 
akṣamālopavītaṃ ca kuṇḍalaṃ ca kamaṇḍalum  LiP 
āsanaṃ ca tathā daṇḍam uṣṇīṣaṃ vastrameva ca 
dattvā teṣāṃ munīndrāṇāṃ devadevāya śaṃbhave  LiP 
mahācaruṃ nivedyaivaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ gomithunaṃ tathā 
ante ca devadevāya dāpayeccūrṇamaṇḍalam  LiP 
yāgopayogadravyāṇi śivāya vinivedayet 
oṅkārādyaṃ japeddhīmān prativarṇam anukramāt  LiP 
evamālikhya yo bhaktyā sarvamaṇḍalamuttamam 
yatphalaṃ labhate martyas tadvadāmi samāsataḥ  LiP 
sāṅgān vedān yathānyāyam adhītya vidhipūrvakam 
iṣṭvā yajñairyathānyāyaṃ jyotiṣṭomādibhiḥ kramāt  LiP 
tato viśvajidantaiś ca putrānutpādya tādṛśān 
vānaprasthāśramaṃ gatvā sadāraḥ sāgnireva ca  LiP 
cāndrāyaṇādikāḥ sarvāḥ kṛtvā nyasya kriyā dvijāḥ 
brahmavidyāmadhītyaiva jñānamāsādya yatnataḥ  LiP 
jñānena jñeyam ālokya yogī yatkāmamāpnuyāt 
tatphalaṃ labhate sarvaṃ varṇamaṇḍaladarśanāt  LiP 
yena kenāpi vā martyaḥ pralipyāyatanāgrataḥ 
uttare dakṣiṇe vāpi pṛṣṭhato vā dvijottamāḥ  LiP 
catuṣkoṇaṃ tu vā cūrṇair alaṃkṛtya samantataḥ 
puṣpākṣatādibhiḥ pūjya sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate  LiP 
yastu garbhagṛhaṃ bhaktyā sakṛdālipya sarvataḥ 
candanādyaiḥ sakarpūrair gandhadravyaiḥ samantataḥ  LiP 
vikīrya gandhakusumair dhūpairdhūpya caturvidhaiḥ 
prārthayeddevamīśānaṃ śivalokaṃ sa gacchati  LiP 
tatra bhuktvā mahābhogān kalpakoṭiśataṃ naraḥ 
svadehagandhakusumaiḥ pūrayañchivamandiram  LiP 
kramādgāndharvamāsādya gandharvaiś ca supūjitaḥ 
kramādāgatya loke 'smin rājā bhavati vīryavān  LiP 
ādidevo mahādevaḥ pralayasthitikārakaḥ 
sargaś ca bhuvanādhīśaḥ śarvavyāpī sadāśivaḥ 
śivabrahmāmṛtaṃ grāhyaṃ mokṣasādhanam uttamam  LiP 
vyaktāvyaktaṃ sadā nityam acintyam arcayet prabhum  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge upalepanādikathanaṃ nāma saptasaptatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
LiP  
sūta uvāca
vastrapūtena toyena kāryaṃ caivopalepanam 
śivakṣetre muniśreṣṭhā nānyathā siddhiriṣyate  LiP 
āpaḥ pūtā bhavantyetā vastrapūtāḥ samuddhṛtāḥ 
aphenā muniśārdūlā nādeyāś ca viśeṣataḥ  LiP 
tasmādvai sarvakāryāṇi daivikāni dvijottamāḥ 
adbhiḥ kāryāṇi pūtābhiḥ sarvakāryaprasiddhaye  LiP 
jantubhir miśritā hyāpaḥ sūkṣmābhistānnihatya tu 
yatpāpaṃ sakalaṃ cādbhir apūtābhiściraṃ labhet  LiP 
saṃmārjane tathā nṝṇāṃ mārjane ca viśeṣataḥ 
agnau kaṇḍanake caiva peṣaṇe toyasaṃgrahe  LiP 
hiṃsā sadā gṛhasthānāṃ tasmāddhiṃsāṃ vivarjayet 
ahiṃseyaṃ paro dharmaḥ sarveṣāṃ prāṇināṃ dvijāḥ  LiP 
tasmātsarvaprayatnena vastrapūtaṃ samācaret 
taddānamabhayaṃ puṇyaṃ sarvadānottamottamam  LiP 
tasmāttu parihartavyā hiṃsā sarvatra sarvadā 
manasā karmaṇā vācā sarvadāhiṃsakaṃ naram  LiP 
rakṣanti jantavaḥ sarve hiṃsakaṃ bādhayanti ca 
trailokyamakhilaṃ dattvā yatphalaṃ vedapārage  LiP 
tatphalaṃ koṭiguṇitaṃ labhate 'hiṃsako naraḥ 
manasā karmaṇā vācā sarvabhūtahite ratāḥ  LiP 
dayādarśitapanthāno rudralokaṃ vrajanti ca 
svāmivatparirakṣanti bahūni vividhāni ca  LiP 
ye putrapautravatsnehād rudralokaṃ vrajanti te 
tasmātsarvaprayatnena vastrapūtena vāriṇā  LiP 
kāryamabhyukṣaṇaṃ nityaṃ snapanaṃ ca viśeṣataḥ 
trailokyamakhilaṃ hatvā yatphalaṃ parikīrtyate  LiP 
śivālaye nihatyaikam api tatsakalaṃ labhet 
śivārthaṃ sarvadā kāryā puṣpahiṃsā dvijottamāḥ  LiP 
yajñārthaṃ paśuhiṃsā ca kṣatriyairduṣṭaśāsanam 
vihitāvihitaṃ nāsti yogināṃ brahmavādinām  LiP 
yatastasmānna hantavyā niṣiddhānāṃ niṣevaṇāt 
sarvakarmāṇi vinyasya saṃnyastā brahmavādinaḥ  LiP 
na hantavyāḥ sadā pūjyāḥ pāpakarmaratā api 
pavitrāstu striyaḥ sarvā atreś ca kulasaṃbhavāḥ  LiP 
brahmahatyāsamaṃ pāpam ātreyīṃ vinihatya ca 
striyaḥ sarvā na hantavyāḥ pāpakarmaratā api  LiP 
na yajñārthaṃ striyo grāhyāḥ sarvaiḥ sarvatra sarvadā 
sarvavarṇeṣu viprendrāḥ pāpakarmaratā api  LiP 
malinā rūpavatyaś ca virūpā malināṃbarāḥ 
na hantavyāḥ sadā martyaiḥ śivavacchaṅkayā tathā  LiP 
vedabāhyavratācārāḥ śrautasmārtabahiṣkṛtāḥ 
pāṣaṇḍina iti khyātā na saṃbhāṣyā dvijātibhiḥ  LiP 
na spṛṣṭavyā na draṣṭavyā dṛṣṭvā bhānuṃ samīkṣate 
tathāpi tena vadhyāś ca nṛpairanyaiś ca jantubhiḥ  LiP 
prasaṃgādvāpi yo martyaḥ satāṃ sakṛdaho dvijāḥ 
rudralokamavāpnoti samabhyarcya maheśvaram  LiP 
bhavanti duḥkhitāḥ sarve nirdayā munisattamāḥ 
bhaktihīnā narāḥ sarve bhave paramakāraṇe  LiP 
ye bhaktā devadevasya śivasya parameṣṭhinaḥ 
bhāgyavanto vimucyante bhuktvā bhogānihaiva te  LiP 
putreṣu dāreṣu gṛheṣu nṝṇāṃ bhaktaṃ yathā cittamathādideve 
sakṛtprasaṃgādyatitāpasānāṃ teṣāṃ na dūraḥ parameśalokaḥ  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge bhaktimahimavarṇanaṃ nāmāṣṭasaptatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
LiP  
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
kathaṃ pūjyo mahādevo martyairmandairmahāmate 
kalpāyuṣair alpavīryair alpasattvaiḥ prajāpatiḥ  LiP 
saṃvatsarasahasraiś ca tapasā pūjya śaṅkaram 
na paśyanti surāścāpi kathaṃ devaṃ yajanti te  LiP 
sūta uvāca
kathitaṃ tathyam evātra yuṣmābhir munipuṅgavāḥ 
tathāpi śraddhayā dṛśyaḥ pūjyaḥ saṃbhāṣya eva ca  LiP 
prasaṃgāccaiva sampūjya bhaktihīnairapi dvijāḥ 
bhāvānurūpaphalado bhagavāniti kīrtitaḥ  LiP 
ucchiṣṭaḥ pūjayanyāti paiśācaṃ tu dvijādhamaḥ 
saṃkruddho rākṣasaṃ sthānaṃ prāpnuyān mūḍhadhīr dvijāḥ  LiP 
abhakṣyabhakṣī sampūjya yākṣaṃ prāpnoti durjanaḥ 
gānaśīlaś ca gāndharvaṃ nṛtyaśīlastathaiva ca  LiP 
khyātiśīlas tathā cāndraṃ strīṣu sakto narādhamaḥ 
madārtaḥ pūjayan rudraṃ somasthānamavāpnuyāt  LiP 
gāyatryā devamabhyarcya prājāpatyamavāpnuyāt 
brāhmaṃ hi praṇavenaiva vaiṣṇavaṃ cābhinandya ca  LiP 
śraddhayā sakṛdevāpi samabhyarcya maheśvaram 
rudralokamanuprāpya rudraiḥ sārdhaṃ pramodate  LiP 
saṃśodhya ca śubhaṃ liṅgam amarāsurapūjitam 
jalaiḥ pūtaistathā pīṭhe devamāvāhya bhaktitaḥ  LiP 
dṛṣṭvā devaṃ yathānyāyaṃ praṇipatya ca śaṅkaram 
kalpite cāsane sthāpya dharmajñānamaye śubhe  LiP 
vairāgyaiśvaryasampanne sarvalokanamaskṛte 
oṅkārapadmamadhye tu somasūryāgnisaṃbhave  LiP 
pādyamācamanaṃ cārghyaṃ dattvā rudrāya śaṃbhave 
snāpayeddivyatoyaiś ca ghṛtena payasā tathā  LiP 
dadhnā ca snāpayedrudraṃ śodhayecca yathāvidhi 
tataḥ śuddhāṃbunā snāpya candanādyaiś ca pūjayet  LiP 
rocanādyaiś ca sampūjya divyapuṣpaiś ca pūjayet 
bilvapatrairakhaṇḍaiś ca padmairnānāvidhais tathā  LiP 
nīlotpalaiś ca rājīvair nadyāvartaiś ca mallikaiḥ 
campakair jātipuṣpaiśca bakulaiḥ karavīrakaiḥ  LiP 
śamīpuṣpair bṛhatpuṣpair unmattāgastyajairapi 
apāmārgakadambaiś ca bhūṣaṇairapi śobhanaiḥ  LiP 
dattvā pañcavidhaṃ dhūpaṃ pāyasaṃ ca nivedayet 
dadhibhaktaṃ ca madhvājya pariplutamataḥ param  LiP 
śuddhānnaṃ caiva mudgānnaṃ ṣaḍvidhaṃ ca nivedayet 
atha pañcavidhaṃ vāpi saghṛtaṃ vinivedayet  LiP 
kevalaṃ cāpi śuddhānnam āḍhakaṃ taṇḍulaṃ pacet 
kṛtvā pradakṣiṇaṃ cānte namaskṛtya muhurmuhuḥ  LiP 
stutvā ca devamīśānaṃ punaḥ sampūjya śaṅkaram 
īśānaṃ puruṣaṃ caiva aghoraṃ vāmameva ca  LiP 
sadyojātaṃ japaṃścāpi pañcabhiḥ pūjayecchivam 
anena vidhinā devaḥ prasīdati maheśvaraḥ  LiP 
vṛkṣāḥ puṣpādipatrādyair upayuktāḥ śivārcane 
gāvaścaiva dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ prayānti paramāṃ gatim  LiP 
pūjayedyaḥ śivaṃ rudraṃ śarvaṃ bhavamajaṃ sakṛt 
sa yāti śivasāyujyaṃ punarāvṛttivarjitam  LiP 
arcitaṃ parameśānaṃ bhavaṃ śarvamumāpatim 
sakṛtprasaṃgādvā dṛṣṭvā sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate  LiP 
pūjitaṃ vā mahādevaṃ pūjyamānamathāpi vā 
dṛṣṭvā prayāti vai martyo brahmalokaṃ na saṃśayaḥ  LiP 
śrutvānumodayeccāpi sa yāti paramāṃ gatim 
yo dadyād ghṛtadīpaṃ ca sakṛlliṅgasya cāgrataḥ  LiP 
sa tāṃ gatim avāpnoti svāśramair durlabhāṃ sthirām 
dīpavṛkṣaṃ pārthivaṃ vā dāravaṃ vā śivālaye  LiP 
dattvā kulaśataṃ sāgraṃ śivaloke mahīyate 
āyasaṃ tāmrajaṃ vāpi raupyaṃ sauvarṇikaṃ tathā  LiP 
śivāya dīpaṃ yo dadyād vidhinā vāpi bhaktitaḥ 
sūryāyutasamaiḥ ślakṣṇair yānaiḥ śivapuraṃ vrajet  LiP 
kārtike māsi yo dadyād ghṛtadīpaṃ śivāgrataḥ 
sampūjyamānaṃ vā paśyed vidhinā parameśvaram  LiP 
sa yāti brahmaṇo lokaṃ śraddhayā munisattamāḥ 
āvāhanaṃ susānnidhyaṃ sthāpanaṃ pūjanaṃ tathā  LiP 
samproktaṃ rudragāyatryā āsanaṃ praṇavena vai 
pañcabhiḥ snapanaṃ proktaṃ rudrādyaiś ca viśeṣataḥ  LiP 
evaṃ sampūjayennityaṃ devadevamumāpatim 
brahmāṇaṃ dakṣiṇe tasya praṇavena samarcayet  LiP 
uttare devadeveśaṃ viṣṇuṃ gāyatriyā yajet 
vahnau hutvā yathānyāyaṃ pañcabhiḥ praṇavena ca  LiP 
sa yāti śivasāyujyam evaṃ sampūjya śaṅkaram 
iti saṃkṣepataḥ prokto liṅgārcanavidhikramaḥ  LiP 
vyāsena kathitaḥ pūrvaṃ śrutvā rudramukhātsvayam  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge śivārcanavidhir nāmaikonāśītitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
LiP  
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
kathaṃ paśupatiṃ dṛṣṭvā paśupāśavimokṣaṇam 
paśutvaṃ tatyajurdevās tanno vaktumihārhasi  LiP 
sūta uvāca
purā kailāsaśikhare bhogyākhye svapure sthitam 
sametya devāḥ sarvajñam ājagmustatprasādataḥ  LiP 
hitāya sarvadevānāṃ brahmaṇā ca janārdanaḥ 
garuḍasya tathā skandham āruhya puruṣottamaḥ  LiP 
jagāma devatābhir vai devadevāntikaṃ hariḥ 
sarve samprāpya devasya sārdhaṃ girivaraṃ śubham  LiP 
sendrāḥ sasādhyāḥ sayamāḥ praṇemur girimuttamam 
bhagavān vāsudevo 'sau garuḍād garuḍadhvajaḥ 
avatīrya giriṃ merum āruroha surottamaiḥ  LiP 
description of Mt Meru
sakaladuritahīnaṃ sarvadaṃ bhogamukhyaṃ muditakuraravṛndaṃ nāditaṃ nāgavṛndaiḥ 
madhuraraṇitagītaṃ sānukūlāndhakāraṃ padaracitavanāntaṃ kāntavātāntatoyam  LiP 
bhavanaśatasahasrair juṣṭam ādityakalpair lalitagatividagdhair haṃsavṛndaiś ca bhinnam 
dhavakhadirapalāśaiś candanādyaiś ca vṛkṣair dvijavaragaṇavṛndaiḥ kokilādyairdvirephaiḥ  LiP 
kvacidaśeṣasuradrumasaṃkulaṃ kurabakaiḥ priyakaistilakais tathā 
bahukadambatamālalatāvṛtaṃ girivaraṃ śikharairvividhais tathā  LiP 
description of Śivas city on Mt Meru
gireḥ pṛṣṭhe paraṃ śārvaṃ kalpitaṃ viśvakarmaṇā 
krīḍārthaṃ devadevasya bhavasya parameṣṭhinaḥ  LiP 
apaśyaṃstatpuraṃ devāḥ sendropendrāḥ samāhitāḥ 
praṇemurdūrataścaiva prabhāvādeva śūlinaḥ  LiP 
sahasrasūryapratimaṃ mahāntaṃ sahasraśaḥ sarvaguṇaiś ca bhinnam 
jagāma kailāsagiriṃ mahātmā meruprabhāge puramādidevaḥ  LiP 
tato 'tha nārigajavājisaṃkulaṃ rathair anekair amarārisūdanaḥ 
gaṇairgaṇeśaiś ca girīndrasaṃnibhaṃ mahāpuradvāramajo hariś ca  LiP 
atha jāṃbūnadamayair bhavanairmaṇibhūṣitaiḥ 
vimānairvividhākāraiḥ prākāraiś ca samāvṛtam  LiP 
dṛṣṭvā śaṃbhoḥ puraṃ bāhyaṃ devaiḥ sabrahmakairhariḥ 
prahṛṣṭavadano bhūtvā praviveśa tataḥ puram  LiP 
harmyaprāsādasambādhaṃ mahāṭṭālasamanvitam 
dvitīyaṃ devadevasya caturdvāraṃ suśobhanam  LiP 
vajravaiḍūryamāṇikya maṇijālaiḥ samāvṛtam 
dolāvikṣepasaṃyuktaṃ ghaṇṭācāmarabhūṣitam  LiP 
mṛdaṅgamurajairjuṣṭaṃ vīṇāveṇunināditam 
nṛtyadbhir apsaraḥsaṃghair bhūtasaṃghaiś ca saṃvṛtam 
devendrabhavanākārair bhavanair dṛṣṭimohanaiḥ  LiP 
prāsādaśṛṅgeṣvatha pauranāryaḥ sahasraśaḥ puṣpaphalākṣatādyaiḥ 
sthitāḥ karaistasya hareḥ samantāt pracikṣipurmūrdhni yathā bhavasya  LiP 
dṛṣṭvā nāryastadā viṣṇuṃ madāghūrṇitalocanāḥ  LiP 
viśālajaghanāḥ sadyo nanṛturmumudurjaguḥ 
kāściddṛṣṭvā hariṃ nāryaḥ kiṃcit prahasitānanāḥ  LiP 
kiṃcid visrastavastrāś ca srastakāñcīguṇā jaguḥ 
caturthaṃ pañcamaṃ caiva ṣaṣṭhaṃ ca saptamaṃ tathā  LiP 
aṣṭamaṃ navamaṃ caiva daśamaṃ ca purottamam 
atītyāsādya devasya puraṃ śaṃbhoḥ suśobhanam  LiP 
suvṛttaṃ sutarāṃ śubhraṃ kailāsaśikhare śubhe 
sūryamaṇḍalasaṃkāśair vimānaiś ca vibhūṣitam  LiP 
sphāṭikair maṇḍapaiḥ śubhrair jāṃbūnadamayais tathā 
nānāratnamayaiścaiva digvidikṣu vibhūṣitam  LiP 
gopurairgopateḥ śaṃbhor nānābhūṣaṇabhūṣitaiḥ 
anekaiḥ sarvatobhadraiḥ sarvaratnamayais tathā  LiP 
prākārairvividhākārair aṣṭāviṃśatibhir vṛtam 
upadvārairmahādvārair vidikṣu vividhairdṛḍhaiḥ  LiP 
guhyālayairguhyagṛhair guhasya bhavanaiḥ śubhaiḥ 
grāmyair anyair mahābhāgā mauktikair dṛṣṭimohanaiḥ  LiP 
gaṇeśāyatanair divyaiḥ padmarāgamayais tathā 
candanairvividhākāraiḥ puṣpodyānaiś ca śobhanaiḥ  LiP 
taḍāgair dirghikābhiś ca hemasopānapaṅktibhiḥ 
strīṇāṃ gatijitair haṃsaiḥ sevitābhiḥ samantataḥ  LiP 
mayūraiścaiva kāraṇḍaiḥ kokilaiścakravākakaiḥ 
śobhitābhiś ca vāpībhir divyāmṛtajalais tathā  LiP 
saṃlāpālāpakuśalaiḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitaiḥ 
stanabhārāvanamraiś ca madāghūrṇitalocanaiḥ  LiP 
geyanādaratairdivyai rudrakanyāsahasrakaiḥ 
nṛtyadbhir apsaraḥsaṃghair amarairapi durlabhaiḥ  LiP

ratotsavarataiścaiva lalitaiś ca pade pade 
grāmarāgānuraktaiś ca padmarāgasamaprabhaiḥ  LiP 
strīsaṃghair devadevasya bhavasya paramātmanaḥ 
dṛṣṭvā vismayamāpannās tasthurdevāḥ samantataḥ  LiP 
tatraiva dadṛśurdevā vṛndaṃ rudragaṇasya ca 
gaṇeśvarāṇāṃ vīrāṇām api vṛndaṃ sahasraśaḥ  LiP 
suvarṇakṛtasopānān vajravaiḍūryabhūṣitān 
sphāṭikān devadevasya dadṛśuste vimānakān  LiP 
teṣāṃ śṛṅgeṣu hṛṣṭāś ca nāryaḥ kamalalocanāḥ 
viśālajaghanā yakṣā gandharvāpsarasas tathā  LiP 
kinnaryaḥ kiṃnarāścaiva bhujaṅgāḥ siddhakanyakāḥ 
nānāveṣadharāścānyā nānābhūṣaṇabhūṣitāḥ  LiP 
nānāprabhāvasaṃyuktā nānābhogaratipriyāḥ 
nīlotpaladalaprakhyāḥ padmapatrāyatekṣaṇāḥ  LiP 
padmakiñjalkasaṃkāśair aṃśukairatiśobhanāḥ 
valayairnūpurairhāraiś chatraiścitraistathāṃśukaiḥ  LiP 
bhūṣitā bhūṣitaiś cānyair maṇḍitā maṇḍanapriyāḥ 
dṛṣṭvātha vṛndaṃ surasundarīṇāṃ gaṇeśvarāṇāṃ surasundarīṇām 
jagmurgaṇeśasya puraṃ sureśāḥ puradviṣaḥ śakrapurogamāś ca  LiP 
dṛṣṭvā ca tasthuḥ surasiddhasaṃghāḥ purasya madhye puruhūtapūrvāḥ 
bhavasya bālārkasahasravarṇaṃ vimānamādyaṃ parameśvarasya  LiP 
atha tasya vimānasya dvāri saṃsthaṃ gaṇeśvaram 
nandinaṃ dadṛśuḥ sarve devāḥ śakrapurogamāḥ  LiP 
taṃ dṛṣṭvā nandinaṃ sarve praṇamyāhur gaṇeśvaram 
jayeti devāstaṃ dṛṣṭvā so 'pyāha ca gaṇeśvaraḥ  LiP 
bho bho devā mahābhāgāḥ sarve nirdhūtakalmaṣāḥ 
samprāptāḥ sarvalokeśā vaktumarhatha suvratāḥ  LiP 
tamāhurvaradaṃ devaṃ vāraṇendrasamaprabham 
paśupāśavimokṣārthaṃ darśayāsmān maheśvaram  LiP 
purā puratrayaṃ dagdhuṃ paśutvaṃ paribhāṣitam 
śaṅkitāś ca vayaṃ tatra paśutvaṃ prati suvrata  LiP 
vrataṃ pāśupataṃ proktaṃ bhavena parameṣṭhinā 
vratenānena bhūteśa paśutvaṃ naiva vidyate  LiP 
atha dvādaśavarṣaṃ vā māsadvādaśakaṃ tu vā 
dinadvādaśakaṃ vāpi kṛtvā tad vratam uttamam  LiP 
mucyante paśavaḥ sarve paśupāśairbhavasya tu 
darśayāmāsa tāndevān nārāyaṇapurogamān  LiP 
nandī śilādatanayaḥ sarvabhūtagaṇāgraṇīḥ 
taṃ dṛṣṭvā devamīśānaṃ sāṃbaṃ sagaṇam avyayam  LiP 
praṇemus tuṣṭuvuś caiva prītikaṇṭakitatvacaḥ 
vijñāpya śitikaṇṭhāya paśupāśavimokṣaṇam  LiP 
tasthustadāgrataḥ śaṃbhoḥ praṇipatya punaḥ punaḥ 
tataḥ samprekṣya tān sarvān devadevo vṛṣadhvajaḥ  LiP 
viśodhya teṣāṃ devānāṃ paśutvaṃ parameśvaraḥ 
vrataṃ pāśupataṃ caiva svayaṃ devo maheśvaraḥ  LiP 
upadiśya munīnāṃ ca sahāste cāṃbayā bhavaḥ

tato dvādaśavarṣānte muktapāśāḥ surottamāḥ

yaḥ śrāvayecchucir viprāñ chṛṇuyādvā śucirnaraḥ 
sa dehabhedamāsādya paśupāśaiḥ pramucyate  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge pāśupatavratamāhātmyaṃ nāmāśītitamo 'dhyāyaḥ

result of liṅga worship
devairdaityais tathā siddhair gandharvaiḥ siddhacāraṇaiḥ  LiP 
munibhiś ca mahābhāgair anuṣṭhitamanuttamam 
vrataṃ dvādaśaliṅgākhyaṃ paśupāśavimokṣaṇam  LiP 
bhogadaṃ yogadaṃ caiva kāmadaṃ muktidaṃ śubham 
aviyogakaraṃ puṇyaṃ bhaktānāṃ bhayanāśanam  LiP 
ṣaḍaṅgasahitān vedān mathitvā tena nirmitam 
sarvadānottamaṃ puṇyam aśvamedhāyutādhikam  LiP 
sarvamaṅgaladaṃ puṇyaṃ sarvaśatruvināśanam 
saṃsārārṇavamagnānāṃ jantūnāmapi mokṣadam  LiP 
sarvavyādhiharaṃ caiva sarvajvaravināśanam 
devairanuṣṭhitaṃ pūrvaṃ brahmaṇā viṣṇunā tathā  LiP 
creation of a liṅga
kṛtvā kanīyasaṃ liṅgaṃ snāpya candanavāriṇā 
caitramāsādi viprendrāḥ śivaliṅgavrataṃ caret  LiP 
kṛtvā haimaṃ śubhaṃ padmaṃ karṇikākesarānvitam 
navaratnaiś ca khacitam aṣṭapatraṃ yathāvidhi  LiP 
karṇikāyāṃ nyaselliṅgaṃ sphāṭikaṃ pīṭhasaṃyutam 
tatra bhaktyā yathānyāyam arcayed bilvapatrakaiḥ  LiP 
sitaiḥ sahasrakamalai raktairnīlotpalairapi 
śvetārkakarṇikāraiś ca karavīrairbakairapi  LiP 
etairanyair yathālābhaṃ gāyatryā tasya suvratāḥ 
sampūjya caiva gandhādyair dhūpairdīpaiś ca maṅgalaiḥ  LiP 
nīrājanādyaiścānyaiś ca liṅgamūrtimaheśvaram 
agaruṃ dakṣiṇe dadyād aghoreṇa dvijottamāḥ  LiP 
paścime sadyamantreṇa divyāṃ caiva manaḥśilām 
uttare vāmadevena candanaṃ vāpi dāpayet  LiP 
puruṣeṇa muniśreṣṭhā haritālaṃ ca pūrvataḥ 
sitāgarūdbhavaṃ viprās tathā kṛṣṇāgarūdbhavam  LiP 
tathā gugguludhūpaṃ ca saugandhikamanuttamam 
sitāraṃ nāma dhūpaṃ ca dadyād īśāya bhaktitaḥ  LiP 
mahācarurnivedyaḥ syād āḍhakānnamathāpi vā 
etad vaḥ kathitaṃ puṇyaṃ śivaliṅgamahāvratam  LiP 
time for this vrata
sarvamāseṣu sāmānyaṃ viśeṣo 'pi ca kīrtyate 
vaiśākhe vajraliṅgaṃ ca jyeṣṭhe mārakataṃ tathā  LiP 
āṣāḍhe mauktikaṃ liṅgaṃ śrāvaṇe nīlanirmitam 
māsi bhādrapade liṅgaṃ padmarāgamayaṃ śubham  LiP 
āśvine caiva viprendrāḥ gomedakamayaṃ śubham 
pravālenaiva kārtikyāṃ tathā vai mārgaśīrṣake  LiP 
material for a liṅga
vaiḍūryanirmitaṃ liṅgaṃ puṣparāgeṇa puṣyake 
māghe ca sūryakāntena phālgune sphāṭikena ca  LiP 
sarvamāseṣu kamalaṃ haimamekaṃ vidhīyate 
alābhe rājataṃ vāpi kevalaṃ kamalaṃ tu vā  LiP 
ratnānām apyalābhe tu hemnā vā rājatena vā 
rajatasyāpyalābhe tu tāmralohena kārayet  LiP 
śailaṃ vā dārujaṃ vāpi mṛnmayaṃ vā savedikam 
sarvagandhamayaṃ vāpi kṣaṇikaṃ parikalpayet  LiP 
haimantike mahādevaṃ śrīpattreṇaiva pūjayet 
sarvamāseṣu kamalaṃ haimamekamathāpi vā  LiP 
rājataṃ vāpi kamalaṃ haimakarṇikamuttamam 
rājatasyāpyabhāve tu bilvapatraiḥ samarcayet  LiP 
sahasrakamalālābhe tadardhenāpi pūjayet 
tadardhārdhena vā rudram aṣṭottaraśatena vā  LiP 
flower  deity
bilvapatre sthitā lakṣmīr devī lakṣaṇasaṃyutā 
nīlotpale 'ṃbikā sākṣād utpale ṣaṇmukhaḥ svayam  LiP

bhojayedbrāhmaṇānbhaktyā śrotriyān vedapāragān  LiP 
tal liṅgaṃ pūjitaṃ tena sarvadravyasamanvitam 
sthāpayed vā śivakṣetre dāpayed brāhmaṇāya vā  LiP 
ya evaṃ sarvamāseṣu śivaliṅgamahāvratam

sūryakoṭipratīkāśair vimānai ratnabhūṣitaiḥ 
gatvā śivapuraṃ divyaṃ nehāyāti kadācana  LiP

śivalokamavāpnoti nātra kāryā vicāraṇā  LiP 
athavā saktacittaśced yānyān saṃcintayedvarān

vyapohanastavaṃ vakṣye sarvasiddhipradaṃ śubham

caitre 'pi rudramabhyarcya kuryādvai naktabhojanam 
śālyannaṃ payasā yuktaṃ ghṛtena ca yathāsukham  LiP 
goṣṭhaśāyī muniśreṣṭhāḥ kṣitau niśi bhavaṃ smaret 
paurṇamāsyāṃ śivaṃ snāpya dadyādgomithunaṃ sitam  LiP 
brāhmaṇān bhojayeccaiva nirṛteḥ sthānamāpnuyāt 
vaiśākhe ca tathā māse kṛtvā vai naktabhojanam  LiP 
paurṇamāsyāṃ bhavaṃ snāpya pañcagavyaghṛtādibhiḥ 
śvetaṃ gomithunaṃ dattvā so 'śvamedhaphalaṃ labhet  LiP 
jyeṣṭhe māse ca deveśaṃ bhavaṃ śarvamumāpatim 
sampūjya śraddhayā bhaktyā kṛtvā vai naktabhojanam  LiP 
raktaśālyannamadhvā ca adbhiḥ pūtaṃ ghṛtādibhiḥ 
vīrāsano niśārdhaṃ ca gavāṃ śuśrūṣaṇe rataḥ  LiP 
paurṇamāsyāṃ tu sampūjya devadevamumāpatim 
snāpya śaktyā yathānyāyaṃ caruṃ dadyāc ca śūline  LiP 
brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca yathāvibhavavistaram 
dhūmraṃ gomithunaṃ dattvā vāyuloke mahīyate  LiP 
āṣāḍhe māsi cāpyevaṃ naktabhojanatatparaḥ 
bhūrikhaṇḍājyasaṃmiśraṃ saktubhiścaiva gorasam  LiP 
paurṇamāsyāṃ ghṛtādyaistu snāpya pūjya yathāvidhi 
brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca śrotriyān vedapāragān  LiP 
dadyādgomithunaṃ gauraṃ vāruṇaṃ lokamāpnuyāt 
śrāvaṇe ca dvijā māse kṛtvā vai naktabhojanam  LiP 
kṣīraṣaṣṭikabhaktena sampūjya vṛṣabhadhvajam 
paurṇamāsyāṃ ghṛtādyaistu snāpya pūjya yathāvidhi  LiP 
brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca śrotriyān vedapāragān 
śvetāgrapādaṃ pauṇḍraṃ ca dadyādgomithunaṃ punaḥ  LiP 
sa yāti vāyusāyujyaṃ vāyuvatsarvago bhavet 
prāpte bhādrapade māse kṛtvaivaṃ naktabhojanam  LiP 
hutaśeṣaṃ ca viprendrān vṛkṣamūlāśrito divā 
paurṇamāsyāṃ tu deveśaṃ snāpya sampūjya śaṅkaram  LiP 
nīlaskandhaṃ vṛṣaṃ gāṃ ca dattvā bhaktyā yathāvidhi 
brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca vedavedāṅgapāragān  LiP 
yakṣalokamanuprāpya yakṣarājo bhavennaraḥ 
tataścāśvayuje māsi kṛtvaivaṃ naktabhojanam  LiP 
saghṛtaṃ śaṅkaraṃ pūjya paurṇamāsyāṃ ca pūrvavat 
brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca śivabhaktān sadā śucīn  LiP 
vṛṣabhaṃ nīlavarṇābham urodeśasamunnatam 
gāṃ ca dattvā yathānyāyam aiśānaṃ lokamāpnuyāt  LiP 
kārtike ca tathā māse kṛtvā vai naktabhojanam 
kṣīraudanena sājyena sampūjya ca bhavaṃ prabhum  LiP 
paurṇamāsyāṃ ca vidhivat snāpya dattvā caruṃ punaḥ 
brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca yathāvibhavavistaram  LiP 
dattvā gomithunaṃ caiva kāpilaṃ pūrvavad dvijāḥ 
sūryasāyujyamāpnoti nātra kāryā vicāraṇā  LiP 
mārgaśīrṣe ca māse 'pi kṛtvaivaṃ naktabhojanam 
yavānnena yathānyāyam ājyakṣīrādibhiḥ samam  LiP 
paurṇamāsyāṃ ca pūrvoktaṃ kṛtvā śarvāya śaṃbhave 
brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca daridrānvedapāragān  LiP 
dattvā gomithunaṃ caiva pāṇḍuraṃ vidhipūrvakam 
somalokamanuprāpya somena saha modate  LiP 
ahiṃsā satyamasteyaṃ brahmacaryaṃ kṣamā dayā 
triḥsnānaṃ cāgnihotraṃ ca bhūśayyā naktabhojanam  LiP 
pakṣayorupavāsaṃ ca caturdaśyaṣṭamīṣu ca  LiP 
ityetadakhilaṃ proktaṃ pratimāsaṃ śivavratam  LiP 
kuryādvarṣaṃ krameṇaiva vyutkrameṇāpi vā dvijāḥ 
sa yāti śivasāyujyaṃ jñānayogamavāpnuyāt  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge śivavratakathanaṃ nāma tryaśītitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
LiP  
sūta uvāca
umāmaheśvaraṃ vakṣye vratamīśvarabhāṣitam 
naranāryādijantūnāṃ hitāya munisattamāḥ  LiP 
paurṇamāsyāmamāvāsyāṃ caturdaśyaṣṭamīṣu ca 
naktamabdaṃ prakurvīta haviṣyaṃ pūjayedbhavam  LiP 
umāmaheśapratimāṃ hemnā kṛtvā suśobhanām 
rājatīṃ vātha varṣānte pratiṣṭhāpya yathāvidhi  LiP 
brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca dattvā śaktyā ca dakṣiṇām 
rathādyairvāpi deveśaṃ nītvā rudrālayaṃ prati  LiP 
sarvātiśayasaṃyuktaiś chatracāmarabhūṣaṇaiḥ 
nivedayedvrataṃ caiva śivāya parameṣṭhine  LiP 
sa yāti śivasāyujyaṃ nārī devyā yadi prabho 
aṣṭamyāṃ ca caturdaśyāṃ niyatā brahmacāriṇī  LiP 
varṣamekaṃ na bhuñjati kanyā vā vidhavāpi vā 
varṣānte pratimāṃ kṛtvā pūrvoktavidhinā tataḥ  LiP 
pratiṣṭhāpya yathānyāyaṃ dattvā rudrālaye punaḥ 
brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca bhavānyā saha modate  LiP 
yā nāryevaṃ caredabdaṃ kṛṣṇāmekāṃ caturdaśīm 
varṣānte pratimāṃ kṛtvā yena kenāpi vā dvijāḥ  LiP 
pūrvoktamakhilaṃ kṛtvā bhavānyā saha modate 
amāvāsyāṃ nirāhārā bhavedabdaṃ suyantritā  LiP 
śūlaṃ ca vidhinā kṛtvā varṣānte vinivedayet 
snāpyeśānaṃ yajedbhaktyā sahasraiḥ kamalaiḥ sitaiḥ  LiP 
rājataṃ kamalaṃ caiva jāṃbūnadasukarṇikam 
dattvā bhavāya viprebhyaḥ pradadyād dakṣiṇām api  LiP 
kāmato 'pi kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ bhrūṇahatyādikaṃ ca yat 
tatsarvaṃ śūladānena bhindyānnārī na saṃśayaḥ  LiP 
sāyujyaṃ caivamāpnoti bhavānyā dvijasattamāḥ 
kuryādyadvā naraḥ so 'pi rudrasāyujyamāpnuyāt  LiP 
paurṇamāsyāmamāvāsyāṃ varṣamekamatandritā 
upavāsaratā nārī naro 'pi dvijasattamāḥ  LiP 
niyogādeva tatkāryaṃ bhartṝṇāṃ dvijasattamāḥ 
japaṃ dānaṃ tapaḥ sarvam asvatantrā yataḥ striyaḥ  LiP 
varṣānte sarvagandhāḍhyāṃ pratimāṃ saṃnivedayet 
sā bhavānyāś ca sāyujyaṃ sārūpyaṃ cāpi suvratā  LiP 
labhate nātra saṃdehaḥ satyaṃ satyaṃ vadāmyaham 
kārtikyāṃ vā tu yā nārī ekabhaktena vartate  LiP 
kṣamāhiṃsādiniyamaiḥ saṃyuktā brahmacāriṇī 
dadyātkṛṣṇatilānāṃ ca bhāramekam atandritā  LiP 
saghṛtaṃ saguḍaṃ caiva odanaṃ parameṣṭhine 
dattvā ca brāhmaṇebhyaś ca yathā vibhavavistaram  LiP 
aṣṭamyāṃ ca caturdaśyām upavāsaratā ca sā 
bhavānyā modate sārdhaṃ sārūpyaṃ prāpya suvratā  LiP 
kṣamā satyaṃ dayā dānaṃ śaucamindriyanigrahaḥ 
sarvavrateṣvayaṃ dharmaḥ sāmānyo rudrapūjanam  LiP 
samāsādvaḥ pravakṣyāmi pratimāsamanukramāt 
mārgaśīrṣakamāsādi kārttikāntaṃ yathākramam  LiP 
vrataṃ suvipulaṃ puṇyaṃ nandinā paribhāṣitam 
mārgaśīrṣakamāse 'tha vṛṣaṃ pūrṇāṅgamuttamam  LiP 
alaṃkṛtya yathānyāyaṃ śivāya vinivedayet 
sā ca sārdhaṃ bhavānyā vai modate nātra saṃśayaḥ  LiP 
puṣyamāse tu vai śūlaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya nivedayet 
pūrvoktamakhilaṃ kṛtvā bhavānyā saha modate  LiP 
māghamāse rathaṃ kṛtvā sarvalakṣaṇalakṣitam 
dadyāt sampūjya deveśaṃ brāhmaṇāṃścaiva bhojayet  LiP 
sā ca devyā mahābhāgā modate nātra saṃśayaḥ 
phālgune pratimāṃ kṛtvā hiraṇyena yathāvidhi  LiP 
rājatenāpi tāmreṇa yathāvibhavavistaram 
pratiṣṭhāpya samabhyarcya sthāpayecchaṅkarālaye  LiP 
sā ca sārdhaṃ mahādevyā modate nātra saṃśayaḥ 
caitre bhavaṃ kumāraṃ ca bhavānīṃ ca yathāvidhi  LiP 
tāmrādyairvidhivatkṛtvā pratiṣṭhāpya yathāvidhi 
bhavānyā modate sārdhaṃ dattvā rudrāya śaṃbhave  LiP 
kṛtvālayaṃ hi kauberaṃ rājataṃ rajatena vai 
īśvaromāsamāyuktaṃ gaṇeśaiś ca samantataḥ  LiP 
sarvaratnasamāyuktaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya yathāvidhi 
sthāpayetparameśasya bhavasyāyatane śubhe  LiP 
vaiśākhe vai cared evaṃ kailāsākhyaṃ vratottamam 
kailāsaparvataṃ prāpya bhavānyā saha modate  LiP 
jyeṣṭhe māsi mahādevaṃ liṅgamūrtimumāpatim 
kṛtāñjalipuṭenaiva brahmaṇā viṣṇunā tathā  LiP 
madhye bhavena saṃyuktaṃ liṅgamūrti dvijottamāḥ 
haṃsena ca varāheṇa kṛtvā tāmrādibhiḥ śubhām  LiP 
pratiṣṭhāpya yathānyāyaṃ brāhmaṇān bhojayettataḥ 
śivāya śivamāsādya śivasthāne yathāvidhi  LiP 
brāhmaṇaiḥ sahitāṃ sthāpya devyāḥ sāyujyamāpnuyāt 
āṣāḍhe ca śubhe māse gṛhaṃ kṛtvā suśobhanam  LiP 
pakveṣṭakābhir vidhivad yathāvibhavavistaram 
sarvabījarasaiścāpi sampūrṇaṃ sarvaśobhanaiḥ  LiP 
gṛhopakaraṇaiścaiva musalolūkhalādibhiḥ 
dāsīdāsādibhiścaiva śayanairaśanādibhiḥ  LiP 
sampūrṇaiś ca gṛhaṃ vastrair ācchādya ca samantataḥ 
devaṃ ghṛtādibhiḥ snāpya mahādevamumāpatim  LiP 
brāhmaṇānāṃ sahasraṃ ca bhojayitvā yathāvidhi 
vidyāvinayasampannaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ vedapāragam  LiP 
prathamāśramiṇaṃ bhaktyā sampūjya ca yathāvidhi 
kanyāṃ sumadhyamāṃ yāvat kālajīvanasaṃyutām  LiP 
kṣetraṃ gomithunaṃ caiva tadgṛhe ca nivedayet 
sāyanair vividhair divyair meruparvatasannibhaiḥ  LiP 
golokaṃ samanuprāpya bhavānyā saha modate 
bhavānyā sadṛśībhūtvā sarvakalpeṣu sāvyayā  LiP 
bhavānyāścaiva sāyujyaṃ labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ 
sarvadhātusamākīrṇaṃ vicitradhvajaśobhitam  LiP 
nivedayīta śarvāya śrāvaṇe tilaparvatam 
vitānadhvajavastrādyair dhātubhiś ca nivedayet  LiP 
brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca pūrvoktamakhilaṃ bhavet 
kṛtvā bhādrapade māsi śobhanaṃ śāliparvatam  LiP 
vitānadhvajavastrādyair dhātubhiś ca nivedayet 
brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca dāpayecca yathāvidhi  LiP 
sā ca sūryāṃśusaṃkāśā bhavānyā saha modate 
kṛtvā cāśvayuje māsi vipulaṃ dhānyaparvatam  LiP 
suvarṇavastrasaṃyuktaṃ dattvā sampūjya śaṅkaram 
brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca pūrvoktamakhilaṃ bhavet  LiP 
sarvadhānyasamāyuktaṃ sarvabījarasādibhiḥ 
sarvadhātusamāyuktaṃ sarvaratnopaśobhitam  LiP 
śṛṅgaiścaturbhiḥ saṃyuktaṃ vitānacchatraśobhitam 
gandhamālyais tathā dhūpaiś citraiścāpi suśobhitam  LiP 
vicitrairnṛtyageyaiś ca śaṅkhavīṇādibhis tathā 
brahmaghoṣairmahāpuṇyaṃ maṅgalaiś ca viśeṣataḥ  LiP 
mahādhvajāṣṭasaṃyuktaṃ vicitrakusumojjvalam 
nagendraṃ merunāmānaṃ trailokyādhāramuttamam  LiP 
tasya mūrdhni śivaṃ kuryān madhyato dhātunaiva tu 
dakṣiṇe ca yathānyāyaṃ brahmāṇaṃ ca caturmukham  LiP 
uttare devadeveśaṃ nārāyaṇamanāmayam 
indrādilokapālāṃś ca kṛtvā bhaktyā yathāvidhi  LiP 
pratiṣṭhāpya tataḥ snāpya samabhyarcya maheśvaram 
devasya dakṣiṇe haste śūlaṃ tridaśapūjitam  LiP 
vāme pāśaṃ bhavānyāś ca kamalaṃ hemabhūṣitam 
viṣṇoś ca śaṅkhaṃ cakraṃ ca gadāmabjaṃ prayatnataḥ  LiP 
brahmaṇaścākṣasūtraṃ ca kamaṇḍalumanuttamam 
indrasya vajram agneś ca śaktyākhyaṃ paramāyudham  LiP 
yamasya daṇḍaṃ nirṛteḥ khaḍgaṃ niśicarasya tu 
varuṇasya mahāpāśaṃ nāgākhyaṃ rudramadbhutam  LiP 
vāyor yaṣṭiṃ kuberasya gadāṃ lokaprapūjitām 
ṭaṅkaṃ ceśānadevasya nivedyaivaṃ krameṇa ca  LiP 
śivasya mahatīṃ pūjāṃ kṛtvā carusamanvitām 
pūjayetsarvadevāṃś ca yathāvibhavavistaram  LiP 
brāhmaṇānbhojayitvā ca pūjāṃ kṛtvā prayatnataḥ 
mahāmeruvrataṃ kṛtvā mahādevāya dāpayet  LiP 
mahāmerumanuprāpya mahādevyā pramodate 
ciraṃ sāyujyam āpnoti mahādevyā na saṃśayaḥ  LiP 
kārtikyāmapi yā nārī kṛtvā devīmumāṃ śubhām 
sarvābharaṇasampūrṇāṃ sarvalakṣaṇalakṣitām  LiP 
hematāmrādibhiścaiva pratiṣṭhāpya vidhānataḥ 
devaṃ ca kṛtvā deveśaṃ sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutam  LiP 
tayoragre hutāśaṃ ca sruvahastaṃ pitāmaham 
nārāyaṇaṃ ca dātāraṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam  LiP 
lokapālais tathā siddhaiḥ saṃvṛtaṃ sthāpya yatnataḥ 
rudrālaye vrataṃ tasmai dāpayedbhaktipūrvakam  LiP 
sā bhavānyāstanuṃ gatvā bhavena saha modate 
ekabhaktavrataṃ puṇyaṃ pratimāsamanukramāt  LiP 
mārgaśīrṣakamāsādi kārtikāntaṃ pravartitam 
naranāryādijantūnāṃ hitāya munisattamāḥ  LiP 
naraḥ kṛtvā vrataṃ caiva śivasāyujyamāpnuyāt 
nārī devyā na saṃdehaḥ śivena paribhāṣitam  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge umāmaheśvaravrataṃ nāma caturaśītitamo 'dhyāyaḥ

sūta uvāca
sarvavrateṣu sampūjya devadevamumāpatim 
japetpañcākṣarīṃ vidyāṃ vidhinaiva dvijottamāḥ  LiP 
japādeva na saṃdeho vratānāṃ vai viśeṣataḥ 
samāptirnānyathā tasmāj japetpañcākṣarīṃ śubhām  LiP 
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
kathaṃ pañcākṣarī vidyā prabhāvo vā kathaṃ vada 
kramopāyaṃ mahābhāga śrotuṃ kautūhalaṃ hi naḥ  LiP 
sūta uvāca
purā devena rudreṇa devadevena śaṃbhunā 
pārvatyāḥ kathitaṃ puṇyaṃ pravadāmi samāsataḥ  LiP 
śrīdevyuvāca
bhagavandevadeveśa sarvalokamaheśvara 
pañcākṣarasya māhātmyaṃ śrotumicchāmi tattvataḥ  LiP 
śrībhagavānuvāca
pralaya and sṛṣṭi
pañcākṣarasya māhātmyaṃ varṣakoṭiśatairapi 
na śakyaṃ kathituṃ devi tasmāt saṃkṣepataḥ śṛṇu  LiP 
pralaye samanuprāpte naṣṭe sthāvarajaṅgame 
naṣṭe devāsure caiva naṣṭe coragarākṣase  LiP 
sarvaṃ prakṛtimāpannaṃ tvayā pralayameṣyati 
eko 'haṃ saṃsthito devi na dvitīyo 'sti kutracit  LiP 
tasminvedāś ca śāstrāṇi mantre pañcākṣare sthitāḥ 
te nāśaṃ naiva samprāptā macchaktyā hyanupālitāḥ  LiP 
ahameko dvidhāpyāsaṃ prakṛtyātmaprabhedataḥ 
sa tu nārāyaṇaḥ śete devo māyāmayīṃ tanum  LiP 
āsthāya yogaparyaṅka śayane toyamadhyagaḥ 
tannābhipaṅkajājjātaḥ pañcavaktraḥ pitāmahaḥ  LiP 
Brahmā creates  sons
they get power from Śiva
sisṛkṣamāṇo lokānvai trīnaśakto 'sahāyavān 
daśa brahmā sasarjādau mānasānamitaujasaḥ  LiP 
teṣāṃ sṛṣṭiprasiddhyarthaṃ māṃ provāca pitāmahaḥ 
matputrāṇāṃ mahādeva śaktiṃ dehi maheśvara  LiP 
iti tena samādiṣṭaḥ pañcavaktradharo hyaham 
pañcākṣarānpañcamukhaiḥ proktavān padmayonaye  LiP 
tānpañcavadanairgṛhṇan brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ 
vācyavācakabhāvena jñātavānparameśvaram  LiP 
vācyaḥ pañcākṣarairdevi śivastrailokyapūjitaḥ 
vācakaḥ paramo mantras tasya pañcākṣaraḥ sthitaḥ  LiP 
jñātvā prayogaṃ vidhinā ca siddhiṃ labdhvā tathā pañcamukho mahātmā 
provāca putreṣu jagaddhitāya mantraṃ mahārthaṃ kila pañcavarṇam  LiP 
te labdhvā mantraratnaṃ tu sākṣāllokapitāmahāt 
tamārādhayituṃ devaṃ parātparataraṃ śivam  LiP 
tatastutoṣa bhagavān trimūrtīnāṃ paraḥ śivaḥ 
dattavānakhilaṃ jñānam aṇimādiguṇāṣṭakam  LiP 
te 'pi labdhvā varānviprās tadārādhanakāṅkṣiṇaḥ 
merostu śikhare ramye muñjavānnāma parvataḥ  LiP 
matpriyaḥ satataṃ śrīmān madbhūtaiḥ parirakṣitaḥ 
tasyābhyāśe tapastīvraṃ lokasṛṣṭisamutsukāḥ  LiP 
divyavarṣasahasraṃ tu vāyubhakṣāḥ samācaran 
tiṣṭhanto 'nugrahārthāya devi te ṛṣayaḥ purā  LiP 
teṣāṃ bhaktimahaṃ dṛṣṭvā sadyaḥ pratyakṣatāmiyām 
pañcākṣaram ṛṣicchando daivataṃ śaktibījavat  LiP 
nyāsaṃ ṣaḍaṅgaṃ digbandhaṃ viniyogamaśeṣataḥ 
proktavānahamāryāṇāṃ lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā  LiP 
tacchrutvā mantramāhātmyam ṛṣayaste tapodhanāḥ 
mantrasya viniyogaṃ ca kṛtvā sarvamanuṣṭhitāḥ  LiP 
tanmāhātmyāt tadā lokān sadevāsuramānuṣān 
varṇānvarṇavibhāgāṃś ca sarvadharmāṃś ca śobhanān  LiP 
pūrvakalpasamudbhūtāñ chrutavanto yathā purā 
pañcākṣaraprabhāvācca lokā vedā maharṣayaḥ  LiP 
description of pañcākṣara mantra
tiṣṭhanti śāśvatā dharmā devāḥ sarvamidaṃ jagat 
tad idānīṃ pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu cāvahitākhilam  LiP 
alpākṣaraṃ mahārthaṃ ca vedasāraṃ vimuktidam 
ājñāsiddhamasaṃdigdhaṃ vākyametacchivātmakam  LiP 
nānāsiddhiyutaṃ divyaṃ lokacittānurañjakam 
suniścitārthaṃ gaṃbhīraṃ vākyaṃ me pārameśvaram  LiP 
mantraṃ mukhasukhoccāryam aśeṣārthaprasādhakam 
tadbījaṃ sarvavidyānāṃ mantramādyaṃ suśobhanam  LiP

description
sarvapāpaharaṃ caiva trividho nyāsa ucyate

japa
yaḥ puraścaraṇaṃ kṛtvā nityajāpī bhavennaraḥ 
tasya nāsti samo loke sa siddhaḥ siddhido vaśī  LiP 
āsanaṃ ruciraṃ baddhvā maunī caikāgramānasaḥ 
prāṅmukhodaṅmukho vāpi japenmantramanuttamam  LiP

prāṇāyāmādbhavetkṣipraṃ sarvapāpaparikṣayaḥ 
indriyāṇāṃ vaśitvaṃ ca tasmātprāṇāṃś ca saṃyamet  LiP 
gṛhe japaḥ samaṃ vidyād goṣṭhe śataguṇaṃ bhavet 
nadyāṃ śatasahasraṃ tu anantaḥ śivasannidhau  LiP 
samudratīre devahrade girau devālayeṣu ca 
puṇyāśrameṣu sarveṣu japaḥ koṭiguṇo bhavet  LiP 
śivasya saṃnidhāne ca sūryasyāgre gurorapi 
dīpasya gorjalasyāpi japakarma praśasyate  LiP 
aṅgulījapasaṃkhyānam ekamekaṃ śubhānane 
rekhairaṣṭaguṇaṃ proktaṃ putrajīvaphalair daśa  LiP 
śataṃ vai śaṅkhamaṇibhiḥ pravālaiś ca sahasrakam 
sphāṭikair daśasāhasraṃ mauktikairlakṣamucyate  LiP 
padmākṣairdaśalakṣaṃ tu sauvarṇaiḥ koṭirucyate 
kuśagranthyā ca rudrākṣair anantaguṇamucyate  LiP 
pañcaviṃśati mokṣārthaṃ saptaviṃśati pauṣṭikam 
triṃśacca dhanasaṃpattyai pañcāśaccābhicārikam  LiP 
tatpūrvābhimukhaṃ vaśyaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ cābhicārikam 
paścimaṃ dhanadaṃ vidyād uttaraṃ śāntikaṃ bhavet  LiP 
aṅguṣṭhaṃ mokṣadaṃ vidyāt tarjanī śatrunāśanī 
madhyamā dhanadā śāntiṃ karotyeṣā hy anāmikā  LiP 
kaniṣṭhā rakṣaṇīyā sā japakarmaṇi śobhane 
aṅguṣṭhena japejjapyam anyairaṅgulibhiḥ saha  LiP 
aṅguṣṭhena vinā karma kṛtaṃ tadaphalaṃ yataḥ

curse of saṃsāra
na viṣaṃ kālakūṭākhyaṃ saṃsāro viṣamucyate

everything is duḥkha
evamajñānadoṣeṇa nānākarmavaśena ca 
ṣaṭkauśikaṃ samudbhūtaṃ bhajatyeṣa kalevaram  LiP
