aiśvaryāṣṭadalaṃ śvetaṃ paraṃ vairāgyakarṇikam 
chidrāṇi ca diśo yasya prāṇādyāś ca pratiṣṭhitāḥ  LiP 
prāṇādyaiścaiva saṃyuktaḥ paśyate bahudhā kramāt 
daśaprāṇavahā nāḍyaḥ pratyekaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ  LiP 
dvisaptatisahasrāṇi nāḍyaḥ samparikīrtitāḥ 
netrasthaṃ jāgrataṃ vidyāt kaṇṭhe svapnaṃ samādiśet  LiP 
suṣuptaṃ hṛdayasthaṃ tu turīyaṃ mūrdhani sthitam 
jāgre brahmā ca viṣṇuś ca svapne caiva yathākramāt  LiP 
īśvarastu suṣupte tu turīye ca maheśvaraḥ 
vadanty evam athānye 'pi samastakaraṇaiḥ pumān  LiP 
vartamānastadā tasya jāgradityabhidhīyate 
manobuddhir ahaṅkāraṃ cittaṃ ceti catuṣṭayam  LiP 
yadā vyavasthitastvetaiḥ svapna ityabhidhīyate 
karaṇāni vilīnāni yadā svātmani suvratāḥ  LiP 
suṣuptaḥ karaṇairbhinnas turīyaḥ parikīrtyate 
parasturīyātīto 'sau śivaḥ paramakāraṇam  LiP 
jāgratsvapnasuṣuptiś ca turīyaṃ cādhibhautikam 
ādhyātmikaṃ ca viprendrāś cādhidaivikamucyate  LiP 
tatsarvamaham eveti veditavyaṃ vijānatā 
buddhīndriyāṇi viprendrās tathā karmendriyāṇi ca  LiP 
manobuddhir ahaṅkāraś cittaṃ ceti catuṣṭayam 
adhyātmaṃ pṛthagevedaṃ caturdaśavidhaṃ smṛtam  LiP 
draṣṭavyaṃ caiva śrotavyaṃ ghrātavyaṃ ca yathākramam 
rasitavyaṃ muniśreṣṭhāḥ sparśitavyaṃ tathaiva ca  LiP 
mantavyaṃ caiva boddhavyam ahaṃkartavyameva ca 
tathā cetayitavyaṃ ca vaktavyaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ  LiP 
ādātavyaṃ ca gantavyaṃ visargāyitameva ca 
ānanditavyamityete hy adhibhūtamanukramāt  LiP 
ādityo 'pi diśaścaiva pṛthivī varuṇas tathā 
vāyuścandras tathā brahmā rudraḥ kṣetrajña eva ca  LiP 
agnirindras tathā viṣṇur mitro devaḥ prajāpatiḥ 
ādhidaivikamevaṃ hi caturdaśavidhaṃ kramāt  LiP 
rājñī sudarśanā caiva jitā saumyā yathākramam 
moghā rudrāmṛtā satyā madhyamā ca dvijottamāḥ  LiP 
nāḍī rāśiśukā caiva asurā caiva kṛttikā 
bhāsvatī nāḍayaścaitāś caturdaśanibandhanāḥ  LiP 
vāyavo nāḍimadhyasthā vāhakāś ca caturdaśa 
prāṇo vyānastvapānaś ca udānaś ca samānakaḥ  LiP 
vairambhaś ca tathā mukhyo hy antaryāmaḥ prabhañjanaḥ 
kūrmakaś ca tathā śyenaḥ śvetaḥ kṛṣṇas tathānilaḥ  LiP 
nāga ityeva kathitā vāyavaś ca caturdaśa 
yaścakṣuḥṣvatha draṣṭavye tathāditye ca suvratāḥ  LiP 
nāḍyāṃ prāṇe ca vijñāne tv ānande ca yathākramam 
hṛdyākāśe ya etasmin sarvasminnantare paraḥ  LiP 
ātmā ekaś ca carati tamupāsīta māṃ prabhum 
ajaraṃ tamanantaṃ ca aśokamamṛtaṃ dhruvam  LiP 
caturdaśavidheṣveva saṃcaratyeka eva saḥ 
līyante tāni tatraiva yadanyaṃ nāsti vai dvijāḥ  LiP 
eka eva hi sarvajñaḥ sarveśastveka eva saḥ 
eṣa sarvādhipo devas tv antaryāmī mahādyutiḥ  LiP 
upāsyamānaḥ sarvasya sarvasaukhyaḥ sanātanaḥ 
upāsyati na caiveha sarvasaukhyaṃ dvijottamāḥ  LiP 
upāsyamāno vedaiś ca śāstrairnānāvidhairapi 
na vaiṣa vedaśāstrāṇi sarvajño yāsyati prabhuḥ  LiP 
asyaivānnamidaṃ sarvaṃ na so 'nnaṃ bhavati svayam 
svātmanā rakṣitaṃ cādyād annabhūtaṃ na kutracit  LiP 
sarvatra prāṇināmannaṃ prāṇināṃ granthirasmyaham 
praśāstā nayanaścaiva pañcātmā sa vibhāgaśaḥ  LiP 
annamayo 'sau bhūtātmā cādyate hyannamucyate 
prāṇamayaścendriyātmā saṃkalpātmā manomayaḥ  LiP 
kālātmā soma eveha vijñānamaya ucyate 
sadānandamayo bhūtvā maheśaḥ parameśvaraḥ  LiP 
so 'ham evaṃ jagatsarvaṃ mayyeva sakalaṃ sthitam 
paratantraṃ svatantre 'pi tadabhāvādvicārataḥ  LiP 
ekatvamapi nāstyeva dvaitaṃ tatra kutastvaho 
evaṃ nāstyatha martyaṃ ca kuto 'mṛtamajodbhavaḥ  LiP 
ajñāna  source of saṃsāra
nāntaḥprajño bahiḥprajño na cobhayagatas tathā 
na prajñānaghanastvevaṃ na prājño jñānapūrvakaḥ  LiP 
viditaṃ nāsti vedyaṃ ca nirvāṇaṃ paramārthataḥ 
nirvāṇaṃ caiva kaivalyaṃ niḥśreyasamanāmayam  LiP 
amṛtaṃ cākṣaraṃ brahma paramātmā parāparam 
nirvikalpaṃ nirābhāsaṃ jñānaṃ paryāyavācakam  LiP 
prasannaṃ ca yadekāgraṃ tadā jñānamiti smṛtam 
ajñānamitaratsarvaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā  LiP 
itthaṃ prasannaṃ vijñānaṃ gurusaṃparkajaṃ dhruvam 
rāgadveṣānṛtakrodhaṃ kāmatṛṣṇādibhiḥ sadā  LiP 
aparāmṛṣṭamadyaiva vijñeyaṃ muktidaṃ tvidam 
ajñānamalapūrvatvāt puruṣo malinaḥ smṛtaḥ  LiP 
tatkṣayāddhi bhavenmuktir nānyathā janmakoṭibhiḥ 
jñānamekaṃ vinā nāsti puṇyapāpaparikṣayaḥ  LiP 
jñānam evābhyaset tasmān muktyarthaṃ brahmavittamāḥ 
jñānābhyāsāddhi vai puṃsāṃ buddhirbhavati nirmalā  LiP 
tasmātsadābhyasejjñānaṃ tanniṣṭhastatparāyaṇaḥ 
jñānenaikena tṛptasya tyaktasaṃgasya yoginaḥ  LiP 
kartavyaṃ nāsti viprendrā asti cettattvavinna ca 
iha loke pare cāpi kartavyaṃ nāsti tasya vai  LiP 
jīvanmukto yatas tasmād brahmavit paramārthataḥ 
jñānābhyāsarato nityaṃ jñānatattvārthavit svayam  LiP 
kartavyābhyāsamutsṛjya jñānamevādhigacchati 
varṇāśramābhimānī yas tyaktakrodho dvijottamāḥ  LiP 
anyatra ramate mūḍhaḥ so 'jñānī nātra saṃśayaḥ 
saṃsāraheturajñānaṃ saṃsārastanusaṃgrahaḥ  LiP 
mokṣahetus tathā jñānaṃ muktaḥ svātmanyavasthitaḥ 
ajñāne sati viprendrāḥ krodhādyā nātra saṃśayaḥ  LiP 
krodho harṣas tathā lobho moho dambho dvijottamāḥ 
dharmādharmau hi teṣāṃ ca tadvaśāttanusaṃgrahaḥ  LiP 
śarīre sati vai kleśaḥ so 'vidyāṃ saṃtyajedbudhaḥ 
avidyāṃ vidyayā hitvā sthitasyaiva ca yoginaḥ  LiP 
krodhādyā nāśamāyānti dharmādharmau ca vai dvijāḥ 
tatkṣayācca śarīreṇa na punaḥ samprayujyate  LiP 
sa eva muktaḥ saṃsārād duḥkhatrayavivarjitaḥ 
evaṃ jñānaṃ vinā nāsti dhyānaṃ dhyātur dvijarṣabhāḥ  LiP 
jñānaṃ gurorhi saṃparkān na vācā paramārthataḥ 
caturvyūhamiti jñātvā dhyātā dhyānaṃ samabhyaset  LiP 
sahajāgantukaṃ pāpam asthivāgudbhavaṃ tathā 
jñānāgnirdahate kṣipraṃ śuṣkendhanam ivānalaḥ  LiP 
jñānātparataraṃ nāsti sarvapāpavināśanam 
abhyasecca sadā jñānaṃ sarvasaṃgavivarjitaḥ  LiP 
jñāninaḥ sarvapāpāni jīryante nātra saṃśayaḥ 
krīḍannapi na lipyeta pāpairnānāvidhairapi  LiP 
importance of dhyāna
jñānaṃ yathā tathā dhyānaṃ tasmāddhyānaṃ samabhyaset 
dhyānaṃ nirviṣayaṃ proktam ādau saviṣayaṃ tathā  LiP 
ṣaṭprakāraṃ samabhyasya catuḥṣaḍdaśabhis tathā 
tathā dvādaśadhā caiva punaḥ ṣoḍaśadhā kramāt  LiP 
dvidhābhyasya ca yogīndro mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ 
śuddhajāṃbūnadākāraṃ vidhūmāṅgārasannibham  LiP 
pītaṃ raktaṃ sitaṃ vidyut koṭikoṭisamaprabham 
athavā brahmarandhrasthaṃ cittaṃ kṛtvā prayatnataḥ  LiP 
na sitaṃ vāsitaṃ pītaṃ na smared brahmavid bhavet 
ahiṃsakaḥ satyavādī asteyī sarvayatnataḥ  LiP 
parigrahavinirmukto brahmacārī dṛḍhavrataḥ 
saṃtuṣṭaḥ śaucasampannaḥ svādhyāyanirataḥ sadā  LiP 
madraktaścābhyaseddhyānaṃ gurusaṃparkajaṃ dhruvam 
na budhyati tathā dhyātā sthāpya cittaṃ dvijottamāḥ  LiP 
na cābhimanyate yogī na paśyati samantataḥ 
na ghrāti na śṛṇotyeva līnaḥ svātmani yaḥ svayam  LiP 
na ca sparśaṃ vijānāti sa vai samarasaḥ smṛtaḥ 
pārthive paṭale brahmā vāritattve hariḥ svayam  LiP 
vāhneye kālarudrākhyo vāyutattve maheśvaraḥ 
suṣire sa śivaḥ sākṣāt kramādevaṃ vicintayet  LiP 
kṣitau śarvaḥ smṛto devo hy apāṃ bhava iti smṛtaḥ 
rudra eva tathā vahnau ugro vāyau vyavasthitaḥ  LiP 
bhīmaḥ suṣiranāke 'sau bhāskare maṇḍale sthitaḥ 
īśānaḥ somabimbe ca mahādeva iti smṛtaḥ  LiP 
puṃsāṃ paśupatirdevaś cāṣṭadhāhaṃ vyavasthitaḥ 
kāṭhinyaṃ yattanau sarvaṃ pārthivaṃ parigīyate  LiP 
āpyaṃ dravamiti proktaṃ varṇākhyo vahnirucyate 
yatsaṃcarati tadvāyuḥ suṣiraṃ yaddvijottamāḥ  LiP 
tadākāśaṃ ca vijñānaṃ śabdajaṃ vyomasaṃbhavam 
tathaiva viprā vijñānaṃ sparśākhyaṃ vāyusaṃbhavam  LiP 
rūpaṃ vāhneyamityuktam āpyaṃ rasamayaṃ dvijāḥ 
gandhākhyaṃ pārthivaṃ bhūyaś cintayedbhāskaraṃ kramāt  LiP 
netre ca dakṣiṇe vāme somaṃ hṛdi vibhuṃ dvijāḥ 
ājānu pṛthivītattvam ānābher vārimaṇḍalam  LiP 
ākaṇṭhaṃ vahnitattvaṃ syāl lalāṭāntaṃ dvijottamāḥ 
vāyavyaṃ vai lalāṭādyaṃ vyomākhyaṃ vā śikhāgrakam  LiP 
haṃsākhyaṃ ca tato brahma vyomnaścordhvaṃ tataḥ param 
vyomākhyo vyomamadhyastho hy ayaṃ prāthamikaḥ smaret  LiP 
na jīvaḥ prakṛtiḥ sattvaṃ rajaścātha tamaḥ punaḥ 
mahāṃstathābhimānaś ca tanmātrāṇīndriyāṇi ca  LiP 
vyomādīni ca bhūtāni naiveha paramārthataḥ 
vyāpya tiṣṭhadyato viśvaṃ sthāṇurityabhidhīyate  LiP 
udeti sūryo bhītaś ca pavate vāta eva ca 
dyotate candramā vahnir jvalatyāpo vahanti ca  LiP 
dadhāti bhūmirākāśam avakāśaṃ dadāti ca 
tadājñayā tataṃ sarvaṃ tasmādvai cintayeddvijāḥ  LiP 
tenaivādhiṣṭhitaṃ tasmād etatsarvaṃ dvijottamāḥ 
sarvarūpamayaḥ śarva iti matvā smaredbhavam  LiP 
saṃsāraviṣataptānāṃ jñānadhyānāmṛtena vai 
pratīkāraḥ samākhyāto nānyathā dvijasattamāḥ  LiP 
jñānaṃ dharmodbhavaṃ sākṣāj jñānād vairāgyasaṃbhavaḥ 
vairāgyātparamaṃ jñānaṃ paramārthaprakāśakam  LiP 
jñānavairāgyayuktasya yogasiddhirdvijottamāḥ 
yogasiddhyā vimuktiḥ syāt sattvaniṣṭhasya nānyathā  LiP 
tamovidyāpadacchannaṃ citraṃ yatpadamavyayam 
sattvaśaktiṃ samāsthāya śivamabhyarcayeddvijāḥ  LiP 
yaḥ sattvaniṣṭho madbhakto madarcanaparāyaṇaḥ 
sarvato dharmaniṣṭhaś ca sadotsāhī samāhitaḥ  LiP 
sarvadvandvasaho dhīraḥ sarvabhūtahite rataḥ 
ṛjusvabhāvaḥ satataṃ svasthacitto mṛduḥ sadā  LiP 
amānī buddhimāñchāntas tyaktaspardho dvijottamāḥ 
sadā mumukṣurdharmajñaḥ svātmalakṣaṇalakṣaṇaḥ  LiP 
ṛṇatrayavinirmuktaḥ pūrvajanmani puṇyabhāk 
jarāyukto dvijo bhūtvā śraddhayā ca guroḥ kramāt  LiP 
anyathā vāpi śuśrūṣāṃ kṛtvā kṛtrimavarjitaḥ 
svargalokamanuprāpya bhuktvā bhogānanukramāt  LiP 
āsādya bhārataṃ varṣaṃ brahmavijjāyate dvijāḥ 
saṃparkājjñānamāsādya jñānino yogavidbhavet  LiP 
kramo 'yaṃ malapūrṇasya jñānaprāpterdvijottamāḥ 
tasmādanena mārgeṇa tyaktasaṃgo dṛḍhavrataḥ  LiP 
saṃsārakālakūṭākhyān mucyate munipuṅgavāḥ 
evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ proktaṃ mayā yuṣmākamacyutam  LiP 
jñānasyaiveha māhātmyaṃ prasaṃgādiha śobhanam 
evaṃ pāśupataṃ yogaṃ kathitaṃ tvīśvareṇa tu  LiP 
na deyaṃ yasya kasyāpi śivoktaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ 
dātavyaṃ yogine nityaṃ bhasmaniṣṭhāya supriyam  LiP 
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi saṃsāraśamanaṃ naraḥ 
sa yāti brahmasāyujyaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge saṃsāraviṣakathanaṃ nāma ṣaḍaśītitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
LiP  
sūta uvāca
niśamya te mahāprājñāḥ kumārādyāḥ pinākinam 
procuḥ praṇamya vai bhītāḥ prasannaṃ parameśvaram  LiP 
evaṃ cedanayā devyā haimavatyā maheśvara 
krīḍase vividhairbhogaiḥ kathaṃ vaktumihārhasi  LiP 
sūta uvāca
evamuktaḥ prahasyeśaḥ pinākī nīlalohitaḥ 
prāha tām aṃbikāṃ prekṣya praṇipatya sthitān dvijān  LiP 
bandhamokṣau na caiveha mama svecchā śarīriṇaḥ 
akartajñaḥ paśurjīvo vibhurbhoktā hyaṇuḥ pumān  LiP 
māyī ca māyayā baddhaḥ karmabhir yujyate tu saḥ 
jñānaṃ dhyānaṃ ca bandhaś ca mokṣo nāstyātmano dvijāḥ  LiP 
yadaivaṃ mayi vidvān yas tasyāpi na ca sarvataḥ 
eṣā vidyā hyahaṃ vedyaḥ prajñaiṣā ca śrutiḥ smṛtiḥ  LiP 
dhṛtireṣā mayā niṣṭhā jñānaśaktiḥ kriyā tathā 
icchākhyā ca tathā hyājñā dve vidye na ca saṃśayaḥ  LiP 
na hyeṣā prakṛtirjaivī vikṛtiś ca vicārataḥ 
vikāro naiva māyaiṣā sadasadvyaktivarjitā  LiP 
purā mamājñā madvaktrāt samutpannā sanātanī 
pañcavaktrā mahābhāgā jagatāmabhayapradā  LiP 
tāmājñāṃ sampraviśyāhaṃ cintayan jagatāṃ hitam 
saptaviṃśatprakāreṇa sarvaṃ vyāpyānayā śivaḥ  LiP 
tadāprabhṛti vai mokṣa pravṛttirdvijasattamāḥ 
sūta uvāca
evamuktvā tadāpaśyad bhavānīṃ parameśvaraḥ  LiP 
bhavānī ca tamālokya māyāmaharadavyayā 
te māyāmalanirmuktā munayaḥ prekṣya pārvatīm  LiP 
prītā babhūvurmuktāś ca tasmādeṣā parā gatiḥ 
umāśaṅkarayorbhedo nāstyeva paramārthataḥ  LiP 
dvidhāsau rūpamāsthāya sthita eva na saṃśayaḥ 
yadā vidvānasaṃgaḥ syād ājñayā parameṣṭhinaḥ  LiP 
tadā muktiḥ kṣaṇādeva nānyathā karmakoṭibhiḥ 
kramo 'vivakṣito bhūta vivṛddhaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ  LiP 
prasādena kṣaṇānmuktiḥ pratijñaiṣā na saṃśayaḥ 
garbhastho jāyamāno vā bālo vā taruṇo 'pi vā  LiP 
vṛddho vā mucyate jantuḥ prasādātparameṣṭhinaḥ 
aṇḍajaś codbhijjo vāpi svedajo vāpi mucyate  LiP 
prasādāddevadevasya nātra kāryā vicāraṇā 
eṣa eva jagannātho bandhamokṣakaraḥ śivaḥ  LiP 
bhūrbhūvaḥsvarmahaś caiva janaḥ sākṣāttapaḥ svayam 
satyalokas tathāṇḍānāṃ koṭikoṭiśatāni ca  LiP 
vigrahaṃ devadevasya tathāṇḍāvaraṇāṣṭakam 
saptadvīpeṣu sarveṣu parvateṣu vaneṣu ca  LiP 
samudreṣu ca sarveṣu vāyuskandheṣu sarvataḥ 
tathānyeṣu ca lokeṣu vasanti ca carācarāḥ  LiP 
sarve bhavāṃśajā nūnaṃ gatistveṣāṃ sa eva vai 
sarvo rudro namastasmai puruṣāya mahātmane  LiP 
viśvaṃ bhūtaṃ tathā jātaṃ bahudhā rudra eva saḥ 
rudrājñaiṣā sthitā devī hy anayā muktiraṃbikā  LiP 
ityevaṃ khecarāḥ siddhā jajalpuḥ prītamānasāḥ 
yadāvalokya tān sarvān prasādādanayāṃbikā  LiP 
tadā tiṣṭhanti sāyujyaṃ prāptāste khecarāḥ prabhoḥ  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge munimohaśamanaṃ nāma saptāśītitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
LiP  
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
kena yogena vai sūta guṇaprāptiḥ satāmiha 
aṇimādiguṇopetā bhavantyeveha yoginaḥ 
tatsarvaṃ vistarātsūta vaktumarhasi sāṃpratam  LiP 
sūta uvāca
ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi yogaṃ paramadurlabham 
pañcadhā saṃsmaredādau sthāpya citte sanātanam  LiP 
kalpayeccāsanaṃ padmaṃ somasūryāgnisaṃyutam 
ṣaḍviṃśacchaktisaṃyuktam aṣṭadhā ca dvijottamāḥ  LiP 
tataḥ ṣoḍaśadhā caiva punardvādaśadhā dvijāḥ 
smarec ca tat tathā madhye devyā devam umāpatim  LiP 
aṣṭaśaktisamāyuktam aṣṭamūrtimajaṃ prabhum 
tābhiścāṣṭavidhā rudrāś catuḥṣaṣṭividhāḥ punaḥ  LiP 
śaktayaś ca tathā sarvā guṇāṣṭakasamanvitāḥ 
evaṃ smaretkrameṇaiva labdhvā jñānamanuttamam  LiP 
evaṃ pāśupataṃ yogaṃ mokṣasiddhipradāyakam 
tasyāṇimādayo viprā nānyathā karmakoṭibhiḥ  LiP 
aiśvarya
tatrāṣṭaguṇamaiśvaryaṃ yogināṃ samudāhṛtam 
tatsarvaṃ kramayogena hy ucyamānaṃ nibodhata  LiP 
aṇimā laghimā caiva mahimā prāptireva ca 
prākāmyaṃ caiva sarvatra īśitvaṃ caiva sarvataḥ  LiP 
vaśitvamatha sarvatra yatra kāmāvasāyitā 
taccāpi trividhaṃ jñeyam aiśvaryaṃ sārvakāmikam  LiP 
sāvadyaṃ niravadyaṃ ca sūkṣmaṃ caiva pravartate 
sāvadyaṃ nāma yattatra pañcabhūtātmakaṃ smṛtam  LiP 
indriyāṇi manaścaiva ahaṅkāraś ca yaḥ smṛtaḥ 
tatra sūkṣmapravṛttistu pañcabhūtātmikā punaḥ  LiP 
indriyāṇi manaścitta buddhyahaṅkārasaṃjñitam 
tathā sarvamayaṃ caiva ātmasthā khyātireva ca  LiP 
saṃyoga eva trividhaḥ sūkṣmeṣveva pravartate 
punaraṣṭaguṇaścāpi sūkṣmeṣveva vidhīyate  LiP 
tasya rūpaṃ pravakṣyāmi yathāha bhagavānprabhuḥ 
trailokye sarvabhūteṣu yathāsya niyamaḥ smṛtaḥ  LiP 
aṇimādyaṃ tathāvyaktaṃ sarvatraiva pratiṣṭhitam 
trailokye sarvabhūtānāṃ duṣprāpyaṃ samudāhṛtam  LiP 
tat tasya bhavati prāpyaṃ prathamaṃ yogināṃ balam 
laṅghanaṃ plavanaṃ loke rūpamasya sadā bhavet  LiP 
śīghratvaṃ sarvabhūteṣu dvitīyaṃ tu padaṃ smṛtam 
trailokye sarvabhūtānāṃ mahimnā caiva vanditam  LiP 
mahitvaṃ cāpi loke 'smiṃs tṛtīyo yoga ucyate

prākāmān viṣayān bhuṅkte tathāpratihataḥ kvacit 
trailokye sarvabhūtānāṃ sukhaduḥkhaṃ pravartate  LiP 
īśo bhavati sarvatra pravibhāgena yogavit

pravartante 'sya cecchāto na bhavanti yathecchayā  LiP 
yogin is freed from attachment
na jāyate na mriyate chidyate na ca bhidyate 
na dahyate na muhyeta līyate na ca lipyate  LiP 
na kṣīyate na kṣarati khidyate na kadācana 
kriyate vā na sarvatra tathā vikriyate na ca  LiP

brahman guarantees liberation
tathā sukṛtakarmā tu phalaṃ svarge samaśnute  LiP 
tasmātsthānātpunaḥ śreṣṭho mānuṣyamupapadyate 
tasmādbrahma paraṃ saukhyaṃ brahma śāśvatam uttamam  LiP 
brahma eva hi seveta brahmaiva hi paraṃ sukham 
pariśramo hi yajñānāṃ mahatārthena vartate  LiP 
bhūyo mṛtyuvaśaṃ yāti tasmānmokṣaḥ paraṃ sukham 
athavā dhyānasaṃyukto brahmatattvaparāyaṇaḥ  LiP 
na tu cyāvayituṃ śakyo manvantaraśatairapi

viśvapādaśirogrīvaṃ viśveśaṃ viśvarūpiṇam

gobhir mahīṃ saṃpatate patatriṇo naivaṃ bhūyo janayatyevameva

yogena paśyenna ca cakṣuṣā punar nirindriyaṃ puruṣaṃ rukmavarṇam

paśyanti yuktyā hyacalaprakāśaṃ tadbhāvitāstejasā dīpyamānam 
apāṇipādodarapārśvajihvo hyatīndriyo vāpi susūkṣma ekaḥ  LiP

acetanāṃ sarvagatāṃ sūkṣmāṃ prasavadharmiṇīm

development of an embryo
atha celluptadharmā tu sāvaśeṣaiḥ svakarmabhiḥ 
tatastu brahmagarbhe vai śukraśoṇitasaṃyute  LiP

tatastu garbhakālena kalalaṃ nāma jāyate  LiP

hell
tataḥ svakarmabhiḥ pāpair nirayaṃ samprapadyate  LiP 
asipatravanaṃ caiva śālmalicchedanaṃ tathā 
tāḍanaṃ bhakṣaṇaṃ caiva pūyaśoṇitabhakṣaṇam  LiP 
yathā hyāpastu saṃchinnāḥ saṃśleṣmam upayānti vai 
tathā chinnāś ca bhinnāśca yātanāsthānam āgatāḥ  LiP 
evaṃ jīvāstu taiḥ pāpais tapyamānāḥ svayaṃkṛtaiḥ 
prāpnuyuḥ karmabhiḥ śeṣair duḥkhaṃ vā yadi vetarat  LiP 
ekenaiva tu gantavyaṃ sarvamutsṛjya vai janam 
ekenaiva tu bhoktavyaṃ tasmātsukṛtamācaret  LiP 
na hyenaṃ prasthitaṃ kaścid gacchantam anugacchati 
yadanena kṛtaṃ karma tadenamanugacchati  LiP 
te nityaṃ yamaviṣayeṣu sampravṛttāḥ krośantaḥ satatamaniṣṭasaṃprayogaiḥ 
śuṣyante parigatavedanāḥ śarīrā bahvībhiḥ subhṛśamanantayātanābhiḥ  LiP 
diff forms of rebirth
karmaṇā manasā vācā yadabhīkṣṇaṃ niṣevate 
tadabhyāso haratyenaṃ tasmātkalyāṇamācaret  LiP 
anādimānprabandhaḥ syāt pūrvakarmaṇi dehinaḥ 
saṃsāraṃ tāmasaṃ ghoraṃ ṣaḍvidhaṃ pratipadyate  LiP 
mānuṣyātpaśubhāvaś ca paśubhāvān mṛgo bhavet 
mṛgatvātpakṣibhāvaś ca tasmāccaiva sarīsṛpaḥ  LiP 
sarīsṛpatvādgacchedvai sthāvaratvaṃ na saṃśayaḥ 
sthāvaratve punaḥ prāpte yāvad unmilate janaḥ  LiP 
kulālacakravadbhrāntas tatraiva parivartate 
ityevaṃ hi manuṣyādiḥ saṃsāraḥ sthāvarāntikaḥ  LiP

brāhme tu kevalaṃ sattvaṃ sthāvare kevalaṃ tamaḥ  LiP 
caturdaśānāṃ sthānānāṃ madhye viṣṭambhakaṃ rajaḥ 
marmasu chidyamāneṣu vedanārtasya dehinaḥ  LiP 
tatastatparamaṃ brahma kathaṃ vipraḥ smariṣyati 
saṃsāraḥ pūrvadharmasya bhāvanābhiḥ praṇoditaḥ  LiP 
mānuṣaṃ bhajate nityaṃ tasmāddhyānaṃ samācaret 
caturdaśavidhaṃ hyetad buddhvā saṃsāramaṇḍalam  LiP 
nityaṃ samārabheddharmaṃ saṃsārabhayapīḍitaḥ 
tatastarati saṃsāraṃ krameṇa parivartitaḥ  LiP 
tasmācca satataṃ yukto dhyānatatparayuñjakaḥ 
tathā samārabhedyogaṃ yathātmānaṃ sa paśyati  LiP 
eṣa āpaḥ paraṃ jyotir eṣa seturanuttamaḥ 
vivṛtyā hyeṣa saṃbhedād bhūtānāṃ caiva śāśvataḥ  LiP 
tadenaṃ setumātmānam agniṃ vai viśvatomukham 
hṛdisthaṃ sarvabhūtānām upāsīta maheśvaram  LiP 
tathāntaḥ saṃsthitaṃ devaṃ svaśaktyā parimaṇḍitam 
aṣṭadhā cāṣṭadhā caiva tathā cāṣṭavidhena ca  LiP 
sṛṣṭyarthaṃ saṃsthitaṃ vahniṃ saṃkṣipya ca hṛdi sthitam 
dhyātvā yathāvaddeveśaṃ rudraṃ bhuvananāyakam  LiP 
hutvā pañcāhutīḥ samyak taccintāgatamānasaḥ 
vaiśvānaraṃ hṛdisthaṃ tu yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ  LiP 
āpaḥ pūtāḥ sakṛtprāśya tūṣṇīṃ hutvā hyupāviśan 
prāṇāyeti tatastasya prathamā hyāhutiḥ smṛtā  LiP 
apānāya dvitīyā ca vyānāyeti tathā parā 
udānāya caturthī syāt samānāyeti pañcamī  LiP 
svāhākāraiḥ pṛthagghutvā śeṣaṃ bhuñjīta kāmataḥ 
apaḥ punaḥ sakṛtprāśya ācamya hṛdayaṃ spṛśet  LiP 
prāṇānāṃ granthirasyātmā rudro hyātmā viśāntakaḥ 
rudro vai hyātmanaḥ prāṇa evamāpyāyayetsvayam  LiP 
prāṇe niviṣṭo vai rudras tasmātprāṇamayaḥ svayam 
prāṇāya caiva rudrāya juhotyamṛtamuttamam  LiP 
śivāviśeha māmīśa svāhā brahmātmane svayam 
evaṃ pañcāhutīścaiva prabhuḥ prīṇātu śāśvataḥ  LiP 
puruṣo 'si pure śeṣe tvaṃ aṅguṣṭhapramāṇataḥ 
āśritaścaiva cāṅguṣṭham īśaḥ paramakāraṇam  LiP 
sarvasya jagataścaiva prabhuḥ prīṇātu śāśvataḥ 
tvaṃ devānāmasi jyeṣṭho rudrastvaṃ ca puro vṛṣā  LiP 
mṛdustvamannamasmabhyam etadastu hutaṃ tava 
ityevaṃ kathitaṃ sarvaṃ guṇaprāptiviśeṣataḥ  LiP 
yogācāraḥ svayaṃ tena brahmaṇā kathitaḥ purā 
evaṃ pāśupataṃ jñānaṃ jñātavyaṃ ca prayatnataḥ  LiP 
bhasmasnāyī bhaven nityaṃ bhasmaliptaḥ sadā bhavet 
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi śrāvayedvā dvijottamān  LiP 
daive karmaṇi pitrye vā sa yāti paramāṃ gatim  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge 'ṇimādyaṣṭasiddhitriguṇasaṃsāraprāgnau homādivarṇanaṃ nāmāṣṭāśītitamo 'dhyāyaḥ

sūta uvāca
ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi śaucācārasya lakṣaṇam 
yadanuṣṭhāya śuddhātmā paretya gatimāpnuyāt  LiP

cakṣuḥpūtaṃ carenmārgaṃ vastrapūtaṃ jalaṃ pibet 
satyapūtaṃ vadedvākyaṃ manaḥpūtaṃ samācaret  LiP 
matsyagṛhyasya yatpāpaṃ ṣaṇmāsābhyantare bhavet

tridhā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya śudhyate nātra saṃśayaḥ  LiP 
ātithyaśrāddhayajñeṣu na gacchedyogavitkvacit 
evaṃ hyahiṃsako yogī bhavediti vicāritam  LiP 
rules for bhaikṣyacaraṇa
vahnau vidhūme 'tyaṅgāre sarvasminbhuktavajjane 
carettu matimān bhaikṣyaṃ na tu teṣveva nityaśaḥ  LiP 
athainam avamanyante pare paribhavanti ca 
tathā yuktaṃ caredbhaikṣyaṃ satāṃ dharmamadūṣayan  LiP 
bhaikṣyaṃ caredvanastheṣu yāyāvaragṛheṣu ca 
śreṣṭhā tu prathamā hīyaṃ vṛttirasyopajāyate  LiP 
ata ūrdhvaṃ gṛhastheṣu śīlīneṣu careddvijāḥ 
śraddadhāneṣu dānteṣu śrotriyeṣu mahātmasu  LiP 
ata ūrdhvaṃ punaścāpi aduṣṭāpatiteṣu ca 
bhaikṣyacaryā hi varṇeṣu jaghanyā vṛttirucyate  LiP 
bhaikṣyaṃ yavāgūstakraṃ vā payo yāvakameva ca 
phalamūlādi pakvaṃ vā kaṇapiṇyākasaktavaḥ  LiP 
ityeva te mayā proktā yogināṃ siddhivarddhanāḥ 
āhārāsteṣu siddheṣu śreṣṭhaṃ bhaikṣyamiti smṛtam  LiP 
abbinduṃ yaḥ kuśāgreṇa māsi māsi samaśnute 
nyāyato yaścaredbhaikṣyaṃ pūrvoktātsa viśiṣyate  LiP 
jarāmaraṇagarbhebhyo bhītasya narakādiṣu 
evaṃ dāyayate tasmāt tadbhaikṣyamiti saṃsmṛtam  LiP 
dadhibhakṣāḥ payobhakṣā ye cānye jīvakṣīṇakāḥ 
sarve te bhaikṣyabhakṣasya kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm  LiP 
bhasmaśāyī bhavennityaṃ bhikṣācārī jitendriyaḥ 
ya icchet paramaṃ sthānaṃ vrataṃ pāśupataṃ caret  LiP 
behaviour of a yogin
yogināṃ caiva sarveṣāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ cāndrāyaṇaṃ bhavet 
ekaṃ dve trīṇi catvāri śaktito vā samācaret  LiP 
asteyaṃ brahmacaryaṃ ca alobhastyāga eva ca 
vratāni pañca bhikṣūṇām ahiṃsā paramā tviha  LiP 
akrodho guruśuśrūṣā śaucamāhāralāghavam 
nityaṃ svādhyāya ityete niyamāḥ parikīrtitāḥ  LiP 
bījayoniguṇā vastu bandhaḥ karmabhir eva ca 
yathā dvipa ivāraṇye manuṣyāṇāṃ vidhīyate  LiP 
devaistulyāḥ sarvayajñakriyāstu yajñājjāpyaṃ jñānamāhuś ca jāpyāt 
jñānād dhyānaṃ saṃgarāgādapetaṃ tasminprāpte śāśvatasyopalambhaḥ  LiP 
damaḥ śamaḥ satyamakalmaṣatvaṃ maunaṃ ca bhūteṣvakhileṣu cārjavam 
atīndriyaṃ jñānamidaṃ tathā śivaṃ prāhus tathā jñānaviśuddhabuddhayaḥ  LiP 
samāhito brahmaparo 'pramādī śucis tathaikāntaratir jitendriyaḥ 
samāpnuyādyogamimaṃ mahātmā maharṣayaścaivam aninditāmalāḥ  LiP 
prāpyate 'bhimatān deśān aṅkuśena nivāritaḥ 
etanmārgeṇa śuddhena dagdhabījo hyakalmaṣaḥ  LiP 
sadācāraratāḥ śāntāḥ svadharmaparipālakāḥ 
sarvāṃllokān vinirjitya brahmalokaṃ vrajanti te  LiP 
salutation of superiors
pitāmahenopadiṣṭo dharmaḥ sākṣātsanātanaḥ 
sarvalokopakārārthaṃ śṛṇudhvaṃ pravadāmi vaḥ  LiP 
gurūpadeśayuktānāṃ vṛddhānāṃ kramavarttinām 
abhyutthānādikaṃ sarvaṃ praṇāmaṃ caiva kārayet  LiP 
aṣṭāṅgapraṇipātena tridhā nyastena suvratāḥ 
triḥpradakṣiṇayogena vandyo vai brahmaṇo guruḥ  LiP 
jyeṣṭhānye 'pi ca te sarve vandanīyā vijānatā 
ājñābhaṅgaṃ na kurvīta yadīcchet siddhim uttamām  LiP 
dhātuśūnyabilakṣetra kṣudramantropajīvanam 
viṣagrahaviḍambādīn varjayet sarvayatnataḥ  LiP 
kaitavaṃ vittaśāṭhyaṃ ca paiśunyaṃ varjayetsadā 
atihāsam avaṣṭambhaṃ līlāsvecchāpravartanam  LiP 
varjayetsarvayatnena gurūṇāmapi saṃnidhau 
tadvākyapratikūlaṃ ca ayuktaṃ vai gurorvacaḥ  LiP 
na vadetsarvayatnena aniṣṭaṃ na smaretsadā 
yatīnāmāsanaṃ vastraṃ daṇḍādyaṃ pāduke tathā  LiP 
mālyaṃ ca śayanasthānaṃ pātraṃ chāyāṃ ca yatnataḥ 
yajñopakaraṇāṅgaṃ ca na spṛśed vai padena ca  LiP 
devadrohaṃ gurudrohaṃ na kuryātsarvayatnataḥ 
kṛtvā pramādato viprāḥ praṇavasyāyutaṃ japet  LiP 
devadrohagurudrohāt koṭimātreṇa śudhyati 
mahāpātakaśuddhyarthaṃ tathaiva ca yathāvidhi  LiP 
pātakī ca tadardhena śudhyate vṛttavānyadi 
upapātakinaḥ sarve tadardhenaiva suvratāḥ  LiP 
saṃdhyālope kṛte vipraḥ trirāvṛttyaiva śudhyati 
āhnikacchedane jāte śatamekamudāhṛtam  LiP 
laṅghane samayānāṃ tu abhakṣyasya ca bhakṣaṇe 
avācyavācane caiva sahasrācchuddhirucyate  LiP 
kākolūkakapotānāṃ pakṣiṇāmapi ghātane 
śatamaṣṭottaraṃ japtvā mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ  LiP 
yaḥ punastattvavettā ca brahmavid brāhmaṇottamaḥ 
smaraṇācchuddhimāpnoti nātra kāryā vicāraṇā  LiP 
naivamātmavidāmasti prāyaścittāni codanā 
viśvasyaiva hi te śuddhā brahmavidyāvido janāḥ  LiP 
yogadhyānaikaniṣṭhāś ca nirlepāḥ kāñcanaṃ yathā 
śuddhānāṃ śodhanaṃ nāsti viśuddhā brahmavidyayā  LiP 
cleaning of water
uddhṛtānuṣṇaphenābhiḥ pūtābhir vastracakṣuṣā 
adbhiḥ samācaretsarvaṃ varjayetkaluṣodakam  LiP 
gandhavarṇarasairduṣṭam aśucisthānasaṃsthitam 
paṅkāśmadūṣitaṃ caiva sāmudraṃ palvalodakam  LiP 
saśaivālaṃ tathānyairvā doṣairduṣṭaṃ vivarjayet 
cleaning of clothes
vastraśaucānvitaḥ kuryāt sarvakāryāṇi vai dvijāḥ  LiP 
namaskārādikaṃ sarvaṃ guruśuśrūṣaṇādikam 
vastraśaucavihīnātmā hy aśucirnātra saṃśayaḥ  LiP 
devakāryopayuktānāṃ pratyahaṃ śaucamiṣyate 
itareṣāṃ hi vastrāṇāṃ śaucaṃ kāryaṃ malāgame  LiP 
varjayetsarvayatnena vāso 'nyair vidhṛtaṃ dvijāḥ 
kauśeyāvikayo rūkṣaiḥ kṣaumāṇāṃ gaurasarṣapaiḥ  LiP 
śrīphalairaṃśupaṭṭānāṃ kutapānāmariṣṭakaiḥ 
carmaṇāṃ vidalānāṃ ca vetrāṇāṃ vastravanmatam  LiP 
valkalānāṃ tu sarveṣāṃ chatracāmarayorapi 
cailavacchaucamākhyātaṃ brahmavidbhir munīśvaraiḥ  LiP 
cleaning of objects
bhasmanā śudhyate kāṃsyaṃ kṣāreṇāyasam ucyate 
tāmramamlena vai viprās trapusīsakayorapi  LiP 
haimam adbhiḥ śubhaṃ pātraṃ raupyapātraṃ dvijottamāḥ 
maṇyaśmaśaṅkhamuktānāṃ śaucaṃ taijasavatsmṛtam  LiP 
agner apāṃ ca saṃyogād atyantopahatasya ca 
rasānāmiha sarveṣāṃ śuddhirutplavanaṃ smṛtam  LiP 
tṛṇakāṣṭhādivastūnāṃ śubhenābhyukṣaṇaṃ smṛtam 
uṣṇena vāriṇā śuddhis tathā sruksruvayorapi  LiP 
tathaiva yajñapātrāṇāṃ muśalolūkhalasya ca 
śṛṅgāsthidārudantānāṃ takṣaṇenaiva śodhanam  LiP 
saṃhatānāṃ mahābhāgā dravyāṇāṃ prokṣaṇaṃ smṛtam 
asaṃhatānāṃ dravyāṇāṃ pratyekaṃ śaucamucyate  LiP 
abhuktarāśidhānyānām ekadeśasya dūṣaṇe 
tāvanmātraṃ samuddhṛtya prokṣayedvai kuśāṃbhasā  LiP 
śākamūlaphalādīnāṃ dhānyavacchuddhiriṣyate 
mārjanonmārjanair veśma punaḥpākena mṛnmayam  LiP 
ullekhanenāñjanena tathā saṃmārjanena ca 
gonivāsena vai śuddhā secanena dharā smṛtā  LiP 
bhūmistham udakaṃ śuddhaṃ vaitṛṣṇyaṃ yatra gaurvrajet 
avyāptaṃ yadamedhyena gandhavarṇarasānvitam  LiP 
vatsaḥ śuciḥ prasravaṇe śakuniḥ phalapātane 
svadārāsyaṃ gṛhasthānāṃ ratau bhāryābhikāṅkṣayā  LiP 
hastābhyāṃ kṣālitaṃ vastraṃ kāruṇā ca yathāvidhi 
kuśāṃbunā susaṃprokṣya gṛhṇīyāddharmavittamaḥ  LiP 
paṇyaṃ prasāritaṃ caiva varṇāśramavibhāgaśaḥ 
śucirākarajaṃ teṣāṃ śvā mṛgagrahaṇe śuciḥ  LiP 
chāyā ca vipluṣo viprā makṣikādyā dvijottamāḥ 
rajo bhūr vāyur agniś ca medhyāni sparśane sadā  LiP 
suptvā bhuktvā ca vai viprāḥ kṣuttvā pītvā ca vai tathā 
ṣṭhīvitvādhyayanādau ca śucirapyācametpunaḥ  LiP 
pādau spṛśanti ye cāpi parācamanabindavaḥ 
te pārthivaiḥ samā jñeyā na tairaprayato bhavet  LiP 
kṛtvā ca maithunaṃ spṛṣṭvā patitaṃ kukkuṭādikam 
sūkaraṃ caiva kākādi śvānamuṣṭraṃ kharaṃ tathā  LiP 
yūpaṃ cāṇḍālakādyāṃś ca spṛṣṭvā snānena śudhyati 
rajasvalāṃ sūtikāṃ ca na spṛśedantyajāmapi  LiP 
sūtikāśaucasaṃyuktaḥ śāvāśaucasamanvitaḥ 
saṃspṛśenna rajastāsāṃ spṛṣṭvā snātvaiva śudhyati  LiP 
undefilable people
naivāśaucaṃ yatīnāṃ ca vanasthabrahmacāriṇām 
naiṣṭhikānāṃ nṛpāṇāṃ ca maṇḍalīnāṃ ca suvratāḥ  LiP 
tataḥ kāryavirodhāddhi nṛpāṇāṃ nānyathā bhavet 
vaikhānasānāṃ viprāṇāṃ patitānāmasaṃbhavāt  LiP 
asaṃcayād dvijānāṃ ca snānamātreṇa nānyathā 
tathā saṃnihitānāṃ ca yajñārthaṃ dīkṣitasya ca  LiP 
ekāhād yajñayājināṃ śuddhiruktā svayaṃbhuvā 
tatastvadhītaśākhānāṃ caturbhiḥ sarvadehinām  LiP 
duration of defilement
sūtakaṃ pretakaṃ nāsti tryahād ūrdhvam amutra vai 
arvāg ekādaśāhāntaṃ bāndhavānāṃ dvijottamāḥ  LiP 
snānamātreṇa vai śuddhir maraṇe samupasthite 
tata ṛtutrayādarvāg ekāhaḥ parigīyate  LiP 
saptavarṣāt tataścārvāk trirātraṃ hi tataḥ param 
daśāhaṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ vai prathame 'hani vā pituḥ  LiP 
daśāhaṃ sūtikāśaucaṃ māturapyevamavyayāḥ 
arvāk trivarṣātsnānena bāndhavānāṃ pituḥ sadā  LiP 
aṣṭābdād ekarātreṇa śuddhiḥ syād bāndhavasya tu 
dvādaśābdāttataścārvāk trirātraṃ strīṣu suvratāḥ  LiP 
sapiṇḍatā ca puruṣe saptame vinivartate 
atikrānte daśāhe tu trirātramaśucirbhavet  LiP 
tataḥ saṃnihito vipraś cārvāk pūrvaṃ tadeva vai 
saṃvatsare vyatīte tu snānamātreṇa śudhyati  LiP 
purification after touching a dead body
spṛṣṭvā pretaṃ trirātreṇa dharmārthaṃ snānamucyate 
dāhakānāṃ ca netṝṇāṃ snānamātramabāndhave  LiP 
anugamya ca vai snātvā ghṛtaṃ prāśya viśudhyati 
ācāryamaraṇe caiva trirātraṃ śrotriye mṛte  LiP 
pakṣiṇī mātulānāṃ ca sodarāṇāṃ ca vā dvijāḥ 
bhūpānāṃ maṇḍalīnāṃ ca sadyo nīrāṣṭravāsinām  LiP 
kevalaṃ dvādaśāhena kṣattriyāṇāṃ dvijottamāḥ 
nābhiṣiktasya cāśaucaṃ saṃpramādeṣu vai raṇe  LiP 
vaiśyaḥ pañcadaśāhena śūdro māsena śudhyati 
iti saṃkṣepataḥ proktā dravyaśuddhiranuttamā  LiP 
aśaucaṃ cānupūrvyeṇa yatīnāṃ naiva vidyate 
menstruation
tretāprabhṛti nārīṇāṃ māsi māsyārtavaṃ dvijāḥ  LiP 
kṛte sakṛd yugavaśāj jāyante vai sahaiva tu 
prayānti ca mahābhāgā bhāryābhiḥ kuravo yathā  LiP 
varṇāśramavyavasthā ca tretāprabhṛti suvratāḥ 
bhārate dakṣiṇe varṣe vyavasthā netareṣvatha  LiP 
mahāvīte suvīte ca jaṃbūdvīpe tathāṣṭasu 
śākadvīpādiṣu prokto dharmo vai bhārate yathā  LiP 
rasollāsā kṛte vṛttis tretāyāṃ gṛhavṛkṣajā 
saivārtavakṛtād doṣād rāgadveṣādibhir nṛṇām  LiP 
maithunātkāmato viprās tathaiva paruṣādibhiḥ 
yavādyāḥ samprajāyante grāmyāraṇyāścaturdaśa  LiP 
oṣadhyaś ca rajodoṣāḥ strīṇāṃ rāgādibhir nṛṇām 
akālakṛṣṭā vidhvastāḥ punarutpāditās tathā  LiP 
tasmātsarvaprayatnena na saṃbhāṣyā rajasvalā 
prathame 'hani cāṇḍālī yathā varjyā tathāṅganā  LiP 
dvitīye 'hani viprā hi yathā vai brahmaghātinī 
tṛtīye 'hni tadardhena caturthe 'hani suvratāḥ  LiP 
snātvārdhamāsāt saṃśuddhā tataḥ śuddhirbhaviṣyati 
ā ṣoḍaśāt tataḥ strīṇāṃ mūtravacchaucamiṣyate  LiP 
pañcarātraṃ tathāspṛśyā rajasā vartate yadi 
sā viṃśaddivasādūrdhvaṃ rajasā pūrvavattathā  LiP 
snānaṃ śaucaṃ tathā gānaṃ rodanaṃ hasanaṃ tathā 
yānamabhyañjanaṃ nārī dyūtaṃ caivānulepanam  LiP 
divāsvapnaṃ viśeṣeṇa tathā vai dantadhāvanam 
maithunaṃ mānasaṃ vāpi vācikaṃ devatārcanam  LiP 
varjayetsarvayatnena namaskāraṃ rajasvalā 
rajasvalāṅganāsparśa saṃbhāṣe ca rajasvalā  LiP 
saṃtyāgaṃ caiva vastrāṇāṃ varjayetsarvayatnataḥ 
snātvānyapuruṣaṃ nārī na spṛśettu rajasvalā  LiP 
īkṣayedbhāskaraṃ devaṃ brahmakūrcaṃ tataḥ pibet 
kevalaṃ pañcagavyaṃ vā kṣīraṃ vā cātmaśuddhaye  LiP 
caturthyāṃ strī na gamyā tu gato 'lpāyuḥ prasūyate 
vidyāhīnaṃ vratabhraṣṭaṃ patitaṃ pāradārikam  LiP 
dāridryārṇavamagnaṃ ca tanayaṃ sā prasūyate 
kanyārthinaiva gantavyā pañcamyāṃ vidhivatpunaḥ  LiP 
raktādhikyādbhavennārī śukrādhikye bhavetpumān 
same napuṃsakaṃ caiva pañcamyāṃ kanyakā bhavet  LiP 
ṣaṣṭhyāṃ gamyā mahābhāgā satputrajananī bhavet 
putratvaṃ vyañjayettasya jātaputro mahādyutiḥ  LiP 
pumiti narakasyākhyā duḥkhaṃ ca narakaṃ viduḥ 
puṃsastrāṇānvitaṃ putraṃ tathābhūtaṃ prasūyate  LiP 
saptamyāṃ caiva kanyārthī gacchetsaiva prasūyate 
aṣṭamyāṃ sarvasampannaṃ tanayaṃ samprasūyate  LiP 
navamyāṃ dārikāyārthī daśamyāṃ paṇḍito bhavet 
ekādaśyāṃ tathā nārīṃ janayetsaiva pūrvavat  LiP 
dvādaśyāṃ dharmatattvajñaṃ śrautasmārtapravartakam 
trayodaśyāṃ jaḍāṃ nārīṃ sarvasaṃkarakāriṇīm  LiP 
janayatyaṅganā yasmān na gacchetsarvayatnataḥ 
caturdaśyāṃ yadā gacchet sā putrajananī bhavet  LiP 
pañcadaśyāṃ ca dharmiṣṭhāṃ ṣoḍaśyāṃ jñānapāragam 
strīṇāṃ vai maithune kāle vāmapārśve prabhañjanaḥ  LiP 
caredyadi bhavennārī pumāṃsaṃ dakṣiṇe labhet 
strīṇāṃ maithunakāle tu pāpagrahavivarjite  LiP 
uktakāle śucirbhūtvā śuddhāṃ gacchecchucismitām 
ityevaṃ saṃprasaṃgena yatīnāṃ dharmasaṃgrahe  LiP 
sarveṣāmeva bhūtānāṃ sadācāraḥ prakīrtitaḥ 
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyād vāpi sadācāraṃ śucirnaraḥ  LiP 
śrāvayedvā yathānyāyaṃ brāhmaṇān dagdhakilbiṣān 
brahmalokamanuprāpya brahmaṇā saha modate  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge sadācārakathanaṃ nāmaikonanavatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ

sūta uvāca
ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi yatīnāmiha niścitam 
prāyaścittaṃ śivaproktaṃ yatīnāṃ pāpaśodhanam  LiP 
pāpaṃ hi trividhaṃ jñeyaṃ vāṅmanaḥkāyasaṃbhavam 
satataṃ hi divā rātrau yenedaṃ veṣṭyate jagat  LiP 
tatkarmaṇā vināpyeṣa tiṣṭhatīti parā śrutiḥ 
kṣaṇamevaṃ prayojyaṃ tu āyuṣyaṃ tu vidhāraṇam  LiP 
bhavedyogo 'pramattasya yogo hi paramaṃ balam 
na hi yogātparaṃ kiṃcin narāṇāṃ dṛśyate śubham  LiP 
tasmād yogaṃ praśaṃsanti dharmayuktā manīṣiṇaḥ 
avidyāṃ vidyayā jitvā prāpyaiśvaryamanuttamam  LiP 
dṛṣṭvā parāvaraṃ dhīrāḥ paraṃ gacchanti tatpadam 
vratāni yāni bhikṣūṇāṃ tathaivopavratāni ca  LiP 
ekaikātikrame teṣāṃ prāyaścittaṃ vidhīyate 
upetya tu striyaṃ kāmāt prāyaścittaṃ vinirdiśet  LiP 
prāṇāyāmasamāyuktaṃ caretsāṃtapanaṃ vratam 
tataścarati nirdeśāt kṛcchraṃ cānte samāhitaḥ  LiP 
punar āśramam āgatya caredbhikṣuratandritaḥ 
na dharmayuktamanṛtaṃ hinastīti manīṣiṇaḥ  LiP 
tathāpi na ca kartavyaṃ prasaṃgo hyeṣa dāruṇaḥ 
ahorātropavāsaś ca prāṇāyāmaśataṃ tathā  LiP 
asadvādo na kartavyo yatinā dharmalipsunā 
paramāpadgatenāpi na kāryaṃ steyamapyuta  LiP 
importance of possession
steyādabhyadhikaḥ kaścin nāstyadharma iti śrutiḥ 
hiṃsā hyeṣā parā sṛṣṭā stainyaṃ vai kathitaṃ tathā  LiP 
yadetaddraviṇaṃ nāma prāṇā hyete bahiścarāḥ 
sa tasya harate prāṇān yo yasya harate dhanam  LiP 
evaṃ kṛtvā suduṣṭātmā bhinnavṛtto vratāccyutaḥ 
bhūyo nirvedamāpannaś careccāndrāyaṇaṃ vratam  LiP 
vidhinā śāstradṛṣṭena saṃvatsaramiti śrutiḥ 
tataḥ saṃvatsarasyānte bhūyaḥ prakṣīṇakalmaṣaḥ 
punarnirvedamāpannaś caredbhikṣuratandritaḥ  LiP 
ahiṃsā sarvabhūtānāṃ karmaṇā manasā girā 
akāmādapi hiṃseta yadi bhikṣuḥ paśūn kṛmīn  LiP 
kṛcchrātikṛcchraṃ kurvīta cāndrāyaṇamathāpi vā 
skandedindriyadaurbalyāt striyaṃ dṛṣṭvā yatiryadi  LiP 
tena dhārayitavyā vai prāṇāyāmāstu ṣoḍaśa 
divā skannasya viprasya prāyaścittaṃ vidhīyate  LiP 
trirātramupavāsāś ca prāṇāyāmaśataṃ tathā 
rātrau skannaḥ śuciḥ snātvā dvādaśaiva tu dhāraṇā  LiP 
prāṇāyāmena śuddhātmā virajā jāyate dvijāḥ 
ekānnaṃ madhumāṃsaṃ vā aśṛtānnaṃ tathaiva ca  LiP 
abhojyāni yatīnāṃ tu pratyakṣalavaṇāni ca 
ekaikātikramātteṣāṃ prāyaścittaṃ vidhīyate  LiP 
prājāpatyena kṛcchreṇa tataḥ pāpātpramucyate 
vyatikramāś ca ye kecid vāṅmanaḥkāyasaṃbhavāḥ  LiP 
sadbhiḥ saha viniścitya yadbrūyustatsamācaret  LiP 
careddhi śuddhaḥ samaloṣṭakāñcanaḥ samastabhūteṣu ca satsamāhitaḥ 
sthānaṃ dhruvaṃ śāśvatamavyayaṃ tu paraṃ hi gatvā na punarhi jāyate  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge yatiprāyaścittaṃ nāma navatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
LiP  
sūta uvāca
ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi ariṣṭāni nibodhata 
yena jñānaviśeṣeṇa mṛtyuṃ paśyanti yoginaḥ  LiP 
arundhatīṃ dhruvaṃ caiva somachāyāṃ mahāpatham 
yo na paśyenna jīvetsa naraḥ saṃvatsarātparam  LiP 
ariśmavantam ādityaṃ raśmivantaṃ ca pāvakam 
yaḥ paśyati na jīvedvai māsādekādaśātparam  LiP 
vamenmūtraṃ purīṣaṃ ca suvarṇaṃ rajataṃ tathā 
pratyakṣamathavā svapne daśamāsānna jīvati  LiP 
rukmavarṇaṃ drumaṃ paśyed gandharvanagarāṇi ca 
paśyet pretapiśācāṃś ca navamāsān sa jīvati  LiP 
akasmācca bhavetsthūlo hy akasmācca kṛśo bhavet 
prakṛteś ca nivarteta cāṣṭau māsāṃś ca jīvati  LiP 
agrataḥ pṛṣṭhato vāpi khaṇḍaṃ yasya padaṃ bhavet 
pāṃsuke kardame vāpi saptamāsānsa jīvati  LiP 
kākaḥ kapoto gṛdhro vā nilīyedyasya mūrdhani 
kravyādo vā khago yasya ṣaṇmāsān nātivartate  LiP 
gacched vāyasapaṅktībhiḥ pāṃsuvarṣeṇa vā punaḥ 
svacchāyāṃ vikṛtāṃ paśyec catuḥpañca sa jīvati  LiP 
anabhre vidyutaṃ paśyed dakṣiṇāṃ diśamāsthitām 
udake dhanur aindraṃ vā trīṇi dvau vā sa jīvati  LiP 
apsu vā yadi vādarśe yo hyātmānaṃ na paśyati 
aśiraskaṃ tathā paśyen māsād ūrdhvaṃ na jīvati  LiP 
śavagandhi bhavedgātraṃ vasāgandhamathāpi vā 
mṛtyurhyupāgatastasya ardhamāsānna jīvati  LiP 
yasya vai snātamātrasya hṛdayaṃ pariśuṣyati 
dhūmaṃ vā mastakātpaśyed daśāhānna sa jīvati  LiP 
saṃbhinno māruto yasya marmasthānāni kṛntati 
adbhiḥ spṛṣṭo na hṛṣyeta tasya mṛtyurupasthitaḥ  LiP 
ṛkṣavānarayuktena rathenāśāṃ ca dakṣiṇām 
gāyannṛtyan vrajet svapne vidyānmṛtyurupasthitaḥ  LiP 
kṛṣṇāṃbaradharā śyāmā gāyantī vāpyathāṅganā 
yaṃ nayeddakṣiṇāmāśāṃ svapne so 'pi na jīvati  LiP 
chidraṃ vā svasya kaṇṭhasya svapne yo vīkṣate naraḥ 
nagnaṃ vā śramaṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā vidyānmṛtyumupasthitam  LiP 
ā mastakatalādyas tu nimajjetpaṅkasāgare 
dṛṣṭvā tu tādṛśaṃ svapnaṃ sadya eva na jīvati  LiP 
bhasmāṅgārāṃś ca keśāṃś ca nadīṃ śuṣkāṃ bhujaṅgamān 
paśyedyo daśarātraṃ tu na sa jīvati tādṛśaḥ  LiP 
kṛṣṇaiś ca vikaṭaiścaiva puruṣairudyatāyudhaiḥ 
pāṣāṇaistāḍyate svapne yaḥ sadyo na sa jīvati  LiP 
sūryodaye pratyuṣasi pratyakṣaṃ yasya vai śivāḥ 
krośantyabhimukhaṃ pretya sa gatāyurbhavennaraḥ  LiP 
yasya vā snātamātrasya hṛdayaṃ pīḍyate bhṛśam 
jāyate dantaharṣaś ca taṃ gatāyuṣamādiśet  LiP 
bhūyobhūyastrasedyastu rātrau vā yadi vā divā 
dīpagandhaṃ ca nāghrāti vidyānmṛtyum upasthitam  LiP 
rātrau cendradhanuḥ paśyed divā nakṣatramaṇḍalam 
paranetreṣu cātmānaṃ na paśyenna sa jīvati  LiP 
netramekaṃ sravedyasya karṇau sthānācca bhraśyataḥ 
vakrā ca nāsā bhavati vijñeyo gatajīvitaḥ  LiP 
yasya kṛṣṇā kharā jihvā padmābhāsaṃ ca vai mukham 
gaṇḍe vā piṇḍikārakte tasya mṛtyurupasthitaḥ  LiP 
muktakeśo hasaṃścaiva gāyannṛtyaṃś ca yo naraḥ 
yāmyāmabhimukhaṃ gacchet tadantaṃ tasya jīvitam  LiP 
yasya śvetaghanābhāsā śvetasarṣapasaṃnibhā 
śvetā ca mūrtirhyasakṛt tasya mṛtyurupasthitaḥ  LiP 
uṣṭrā vā rāsabhā vābhi yuktāḥ svapne rathe śubhāḥ 
yasya so 'pi na jīvettu dakṣiṇābhimukho gataḥ  LiP 
dve vātha parame 'riṣṭe ekībhūtaḥ paraṃ bhavet 
ghoṣaṃ na śṛṇuyātkarṇe jyotir netre na paśyati  LiP 
śvabhre yo nipatetsvapne dvāraṃ cāpi pidhīyate 
na cottiṣṭhati yaḥ śvabhrāt tadantaṃ tasya jīvitam  LiP 
ūrdhvā ca dṛṣṭirna ca sampratiṣṭhā raktā punaḥ samparivartamānā 
mukhasya śoṣaḥ suṣirā ca nābhiratyuṣṇamūtro viṣamastha eva  LiP 
divā vā yadi vā rātrau pratyakṣaṃ yo nihanyate 
hantāraṃ na ca paśyecca sa gatāyurna jīvati  LiP 
agnipraveśaṃ kurute svapnānte yastu mānavaḥ 
smṛtiṃ nopalabheccāpi tadantaṃ tasya jīvitam  LiP 
yastu prāvaraṇaṃ śuklaṃ svakaṃ paśyati mānavaḥ 
kṛṣṇaṃ raktamapi svapne tasya mṛtyurupasthitaḥ  LiP 
preparation for death
ariṣṭe sūcite dehe tasminkāla upasthite 
tyaktvā khedaṃ viṣādaṃ ca upekṣed buddhimān naraḥ  LiP 
prācīṃ vā yadi vodīcīṃ diśaṃ niṣkramya vai śuciḥ 
same 'tisthāvare deśe vivikte jantuvarjite  LiP 
udaṅmukhaḥ prāṅmukho vā svasthaś cācānta eva ca 
svastikenopaviṣṭastu namaskṛtvā maheśvaram  LiP 
samakāyaśirogrīvo dhārayan nāvalokayet 
yathā dīpo nivātastho neṅgate sopamā smṛtā  LiP 
prāgudakpravaṇe deśe tathā yuñjīta śāstravit 
kāmaṃ vitarkaṃ prītiṃ ca sukhaduḥkhe ubhe tathā  LiP 
nigṛhya manasā sarvaṃ śuklaṃ dhyānam anusmaret 
ghrāṇe ca rasane nityaṃ cakṣuṣī sparśane tathā  LiP 
śrotre manasi buddhau ca tatra vakṣasi dhārayet 
kālakarmāṇi vijñāya samūheṣveva nityaśaḥ  LiP 
dvādaśādhyātmamityevaṃ yogadhāraṇamucyate 
śatamardhaśataṃ vāpi dhāraṇāṃ mūrdhni dhārayet  LiP 
khinnasya dhāraṇāyogād vāyurūrdhvaṃ pravartate 
tataścāpūrayed deham oṅkāreṇa samanvitaḥ  LiP 
tathauṃkāramayo yogī akṣare tvakṣarī bhavet 
oṃkāra
ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi oṅkāraprāptilakṣaṇam  LiP 
eṣa trimātro vijñeyo vyañjanaṃ cātra ceśvaraḥ 
prathamā vidyutī mātrā dvitīyā tāmasī smṛtā  LiP 
tṛtīyāṃ nirguṇāṃ caiva mātrāmakṣaragāminīm 
gāndhārī caiva vijñeyā gāndhārasvarasaṃbhavā  LiP 
pipīlikāgatisparśā prayuktā mūrdhni lakṣyate 
yathā prayukta oṅkāraḥ pratiniryāti mūrdhani  LiP 
tathauṃkāramayo yogī tv akṣarī tvakṣarī bhavet 
praṇavo dhanuḥ śaro hyātmā brahmalakṣaṇamucyate  LiP 
apramattena veddhavyaṃ śaravat tanmayo bhavet 
omityekākṣaraṃ hyetad guhāyāṃ nihitaṃ padam  LiP 
omityetattrayo lokās trayo vedāstrayo 'gnayaḥ 
viṣṇukramāstrayastvete ṛksāmāni yajūṃṣi ca  LiP 
mātrā cārdhaṃ ca tisrastu vijñeyāḥ paramārthataḥ 
tatprayuktastu yo yogī tasya sālokyamāpnuyāt  LiP 
akāro hyakṣaro jñeya ukāraḥ sahitaḥ smṛtaḥ 
makārasahitauṃkāras trimātra iti saṃjñitaḥ  LiP 
akāras tveṣa bhūrloka ukāro bhuva ucyate 
savyañjano makārastu svarloka iti gīyate  LiP 
oṅkārastu trayo lokāḥ śirastasya triviṣṭapam 
bhuvanāṅgaṃ ca tatsarvaṃ brāhmaṃ tatpadamucyate  LiP 
mātrāpādo rudraloko hy amātraṃ tu śivaṃ padam 
evaṃ jñānaviśeṣeṇa tatpadaṃ samupāsyate  LiP 
tasmāddhyānaratirnityam amātraṃ hi tadakṣaram 
upāsyaṃ hi prayatnena śāśvataṃ sukhamicchatā  LiP 
hrasvā tu prathamā mātrā tato dīrghā tvanantaram 
tataḥ plutavatī caiva tṛtīyā copadiśyate  LiP 
etāstu mātrā vijñeyā yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ 
yāvadeva tu śakyante dhāryante tāvadeva hi  LiP 
indriyāṇi mano buddhiṃ dhyāyannātmani yaḥ sadā 
ardhaṃ tanmātram api cec chṛṇu yat phalamāpnuyāt  LiP 
māse māse 'śvamedhena yo yajeta śataṃ samāḥ 
tena yatprāpyate puṇyaṃ mātrayā tadavāpnuyāt  LiP 
na tathā tapasogreṇa na yajñairbhūridakṣiṇaiḥ 
yatphalaṃ prāpyate samyaṅ mātrayā tadavāpnuyāt  LiP 
tatra caiṣā tu yā mātrā plutā nāmopadiśyate 
eṣā eva bhavetkāryā gṛhasthānāṃ tu yoginām  LiP 
eṣāṃ caiva viśeṣeṇa aiśvarye hyaṣṭalakṣaṇe 
aṇimādye tu vijñeyā tasmādyuñjīta tāṃ dvijāḥ  LiP 
evaṃ hi yogasaṃyuktaḥ śucir dānto jitendriyaḥ 
ātmānaṃ vidyate yastu sa sarvaṃ vindate dvijāḥ  LiP 
tasmātpāśupatairyogair ātmānaṃ cintayedbudhaḥ 
ātmānaṃ jānate ye tu śucayaste na saṃśayaḥ  LiP 
ṛco yajūṃṣi sāmāni vedopaniṣadas tathā 
yogajñānādavāpnoti brāhmaṇo 'dhyātmacintakaḥ  LiP 
sarvadevamayo bhūtvā abhūtaḥ sa tu jāyate 
yonisaṃkramaṇaṃ tyaktvā yāti vai śāśvataṃ padam  LiP 
yathā vṛkṣāt phalaṃ pakvaṃ pavanena samīritam 
namaskāreṇa rudrasya tathā pāpaṃ praṇaśyati  LiP 
yatra rudranamaskāraḥ sarvakarmaphalo dhruvaḥ 
anyadevanamaskārān na tatphalamavāpnuyāt  LiP 
tasmāttriḥpravaṇaṃ yogī upāsīta maheśvaram 
daśavistārakaṃ brahma tathā ca brahmavistaraiḥ  LiP 
evaṃ dhyānasamāyuktaḥ svadehaṃ yaḥ parityajet 
sa yāti śivasāyujyaṃ samuddhṛtya kulatrayam  LiP 
athavāriṣṭamālokya maraṇe samupasthite 
avimukteśvaraṃ gatvā vārāṇasyāṃ tu śodhanam  LiP 
yena kenāpi vā dehaṃ saṃtyajen mucyate naraḥ 
śrīparvate vā viprendrāḥ saṃtyajetsvatanuṃ naraḥ  LiP 
sa yāti śivasāyujyaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā 
avimuktaṃ paraṃ kṣetraṃ jantūnāṃ muktidaṃ sadā  LiP 
seveta satataṃ dhīmān viśeṣānmaraṇāntike  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge ariṣṭakathanaṃ nāma ekanavatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
LiP  
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
evaṃ vārāṇasī puṇyā yadi sūta mahāmate 
vaktumarhasi cāsmākaṃ tatprabhāvaṃ hi sāṃpratam  LiP 
kṣetrasyāsya ca māhātmyam avimuktasya śobhanam 
vistareṇa yathānyāyaṃ śrotuṃ kautūhalaṃ hi naḥ  LiP 
sūta uvāca
description of Avimukta
vakṣye saṃkṣepataḥ samyak vārāṇasyāḥ suśobhanam 
avimuktasya māhātmyaṃ yathāha bhagavān bhavaḥ  LiP 
vistareṇa mayā vaktuṃ brahmaṇā ca mahātmanā 
śakyate naiva viprendrā varṣakoṭiśatairapi  LiP 
devaḥ purā kṛtodvāhaḥ śaṅkaro nīlalohitaḥ 
himavacchikharāddevyā haimavatyā gaṇeśvaraiḥ  LiP 
vārāṇasīmanuprāpya darśayāmāsa śaṅkaraḥ 
avimukteśvaraṃ liṅgaṃ vāsaṃ tatra cakāra saḥ  LiP 
vārāṇasīkurukṣetra śrīparvatamahālaye 
tuṅgeśvare ca kedāre tatsthāne yo yatirbhavet  LiP 
yoge pāśupate samyak dinamekaṃ yatirbhavet 
tasmātsarvaṃ parityajya caret pāśupataṃ vratam  LiP 
devodyāne vasettatra śarvodyānamanuttamam 
manasā nirmame rudro vimānaṃ ca suśobhanam  LiP 
darśayāmāsa ca tadā devodyānamanuttamam 
haimavatyāḥ svayaṃ devaḥ sanandī parameśvaraḥ  LiP 
kṣetrasyāsya ca māhātmyam avimuktasya śaṅkaraḥ 
uktavānparameśānaḥ pārvatyāḥ prītaye bhavaḥ  LiP 
praphullanānāvidhagulmaśobhitaṃ latāpratānādimanoharaṃ bahiḥ 
virūḍhapuṣpaiḥ paritaḥ priyaṅgubhiḥ supuṣpitaiḥ kaṇṭakitaiś ca ketakaiḥ  LiP 
tamālagulmairnicitaṃ sugandhibhir nikāmapuṣpairvakulaiś ca sarvataḥ 
aśokapunnāgaśataiḥ supuṣpitair dvirephamālākulapuṣpasaṃcayaiḥ  LiP 
kvacit praphullāmbujareṇubhūṣitair vihaṅgamaiś cānukalapraṇādibhiḥ 
vināditaṃ sārasacakravākaiḥ pramattadātyūhavaraiś ca sarvataḥ  LiP 
kvacicca kekārutanāditaṃ śubhaṃ kvacicca kāraṇḍavanādanāditam 
kvacicca mattālikulākulīkṛtaṃ madākulābhir bhramarāṅganādibhiḥ  LiP 
niṣevitaṃ cārusugandhipuṣpakaiḥ kvacit supuṣpaiḥ sahakāravṛkṣaiḥ 
latopagūḍhaistilakaiś ca gūḍhaṃ pragītavidyādharasiddhacāraṇam  LiP 
pravṛttanṛttānugatāpsarogaṇaṃ prahṛṣṭanānāvidhapakṣisevitam 
pranṛttahārītakulopanāditaṃ mṛgendranādākulamattamānasaiḥ  LiP 
kvacit kvacid gandhakadambakair mṛgair vilūnadarbhāṅkurapuṣpasaṃcayam 
praphullanānāvidhacārupaṅkajaiḥ sarastaḍāgairupaśobhitaṃ kvacit  LiP 
viṭapanicayalīnaṃ nīlakaṇṭhābhirāmaṃ madamuditavihaṅgaṃ prāptanādābhirāmam 
kusumitataruśākhālīnamattadvirephaṃ navakisalayaśobhāśobhitaṃ prāṃśuśākham  LiP 
kvacicca dantakṣatacāruvīrudhaṃ kvacillatāliṅgitacāruvṛkṣakam 
kvacidvilāsālasagāminībhir niṣevitaṃ kiṃpuruṣāṅganābhiḥ  LiP 
pārāvatadhvanivikūjitacāruśṛṅgair abhraṅkaṣaiḥ sitamanoharacārurūpaiḥ 
ākīrṇapuṣpanikarapravibhaktahaṃsair vibhrājitaṃ tridaśadivyakulairanekaiḥ  LiP 
phullotpalāṃbujavitānasahasrayuktaṃ toyāśayaiḥ samanuśobhitadevamārgam 
mārgāntarākalitapuṣpavicitrapaṅkti sambaddhagulmaviṭapair vividhairupetam  LiP 
tuṅgāgrair nīlapuṣpastabakabharanataprāṃśuśākhair aśokair dolāprāntāntanīlaśrutisukhajanakair bhāsitāntaṃ manojñaiḥ 
rātrau candrasya bhāsā kusumitatilakairekatāṃ samprayātaṃ chāyāsuptaprabuddhasthitahariṇakulāluptadūrvāṅkurāgram  LiP 
haṃsānāṃ pakṣavātapracalitakamalasvacchavistīrṇatoyaṃ toyānāṃ tīrajātapracakitakadalīcāṭunṛtyanmayūram 
māyūraiḥ pakṣacandraiḥ kvacidavanigatai rañjitakṣmāpradeśaṃ deśe deśe vilīnapramuditavilasanmattahārītavṛndam  LiP 
sāraṅgaiḥ kvacidupaśobhitapradeśaṃ pracchannaṃ kusumacayaiḥ kvacidvicitraiḥ 
hṛṣṭābhiḥ kvacidapi kinnarāṅganābhir vīṇābhiḥ sumadhuragītanṛttakaṇṭham  LiP 
saṃsṛṣṭaiḥ kvacidupaliptakīrṇapuṣpair āvāsaiḥ parivṛtapādapaṃ munīnām 
ā mūlāt phalanicitaiḥ kvacidviśālair uttuṅgaiḥ panasamahīruhairupetam  LiP 
phullātimuktakalatāgṛhanītasiddhasiddhāṅganākanakanūpurarāvaramyam 
ramyaṃ priyaṅgutarumañjarisaktabhṛṅgaṃ bhṛṅgāvalīkavalitāmrakadambapuṣpam  LiP 
puṣpotkarānilavighūrṇitavāriramyaṃ ramyadvirephavinipātitamañjugulmam 
gulmāntaraprasabhabhītamṛgīsamūhaṃ vāteritaṃ tanubhṛtāmapavargadātṛ  LiP 
candrāṃśujālaśabalais tilakair manojñaiḥ sindūrakuṅkumakusumbhanibhair aśokaiḥ 
cāmīkaradyutisamairatha karṇikāraiḥ puṣpotkarairupacitaṃ suviśālaśākhaiḥ  LiP 
kvacidañjanacūrṇābhaiḥ kvacid vidrumasannibhaiḥ 
kvacitkāñcanasaṃkāśaiḥ puṣpair ācitabhūtalam  LiP 
punnāgeṣu dvijaśatavirutaṃ raktāśokastabakabharanatam 
ramyopāntaklamahārabhavanaṃ phullābjeṣu bhramaravilasitam  LiP 
sakalabhuvanabhartā lokanāthastadānīṃ tuhinaśikharaputryā sārdhamiṣṭairgaṇeśaiḥ 
vividhataruviśālaṃ mattahṛṣṭānnapuṣṭair upavanam atiramyaṃ darśayāmāsa devyāḥ  LiP 
puṣpairvanyaiḥ śubhaśubhatamaiḥ kalpitairdivyabhūṣair devīṃ divyāmupavanagatāṃ bhūṣayāmāsa śarvaḥ 
sā cāpyenaṃ tuhinagirisutā śaṅkaraṃ devadevaṃ puṣpairdivyaiḥ śubhataratamair bhūṣayāmāsa bhaktyā  LiP 
sampūjya pūjyaṃ tridaśeśvarāṇāṃ samprekṣya codyānam atīva ramyam 
gaṇeśvarair nandimukhaiś ca sārdham uvāca devaṃ praṇipatya devī  LiP 
śrīdevyuvāca
udyānaṃ darśitaṃ deva prabhayā parayā yutam 
kṣetrasya ca guṇānsarvān punarme vaktumarhasi  LiP 
asya kṣetrasya māhātmyam avimuktasya sarvathā 
vaktumarhasi deveśa devadeva vṛṣadhvaja  LiP 
sūta uvāca
devyāstadvacanaṃ śrutvā devadevo varaprabhuḥ 
āghrāya vadanāmbhojaṃ tadāha girijāṃ hasan  LiP 
holiness of Avimukta
śrībhagavānuvāca
idaṃ guhyatamaṃ kṣetraṃ sadā vārāṇasī mama 
sarveṣāmeva jantūnāṃ heturmokṣasya sarvadā  LiP 
asminsiddhāḥ sadā devi madīyaṃ vratamāsthitāḥ 
nānāliṅgadharā nityaṃ mama lokābhikāṅkṣiṇaḥ  LiP 
abhyasyanti paraṃ yogaṃ yuktātmāno jitendriyāḥ 
nānāvṛkṣasamākīrṇe nānāvihagaśobhite  LiP 
kamalotpalapuṣpāḍhyaiḥ sarobhiḥ samalaṃkṛte 
apsarogaṇagandharvaiḥ sadā saṃsevite śubhe  LiP 
rocate me sadā vāso yena kāryeṇa tacchṛṇu 
manmanā mama bhaktaś ca mayi nityārpitakriyaḥ  LiP 
yathā mokṣamavāpnoti anyatra na tathā kvacit 
kāmaṃ hyatra mṛto devi janturmokṣāya kalpate  LiP 
etanmama puraṃ divyaṃ guhyādguhyatamaṃ mahat 
brahmādayo vijānanti ye ca siddhā mumukṣavaḥ  LiP 
ataḥ paramidaṃ kṣetraṃ parā ceyaṃ gatirmama 
vimuktaṃ na mayā yasmān mokṣyate vā kadācana  LiP 
mama kṣetramidaṃ tasmād avimuktamiti smṛtam 
naimiṣe ca kurukṣetre gaṅgādvāre ca puṣkare  LiP 
snānātsaṃsevanādvāpi na mokṣaḥ prāpyate yataḥ 
iha samprāpyate yena tata etadviśiṣyate  LiP 
prayāge vā bhavenmokṣa iha vā matparigrahāt 
prayāgādapi tīrthāgryād avimuktamidaṃ śubham  LiP 
dharmasyopaniṣat satyaṃ mokṣasyopaniṣac chamaḥ 
kṣetratīrthopaniṣadaṃ na vidurbudhasattamāḥ  LiP 
kāmaṃ bhuñjan svapan krīḍan kurvan hi vividhāḥ kriyāḥ 
avimukte tyajetprāṇān janturmokṣāya kalpate  LiP 
kṛtvā pāpasahasrāṇi piśācatvaṃ varaṃ nṛṇām 
na tu śakrasahasratvaṃ svarge kāśīpurīṃ vinā  LiP 
tasmātsaṃsevanīyaṃ hi avimuktaṃ hi muktaye 
jaigīṣavyaḥ parāṃ siddhiṃ gato yatra mahātapāḥ  LiP 
asya kṣetrasya māhātmyād bhaktyā ca mama bhāvitaḥ 
jaigīṣavyaguhā śreṣṭhā yogināṃ sthānamiṣyate  LiP 
dhyāyantastatra māṃ nityaṃ yogāgnirdīpyate bhṛśam 
kaivalyaṃ paramaṃ yāti devānāmapi durlabham  LiP 
avyaktaliṅgairmunibhiḥ sarvasiddhāntavedibhiḥ 
iha samprāpyate mokṣo durlabho 'nyatra karhicit  LiP 
tebhyaścāhaṃ pravakṣyāmi yogaiśvaryamanuttamam 
ātmanaścaiva sāyujyam īpsitaṃ sthānameva ca  LiP 
kubero 'tra mama kṣetre mayi sarvārpitakriyaḥ 
kṣetrasaṃsevanādeva gaṇeśatvamavāpa ha  LiP 
saṃvarto bhavitā yaś ca so 'pi bhakto mamaiva tu 
ihaivārādhya māṃ devi siddhiṃ yāsyatyanuttamām  LiP 
parāśarasutau yogī ṛṣirvyāso mahātapāḥ 
mama bhakto bhaviṣyaś ca vedasaṃsthāpravartakaḥ  LiP 
raṃsyate so 'pi padmākṣi kṣetre 'sminmunipuṅgavaḥ 
brahmā devarṣibhiḥ sārddhaṃ viṣṇurvāpi divākaraḥ  LiP 
devarājastathā śakro ye 'pi cānye divaukasaḥ 
upāsate mahātmānaḥ sarve māmiha suvrate  LiP 
anye 'pi yogino divyāś channarūpā mahātmanaḥ 
ananyamanaso bhūtvā māmihopāsate sadā  LiP 
viṣayāsaktacitto 'pi tyaktadharmaratirnaraḥ 
iha kṣetre mṛtaḥ so 'pi saṃsāre na punarbhavet  LiP 
ye punarnirmamā dhīrāḥ sattvasthā vijitendriyāḥ 
vratinaś ca nirārambhāḥ sarve te mayi bhāvitāḥ  LiP 
devadevaṃ samāsādya dhīmantaḥ saṃgavarjitāḥ 
gatā iha paraṃ mokṣaṃ prasādānmama suvrate  LiP 
janmāntarasahasreṣu yaṃ na yogī samāpnuyāt 
tamihaiva paraṃ mokṣaṃ prasādānmama suvrate  LiP 
goprekṣakam idaṃ kṣetraṃ brahmaṇā sthāpitaṃ purā 
kailāsabhavanaṃ cātra paśya divyaṃ varānane  LiP 
goprekṣakam athāgamya dṛṣṭvā māmatra mānavaḥ 
na durgatimavāpnoti kalmaṣaiś ca vimucyate  LiP 
kapilāhradam ityevaṃ tathā vai brahmaṇā kṛtam 
gavāṃ stanyajatoyena tīrthaṃ puṇyatamaṃ mahat  LiP 
atrāpi svayamevāhaṃ vṛṣadhvaja iti smṛtaḥ 
sānnidhyaṃ kṛtavān devi sadāhaṃ dṛśyate tvayā  LiP 
bhadratoyaṃ ca paśyeha brahmaṇā ca kṛtaṃ hradam 
sarvairdevairahaṃ devi asmindeśe prasāditaḥ  LiP 
gacchopaśamam īśeti upaśāntaḥ śivas tathā 
atrāhaṃ brahmaṇānīya sthāpitaḥ parameṣṭhinā  LiP 
brahmaṇā cāpi saṃgṛhya viṣṇunā sthāpitaḥ punaḥ 
brahmaṇāpi tato viṣṇuḥ proktaḥ saṃvignacetasā  LiP 
mayānītamidaṃ liṅgaṃ kasmāt sthāpitavān asi 
tamuvāca punar viṣṇur brahmāṇaṃ kupitānanam  LiP 
rudre deve mamātyantaṃ parā bhaktirmahattarā 
mayaiva sthāpitaṃ liṅgaṃ tava nāmnā bhaviṣyati  LiP 
hiraṇyagarbha ityevaṃ tato 'trāhaṃ samāsthitaḥ 
dṛṣṭvainamapi deveśaṃ mama lokaṃ vrajennaraḥ  LiP 
tataḥ punarapi brahmā mama liṅgamidaṃ śubham 
sthāpayāmāsa vidhivad bhaktyā paramayā yutaḥ  LiP 
svarlīneśvara ityevam atrāhaṃ svayamāgataḥ 
prāṇān iha narastyaktvā na punarjāyate kvacit  LiP 
ananyā sā gatistasya yogināṃ caiva yā smṛtā 
Vyāghreśvara
asminnapi mayā deśe daityo daivatakaṇṭakaḥ  LiP 
vyāghrarūpaṃ samāsthāya nihato darpito balī 
vyāghreśvara iti khyāto nityamatrāhamāsthitaḥ  LiP 
na punardurgatiṃ yāti dṛṣṭvainaṃ vyāghramīśvaram 
utpalo vidalaścaiva yau daityau brahmaṇā purā  LiP 
strīvadhyau darpitau dṛṣṭvā tvayaiva nihatau raṇe 
sāvajñaṃ kandukenātra tasyedaṃ dehamāsthitam  LiP 
ādāvatrāhamāgamya prasthito gaṇapaiḥ saha 
jyeṣṭhasthānamidaṃ tasmād etanme puṇyadarśanam  LiP 
devaiḥ samantād etāni liṅgāni sthāpitānyataḥ 
dṛṣṭvāpi niyato martyo dehabhede gaṇo bhavet  LiP 
pitrā te śailarājena purā himavatā svayam 
mama priyahitaṃ sthānaṃ jñātvā liṅgaṃ pratiṣṭhitam  LiP 
śaileśvaramiti khyātaṃ dṛśyatāmiha cādarāt 
dṛṣṭvaitanmanujo devi na durgatimato vrajet  LiP 
nadyeṣā varuṇā devi puṇyā pāpapramocanī 
kṣetrametad alaṃkṛtya jāhnavyā saha saṃgatā  LiP 
sthāpitaṃ brahmaṇā cāpi saṃgame liṅgamuttamam 
saṃgameśvaram ityevaṃ khyātaṃ jagati dṛśyatām  LiP 
saṃgame devanadyā hi yaḥ snātvā manujaḥ śuciḥ 
arcayet saṃgameśvaraṃ tasya janmabhayaṃ kutaḥ  LiP 
idaṃ manye mahākṣetraṃ nivāso yogināṃ param 
kṣetramadhye ca yatrāhaṃ svayaṃ bhūtvāgramāsthitaḥ  LiP 
madhyameśvaramityevaṃ khyātaḥ sarvasurāsuraiḥ 
siddhānāṃ sthānametaddhi madīyavratadhāriṇām  LiP 
yogināṃ mokṣalipsūnāṃ jñānayogaratātmanām 
dṛṣṭvainaṃ madhyameśānaṃ janma prati na śocati  LiP 
sthāpitaṃ liṅgametattu śukreṇa bhṛgusūnunā 
nāmnā śukreśvaraṃ nāma sarvasiddhāmarārcitam  LiP 
dṛṣṭvainaṃ niyataḥ sadyo mucyate sarvakilbiṣaiḥ 
mṛtaś ca na punarjantuḥ saṃsārī tu bhavennaraḥ  LiP 
purā jambūkarūpeṇa asuro devakaṇṭakaḥ 
brahmaṇo hi varaṃ labdhvā gomāyurbandhaśaṅkitaḥ  LiP

adyāpi jagati khyātaṃ surāsuranamaskṛtam  LiP

grahaiḥ śukrapurogaiś ca etāni sthāpitāni ha  LiP 
paśya puṇyāni liṅgāni sarvakāmapradāni tu 
evametāni puṇyāni mannivāsāni pārvati  LiP 
kathitāni mama kṣetre guhyaṃ cānyadidaṃ śṛṇu 
catuḥkrośaṃ caturdikṣu kṣetrametatprakīrtitam  LiP 
yojanaṃ viddhi cārvaṅgi mṛtyukāle 'mṛtapradam 
mahālayagiristhaṃ māṃ kedāre ca vyavasthitam  LiP 
gaṇatvaṃ labhate dṛṣṭvā hy asminmokṣo hyavāpyate 
gāṇapatyaṃ labhedyasmād yataḥ sā muktiruttamā  LiP 
tato mahālayāt tasmāt kedārānmadhyamādapi 
smṛtaṃ puṇyatamaṃ kṣetram avimuktaṃ varānane  LiP 
kedāraṃ madhyamaṃ kṣetraṃ sthānaṃ caiva mahālayam 
mama puṇyāni bhūrloke tebhyaḥ śreṣṭhatamaṃ tvidam  LiP 
yataḥ sṛṣṭāstvime lokās tataḥ kṣetramidaṃ śubham 
kadācinna mayā muktam avimuktaṃ tato 'bhavat  LiP 
avimukteśvaraṃ liṅgaṃ mama dṛṣṭveha mānavaḥ 
sadyaḥ pāpavinirmuktaḥ paśupāśairvimucyate  LiP 
śaileśaṃ saṃgameśaṃ ca svarlīnaṃ madhyameśvaram 
hiraṇyagarbham īśānaṃ goprekṣaṃ vṛṣabhadhvajam  LiP 
upaśāntaṃ śivaṃ caiva jyeṣṭhasthānanivāsinam 
śukreśvaraṃ ca vikhyātaṃ vyāghreśaṃ jambukeśvaram  LiP 
dṛṣṭvā na jāyate martyaḥ saṃsāre duḥkhasāgare 
sūta uvāca
evam uktvā mahādevo diśaḥ sarvā vyalokayat  LiP 
vilokya saṃsthite paścād devadeve maheśvare 
akasmādabhavatsarvaḥ sa deśojjvalito yathā  LiP 
tataḥ pāśupatāḥ siddhā bhasmābhyaṅgasitaprabhāḥ 
māheśvarā mahātmānas tathā vai niyatavratāḥ  LiP 
bahavaḥ śataśo 'bhyetya namaścakrurmaheśvaram

tasthurātmānamāsthāya līyamānā iveśvare

kṛtsnaṃ jagadihaikasthaṃ kartum anta iva sthitaḥ  LiP 
tasya tāṃ paramāṃ mūrtim āsthitasya jagatprabhoḥ

tatastvadṛṣṭamākāraṃ buddhvā sā prakṛtisthitam 
prakṛtermūrtimāsthāya yogena parameśvarī  LiP 
taṃ śaśāka punardraṣṭuṃ harasya ca mahātmanaḥ 
tataste layamādhāya yoginaḥ puruṣasya tu  LiP

śrībhagavānuvāca
madīyaṃ vratamāśritya bhaktimadbhir dvijottamaiḥ  LiP

saṃdhyā ca ṛtavaścaiva sarvā nadyaḥ sarāṃsi ca

bhāgīrathīṃ sameṣyanti sarvaparvasu suvrate

bhavanti hi sureśāni sarvaparvasu parvasu  LiP

śrīśaila
ityuktvā bhagavān devas tayā sārdham umāpatiḥ

mallikārjunakaṃ caiva mama vāsamidaṃ śubham  LiP

andhakānugrahaṃ caiva mandare śoṣaṇaṃ tathā  LiP

tvayi bhaktiḥ prasīdeśa yadi deyo varaś ca me  LiP 
śrutvā bhavo 'pi vacanam andhakasya mahātmanaḥ 
pradadau durlabhāṃ śraddhāṃ daityendrāya mahādyutiḥ  LiP 
gāṇapatyaṃ ca daityāya pradadau cāvaropya tam 
praṇemustaṃ surendrādyā gāṇapatye pratiṣṭhitam  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge andhakagāṇapatyātmako nāma trinavatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
LiP  
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
kathamasya pitā daityo hiraṇyākṣaḥ sudāruṇaḥ 
viṣṇunā sūdito viṣṇur vārāhatvaṃ kathaṃ gataḥ  LiP 
tasya śṛṅgaṃ maheśasya bhūṣaṇatvaṃ kathaṃ gatam 
etatsarvaṃ viśeṣeṇa sūta vaktumihārhasi  LiP 
sūta uvāca
hiraṇyakaśiporbhrātā hiraṇyākṣa iti smṛtaḥ 
purāndhakāsureśasya pitā kālāntakopamaḥ  LiP 
devāñjitvātha daityendro baddhvā ca dharaṇīmimām 
nītvā rasātalaṃ cakre vandīm indīvaraprabhām  LiP 
tataḥ sabrahmakā devāḥ parimlānamukhaśriyaḥ 
bādhitāstāḍitā baddhvā hiraṇyākṣeṇa tena vai  LiP 
balinā daityamukhyena krūreṇa sudurātmanā 
praṇamya śirasā viṣṇuṃ daityakoṭivimardanam  LiP 
sarve vijñāpayāmāsur dharaṇībandhanaṃ hareḥ 
śrutvaitadbhagavān viṣṇur dharaṇībandhanaṃ hariḥ  LiP 
bhūtvā yajñavarāho 'sau yathā liṅgodbhave tathā 
daityaiś ca sārdhaṃ daityendraṃ hiraṇyākṣaṃ mahābalam  LiP 
daṃṣṭrāgrakoṭyā hatvainaṃ reje daityāntakṛtprabhuḥ 
kalpādiṣu yathāpūrvaṃ praviśya ca rasātalam  LiP 
ānīya vasudhāṃ devīm aṅkasthāmakarodbahiḥ 
tatas tuṣṭāva deveśaṃ devadevaḥ pitāmahaḥ  LiP 
śakrādyaiḥ sahito bhūtvā harṣagadgadayā girā 
śāśvatāya varāhāya daṃṣṭriṇe daṇḍine namaḥ  LiP 
nārāyaṇāya sarvāya brahmaṇe paramātmane 
kartre dhartre dharāyāstu hartre devāriṇāṃ svayam 
kartre netre surendrāṇāṃ śāstre ca sakalasya ca  LiP 
tvamaṣṭamūrtistvamanantamūrtis tvamādidevastvamanantaveditaḥ 
tvayā kṛtaṃ sarvamidaṃ prasīda sureśa lokeśa varāha viṣṇo  LiP 
tathaikadaṃṣṭrāgramukhāgrakoṭi bhāgaikabhāgārdhatamena viṣṇo 
hatāḥ kṣaṇāt kāmada daityamukhyāḥ svadaṃṣṭrakoṭyā saha putrabhṛtyaiḥ  LiP 
tvayoddhṛtā deva dharā dhareśa dharādharākāra dhṛtāgradaṃṣṭre 
dharādharaiḥ sarvajanaiḥ samudraiḥ surāsuraiḥ sevitacandravaktra  LiP 
tvayaiva deveśa vibho kṛtaś ca jayaḥ surāṇāmasureśvarāṇām 
aho pradattastu varaḥ prasīda vāgdevatā vārijasaṃbhavāya  LiP 
tava romṇi sakalāmareśvarānayanadvaye śaśiravī padadvaye 
nihitā rasātalagatā vasuṃdharā tava pṛṣṭhataḥ sakalatārakādayaḥ  LiP 
jagatāṃ hitāya bhavatā vasuṃdharā bhagavan rasātalapuṭaṃ gatā tadā 
abaloddhṛtā ca bhagavaṃstavaiva sakalaṃ tvayaiva hi dhṛtaṃ jagadguro  LiP 
iti vākpatirbahuvidhaistavārcanaiḥ praṇipatya viṣṇumamaraiḥ prajāpatiḥ 
vividhānvarān harimukhāttu labdhavān harinābhivārijadehabhṛt svayam  LiP 
atha tāmuddhṛtāṃ tena dharāṃ devā munīśvarāḥ 
mūrdhnyāropya namaścakruś cakriṇaḥ saṃnidhau tadā  LiP 
anenaiva varāheṇa coddhṛtāsi varaprade 
kṛṣṇenākliṣṭakāryeṇa śatahastena viṣṇunā  LiP 
dharaṇi tvaṃ mahābhoge bhūmistvaṃ dhenuravyaye 
lokānāṃ dhāriṇī tvaṃ hi mṛttike hara pātakam  LiP 
manasā karmaṇā vācā varade vārijekṣaṇe 
tvayā hatena pāpena jīvāmastvatprasādataḥ  LiP 
ityuktā sā tadā devī dharā devair athābravīt 
varāhadaṃṣṭrābhinnāyāṃ dharāyāṃ mṛttikāṃ dvijāḥ  LiP 
mantreṇānena yo bibhrat mūrdhni pāpātpramucyate 
āyuṣmān balavān dhanyaḥ putrapautrasamanvitaḥ  LiP 
kramādbhuvi divaṃ prāpya karmānte modate suraiḥ 
atha deve gate tyaktvā varāhe kṣīrasāgaram  LiP 
vārāharūpamanaghaṃ cacāla ca dharā punaḥ 
tasya daṃṣṭrābharākrāntā devadevasya dhīmataḥ  LiP 
yadṛcchayā bhavaḥ paśyan jagāma jagadīśvaraḥ 
daṃṣṭrāṃ jagrāha dṛṣṭvā tāṃ bhūṣaṇārthamathātmanaḥ  LiP 
dadhāra ca mahādevaḥ kūrcānte vai mahorasi 
devāś ca tuṣṭuvuḥ sendrā devadevasya vaibhavam  LiP 
dharā pratiṣṭhitā hyevaṃ devadevena līlayā 
bhūtānāṃ saṃplave cāpi viṣṇoścaiva kalevaram  LiP 
brahmaṇaś ca tathānyeṣāṃ devānāmapi līlayā 
vibhuraṅgavibhāgena bhūṣito na yadi prabhuḥ  LiP 
kathaṃ vimuktirviprāṇāṃ tasmāddaṃṣṭrī maheśvaraḥ  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge varāhaprādurbhāvo nāma caturnavatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ

ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
nṛsiṃhena hataḥ pūrvaṃ hiraṇyākṣāgrajaḥ śrutam 
kathaṃ niṣūditastena hiraṇyakaśipurvada  LiP 
sūta uvāca
Viṣṇu transforms into Nṛsiṃha and kills Hiraṇyakaśipu
hiraṇyakaśipoḥ putraḥ prahrāda iti viśrutaḥ 
dharmajñaḥ satyasampannas tapasvī cābhavatsudhīḥ  LiP 
janmaprabhṛti deveśaṃ pūjayāmāsa cāvyayam 
sarvajñaṃ sarvagaṃ viṣṇuṃ sarvadevabhavodbhavam  LiP 
tamādipuruṣaṃ bhaktyā parabrahmasvarūpiṇam 
brahmaṇo 'dhipatiṃ sṛṣṭi sthitisaṃhārakāraṇam  LiP 
so 'pi viṣṇostathābhūtaṃ dṛṣṭvā putraṃ samāhitam 
namo nārāyaṇāyeti govindeti muhurmuhuḥ  LiP 
stuvantaṃ prāha devāriḥ pradahanniva pāpadhīḥ 
na māṃ jānāsi durbuddhe sarvadaityāmareśvaram  LiP 
prahrāda vīra duṣputra dvijadevārtikāraṇam 
ko viṣṇuḥ padmajo vāpi śakraś ca varuṇo 'thavā  LiP 
vāyuḥ somastatheśānaḥ pāvako mama yaḥ samaḥ 
māmevārcaya bhaktyā ca svalpaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ sadā  LiP 
prahrāda jīvite vāñchā tavaiṣā śṛṇu cāsti cet 
śrutvāpi tasya vacanaṃ hiraṇyakaśipoḥ sudhīḥ  LiP 
prahrādaḥ pūjayāmāsa namo nārāyaṇeti ca 
namo nārāyaṇāyeti sarvadaityakumārakān  LiP 
adhyāpayāmāsa ca tāṃ brahmavidyāṃ suśobhanām 
durlaṅghyāṃ cātmano dṛṣṭvā śakrādibhir api svayam  LiP 
putreṇa laṅghitāmājñāṃ hiraṇyaḥ prāha dānavān 
etaṃ nānāvidhairvadhyaṃ duṣputraṃ hantumarhatha  LiP 
evamuktāstadā tena daityena sudurātmanā 
nijaghnurdevadevasya bhṛtyaṃ prahrādamavyayam  LiP 
tatra tatpratikṛtaṃ tadā surair daityarājatanayaṃ dvijottamāḥ 
kṣīravārinidhiśāyinaḥ prabhor niṣphalaṃ tvatha babhūva tejasā  LiP 
tadātha garvabhinnasya hiraṇyakaśipoḥ prabhuḥ 
tatraivāvirabhūddhantuṃ nṛsiṃhākṛtimāsthitaḥ  LiP 
jaghāna ca sutaṃ prekṣya pitaraṃ dānavādhamam 
bibheda tatkṣaṇādeva karajair niśitaiḥ śataiḥ  LiP 
tato nihatya taṃ daityaṃ sabāndhavamaghāpahaḥ 
pīḍayāmāsa daityendraṃ yugāntāgnirivāparaḥ  LiP 
nādaistasya nṛsiṃhasya ghorairvitrāsitaṃ jagat 
ā brahmabhuvanād viprāḥ pracacāla ca suvratāḥ  LiP 
dṛṣṭvā surāsuramahoragasiddhasādhyās tasmin kṣaṇe hariviriñcimukhā nṛsiṃham 
dhairyaṃ balaṃ ca samavāpya yayurvisṛjya ā diṅmukhāntam asurakṣaṇatatparāś ca  LiP 
tatastairgataiḥ saiṣa devo nṛsiṃhaḥ sahasrākṛtiḥ sarvapāt sarvabāhuḥ 
sahasrekṣaṇaḥ somasūryāgninetras tadā saṃsthitaḥ sarvamāvṛtya māyī  LiP 
taṃ tuṣṭuvuḥ suraśreṣṭhā lokā lokācale sthitāḥ 
sabrahmakāḥ sasādhyāś ca sayamāḥ samarudgaṇāḥ  LiP 
parātparataraṃ brahma tattvāt tattvatamaṃ bhavān 
jyotiṣāṃ tu paraṃ jyotiḥ paramātmā jaganmayaḥ  LiP 
sthūlaṃ sūkṣmaṃ susūkṣmaṃ ca śabdabrahmamayaḥ śubhaḥ 
vāgatīto nirālaṃbo nirdvandvo nirupaplavaḥ  LiP 
yajñabhugyajñamūrtistvaṃ yajñināṃ phaladaḥ prabhuḥ 
bhavānmatsyākṛtiḥ kaurmam āsthāya jagati sthitaḥ  LiP 
vārāhīṃ caiva tāṃ saiṃhīm āsthāyehavyavasthitaḥ 
devānāṃ devarakṣārthaṃ nihatya ditijeśvaram  LiP 
dvijaśāpacchalenaivam avatīrṇo 'si līlayā 
na dṛṣṭaṃ yattvadanyaṃ hi bhavān sarvaṃ carācaram  LiP 
bhavānviṣṇurbhavān rudro bhavāneva pitāmahaḥ 
bhavānādirbhavānanto bhavāneva vayaṃ vibho  LiP 
bhavāneva jagatsarvaṃ pralāpena kimīśvara 
māyayā bahudhā saṃstham advitīyamayaṃ prabho  LiP 
stoṣyāmastvāṃ kathaṃ bhāsi devadeva mṛgādhipa 
stuto 'pi vividhaiḥ stutyair bhāvairnānāvidhaiḥ prabhuḥ  LiP 
na jagāma dvijāḥ śāntiṃ mānayanyonimātmanaḥ 
yo nṛsiṃhastavaṃ bhaktyā paṭhedvārthaṃ vicārayet  LiP 
śrāvayedvā dvijānsarvān viṣṇuloke mahīyate 
devas take refuge to Śiva
tadantare śivaṃ devāḥ sendrāḥ sabrahmakāḥ prabhum  LiP 
samprāpya tuṣṭuvuḥ sarvaṃ vijñāpya mṛgarūpiṇaḥ 
tato brahmādayastūrṇaṃ saṃstūya parameśvaram  LiP 
ātmatrāṇāya śaraṇaṃ jagmuḥ paramakāraṇam 
mandarasthaṃ mahādevaṃ krīḍamānaṃ sahomayā  LiP 
sevitaṃ gaṇagandharvaiḥ siddhairapsarasāṃ gaṇaiḥ 
devatābhiḥ saha brahmā bhītabhītaḥ sagadgadam 
praṇamya daṇḍavadbhūmau tuṣṭāva parameśvaram  LiP 
brahmovāca
namaste kālakālāya namaste rudra manyave 
namaḥ śivāya rudrāya śaṅkarāya śivāya te  LiP 
ugro 'si sarvabhūtānāṃ niyantāsi śivo 'si naḥ 
namaḥ śivāya śarvāya śaṅkarāyārttihāriṇe  LiP 
mayaskarāya viśvāya viṣṇave brahmaṇe namaḥ 
antakāya namastubhyam umāyāḥ pataye namaḥ  LiP 
hiraṇyabāhave sākṣād dhiraṇyapataye namaḥ 
śarvāya sarvarūpāya puruṣāya namonamaḥ  LiP 
sadasadvyaktihīnāya mahataḥ kāraṇāya te 
nityāya viśvarūpāya jāyamānāya te namaḥ  LiP 
jātāya bahudhā loke prabhūtāya namonamaḥ 
rudrāya nīlarudrāya kadrudrāya pracetase  LiP 
kālāya kālarūpāya namaḥ kālāṅgahāriṇe 
mīḍhuṣṭamāya devāya śitikaṇṭhāya te namaḥ  LiP 
mahīyase namastubhyaṃ hantre devāriṇāṃ sadā 
tārāya ca sutārāya tāraṇāya namonamaḥ  LiP 
harikeśāya devāya śaṃbhave paramātmane 
devānāṃ śaṃbhave tubhyaṃ bhūtānāṃ śaṃbhave namaḥ  LiP 
śambhave haimavatyāś ca manyave rudrarūpiṇe 
kapardine namastubhyaṃ kālakaṇṭhāya te namaḥ  LiP 
hiraṇyāya maheśāya śrīkaṇṭhāya namonamaḥ 
bhasmadigdhaśarīrāya daṇḍamuṇḍīśvarāya ca  LiP 
namo hrasvāya dīrghāya vāmanāya namonamaḥ 
nama ugratriśūlāya ugrāya ca namo namaḥ  LiP 
bhīmāya bhīmarūpāya bhīmakarmaratāya te 
agrevadhāya vai bhūtvā namo dūrevadhāya ca  LiP 
dhanvine śūline tubhyaṃ gadine haline namaḥ 
cakriṇe varmiṇe nityaṃ daityānāṃ karmabhedine  LiP 
sadyāya sadyarūpāya sadyojātāya te namaḥ 
vāmāya vāmarūpāya vāmanetrāya te namaḥ  LiP 
aghorarūpāya vikaṭāya vikaṭaśarīrāya te namaḥ 
puruṣarūpāya puruṣaikatatpuruṣāya vai namaḥ  LiP 
puruṣārthapradānāya pataye parameṣṭhine 
īśānāya namastubhyam īśvarāya namonamaḥ  LiP 
brahmaṇe brahmarūpāya namaḥ sākṣācchivāya te 
sarvaviṣṇurnṛsiṃhasya rūpamāsthāya viśvakṛt  LiP 
hiraṇyakaśipuṃ hatvā karajairniśitaiḥ svayam 
daityendrairbahubhiḥ sārdhaṃ hitārthaṃ jagatāṃ prabhuḥ  LiP 
saiṃhīṃ samānayanyoniṃ bādhate nikhilaṃ jagat 
yatkṛtyamatra deveśa tatkuruṣva bhavāniha  LiP 
ugro 'si sarvaduṣṭānāṃ niyantāsi śivo 'si naḥ 
kālakūṭādivapuṣā trāhi naḥ śaraṇāgatān  LiP 
śukraṃ tu vṛttaṃ viśveśa krīḍā vai kevalaṃ vayam 
tavonmeṣanimeṣābhyām asmākaṃ pralayodayau  LiP 
unmīlayet tvayi brahman vināśo 'sti na te śiva 
saṃtaptāsmo vayaṃ deva hariṇāmitatejasā  LiP 
sarvalokahitāyainaṃ tattvaṃ saṃhartumicchasi 
sūta uvāca
vijñāpitas tathā devaḥ prahasanprāha tān surān  LiP 
abhayaṃ ca dadau teṣāṃ haniṣyāmīti taṃ prabhuḥ 
so 'pi śakraḥ suraiḥ sārdhaṃ praṇipatya yathāgatam  LiP 
jagāma bhagavān brahmā tathānye ca surottamāḥ 
athotthāya mahādevaḥ śārabhaṃ rūpamāsthitaḥ  LiP 
yayau prānte nṛsiṃhasya garvitasya mṛgāśinaḥ 
apahṛtya tadā prāṇān śarabhaḥ surapūjitaḥ  LiP 
siṃhāttato naro bhūtvā jagāma ca yathākramam 
evaṃ stutastadā devair jagāma sa yathākramam  LiP 
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi saṃstavaṃ śārvamuttamam 
rudralokamanuprāpya rudreṇa saha modate  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge nārasiṃhe pañcanavatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
LiP  
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
kathaṃ devo mahādevo viśvasaṃhārakārakaḥ 
śarabhākhyaṃ mahāghoraṃ vikṛtaṃ rūpamāsthitaḥ  LiP 
kiṃ kiṃ dhairyaṃ kṛtaṃ tena brūhi sarvam aśeṣataḥ 
sūta uvāca
evamabhyarthito devair matiṃ cakre kṛpālayaḥ  LiP 
yattejastu nṛsiṃhākhyaṃ saṃhartuṃ parameśvaraḥ 
tadarthaṃ smṛtavān rudro vīrabhadraṃ mahābalam  LiP 
Bhairava description
ātmano bhairavaṃ rūpaṃ mahāpralayakārakam 
ājagāma purā sadyo gaṇānāmagrato hasan  LiP 
sāṭṭahāsair gaṇavarair utpatadbhir itastataḥ 
nṛsiṃharūpairatyugraiḥ koṭibhiḥ parivāritaḥ  LiP 
tāvadbhir abhito vīrair nṛtyadbhiś ca mudānvitaiḥ 
krīḍadbhiś ca mahādhīrair brahmādyaiḥ kandukairiva  LiP 
adṛṣṭapūrvairanyaiś ca veṣṭito vīravanditaḥ 
kalpāntajvalanajvālo vilasallocanatrayaḥ  LiP 
āttaśastro jaṭājūṭe jvaladbālendumaṇḍitaḥ 
bālendudvitayākāra tīkṣṇadaṃṣṭrāṅkuradvayaḥ  LiP 
ākhaṇḍaladhanuḥkhaṇḍa saṃnibhabhrūlatāyutaḥ 
mahāpracaṇḍahuṅkāra badhirīkṛtadiṅmukhaḥ  LiP 
nīlameghāñjanākāra bhīṣaṇaśmaśruradbhutaḥ 
vādakhaṇḍam akhaṇḍābhyāṃ bhrāmayaṃstriśikhaṃ muhuḥ  LiP 
vīrabhadro 'pi bhagavān vīraśaktivijṛmbhitaḥ 
svayaṃ vijñāpayāmāsa kimatra smṛtikāraṇam  LiP 
ājñāpaya jagatsvāmin prasādaḥ kriyatāṃ mayi 
Śiva orders the destruction of Nṛsiṃha
śrībhagavānuvāca
akāle bhayamutpannaṃ devānāmapi bhairava  LiP 
jvalitaḥ sa nṛsiṃhāgniḥ śamayainaṃ durāsadam 
sāntvayan bodhayādau taṃ tena kiṃ nopaśāmyati  LiP 
tato matparamaṃ bhāvaṃ bhairavaṃ saṃpradarśaya 
sūkṣmaṃ sūkṣmeṇa saṃhṛtya sthūlaṃ sthūlena tejasā  LiP 
vaktramānaya kṛttiṃ ca vīrabhadra mamājñayā 
ityādiṣṭo gaṇādhyakṣaḥ praśāntavapurāsthitaḥ  LiP 
jagāma raṃhasā tatra yatrāste narakesarī 
tatastaṃ bodhayāmāsa vīrabhadro haro harim  LiP 
uvāca vākyamīśānaḥ pitā putramivaurasam 
discussion of Nṛsiṃha and Vīrabhadra
śrīvīrabhadra uvāca
jagatsukhāya bhagavann avatīrṇo 'si mādhava  LiP 
sthityarthena ca yukto 'si pareṇa parameṣṭhinā 
jantucakraṃ bhagavatā rakṣitaṃ matsyarūpiṇā  LiP 
pucchenaiva samābadhya bhramannekārṇave purā 
bibharṣi kūrmarūpeṇa vārāheṇoddhṛtā mahī  LiP 
anena harirūpeṇa hiraṇyakaśipurhataḥ 
vāmanena balirbaddhas tvayā vikramatā punaḥ  LiP 
tvam eva sarvabhūtānāṃ prabhāvaḥ prabhur avyayaḥ 
yadā yadā hi lokasya duḥkhaṃ kiṃcit prajāyate  LiP 
tadā tadāvatīrṇastvaṃ kariṣyasi nirāmayam 
nādhikastvatsamo 'pyasti hare śivaparāyaṇa  LiP 
tvayā dharmāś ca vedāś ca śubhe mārge pratiṣṭhitāḥ 
yadartham avatāro 'yaṃ nihataḥ so 'pi keśava  LiP 
atyantaghoraṃ bhagavan narasiṃha vapustava 
upasaṃhara viśvātmaṃs tvameva mama saṃnidhau  LiP 
sūta uvāca
ityukto vīrabhadreṇa nṛsiṃhaḥ śāntayā girā 
tato 'dhikaṃ mahāghoraṃ kopaṃ prajvālayaddhariḥ  LiP 
śrīnṛsiṃha uvāca
āgato 'si yatastatra gaccha tvaṃ mā hitaṃ vada 
idānīṃ saṃhariṣyāmi jagadetaccarācaram  LiP 
saṃhartur na hi saṃhāraḥ svato vā parato 'pi vā 
śāsitaṃ mama sarvatra śāstā ko 'pi na vidyate  LiP 
matprasādena sakalaṃ samaryādaṃ pravartate 
ahaṃ hi sarvaśaktīnāṃ pravartakanivartakaḥ  LiP 
yad yad vibhūtimat sattvaṃ śrīmadūrjitameva vā 
tattadviddhi gaṇādhyakṣa mama tejovijṛmbhitam  LiP 
devatāparamārthajñā mamaiva paramaṃ viduḥ 
madaṃśāḥ śaktisampannā brahmaśakrādayaḥ surāḥ  LiP 
mannābhipaṅkajājjātaḥ purā brahmā caturmukhaḥ 
tallalāṭasamutpanno bhagavānvṛṣabhadhvajaḥ  LiP 
rajasādhiṣṭhitaḥ sraṣṭā rudrastāmasa ucyate 
ahaṃ niyantā sarvasya matparaṃ nāsti daivatam  LiP 
viśvādhikaḥ svatantraś ca kartā hartākhileśvaraḥ 
idaṃ tu matparaṃ tejaḥ kaḥ punaḥ śrotumicchati  LiP 
ato māṃ śaraṇaṃ prāpya gaccha tvaṃ vigatajvaraḥ 
avehi paramaṃ bhāvam idaṃ bhūtamaheśvaraḥ  LiP 
kālo 'smyahaṃ kālavināśahetur lokān samāhartum ahaṃ pravṛttaḥ 
mṛtyormṛtyuṃ viddhi māṃ vīrabhadra jīvantyete matprasādena devāḥ  LiP 
sūta uvāca
sāhaṅkāramidaṃ śrutvā harer amitavikramaḥ 
vihasyovāca sāvajñaṃ tato visphuritādharaḥ  LiP 
śrīvīrabhadra uvāca
kiṃ na jānāsi viśveśaṃ saṃhartāraṃ pinākinam 
asadvādo vivādaś ca vināśastvayi kevalaḥ  LiP 
tavānyonyāvatārāṇi kāni śeṣāṇi sāṃpratam 
kṛtāni yena kenāpi kathāśeṣo bhaviṣyati  LiP 
doṣaṃ tvaṃ paśya etattvam avasthāmīdṛśīṃ gataḥ 
tena saṃhāradakṣeṇa kṣaṇātsaṃkṣayameṣyasi  LiP 
prakṛtistvaṃ pumān rudras tvayi vīryaṃ samāhitam 
tvannābhipaṅkajājjātaḥ pañcavaktraḥ pitāmahaḥ  LiP 
sṛṣṭyarthena jagatpūrvaṃ śaṅkaraṃ nīlalohitam 
lalāṭe cintayāmāsa tapasyugre vyavasthitaḥ  LiP 
tallalāṭādabhūcchaṃbhoḥ sṛṣṭyarthaṃ tanna dūṣaṇam 
aṃśo 'haṃ devadevasya mahābhairavarūpiṇaḥ  LiP 
tvatsaṃhāre niyukto 'smi vinayena balena ca 
evaṃ rakṣo vidāryaiva tvaṃ śaktikalayā yutaḥ  LiP 
ahaṅkārāvalepena garjasi tvamatandritaḥ 
upakāro hyasādhūnām apakārāya kevalam  LiP 
yadi siṃha maheśānaṃ svapunarbhūta manyase 
na tvaṃ sraṣṭā na saṃhartā na svatantro hi kutracit  LiP 
kulālacakravacchaktyā prerito 'si pinākinā 
adyāpi tava nikṣiptaṃ kapālaṃ kūrmarūpiṇaḥ  LiP 
harahāralatāmadhye mugdha kasmānna budhyase 
vismṛtaṃ kiṃ tadaṃśena daṃṣṭrotpātanapīḍitaḥ  LiP 
vārāhavigrahaste 'dya sākrośaṃ tārakāriṇā 
dagdho 'si yasya śūlāgre viṣvaksenacchalādbhavān  LiP 
dakṣayajñe śiraśchinnaṃ mayā te yajñarūpiṇaḥ 
adyāpi tava putrasya brahmaṇaḥ pañcamaṃ śiraḥ  LiP 
chinnaṃ tamenābhisaṃdhaṃ tadaṃśaṃ tasya tadbalam 
nirjitastvaṃ dadhīcena saṃgrāme samarudgaṇaḥ  LiP 
kaṇḍūyamāne śirasi kathaṃ tadvismṛtaṃ tvayā 
cakraṃ vikramato yasya cakrapāṇe tava priyam  LiP 
kutaḥ prāptaṃ kṛtaṃ kena tvayā tadapi vismṛtam 
te mayā sakalā lokā gṛhītāstvaṃ payonidhau  LiP 
nidrāparavaśaḥ śeṣe sa kathaṃ sāttviko bhavān 
tvadādistambaparyantaṃ rudraśaktivijṛmbhitam  LiP 
śaktimānabhitastvaṃ ca hy analastvaṃ ca mohitaḥ 
tattejaso 'pi māhātmyaṃ yuvāṃ draṣṭuṃ na hi kṣamau  LiP 
sthūlā ye hi prapaśyanti tadviṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam 
dyāvāpṛthivyā indrāgni yamasya varuṇasya ca  LiP 
dhvāntodare śaśāṅkasya janitvā parameśvaraḥ 
kālo 'si tvaṃ mahākālaḥ kālakālo maheśvaraḥ  LiP 
atastvamugrakalayā mṛtyormṛtyurbhaviṣyasi 
sthiradhanvā kṣayo vīro vīro viśvādhikaḥ prabhuḥ  LiP 
upahastā jvaraṃ bhīmo mṛgapakṣihiraṇmayaḥ 
śāstāśeṣasya jagato na tvaṃ naivacaturmukhaḥ  LiP 
itthaṃ sarvaṃ samālokya saṃharātmānam ātmanā 
no cedidānīṃ krodhasya mahābhairavarūpiṇaḥ  LiP 
vajrāśaniriva sthāṇos tv evaṃ mṛtyuḥ patiṣyati 
sūta uvāca
ityukto vīrabhadreṇa nṛsiṃhaḥ krodhavihvalaḥ  LiP 
nanāda tanuvegena taṃ gṛhītuṃ pracakrame 
atrāntare mahāghoraṃ vipakṣabhayakāraṇam  LiP 
gaganavyāpi durdharṣa śaivatejaḥsamudbhavam 
vīrabhadrasya tadrūpaṃ tatkṣaṇādeva dṛśyate  LiP 
na taddhiraṇmayaṃ saumyaṃ na sauraṃ nāgnisaṃbhavam 
na taḍiccandrasadṛśam anaupamyaṃ maheśvaram  LiP 
tadā tejāṃsi sarvāṇi tasmin līnāni śāṅkare 
tato vyakto mahātejā vyakte saṃbhavatastataḥ  LiP 
rudrasādhāraṇaṃ caiva cihnitaṃ vikṛtākṛti 
tataḥ saṃhārarūpeṇa suvyaktaḥ parameśvaraḥ  LiP 
paśyatāṃ sarvadevānāṃ jayaśabdādimaṅgalaiḥ 
sahasrabāhur jaṭilaś candrārdhakṛtaśekharaḥ  LiP 
sa mṛgārdhaśarīreṇa pakṣābhyāṃ cañcunā dvijāḥ 
atitīkṣṇamahādaṃṣṭro vajratulyanakhāyudhaḥ  LiP 
kaṇṭhe kālo mahābāhuś catuṣpād vahnisaṃbhavaḥ 
yugāntodyatajīmūta bhīmagaṃbhīraniḥsvanaḥ  LiP 
samaṃ kupitavṛttāgni vyāvṛttanayanatrayaḥ 
spaṣṭadaṃṣṭro 'dharoṣṭhaś ca huṅkāreṇa yuto haraḥ  LiP 
Śiva overcomes Viṣṇu
haristaddarśanādeva vinaṣṭabalavikramaḥ 
bibhrad aurmyaṃ sahasrāṃśor adhaḥ khadyotavibhramam  LiP 
atha vibhramya pakṣābhyāṃ nābhipāde 'bhyudārayan 
pādāvābadhya pucchena bāhubhyāṃ bāhumaṇḍalam  LiP 
bhindannurasi bāhubhyāṃ nijagrāha haro harim 
tato jagāma gaganaṃ devaiḥ saha maharṣibhiḥ  LiP 
sahasaiva bhayādviṣṇuṃ vihagaś ca yathoragam 
utkṣipyotkṣipya saṃgṛhya nipātya ca nipātya ca  LiP 
uḍḍīyoḍḍīya bhagavān pakṣāghātavimohitam 
hariṃ harantaṃ vṛṣabhaṃ viśveśānaṃ tamīśvaram  LiP 
anuyānti surāḥ sarve namovākyena tuṣṭuvuḥ 
nīyamānaḥ paravaśo dīnavaktraḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ  LiP 
tuṣṭāva parameśānaṃ haristaṃ lalitākṣaraiḥ 
Viṣṇu praises Śiva
śrīnṛsiṃha uvāca
namo rudrāya śarvāya mahāgrāsāya viṣṇave  LiP 
nama ugrāya bhīmāya namaḥ krodhāya manyave 
namo bhavāya śarvāya śaṅkarāya śivāya te  LiP 
kālakālāya kālāya mahākālāya mṛtyave 
vīrāya vīrabhadrāya kṣayadvīrāya śūline  LiP 
mahādevāya mahate paśūnāṃ pataye namaḥ 
ekāya nīlakaṇṭhāya śrīkaṇṭhāya pinākine  LiP 
namo 'nantāya sūkṣmāya namaste mṛtyumanyave 
parāya parameśāya parātparatarāya te  LiP 
parātparāya viśvāya namaste viśvamūrttaye 
namo viṣṇukalatrāya viṣṇukṣetrāya bhānave  LiP 
kaivartāya kirātāya mahāvyādhāya śāśvate 
bhairavāya śaraṇyāya mahābhairavarūpiṇe  LiP 
namo nṛsiṃhasaṃhartre kāmakālapurāraye 
mahāpāśaughasaṃhartre viṣṇumāyāntakāriṇe  LiP 
tryaṃbakāya tryakṣarāya śipiviṣṭāya mīḍhuṣe 
mṛtyuñjayāya śarvāya sarvajñāya makhāraye  LiP 
makheśāya vareṇyāya namaste vahnirūpiṇe 
mahāghrāṇāya jihvāya prāṇāpānapravartine  LiP 
triguṇāya triśūlāya guṇātītāya yogine 
saṃsārāya pravāhāya mahāyantrapravartine  LiP 
namaścandrāgnisūryāya muktivaicitryahetave 
varadāyāvatārāya sarvakāraṇahetave  LiP 
kapāline karālāya pataye puṇyakīrttaye 
amoghāyāgninetrāya lakulīśāya śaṃbhave  LiP 
bhiṣaktamāya muṇḍāya daṇḍine yogarūpiṇe 
meghavāhāya devāya pārvatīpataye namaḥ  LiP 
avyaktāya viśokāya sthirāya sthiradhanvine 
sthāṇave kṛttivāsāya namaḥ pañcārthahetave  LiP 
varadāyaikapādāya namaścandrārdhamauline 
namaste 'dhvararājāya vayasāṃ pataye namaḥ  LiP 
yogīśvarāya nityāya satyāya parameṣṭhine 
sarvātmane namastubhyaṃ namaḥ sarveśvarāya te  LiP 
ekadvitricatuḥpañca kṛtvas te 'stu namonamaḥ 
daśakṛtvastu sāhasra kṛtvaste ca namonamaḥ  LiP 
namo 'parimitaṃ kṛtvānantakṛtvo namonamaḥ 
namonamo namo bhūyaḥ punarbhūyo namonamaḥ  LiP 
sūta uvāca
nāmnāmaṣṭaśatenaivaṃ stutvāmṛtamayena tu 
punastu prārthayāmāsa nṛsiṃhaḥ śarabheśvaram  LiP 
yadā yadā mamājñānam atyahaṅkāradūṣitam 
tadā tadāpanetavyaṃ tvayaiva parameśvara  LiP 
evaṃ vijñāpayanprītaḥ śaṅkaraṃ narakesarī 
nanvaśakto bhavān viṣṇo jīvitāntaṃ parājitaḥ  LiP 
tadvaktraśeṣamātrāntaṃ kṛtvā sarvasya vigraham 
śuktiśityaṃ tadā maṅgaṃ vīrabhadraḥ kṣaṇāttataḥ  LiP 
devā ūcuḥ
atha brahmādayaḥ sarve vīrabhadra tvayā dṛśā 
jīvitāḥ smo vayaṃ devāḥ parjanyeneva pādapāḥ  LiP 
yasya bhīṣā dahatyagnir udeti ca raviḥ svayam 
vāto vāti ca so 'si tvaṃ mṛtyurdhāvati pañcamaḥ  LiP 
yadavyaktaṃ paraṃ vyoma kalātītaṃ sadāśivam 
bhagavaṃstvāmeva bhavaṃ vadanti brahmavādinaḥ  LiP 
ke vayameva dhātukye vedane parameśvaraḥ 
na viddhi paramaṃ dhāma rūpalāvaṇyavarṇane  LiP 
upasargeṣu sarveṣu trāyasvāsmān gaṇādhipa 
ekādaśātman bhagavān vartate rūpavān haraḥ  LiP 
īdṛśān te 'vatārāṇi dṛṣṭvā śiva bahūṃstamaḥ 
kadācit saṃdihen nāsmāṃs tvaccintāstamayā tathā  LiP 
guñjāgirivarataṭāmitarūpāṇi sarvaśaḥ 
abhyasaṃhara gamyaṃ te na nītavyaṃ parāparā  LiP 
dve tanū tava rudrasya vedajñā brāhmaṇā viduḥ 
ghorāpyanyā śivāpyanyā te pratyekamanekadhā  LiP 
ihāsmānpāhi bhagavan nityāhatamahābalaḥ 
bhavatā hi jagatsarvaṃ vyāptaṃ svenaiva tejasā  LiP 
brahmaviṣṇvindracandrādi vayaṃ ca pramukhāḥ surāḥ 
surāsurāḥ samprasūtās tvattaḥ sarve maheśvara  LiP 
brahmā ca indro viṣṇuś ca yamādyā na surāsurān 
tato nigṛhya ca hariṃ siṃha ity upacetasam  LiP 
yato bibharṣi sakalaṃ vibhajya tanumaṣṭadhā 
ato 'smān pāhi bhagavan surān dānair abhīpsitaiḥ  LiP 
uvāca tān surāndevo maharṣīṃś ca purātanān 
yathā jale jalaṃ kṣiptaṃ kṣīraṃ kṣīre ghṛtaṃ ghṛte  LiP 
eka eva tadā viṣṇuḥ śivalīno na cānyathā 
eṣa eva nṛsiṃhātmā sadarpaś ca mahābalaḥ  LiP 
jagatsaṃhārakāreṇa pravṛtto narakesarī 
yājanīyo namastasmai madbhaktisiddhikāṅkṣibhiḥ  LiP 
etāvaduktvā bhagavān vīrabhadro mahābalaḥ 
apaśyan sarvabhūtānāṃ tatraivāntaradhīyata  LiP 
nṛsiṃhakṛttivasanas tadāprabhṛti śaṅkaraḥ 
vaktraṃ tanmuṇḍamālāyāṃ nāyakatvena kalpitam  LiP 
tato devā nirātaṅkāḥ kīrtayantaḥ kathāmimām 
vismayotphullanayanā jagmuḥ sarve yathāgatam  LiP 
ya idaṃ paramākhyānaṃ puṇyaṃ vedaiḥ samanvitam 
paṭhitvā śṛṇute caiva sarvaduḥkhavināśanam  LiP 
dhanyaṃ yaśasyam āyuṣyam ārogyaṃ puṣṭivardhanam 
sarvavighnapraśamanaṃ sarvavyādhivināśanam  LiP 
apamṛtyupraśamanaṃ mahāśāntikaraṃ śubham 
aricakrapraśamanaṃ sarvādhipravināśanam  LiP 
tato duḥsvapnaśamanaṃ sarvabhūtanivāraṇam 
viṣagrahakṣayakaraṃ putrapautrādivardhanam  LiP 
yogasiddhipradaṃ samyak śivajñānaprakāśakam 
śeṣalokasya sopānaṃ vāñchitārthaikasādhanam  LiP 
viṣṇumāyānirasanaṃ devatāparamārthadam 
vāñchāsiddhipradaṃ caiva ṛddhiprajñādisādhanam  LiP 
idaṃ tu śarabhākāraṃ paraṃ rūpaṃ pinākinaḥ 
prakāśitavyaṃ bhakteṣu cireṣūdyamiteṣu ca  LiP 
taireva paṭhitavyaṃ ca śrotavyaṃ ca śivātmabhiḥ 
śivotsaveṣu sarveṣu caturdaśyaṣṭamīṣu ca  LiP 
paṭhetpratiṣṭhākāleṣu śivasannidhikāraṇam 
coravyāghrāhisiṃhānta kṛto rājabhayeṣu ca  LiP 
atrānyotpātabhūkampa davāgnipāṃsuvṛṣṭiṣu 
ulkāpāte mahāvāte vinā vṛṣṭyātivṛṣṭiṣu  LiP 
atastatra paṭhedvidvāñ chivabhakto dṛḍhavrataḥ 
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi stavaṃ sarvamanuttamam  LiP 
sa rudratvaṃ samāsādya rudrasyānucaro bhavet  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge śarabhaprādurbhāvo nāma ṣaṇṇavatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
