ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
jalandharaṃ jaṭāmauliḥ purā jambhārivikramam 
kathaṃ jaghāna bhagavān bhaganetraharo haraḥ  LiP 
vaktumarhasi cāsmākaṃ romaharṣaṇa suvrata 
sūta uvāca
jalandhara iti khyāto jalamaṇḍalasaṃbhavaḥ  LiP 
āsīdantakasaṃkāśas tapasā labdhavikramaḥ 
tena devāḥ sagandharvāḥ sayakṣoragarākṣasāḥ  LiP 
nirjitāḥ samare sarve brahmā ca bhagavānajaḥ 
jitvaiva devasaṃghātaṃ brahmāṇaṃ vai jalandharaḥ  LiP 
jagāma devadeveśaṃ viṣṇuṃ viśvaharaṃ gurum 
tayoḥ samabhavadyuddhaṃ divārātram aviśramam  LiP 
jalandhareśayostena nirjito madhusūdanaḥ 
jalandharo 'pi taṃ jitvā devadevaṃ janārdanam  LiP 
provācedaṃ diteḥ putrān nyāyadhīrjetumīśvaram 
sarve jitā mayā yuddhe śaṅkaro hyajito raṇe  LiP 
taṃ jitvā sarvamīśānaṃ gaṇapair nandinā kṣaṇāt 
ahameva bhavatvaṃ ca brahmatvaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ tathā  LiP 
vāsavatvaṃ ca yuṣmākaṃ dāsye dānavapuṅgavāḥ 
jalandharavacaḥ śrutvā sarve te dānavādhamāḥ  LiP 
jagarjuruccaiḥ pāpiṣṭhā mṛtyudarśanatatparāḥ 
daityairetaistathānyaiś ca rathanāgaturaṅgamaiḥ  LiP 
saṃnaddhaiḥ saha saṃnahya śarvaṃ prati yayau balī 
bhavo 'pi dṛṣṭvā daityendraṃ merukūṭamiva sthitam  LiP 
avadhyatvam api śrutvā tathānyair bhaganetrahā 
brahmaṇo vacanaṃ rakṣan rakṣako jagatāṃ prabhuḥ  LiP 
sāṃbaḥ sanandī sagaṇaḥ provāca prahasanniva 
kiṃ kṛtyamasureśāna yuddhenānena sāṃpratam  LiP 
madbāṇairbhinnasarvāṅgo martumabhyudyate mudā 
jalandharo 'pi tadvākyaṃ śrutvā śrotravidāraṇam  LiP 
sureśvaramuvācedaṃ suretarabaleśvaraḥ 
vākyenālaṃ mahābāho devadeva vṛṣadhvaja  LiP 
candrāṃśusannibhaiḥ śastrair hara yoddhumihāgataḥ 
niśamyāsya vacaḥ śūlī pādāṅguṣṭhena līlayā 
mahāṃbhasi cakārāśu rathāṅgaṃ raudramāyudham  LiP 
kṛtvārṇavāṃbhasi sitaṃ bhagavān rathāṅgaṃ smṛtvā jagattrayamanena hatāḥ surāś ca 
dakṣāndhakāntakapuratrayayajñahartā lokatrayāntakakaraḥ prahasaṃtadāha  LiP 
pādena nirmitaṃ daitya jalandhara mahārṇave 
balavān yadi coddhartuṃ tiṣṭha yoddhuṃ na cānyathā  LiP 
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā krodhenādīptalocanaḥ 
pradahanniva netrābhyāṃ prāhālokya jagattrayam  LiP 
jalandhara uvāca
gadāmuddhṛtya hatvā ca nandinaṃ tvāṃ ca śaṅkara 
hatvā lokānsuraiḥ sārdhaṃ ḍuṇḍubhān garuḍo yathā  LiP 
hantuṃ carācaraṃ sarvaṃ samartho 'haṃ savāsavam 
ko maheśvara madbāṇair acchedyo bhuvanatraye  LiP 
bālabhāve ca bhagavān tapasaiva vinirjitaḥ 
brahmā balī yauvane vai munayaḥ surapuṅgavaiḥ  LiP 
dagdhaṃ kṣaṇena sakalaṃ trailokyaṃ sacarācaram 
tapasā kiṃ tvayā rudra nirjito bhagavānapi  LiP 
indrāgniyamavitteśa vāyuvārīśvarādayaḥ 
na sehire yathā nāgā gandhaṃ pakṣipateriva  LiP 
na labdhvā divi bhūmau ca bāhavo mama śaṅkara 
samastānparvatānprāpya gharṣitāś ca gaṇeśvara  LiP 
girīndro mandaraḥ śrīmān nīlo meruḥ suśobhanaḥ 
gharṣito bāhudaṇḍena kaṇḍūnodārtham āpatat  LiP 
gaṅgā niruddhā bāhubhyāṃ līlārthaṃ himavadgirau 
nārīṇāṃ mama bhṛtyaiś ca vajro baddho divaukasām  LiP 
vaḍavāyā mukhaṃ bhagnaṃ gṛhītvā vai kareṇa tu 
tatkṣaṇādeva sakalaṃ caikārṇavamabhūdidam  LiP 
airāvatādayo nāgāḥ kṣiptāḥ sindhujalopari 
saratho bhagavānindraḥ kṣiptaś ca śatayojanam  LiP 
garuḍo 'pi mayā baddho nāgapāśena viṣṇunā 
urvaśyādyā mayā nītā nāryaḥ kārāgṛhāntaram  LiP 
kathaṃcillabdhavān śakraḥ śacīmekāṃ praṇamya mām 
māṃ na jānāsi daityendraṃ jalandharamumāpate  LiP 
sūta uvāca
evamukto mahādevaḥ prādahadvai rathaṃ tadā 
tasya netrāgnibhāgaika kalārdhārdhena cākulam  LiP 
daityānāmatulabalairhayaiś ca nāgair daityendrās tripuraripor nirīkṣaṇena 
nāgād vaiśasam anusaṃvṛtaś ca nāgair deveśaṃ vacanamuvāca cālpabuddhiḥ  LiP 
kiṃ kāryaṃ mama yudhi devadaityasaṃghair hantuṃ yatsakalamidaṃ kṣaṇātsamarthaḥ 
yattasmādbhayamihanāsti yoddhum īśa vāñchaiṣā vipulatarā na saṃśayo 'tra  LiP 
tasmāttvaṃ mama madanāridakṣaśatro yajñāre tripuraripo mamaiva vīraiḥ 
bhūtendrairharivadanena devasaṃghair yoddhuṃ te balamiha cāsti ceddhi tiṣṭha  LiP 
ityuktvātha mahādevaṃ mahādevārinandanaḥ 
na cacāla na sasmāra nihatānbāndhavānyudhi  LiP 
durmadenāvinītātmā dorbhyāmāsphoṭya dorbalāt 
sudarśanākhyaṃ yaccakraṃ tena hantuṃ samudyataḥ  LiP 
durdhareṇa rathāṅgena kṛcchreṇāpi dvijottamāḥ 
sthāpayāmāsa vai skandhe dvidhābhūtaś ca tena vai  LiP 
kuliśena yathā chinno dvidhā girivaro dvijāḥ 
papāta daityo balavān añjanādririvāparaḥ  LiP 
tasya raktena raudreṇa sampūrṇam abhavatkṣaṇāt 
tadraktamakhilaṃ rudra niyogānmāṃsameva ca  LiP 
mahārauravamāsādya raktakuṇḍamabhūdaho 
jalandharaṃ hataṃ dṛṣṭvā devagandharvapārṣadāḥ  LiP 
siṃhanādaṃ mahatkṛtvā sādhu deveti cābruvan 
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi jalandharavimardanam  LiP 
śrāvayedvā yathānyāyaṃ gāṇapatyamavāpnuyāt  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge jalandharavadho nāma saptanavatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ

ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
kathaṃ devena vai sūta devadevānmaheśvarāt 
sudarśanākhyaṃ vai labdhaṃ vaktumarhasi viṣṇunā  LiP 
sūta uvāca
devānām asurendrāṇām abhavacca sudāruṇaḥ 
sarveṣāmeva bhūtānāṃ vināśakaraṇo mahān  LiP 
te devāḥ śaktimuśalaiḥ sāyakairnataparvabhiḥ 
prabhidyamānāḥ kuntaiś ca dudruvurbhayavihvalāḥ  LiP 
parājitāstadā devā devadeveśvaraṃ harim

praṇipatya sthitāndevān idaṃ vacanamabravīt  LiP 
vatsāḥ kimiti vai devāś cyutālaṅkāravikramāḥ 
samāgatāḥ sasaṃtāpā vaktumarhatha suvratāḥ  LiP 
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā tathābhūtāḥ surottamāḥ 
praṇamyāhuryathāvṛttaṃ devadevāya viṣṇave  LiP 
bhagavandevadeveśa viṣṇo jiṣṇo janārdana

tvameva devadeveśa gatirnaḥ puruṣottama

tvameva bhartā hartā ca bhoktā dātā janārdana 
hantumarhasi tasmāttvaṃ dānavāndānavārdana  LiP 
daityāś ca vaiṣṇavairbrāhmai raudrairyāmyaiḥ sudāruṇaiḥ 
kauberaiścaiva saumyaiś ca nairṛtyairvāruṇairdṛḍhaiḥ  LiP

saurai raudrais tathā bhīmaiḥ kampanair jṛmbhaṇair dṛḍhaiḥ  LiP 
avadhyā varalābhātte sarve vārijalocana 
sūryamaṇḍalasambhūtaṃ tvadīyaṃ cakram udyatam  LiP 
kuṇṭhitaṃ hi dadhīcena cyāvanena jagadguro 
daṇḍaṃ śārṅgaṃ tavāstraṃ ca labdhaṃ daityaiḥ prasādataḥ  LiP 
purā jalandharaṃ hantuṃ nirmitaṃ tripurāriṇā 
rathāṅgaṃ suśitaṃ ghoraṃ tena tān hantum arhasi  LiP 
tasmāttena nihantavyā nānyaiḥ śastraśatairapi 
tato niśamya teṣāṃ vai vacanaṃ vārijekṣaṇaḥ  LiP 
vācaspatimukhānāha sa hariścakrabhṛt svayam 
śrīviṣṇur uvāca
bhobho devā mahādevaṃ sarvair devaiḥ sanātanaiḥ  LiP 
samprāpya sāṃprataṃ sarvaṃ kariṣyāmi divaukasām 
devā jalandharaṃ hantuṃ nirmitaṃ hi purāriṇā  LiP

sabāndhavānkṣaṇādeva yuṣmān saṃtārayāmyaham 
sūta uvāca
evam uktvā suraśreṣṭhān suraśreṣṭhamanusmaran  LiP 
suraśreṣṭhastadā śreṣṭhaṃ pūjayāmāsa śaṅkaram 
liṅgaṃ sthāpya yathānyāyaṃ himavacchikhare śubhe  LiP 
meruparvatasaṃkāśaṃ nirmitaṃ viśvakarmaṇā

devaṃ nāmnāṃ sahasreṇa bhavādyena yathākramam

svāhāntairvidhivaddhutvā pratyekamayutaṃ prabhum  LiP

vītadoṣo 'kṣayaguṇo dakṣāriḥ pūṣadantahṛt 
dhūrjaṭiḥ khaṇḍaparaśuḥ sakalo niṣkalo 'naghaḥ  LiP 
ādhāraḥ sakalādhāraḥ pāṇḍurābho mṛḍo naṭaḥ 
pūrṇaḥ pūrayitā puṇyaḥ sukumāraḥ sulocanaḥ  LiP 
sāmageyaḥ priyakaraḥ puṇyakīrtiranāmayaḥ 
manojavastīrthakaro jaṭilo jīviteśvaraḥ  LiP 
jīvitāntakaro nityo vasuretā vasupriyaḥ 
sadgatiḥ satkṛtiḥ saktaḥ kālakaṇṭhaḥ kalādharaḥ  LiP 
mānī mānyo mahākālaḥ sadbhūtiḥ satparāyaṇaḥ 
candrasaṃjīvanaḥ śāstā lokagūḍho 'marādhipaḥ  LiP 
lokabandhurlokanāthaḥ kṛtajñaḥ kṛtibhūṣaṇaḥ 
anapāyyakṣaraḥ kāntaḥ sarvaśāstrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ  LiP 
tejomayo dyutidharo lokamāyo 'graṇīr aṇuḥ 
śucismitaḥ prasannātmā durjayo duratikramaḥ  LiP 
jyotirmayo nirākāro jagannātho jaleśvaraḥ 
tumbavīṇī mahākāyo viśokaḥ śokanāśanaḥ  LiP 
trilokātmā trilokeśaḥ śuddhaḥ śuddhī rathākṣajaḥ 
avyaktalakṣaṇo vyakto vyaktāvyakto viśāṃpatiḥ  LiP 
varaśīlo varatulo māno mānadhano mayaḥ 
brahmā viṣṇuḥ prajāpālo haṃso haṃsagatiryamaḥ  LiP 
vedhā dhātā vidhātā ca attā hartā caturmukhaḥ 
kailāsaśikharāvāsī sarvāvāsī satāṃ gatiḥ  LiP 
hiraṇyagarbho hariṇaḥ puruṣaḥ pūrvajaḥ pitā 
bhūtālayo bhūtapatir bhūtido bhuvaneśvaraḥ  LiP 
saṃyogī yogavidbrahma brahmaṇyo brāhmaṇapriyaḥ 
devapriyo devanātho devajño devacintakaḥ  LiP 
viṣamākṣaḥ kalādhyakṣo vṛṣāṅko vṛṣavardhanaḥ 
nirmado nirahaṅkāro nirmoho nirupadravaḥ  LiP 
darpahā darpito dṛptaḥ sarvartuparivartakaḥ 
saptajihvaḥ sahasrārciḥ snigdhaḥ prakṛtidakṣiṇaḥ  LiP 
bhūtabhavyabhavannāthaḥ prabhavo bhrāntināśanaḥ 
artho 'nartho mahākośaḥ parakāryaikapaṇḍitaḥ  LiP 
niṣkaṇṭakaḥ kṛtānando nirvyājo vyājamardanaḥ 
sattvavān sāttvikaḥ satya kīrtistambhakṛtāgamaḥ  LiP 
akaṃpito guṇagrāhī naikātmā naikakarmakṛt 
suprītaḥ sumukhaḥ sūkṣmaḥ sukaro dakṣiṇo 'nalaḥ  LiP 
skandhaḥ skandhadharo dhuryaḥ prakaṭaḥ prītivardhanaḥ 
aparājitaḥ sarvasaho vidagdhaḥ sarvavāhanaḥ  LiP 
adhṛtaḥ svadhṛtaḥ sādhyaḥ pūrvamūrtiryaśodharaḥ 
varāhaśṛṅgadhṛg vāyur balavān ekanāyakaḥ  LiP 
śrutiprakāśaḥ śrutimān ekabandhur anekadhṛk 
śrīvallabhaśivārambhaḥ śāntabhadraḥ samañjasaḥ  LiP 
bhūśayo bhūtikṛdbhūtir bhūṣaṇo bhūtavāhanaḥ 
akāyo bhaktakāyasthaḥ kālajñānī kalāvapuḥ  LiP 
satyavratamahātyāgī niṣṭhāśāntiparāyaṇaḥ 
parārthavṛttir varado viviktaḥ śrutisāgaraḥ  LiP 
anirviṇṇo guṇagrāhī kalaṅkāṅkaḥ kalaṅkahā 
svabhāvarudro madhyasthaḥ śatrughno madhyanāśakaḥ  LiP 
śikhaṇḍī kavacī śūlī caṇḍī muṇḍī ca kuṇḍalī 
mekhalī kavacī khaḍgī māyī saṃsārasārathiḥ  LiP 
amṛtyuḥ sarvadṛk siṃhas tejorāśir mahāmaṇiḥ 
asaṃkhyeyo 'prameyātmā vīryavān kāryakovidaḥ  LiP 
vedyo vedārthavidgoptā sarvācāro munīśvaraḥ 
anuttamo durādharṣo madhuraḥ priyadarśanaḥ  LiP 
sureśaḥ śaraṇaṃ sarvaḥ śabdabrahma satāṃ gatiḥ 
kālabhakṣaḥ kalaṅkāriḥ kaṅkaṇīkṛtavāsukiḥ  LiP 
maheṣvāso mahībhartā niṣkalaṅko viśṛṅkhalaḥ 
dyumaṇis taraṇir dhanyaḥ siddhidaḥ siddhisādhanaḥ  LiP 
nivṛttaḥ saṃvṛtaḥ śilpo vyūḍhorasko mahābhujaḥ 
ekajyotir nirātaṅko naro nārāyaṇapriyaḥ  LiP 
nirlepo niṣprapañcātmā nirvyagro vyagranāśanaḥ 
stavyastavapriyaḥ stotā vyāsamūrtiranākulaḥ  LiP 
niravadyapadopāyo vidyārāśiravikramaḥ 
praśāntabuddhirakṣudraḥ kṣudrahā nityasundaraḥ  LiP 
dhairyāgryadhuryo dhātrīśaḥ śākalyaḥ śarvarīpatiḥ 
paramārthagurur dṛṣṭir gurur āśritavatsalaḥ  LiP 
raso rasajñaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarvasattvāvalaṃbanaḥ 
sūta uvāca
evaṃ nāmnāṃ sahasreṇa tuṣṭāva vṛṣabhadhvajam  LiP 
snāpayāmāsa ca vibhuḥ pūjayāmāsa paṅkajaiḥ 
parīkṣārthaṃ hareḥ pūjā kamaleṣu maheśvaraḥ  LiP 
gopayāmāsa kamalaṃ tadaikaṃ bhuvaneśvaraḥ 
hṛtapuṣpo haristatra kimidaṃ tvabhyacintayat  LiP 
jñātvā svanetramuddhṛtya sarvasattvāvalambanam 
pūjayāmāsa bhāvena nāmnā tena jagadgurum  LiP 
tatastatra vibhurdṛṣṭvā tathābhūtaṃ haro harim 
tasmādavatatārāśu maṇḍalātpāvakasya ca  LiP 
koṭibhāskarasaṃkāśaṃ jaṭāmukuṭamaṇḍitam 
jvālāmālāvṛtaṃ divyaṃ tīkṣṇadaṃṣṭraṃ bhayaṅkaram  LiP 
śūlaṭaṅkagadācakra kuntapāśadharaṃ haram 
varādabhayahastaṃ ca dvīpicarmottarīyakam  LiP 
itthaṃbhūtaṃ tadā dṛṣṭvā bhavaṃ bhasmavibhūṣitam 
hṛṣṭo namaścakārāśu devadevaṃ janārdanaḥ  LiP 
dudruvustaṃ parikramya sendrā devāstrilocanam 
cacāla brahmabhuvanaṃ cakampe ca vasuṃdharā  LiP 
dadāha tejastacchaṃbhoḥ prāntaṃ vai śatayojanam 
adhastāccordhvataścaiva hāhetyakṛta bhūtale  LiP 
tadā prāha mahādevaḥ prahasanniva śaṅkaraḥ 
samprekṣya praṇayādviṣṇuṃ kṛtāñjalipuṭaṃ sthitam  LiP 
jñātaṃ mayedamadhunā devakāryaṃ janārdana 
sudarśanākhyaṃ cakraṃ ca dadāmi tava śobhanam  LiP 
yadrūpaṃ bhavatā dṛṣṭaṃ sarvalokabhayaṃkaram 
hitāya tava yatnena tava bhāvāya suvrata  LiP 
śāntaṃ raṇājire viṣṇo devānāṃ duḥkhasādhanam 
śāntasya cāstraṃ śāntaḥ syāc chāntenāstreṇa kiṃ phalam  LiP 
śāntasya samare cāstraṃ śāntireva tapasvinām 
yoddhuḥ śāntyā balacchedaḥ parasya balavṛddhidaḥ  LiP 
devairaśāntairyadrūpaṃ madīyaṃ bhāvayāvyayam 
kimāyudhena kāryaṃ vai yoddhuṃ devārisūdana  LiP 
kṣamā yudhi na kāryaṃ vai yoddhuṃ devārisūdana 
anāgate vyatīte ca daurbalye svajanotkare  LiP 
akālike tvadharme ca anarthe vārisūdana 
evamuktvā dadau cakraṃ sūryāyutasamaprabham  LiP 
netraṃ ca netā jagatāṃ prabhurvai padmasannibham 
tadāprabhṛti taṃ prāhuḥ padmākṣamiti suvratam  LiP 
dattvainaṃ nayanaṃ cakraṃ viṣṇave nīlalohitaḥ 
pasparśa ca karābhyāṃ vai suśubhābhyāmuvāca ha  LiP 
varado 'haṃ varaśreṣṭha varānvaraya cepsitān 
bhaktyā vaśīkṛto nūnaṃ tvayāhaṃ puruṣottama  LiP 
ityukto devadevena devadevaṃ praṇamya tam 
tvayi bhaktirmahādeva prasīda varamuttamam  LiP 
nānyamicchāmi bhaktānām ārtayo nāsti yatprabho 
tacchrutvā vacanaṃ tasya dayāvān sutarāṃ bhavaḥ  LiP 
pasparśa ca dadau tasmai śraddhāṃ śītāṃśubhūṣaṇaḥ 
prāha caivaṃ mahādevaḥ paramātmānamacyutam  LiP 
mayi bhaktaś ca vandyaś ca pūjyaścaiva surāsuraiḥ 
bhaviṣyasi na saṃdeho matprasādātsurottama  LiP 
yadā satī dakṣaputrī vinindyaiva sulocanā 
mātaraṃ pitaraṃ dakṣaṃ bhaviṣyati sureśvarī  LiP 
divyā haimavatī viṣṇo tadā tvamapi suvrata 
bhaginīṃ tava kalyāṇīṃ devīṃ haimavatīmumām  LiP 
niyogād brahmaṇaḥ sādhvīṃ pradāsyasi mamaiva tām 
matsaṃbandhī ca lokānāṃ madhye pūjyo bhaviṣyasi  LiP 
māṃ divyena ca bhāvena tadāprabhṛti śaṅkaram 
drakṣyase ca prasannena mitrabhūtamivātmanā  LiP 
ityuktvāntardadhe rudro bhagavānnīlalohitaḥ 
janārdano 'pi bhagavān devānāmapi saṃnidhau  LiP 
ayācata mahādevaṃ brahmāṇaṃ munibhiḥ samam 
mayā proktaṃ stavaṃ divyaṃ padmayone suśobhanam  LiP 
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi śrāvayedvā dvijottamān 
pratināmni hiraṇyasya tat tasya phalam āpnuyāt  LiP 
aśvamedhasahasreṇa phalaṃ bhavati tasya vai 
ghṛtādyaiḥ snāpayedrudraṃ sthālyā vai kalaśaiḥ śubhaiḥ  LiP 
nāmnāṃ sahasreṇānena śraddhayā śivamīśvaram 
so 'pi yajñasahasrasya phalaṃ labdhvāsureśvaraiḥ  LiP 
pūjyo bhavati rudrasya prītirbhavati tasya vai 
tathāstviti tathā prāha padmayonerjanārdanam  LiP 
jagmatuḥ praṇipatyainaṃ devadevaṃ jagadgurum 
tasmānnāmnāṃ sahasreṇa pūjayed anagho dvijāḥ  LiP 
japennāmnāṃ sahasraṃ ca sa yāti paramāṃ gatim  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge sahasranāmabhiḥ pūjanād viṣṇucakralābho nāmāṣṭanavatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
LiP  
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
saṃbhavaḥ sūcito devyās tvayā sūta mahāmate 
savistaraṃ vadasvādya satītve ca yathātatham  LiP 
menājatvaṃ mahādevyā dakṣayajñavimardanam 
viṣṇunā ca kathaṃ dattā devadevāya śaṃbhave  LiP 
kalyāṇaṃ vā kathaṃ tasya vaktumarhasi sāṃpratam 
teṣāṃ tadvacanaṃ śrutvā sūtaḥ paurāṇikottamaḥ  LiP 
saṃbhavaṃ ca mahādevyāḥ prāha teṣāṃ mahātmanām 
sūta uvāca
brahmaṇā kathitaṃ pūrvaṃ daṇḍine tat suvistaram  LiP 
yuṣmābhir vai kumārāya tena vyāsāya dhīmate 
tasmādahamupaśrutya pravadāmi suvistaram  LiP 
vacanādvo mahābhāgāḥ praṇamyomāṃ tathā bhavam 
sā bhagākhyā jagaddhātrī liṅgamūrtestrivedikā  LiP 
liṅgastu bhagavāndvābhyāṃ jagatsṛṣṭirdvijottamāḥ 
liṅgamūrtiḥ śivo jyotis tamasaścopari sthitaḥ  LiP 
liṅgavedisamāyogād ardhanārīśvarobhavat 
brahmāṇaṃ vidadhe devam agre putraṃ caturmukham  LiP 
prāhiṇoti sma tasyaiva jñānaṃ jñānamayo haraḥ 
viśvādhiko 'sau bhagavān ardhanārīśvaro vibhuḥ  LiP 
hiraṇyagarbhaṃ taṃ devo jāyamānamapaśyata 
so 'pi rudraṃ mahādevaṃ brahmāpaśyata śaṅkaram  LiP 
taṃ dṛṣṭvā saṃsthitaṃ devam ardhanārīśvaraṃ prabhum 
tuṣṭāva vāgbhir iṣṭābhir varadaṃ vārijodbhavaḥ  LiP 
vibhajasveti viśveśaṃ viśvātmānamajo vibhuḥ 
sasarja devīṃ vāmāṅgāt patnīṃ caivātmanaḥ samām  LiP 
śraddhā hyasya śubhā patnī tataḥ puṃsaḥ purātanī 
saivājñayā vibhordevī dakṣaputrī babhūva ha  LiP 
satīsaṃjñā tadā sā vai rudramevāśritā patim 
dakṣaṃ vinindya kālena devī mainā hyabhūtpunaḥ  LiP 
nāradasyaiva dakṣo 'pi śāpādevaṃ vinindya ca 
avajñādurmado dakṣo devadevamumāpatim  LiP 
anādṛtya kṛtiṃ jñātvā satī dakṣeṇa tatkṣaṇāt 
bhasmīkṛtvātmano dehaṃ yogamārgeṇa sā punaḥ  LiP 
babhūva pārvatī devī tapasā ca gireḥ prabhoḥ 
jñātvaitadbhagavān bhargo dadāha ruṣitaḥ prabhuḥ  LiP 
dakṣasya vipulaṃ yajñaṃ cyāvaner vacanādapi 
cyavanasya suto dhīmān dadhīca iti viśrutaḥ  LiP 
vijitya viṣṇuṃ samare prasādāt tryaṃbakasya ca 
viṣṇunā lokapālāṃś ca śaśāpa ca munīśvaraḥ  LiP 
rudrasya krodhajenaiva vahninā haviṣā surāḥ 
vināśo vai kṣaṇādeva māyayā śaṅkarasya vai  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge devīsaṃbhavo nāma navanavatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
LiP  
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
vijitya viṣṇunā sārdhaṃ bhagavānparameśvaraḥ 
sarvāndadhīcavacanāt kathaṃ bheje maheśvaraḥ  LiP 
sūta uvāca
dakṣayajñe suvipule devān viṣṇupurogamān 
dadāha bhagavān rudraḥ sarvān munigaṇān api  LiP 
bhadro nāma gaṇastena preṣitaḥ parameṣṭhinā 
viprayogena devyā vai duḥsahenaiva suvratāḥ  LiP 
so 'sṛjad vīrabhadraś ca gaṇeśānromajāñchubhān 
gaṇeśvaraiḥ samāruhya rathaṃ bhadraḥ pratāpavān  LiP 
gantuṃ cakre matiṃ yasya sārathirbhagavānajaḥ 
gaṇeśvarāś ca te sarve vividhāyudhapāṇayaḥ  LiP 
vimānairviśvato bhadrais tamanvayuratho surāḥ 
himavacchikhare ramye hemaśṛṅge suśobhane  LiP 
yajñavāṭas tathā tasya gaṅgādvārasamīpataḥ 
taddeśe caiva vikhyātaṃ śubhaṃ kanakhalaṃ dvijāḥ  LiP 
dagdhuṃ vai preṣitaścāsau bhagavān parameṣṭhinā 
tadotpāto babhūvātha lokānāṃ bhayaśaṃsanaḥ  LiP 
parvatāś ca vyaśīryanta pracakampe vasuṃdharā 
marutaś cāpy aghūrṇanta cukṣubhe makarālayaḥ  LiP 
agnayo naiva dīpyanti na ca dīpyati bhāskaraḥ 
grahāś ca na prakāśyante na devā na ca dānavāḥ  LiP 
tataḥ kṣaṇāt praviśyaiva yajñavāṭaṃ mahātmanaḥ 
romajaiḥ sahito bhadraḥ kālāgnirivacāparaḥ  LiP 
uvāca bhadro bhagavān dakṣaṃ cāmitatejasam 
saṃparkādeva dakṣādya munīndevān pinākinā  LiP 
dagdhuṃ saṃpreṣitaś cāhaṃ bhavantaṃ samunīśvaraiḥ 
ityuktvā yajñaśālāṃ tāṃ dadāha gaṇapuṅgavaḥ  LiP 
gaṇeśvarāś ca saṃkruddhā yūpānutpāṭya cikṣipuḥ 
prastotrā saha hotrā ca dagdhaṃ caiva gaṇeśvaraiḥ  LiP 
gṛhītvā gaṇapāḥ sarvān gaṅgāsrotasi cikṣipuḥ 
vīrabhadro mahātejāḥ śakrasyodyacchataḥ karam  LiP 
vyaṣṭambhayad adīnātmā tathānyeṣāṃ divaukasām 
bhagasya netre cotpāṭya karajāgreṇa līlayā  LiP 
nihatya muṣṭinā dantān pūṣṇaścaivaṃ nyapātayat 
tathā candramasaṃ devaṃ pādāṅguṣṭhena līlayā  LiP 
gharṣayāmāsa bhagavān vīrabhadraḥ pratāpavān 
cicheda ca śirastasya śakrasya bhagavānprabhoḥ  LiP 
vahnerhastadvayaṃ chittvā jihvāmutpāṭya līlayā 
jaghāna mūrdhni pādena vīrabhadro mahābalaḥ  LiP 
yamasya daṇḍaṃ bhagavān pracicheda svayaṃ prabhuḥ 
jaghāna devamīśānaṃ triśūlena mahābalam  LiP 
trayastriṃśatsurānevaṃ vinihatyāprayatnataḥ 
trayaś ca triśataṃ teṣāṃ trisāhasraṃ ca līlayā  LiP 
trayaṃ caiva surendrāṇāṃ jaghāna ca munīśvarān 
anyāṃś ca devān devo 'sau sarvānyuddhāya saṃsthitān  LiP 
jaghāna bhagavān rudraḥ khaḍgamuṣṭyādisāyakaiḥ 
atha viṣṇurmahātejāś cakram udyamya mūrchitaḥ  LiP 
yuyodha bhagavāṃstena rudreṇa saha mādhavaḥ 
tayoḥ samabhavadyuddhaṃ sughoraṃ romaharṣaṇam  LiP 
viṣṇoryogabalāttasya divyadehāḥ sudāruṇāḥ  LiP 
śaṅkhacakragadāhastā asaṃkhyātāś ca jajñire 
tānsarvānapi devo 'sau nārāyaṇasamaprabhān  LiP 
nihatya gadayā viṣṇuṃ tāḍayāmāsa mūrdhani 
tataścorasi taṃ devaṃ līlayaiva raṇājire  LiP 
papāta ca tadā bhūmau visaṃjñaḥ puruṣottamaḥ 
punarutthāya taṃ hantuṃ cakramudyamya sa prabhuḥ  LiP 
krodharaktekṣaṇaḥ śrīmān atiṣṭhat puruṣarṣabhaḥ 
tasya cakraṃ ca yadraudraṃ kālādityasamaprabham  LiP 
vyaṣṭambhayad adīnātmā karasthaṃ na cacāla saḥ 
atiṣṭhat stambhitastena śṛṅgavāniva niścalaḥ  LiP 
tribhiś ca dharṣitaṃ śārṅgaṃ tridhābhūtaṃ prabhostadā 
śārṅgakoṭiprasaṅgād vai cicheda ca śiraḥ prabhoḥ  LiP 
chinnaṃ ca nipapātāsu śirastasya rasātale 
vāyunā preritaṃ caiva prāṇajena pinākinā  LiP 
praviveśa tadā caiva tadīyāhavanīyakam 
tat pratidhvastakalaśaṃ bhagnayūpaṃ satoraṇam  LiP 
pradīpitamahāśālaṃ dṛṣṭvā yajño 'pi dudruve 
taṃ tadā mṛgarūpeṇa dhāvantaṃ gaganaṃ prati  LiP 
vīrabhadraḥ samādhāya viśiraskamathākarot 
tataḥ prajāpatiṃ dharmaṃ kaśyapaṃ ca jagadgurum  LiP 
ariṣṭaneminaṃ vīro bahuputraṃ munīśvaram 
munim aṅgirasaṃ caiva kṛṣṇāśvaṃ ca mahābalaḥ  LiP 
jaghāna mūrdhni pādena dakṣaṃ caiva yaśasvinam 
cicheda ca śirastasya dadāhāgnau dvijottamāḥ  LiP 
sarasvatyāś ca nāsāgraṃ devamātustathaiva ca 
nikṛtya karajāgreṇa vīrabhadraḥ pratāpavān  LiP 
tasthau śriyā vṛto madhye pretasthāne yathā bhavaḥ 
etasminneva kāle tu bhagavānpadmasaṃbhavaḥ  LiP 
bhadramāha mahātejāḥ prārthayanpraṇataḥ prabhuḥ 
alaṃ krodhena vai bhadra naṣṭāścaiva divaukasaḥ  LiP 
prasīda kṣamyatāṃ sarvaṃ romajaiḥ saha suvrata 
so 'pi bhadraḥ prabhāveṇa brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ  LiP 
śamaṃ jagāma śanakaiḥ śāntastasthau tadājñayā 
devo 'pi tatra bhagavān antarikṣe vṛṣadhvajaḥ  LiP 
sagaṇaḥ sarvadaḥ śarvaḥ sarvalokamaheśvaraḥ 
prārthitaścaiva devena brahmaṇā bhagavān bhavaḥ  LiP 
hatānāṃ ca tadā teṣāṃ pradadau pūrvavattanum 
indrasya ca śirastasya viṣṇoścaiva mahātmanaḥ  LiP 
dakṣasya ca munīndrasya tathānyeṣāṃ maheśvaraḥ 
vāgīśyāścaiva nāsāgraṃ devamātustathaiva ca  LiP 
naṣṭānāṃ jīvitaṃ caiva varāṇi vividhāni ca 
dakṣasya dhvastavaktrasya śirasā bhagavānprabhuḥ  LiP 
kalpayāmāsa vai vaktraṃ līlayā ca mahān bhavaḥ 
dakṣo 'pi labdhasaṃjñaś ca samutthāya kṛtāñjaliḥ  LiP 
tuṣṭāva devadeveśaṃ śaṅkaraṃ vṛṣabhadhvajam 
stutastena mahātejāḥ pradāya vividhānvarān  LiP 
gāṇapatyaṃ dadau tasmai dakṣāyākliṣṭakarmaṇe 
devāś ca sarve deveśaṃ tuṣṭuvuḥ parameśvaram  LiP 
nārāyaṇaś ca bhagavān tuṣṭāva ca kṛtāñjaliḥ 
brahmā ca munayaḥ sarve pṛthakpṛthagajodbhavam  LiP 
tuṣṭuvur devadeveśaṃ nīlakaṇṭhaṃ vṛṣadhvajam 
tān devān anugṛhyaiva bhavo 'pyantaradhīyata  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge śivakṛddakṣayajñavidhvaṃsano nāma śatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
LiP  
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
kathaṃ himavataḥ putrī babhūvāṃbā satī śubhā 
kathaṃ vā devadeveśam avāpa patimīśvaram  LiP 
sūta uvāca
sā menātanum āśritya svecchayaiva varāṅganā 
tadā haimavatī jajñe tapasā ca dvijottamāḥ  LiP 
jātakarmādikāḥ sarvāś cakāra ca girīśvaraḥ 
dvādaśe ca tadā varṣe pūrṇe haimavatī śubhā  LiP 
tapastepe tayā sārdham anujā ca śubhānanā 
anyā ca devī hyanujā sarvaloke namaskṛtā  LiP 
ṛṣayaś ca tadā sarve sarvalokamaheśvarīm 
tuṣṭuvus tapasā devīṃ samāvṛtya samantataḥ  LiP 
jyeṣṭhā hyaparṇā hyanujā caikaparṇā śubhānanā 
tṛtīyā ca varārohā tathā caivaikapāṭalā  LiP 
tapasā ca mahādevyāḥ pārvatyāḥ parameśvaraḥ 
vaśīkṛto mahādevaḥ sarvabhūtapatirbhavaḥ  LiP 
etasminneva kāle tu tārako nāma dānavaḥ 
tārātmajo mahātejā babhūva ditinandanaḥ  LiP 
tasya putrāstrayaścāpi tārakākṣo mahāsuraḥ 
vidyunmālī ca bhagavān kamalākṣaś ca vīryavān  LiP 
pitāmahas tathā caiṣāṃ tāro nāma mahābalaḥ 
tapasā labdhavīryaś ca prasādādbrahmaṇaḥ prabhoḥ  LiP 
so 'pi tāro mahātejās trailokyaṃ sacarācaram 
vijitya samare pūrvaṃ viṣṇuṃ ca jitavān asau  LiP 
tayoḥ samabhavadyuddhaṃ sughoraṃ romaharṣaṇam 
divyaṃ varṣasahasraṃ tu divārātram aviśramam  LiP 
sarathaṃ viṣṇumādāya cikṣepa śatayojanam 
tāreṇa vijitaḥ saṃkhye dudrāva garuḍadhvajaḥ  LiP 
tāro varāñchataguṇaṃ labdhvā śataguṇaṃ balam 
pitāmahājjagatsarvam avāpa ditinandanaḥ  LiP 
devendrapramukhāñjitvā devāndeveśvareśvaraḥ 
vārayāmāsa tair devān sarvalokeṣu māyayā  LiP 
devatāś ca sahendreṇa tārakādbhayapīḍitāḥ 
na śāntiṃ lebhire śūrāḥ śaraṇaṃ vā bhayārditāḥ  LiP 
tadāmarapatiḥ śrīmān saṃnipatyāmaraprabhuḥ 
uvācāṅgirasaṃ devo devānāmapi saṃnidhau  LiP 
bhagavaṃstārako nāma tārajo dānavottamaḥ 
tena saṃnihatā yuddhe vatsā gopatinā yathā  LiP 
bhayāttasmānmahābhāga bṛhadyuddhe bṛhaspate 
aniketā bhramantyete śakuntā iva pañjare  LiP 
asmākaṃ yāny amoghāni āyudhāny aṅgiro vara 
tāni moghāni jāyante prabhāvādamaradviṣaḥ  LiP 
daśavarṣasahasrāṇi dviguṇāni bṛhaspate 
viṣṇunā yodhito yuddhe tenāpi na ca sūditaḥ  LiP 
yastenānirjito yuddhe viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā 
kathamasmadvidhastasya sthāsyate samare 'grataḥ  LiP 
evam uktas tu śakreṇa jīvaḥ sārdhaṃ surādhipaiḥ 
sahasrākṣeṇa ca vibhuṃ samprāpyāha kuśadhvajam  LiP 
so 'pi tasya mukhācchrutvā praṇayātpraṇatārtihā 
devairaśeṣaiḥ sendraistu jīvamāha pitāmahaḥ  LiP 
jāne vo 'rtiṃ surendrāṇāṃ tathāpi śṛṇu sāṃpratam 
vinindya dakṣaṃ yā devī satī rudrāṅgasaṃbhavā  LiP 
umā haimavatī jajñe sarvalokanamaskṛtā 
tasyāścaiveha rūpeṇa yūyaṃ devāḥ surottamāḥ  LiP 
vibhoryatadhvamākraṣṭuṃ rudrasyāsya mano mahat 
tayoryogena sambhūtaḥ skandaḥ śaktidharaḥ prabhuḥ  LiP 
ṣaḍāsyo dvādaśabhujaḥ senānīḥ pāvakiḥ prabhuḥ 
svāheyaḥ kārtikeyaś ca gāṅgeyaḥ śaradhāmajaḥ  LiP 
devaḥ śākho viśākhaś ca naigameśaś ca vīryavān 
senāpatiḥ kumārākhyaḥ sarvalokanamaskṛtaḥ  LiP 
līlayaiva mahāsenaḥ prabalaṃ tārakāsuram 
bālo 'pi vinihatyaiko devān saṃtārayiṣyati  LiP 
evam uktas tadā tena brahmaṇā parameṣṭhinā 
bṛhaspatis tathā sendrair devair devaṃ praṇamya tam  LiP 
Śiva burns Kāma
meroḥ śikharamāsādya smaraṃ sasmāra suvrataḥ 
smaraṇāddevadevasya smaro 'pi saha bhāryayā  LiP 
ratyā samaṃ samāgamya namaskṛtya kṛtāñjaliḥ 
saśakramāha taṃ jīvaṃ jagajjīvo dvijottamāḥ  LiP 
smṛto yadbhavatā jīva samprāpto 'haṃ tavāntikam 
brūhi yanme vidhātavyaṃ tamāha surapūjitaḥ  LiP 
tam āha bhagavāñchakraḥ saṃbhāvya makaradhvajam 
śaṅkareṇāṃbikāmadya saṃyojaya yathāsukham  LiP 
tayā sa ramate yena bhagavān vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ 
tena mārgeṇa mārgasva patnyā ratyānayā saha  LiP 
so 'pi tuṣṭo mahādevaḥ pradāsyati śubhāṃ gatim 
viprayuktastayā pūrvaṃ labdhvā tāṃ girijāmumām  LiP 
evamukto namaskṛtya devadevaṃ śacīpatim 
devadevāśramaṃ gantuṃ matiṃ cakre tayā saha  LiP 
gatvā tadāśraye śaṃbhoḥ saha ratyā mahābalaḥ 
vasaṃtena sahāyena devaṃ yoktumanā bhavat  LiP 
tataḥ samprekṣya madanaṃ hasan devas triyaṃbakaḥ 
nayanena tṛtīyena sāvajñaṃ tam avaikṣata  LiP 
tato 'sya netrajo vahnir madanaṃ pārśvataḥ sthitam 
adahattatkṣaṇādeva lalāpa karuṇaṃ ratiḥ  LiP 
ratyāḥ pralāpamākarṇya devadevo vṛṣadhvajaḥ 
kṛpayā parayā prāha kāmapatnīṃ nirīkṣya ca  LiP 
amūrto 'pi dhruvaṃ bhadre kāryaṃ sarvaṃ patistava 
ratikāle dhruve bhadre kariṣyati na saṃśayaḥ  LiP 
yadā viṣṇuś ca bhavitā vāsudevo mahāyaśāḥ 
śāpādbhṛgormahātejāḥ sarvalokahitāya vai  LiP 
tadā tasya suto yaś ca sa patiste bhaviṣyati 
sā praṇamya tadā rudraṃ kāmapatnī śucismitā  LiP 
jagāma madanaṃ labdhvā vasaṃtena samanvitā  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge madanadāho nāmaikādhikaśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
LiP  
sūta uvāca
tapasā ca mahādevyāḥ pārvatyā vṛṣabhadhvaja 
prītiś ca bhagavāñcharvo vacanādbrahmaṇastadā  LiP 
hitāya cāśramāṇāṃ ca krīḍārthaṃ bhagavānbhavaḥ 
tadā haimavatīṃ devīm upayeme yathāvidhi  LiP 
jagāma sa svayaṃ brahmā marīcyādyairmaharṣibhiḥ 
tapovanaṃ mahādevyāḥ pārvatyāḥ padmasaṃbhavaḥ  LiP 
pradakṣiṇīkṛtya ca tāṃ devīṃ sa jagato 'raṇīm 
kim arthaṃ tapasā lokān saṃtāpayasi śailaje  LiP 
tvayā sṛṣṭaṃ jagatsarvaṃ mātastvaṃ mā vināśaya 
tvaṃ hi saṃdhārayellokān imān sarvān svatejasā  LiP 
sarvadeveśvaraḥ śrīmān sarvalokapatirbhavaḥ 
yasya vai devadevasya vayaṃ kiṅkaravādinaḥ  LiP 
sa evaṃ parameśānaḥ svayaṃ ca varayiṣyati 
varade yena sṛṣṭāsi na vinā yastvayāṃbike  LiP 
vartate nātra saṃdehas tava bharttā bhaviṣyati 
ityuktvā tāṃ namaskṛtya muhuḥ samprekṣya pārvatīm  LiP 
gate pitāmahe devo bhagavān parameśvaraḥ 
jagāmānugrahaṃ kartuṃ dvijarūpeṇa cāśramam  LiP 
sā ca dṛṣṭvā mahādevaṃ dvijarūpeṇa saṃsthitam 
pratibhādyaiḥ prabhuṃ jñātvā nanāma vṛṣabhadhvajam  LiP 
sampūjya varadaṃ devaṃ brāhmaṇacchadmanāgatam 
tuṣṭāva parameśānaṃ pārvatī parameśvaram  LiP 
anugṛhya tadā devīm uvāca prahasanniva 
kuladharmāśrayaṃ rakṣan bhūdharasya mahātmanaḥ  LiP 
krīḍārthaṃ ca satāṃ madhye sarvadevapatirbhavaḥ 
svayaṃvare mahādevī tava divyasuśobhane  LiP 
āsthāya rūpaṃ yatsaumyaṃ sameṣye 'haṃ saha tvayā 
ityuktvā tāṃ samālokya devo divyena cakṣuṣā  LiP 
jagāmeṣṭaṃ tadā divyaṃ svapuraṃ prayayau ca sā 
dṛṣṭvā hṛṣṭastadā devīṃ menayā tuhinācalaḥ  LiP 
āliṅgyāghrāya sampūjya putrīṃ sākṣāttapasvinīm 
duhiturdevadevena na jānannabhimantritam  LiP 
svayaṃvaraṃ tadā devyāḥ sarvalokeṣvaghoṣayat 
atha brahmā ca bhagavān viṣṇuḥ sākṣājjanārdanaḥ  LiP 
śakraś ca bhagavān vahnir bhāskaro bhaga eva ca 
tvaṣṭāryamā vivasvāṃś ca yamo varuṇa eva ca  LiP 
vāyuḥ somastatheśāno rudrāś ca munayas tathā 
aśvinau dvādaśādityā gandharvā garuḍas tathā  LiP 
yakṣāḥ siddhāstathā sādhyā daityāḥ kiṃpuruṣoragāḥ 
samudrāś ca nadā vedā mantrāḥ stotrādayaḥ kṣaṇāḥ  LiP 
nāgāś ca parvatāḥ sarve yajñāḥ sūryādayo grahāḥ 
trayastriṃśacca devānāṃ trayaś ca triśataṃ tathā  LiP 
trayaś ca trisahasraṃ ca tathānye bahavaḥ surā 
jagmur girīndraputryāstu svayaṃvaramanuttamam  LiP 
atha śailasutā devī haimamāruhya śobhanam 
vimānaṃ sarvatobhadraṃ sarvaratnair alaṃkṛtam  LiP 
apsarobhiḥ pranṛttābhiḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitaiḥ 
gandharvasiddhairvividhaiḥ kinnaraiś ca suśobhanaiḥ  LiP 
bandibhiḥ stūyamānā ca sthitā śailasutā tadā 
sitātapatraṃ ratnāṃśu miśritaṃ cāvahattathā  LiP 
mālinī giriputryāstu saṃdhyā pūrṇendumaṇḍalam 
cāmarāsaktahastābhir divyastrībhiś ca saṃvṛtā  LiP 
mālāṃ gṛhya jayā tasthau suradrumasamudbhavām 
vijayā vyajanaṃ gṛhya sthitā devyāḥ samīpagā  LiP 
mālāṃ pragṛhya devyāṃ tu sthitāyāṃ devasaṃsadi 
śiśurbhūtvā mahādevaḥ krīḍārthaṃ vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ  LiP 
utsaṅgatalasaṃsupto babhūva bhagavānbhavaḥ 
atha dṛṣṭvā śiśuṃ devās tasyā utsaṃgavarttinam  LiP 
ko 'yam atreti saṃmantrya cukṣubhuś ca samāgatāḥ 
vajramāhārayattasya bāhum udyamya vṛtrahā  LiP 
sa bāhurudyamastasya tathaiva samupasthitaḥ 
stambhitaḥ śiśurūpeṇa devadevena līlayā  LiP 
vajraṃ kṣeptuṃ na śaśāka bāhuṃ cālayituṃ tathā 
vahniḥ śaktiṃ tathā kṣeptuṃ na śaśāka tathā sthitaḥ  LiP 
yamo 'pi daṇḍaṃ khaḍgaṃ ca nirṛtirmunipuṅgavāḥ 
varuṇo nāgapāśaṃ ca dhvajayaṣṭiṃ samīraṇaḥ  LiP 
somo gadāṃ dhaneśaś ca daṇḍaṃ daṇḍabhṛtāṃ varaḥ 
īśānaś ca tathā śūlaṃ tīvramudyamya saṃsthitaḥ  LiP 
rudrāś ca śūlamādityā muśalaṃ vasavas tathā 
mudgaraṃ stambhitāḥ sarve devenāśu divaukasaḥ  LiP 
stambhitā devadevena tathānye ca divaukasaḥ 
śiraḥ prakampayan viṣṇuś cakram udyamya saṃsthitaḥ  LiP 
tasyāpi śiraso bālaḥ sthiratvaṃ pracakāra ha 
cakraṃ kṣeptuṃ na śaśāka bāhūṃścālayituṃ na ca  LiP 
pūṣā dantān daśan dantair bālamaikṣata mohitaḥ 
tasyāpi daśanāḥ petur dṛṣṭamātrasya śaṃbhunā  LiP 
balaṃ tejaś ca yogaṃ ca tathaivāstambhayad vibhuḥ 
atha teṣu sthiteṣveva manyumatsu sureṣvapi  LiP 
brahmā paramasaṃvigno dhyānamāsthāya śaṅkaram 
bubudhe devamīśānam umotsaṃge tamāsthitam  LiP 
sa buddhvā devamīśānaṃ śīghram utthāya vismitaḥ 
vavande caraṇau śaṃbhor astuvacca pitāmahaḥ  LiP 
buddhistvaṃ sarvalokānām ahaṅkāras tvam īśvaraḥ 
bhūtānāmindriyāṇāṃ ca tvameveśa pravarttakaḥ  LiP 
tavāhaṃ dakṣiṇāddhastāt sṛṣṭaḥ pūrvaṃ purātanaḥ 
vāmahastān mahābāho devo nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ  LiP 
iyaṃ ca prakṛtirdevī sadā te sṛṣṭikāraṇa 
patnīrūpaṃ samāsthāya jagatkāraṇamāgatā  LiP 
namastubhyaṃ mahādeva mahādevyai namonamaḥ 
prasādāttava deveśa niyogācca mayā prajāḥ  LiP 
devādyāstu imāḥ sṛṣṭā mūḍhāstvadyogamohitāḥ 
kuru prasādameteṣāṃ yathāpūrvaṃ bhavantvime  LiP 
sūta uvāca
vijñāpyaivaṃ tadā brahmā devadevaṃ maheśvaram 
saṃstambhitāṃstadā tena bhagavān āha padmajaḥ  LiP 
mūḍhāstha devatāḥ sarvā naiva budhyata śaṅkaram 
devadevam ihāyāntaṃ sarvadevanamaskṛtam  LiP 
gacchadhvaṃ śaraṇaṃ śīghraṃ devāḥ śakrapurogamāḥ 
sanārāyaṇakāḥ sarve munibhiḥ śaṅkaraṃ prabhum  LiP 
sārdhaṃ mayaiva deveśaṃ paramātmānamīśvaram 
anayā haimavatyā ca prakṛtyā saha sattamam  LiP 
tatra te stambhitāstena tathaiva surasattamāḥ 
praṇemur manasā sarve sanārāyaṇakāḥ prabhum  LiP 
atha teṣāṃ prasanno bhūd devadevastriyaṃbakaḥ 
yathāpūrvaṃ cakārāśu vacanādbrahmaṇaḥ prabhuḥ  LiP 
tata evaṃ prasanne tu sarvadevanivāraṇam 
vapuścakāra deveśo divyaṃ paramamadbhutam  LiP 
tejasā tasya devāste sendracandradivākarāḥ 
sabrahmakāḥ sasādhyāś ca sanārāyaṇakās tathā  LiP 
sayamāś ca sarudrāś ca cakṣuraprārthayan vibhum 
tebhyaś ca paramaṃ cakṣuḥ sarvadṛṣṭau ca śaktimat  LiP 
dadāvaṃbāpatiḥ śarvo bhavānyāś ca calasya ca 
labdhvā cakṣustadā devā indraviṣṇupurogamāḥ  LiP 
sabrahmakaḥ saśakrāś ca tamapaśyanmaheśvaram 
brahmādyā nemire tūrṇaṃ bhavānī ca girīśvaraḥ  LiP 
munayaś ca mahādevaṃ gaṇeśāḥ śivasaṃmatāḥ 
sasarjuḥ puṣpavṛṣṭiṃ ca khecarāḥ siddhacāraṇāḥ  LiP 
devadundubhayo nedus tuṣṭuvurmunayaḥ prabhum 
jagurgandharvamukhyāś ca nanṛtuścāpsarogaṇāḥ  LiP 
mumuhurgaṇapāḥ sarve mumodāṃbā ca pārvatī 
tasya devī tadā hṛṣṭā samakṣaṃ tridivaukasām  LiP 
pādayoḥ sthāpayāmāsa mālāṃ divyāṃ sugandhinīm 
sādhu sādhviti samprocya tayā tatraiva cārcitam  LiP 
saha devyā namaścakruḥ śirobhir bhūtalāśritaiḥ 
sarve sabrahmakā devāḥ sayakṣoragarākṣasāḥ  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge umāsvayaṃvaro nāma dvyadhikaśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
LiP  
sūta uvāca
atha brahmā mahādevam abhivandya kṛtāñjaliḥ 
udvāhaḥ kriyatāṃ deva ityuvāca maheśvaram  LiP 
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ 
yatheṣṭamiti lokeśaṃ prāha bhūtapatiḥ prabhuḥ  LiP 
udvāhārthaṃ maheśasya tatkṣaṇādeva suvratāḥ 
brahmaṇā kalpitaṃ divyaṃ puraṃ ratnamayaṃ śubham  LiP 
athāditirditiḥ sākṣād danuḥ kadruḥ sukālikā 
pulomā surasā caiva siṃhikā vinatā tathā  LiP 
siddhirmāyā kriyā durgā devī sākṣātsudhā svadhā 
sāvitrī vedamātā ca rajanī dakṣiṇā dyutiḥ  LiP 
svāhā svāhāmatir buddhir ṛddhir vṛddhiḥ sarasvatī 
rākā kuhūḥ sinīvālī devī anumatī tathā  LiP 
dharaṇī dhāraṇī celā śacī nārāyaṇī tathā 
etāścānyāś ca devānāṃ mātaraḥ patnayas tathā  LiP 
udvāhaḥ śaṅkarasyeti jagmuḥ sarvā mudānvitāḥ 
uragā garuḍā yakṣā gandharvāḥ kinnarā gaṇāḥ  LiP 
sāgarā girayo meghā māsāḥ saṃvatsarās tathā 
vedā mantrās tathā yajñāḥ stomā dharmāś ca sarvaśaḥ  LiP 
huṅkāraḥ praṇavaścaiva pratihārāḥ sahasraśaḥ 
koṭirapsaraso divyās tāsāṃ ca paricārikāḥ  LiP 
yāś ca sarveṣu dvīpeṣu devalokeṣu nimnagāḥ 
tāś ca strīvigrahāḥ sarvāḥ saṃjagmurhṛṣṭamānasāḥ  LiP 
gaṇapāś ca mahābhāgāḥ sarvalokanamaskṛtāḥ 
udvāhaḥ śaṅkarasyeti tatrājagmurmudānvitāḥ  LiP 
abhyayuḥ śaṅkhavarṇāś ca gaṇakoṭyo gaṇeśvarāḥ 
daśabhiḥ kekarākṣaś ca vidyuto 'ṣṭābhir eva ca  LiP 
catuḥṣaṣṭyā viśākhāś ca navabhiḥ pārayātrikaḥ 
ṣaḍbhiḥ sarvāntakaḥ śrīmān tathaiva vikṛtānanaḥ  LiP 
jvālākeśo dvādaśabhiḥ koṭibhir gaṇapuṅgavaḥ 
saptabhiḥ samadaḥ śrīmān dundubho 'ṣṭābhir eva ca  LiP 
pañcabhiś ca kapālīśaḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ saṃdārakaḥ śubhaḥ 
koṭikoṭibhir eveha gaṇḍakaḥ kuṃbhakas tathā  LiP 
viṣṭambho 'ṣṭābhir eveha gaṇapaḥ sarvasattamaḥ 
pippalaś ca sahasreṇa saṃnādaś ca tathā dvijāḥ  LiP 
āveṣṭanas tathāṣṭābhiḥ saptabhiścandratāpanaḥ 
mahākeśaḥ sahasreṇa koṭīnāṃ gaṇapo vṛtaḥ  LiP 
kuṇḍī dvādaśabhir vīras tathā parvatakaḥ śubhaḥ 
kālaś ca kālakaścaiva mahākālaḥ śatena vai  LiP 
āgnikaḥ śatakoṭyā vai koṭyāgnimukha eva ca 
ādityamūrdhā koṭyā ca tathā caiva dhanāvahaḥ  LiP 
saṃnāmaś ca śatenaiva kumudaḥ koṭibhis tathā 
amoghaḥ kokilaścaiva koṭikoṭyā sumantrakaḥ  LiP 
kākapāṭo 'paraḥ ṣaṣṭyā ṣaṣṭyā saṃtānakaḥ prabhuḥ 
mahābalaś ca navabhir madhupiṅgaś ca piṅgalaḥ  LiP 
nīlo navatyā deveśaḥ pūrṇabhadrastathaiva ca 
koṭīnāṃ caiva saptatyā caturvaktro mahābalaḥ  LiP 
koṭikoṭisahasrāṇāṃ śatair viṃśatibhir vṛtāḥ 
tatrājagmus tathā devās te sarve śaṅkaraṃ bhavam  LiP 
bhūtakoṭisahasreṇa pramathaḥ koṭibhistribhiḥ 
vīrabhadraścatuḥṣaṣṭyā romajāścaiva koṭibhiḥ  LiP 
karaṇaścaiva viṃśatyā navatyā kevalaḥ śubhaḥ 
pañcākṣaḥ śatamanyuś ca meghamanyus tathaiva ca  LiP 
kāṣṭhakūṭaś catuḥṣaṣṭyā sukeśo vṛṣabhas tathā 
virūpākṣaś ca bhagavān catuḥṣaṣṭyā sanātanaḥ  LiP 
tāluketuḥ ṣaḍāsyaś ca pañcāsyaś ca sanātanaḥ 
saṃvartakas tathā caitro lakulīśaḥ svayaṃ prabhuḥ  LiP 
lokāntakaś ca dīptāsyas tathā daityāntakaḥ prabhuḥ 
mṛtyuhṛt kālahā kālo mṛtyuñjayakaras tathā  LiP 
viṣādo viṣadaścaiva vidyutaḥ kāntakaḥ prabhuḥ 
devo bhṛṅgī riṭiḥ śrīmān devadevapriyas tathā  LiP 
aśanir bhāsakaś caiva catuḥṣaṣṭyā sahasrapāt 
ete cānye ca gaṇapā asaṃkhyātā mahābalāḥ  LiP 
sarve sahasrahastāś ca jaṭāmukuṭadhāriṇaḥ 
candrarekhāvataṃsāś ca nīlakaṇṭhās trilocanāḥ  LiP 
hārakuṇḍalakeyūra mukuṭādyair alaṃkṛtāḥ 
brahmendraviṣṇusaṃkāśā aṇimādiguṇairvṛtāḥ  LiP 
sūryakoṭipratīkāśās tatrājagmurgaṇeśvarāḥ 
pātālacāriṇaścaiva sarvalokanivāsinaḥ  LiP 
tuṃbarurnārado hāhā hūhūścaiva tu sāmagāḥ 
ratnānyādāya vādyāṃś ca tatrājagmustadā puram  LiP 
ṛṣayaḥ kṛtsnaśastatra devagītāstapodhanāḥ 
puṇyān vaivāhikān mantrān ajapur hṛṣṭamānasāḥ  LiP 
tata evaṃ pravṛtte tu sarvataś ca samāgame 
girijāṃ tām alaṃkṛtya svayameva śucismitām  LiP 
puraṃ praveśayāmāsa svayam ādāya keśavaḥ 
sadasyāha ca deveśaṃ nārāyaṇamajo harim  LiP 
bhavānagre samutpanno bhavānyā saha daivataiḥ 
vāmāṅgādasya rudrasya dakṣiṇāṅgādahaṃ prabho  LiP 
manmūrtistuhinādrīśo yajñārthaṃ sṛṣṭa eva hi 
eṣā haimavatī jajñe māyayā parameṣṭhinaḥ  LiP 
śrautasmārtapravṛttyartham udvāhārtham ihāgataḥ 
ato 'sau jagatāṃ dhātrī dhātā tava mamāpi ca  LiP 
asya devasya rudrasya mūrtibhir vihitaṃ jagat 
kṣmābagnikhendusūryātma pavanātmā yato bhavaḥ  LiP 
tathāpi tasmai dātavyā vacanācca girermama 
eṣā hy ajā śuklakṛṣṇā lohitā prakṛtirbhavān  LiP 
śreyo 'pi śailarājena saṃbandho 'yaṃ tavāpi ca 
tava pādme samudbhūtaḥ kalpe nābhyaṃbujādaham  LiP 
madaṃśasyāsya śailasya mamāpi ca gururbhavān 
sūta uvāca
bāḍham ityajam āhāsau devadevo janārdanaḥ  LiP 
devāś ca munayaḥ sarve devadevaś ca śaṅkaraḥ 
tataścotthāya vidvānsaḥ padmanābhaḥ praṇamya tām  LiP 
pādau prakṣālya devasya karābhyāṃ kamalekṣaṇaḥ 
abhyukṣad ātmano mūrdhni brahmaṇaś ca gires tathā  LiP 
tvadīyaiṣā vivāhārthaṃ menajā hyanujā mama 
ityuktvā sodakaṃ dattvā devīṃ deveśvarāya tām  LiP 
svātmānamapi devāya sodakaṃ pradadau hariḥ 
atha sarve muniśreṣṭhāḥ sarvavedārthapāragāḥ  LiP 
ūcurdātā gṛhītā ca phalaṃ dravyaṃ vicārataḥ 
eṣa devo haro nūnaṃ māyayā hi tato jagat  LiP 
ityuktvā taṃ praṇemuś ca prītikaṇṭakitatvacaḥ 
sasṛjuḥ puṣpavarṣāṇi khecarāḥ siddhacāraṇāḥ  LiP 
devadundubhayo nedur nanṛtuścāpsarogaṇāḥ 
vedāś ca mūrtimantaste praṇemustaṃ maheśvaram  LiP 
brahmaṇā munibhiḥ sārdhaṃ devadevamumāpatim 
devo 'pi devīmālokya salajjāṃ himaśailajām  LiP 
na tṛpyatyanavadyāṅgī sā ca devaṃ vṛṣadhvajam 
varado 'smīti taṃ prāha hariṃ so 'pyāha śaṅkaram  LiP 
tvayi bhaktiḥ prasīdeti brahmākhyāṃ ca dadau tu saḥ 
tatastu punarevāha brahmā vijñāpayanprabhum  LiP 
havirjuhomi vahnau tu upādhyāyapade sthitaḥ 
dadāsi mama yadyājñāṃ kartavyo hyakṛto vidhiḥ  LiP 
tamāha śaṅkaro devaṃ devadevo jagatpatiḥ 
yadyadiṣṭaṃ suraśreṣṭha tatkuruṣva yathepsitam  LiP 
kartāsmi vacanaṃ sarvaṃ devadeva pitāmaha 
tataḥ praṇamya hṛṣṭātmā brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ  LiP 
hastaṃ devasya devyāś ca yuyoja paramaṃ prabhuḥ 
jvalanaś ca svayaṃ tatra kṛtāñjalirupasthitaḥ  LiP 
śrautairetairmahāmantrair mūrtimadbhir upasthitaiḥ 
yathoktavidhinā hutvā lājānapi yathākramam  LiP 
ānītānviṣṇunā viprān sampūjya vividhairvaraiḥ 
triś ca taṃ jvalanaṃ devaṃ kārayitvā pradakṣiṇam  LiP 
muktvā hastasamāyogaṃ sahitaiḥ sarvadaivataiḥ 
suraiś ca mānavaiḥ sarvaiḥ prahṛṣṭenāntarātmanā  LiP 
nanāma bhagavānbrahmā devadevamumāpatim 
tataḥ pādyaṃ tayor dattvā śaṃbhorācamanaṃ tathā  LiP 
madhuparkaṃ tathā gāṃ ca praṇamya ca punaḥ śivam 
atiṣṭhadbhagavānbrahmā devairindrapurogamaiḥ  LiP 
bhṛgvādyamunayaḥ sarve cākṣataistilataṇḍulaiḥ 
sūryādayaḥ samabhyarcya tuṣṭuvurvṛṣabhadhvajam  LiP 
śivaḥ samāpya devoktaṃ vahnimāropya cātmani 
tayā samāgato rudraḥ sarvalokahitāya vai  LiP 
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi bhavodvāhaṃ śucismitaḥ 
śrāvayedvā dvijāñchuddhān vedavedāṅgapāragān  LiP 
sa labdhvā gāṇapatyaṃ ca bhavena saha modate 
yatrāyaṃ kīrtyate viprais tāvadāste tadā bhavaḥ  LiP 
tasmāt sampūjya vidhivat kīrtayennānyathā dvijāḥ 
udvāhe ca dvijendrāṇāṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ dvijottamāḥ  LiP 
kīrtanīyamidaṃ sarvaṃ bhavodvāhamanuttamam 
kṛtodvāhastadā devyā haimavatyā vṛṣadhvajaḥ  LiP 
sagaṇo nandinā sārdhaṃ sarvadevagaṇairvṛtaḥ 
purīṃ vārāṇasīṃ divyām ājagāma mahādyutiḥ  LiP 
avimukte sukhāsīnaṃ praṇamya vṛṣabhadhvajam 
apṛcchatkṣetramāhātmyaṃ bhavānī harṣitānanā  LiP 
athāhārdhendutilakaḥ kṣetramāhātmyamuttamam 
avimuktasya māhātmyaṃ vistarācchakyate nahi  LiP 
vaktuṃ mayā sureśāni ṛṣisaṃghābhipūjitam 
kiṃ mayā varṇyate devī hy avimuktaphalodayaḥ  LiP 
pāpināṃ yatra muktiḥ syān mṛtānām ekajanmanā 
anyatra tu kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ vārāṇasyāṃ vyapohati  LiP 
vārāṇasyāṃ kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ paiśācyanarakāvaham 
kṛtvā pāpasahasrāṇi piśācatvaṃ varaṃ nṛṇām  LiP 
na tu śakrasahasratvaṃ svarge kāśīpurīṃ vinā 
yatra triviṣṭapo devo yatra viśveśvaro vibhuḥ  LiP 
oṃkāreśaḥ kṛttivāsā mṛtānāṃ na punarbhavaḥ 
uktvā kṣetrasya māhātmyaṃ saṃkṣepācchaśiśekharaḥ  LiP 
darśayāmāsa codyānaṃ parityajya gaṇeśvarān 
tatraiva bhagavān jāto gajavaktro vināyakaḥ  LiP 
daityānāṃ vighnarūpārtham avighnāya divaukasām 
etadvaḥ kathitaṃ sarvaṃ kathāsarvasvamuttamam  LiP 
yathāśrutaṃ mayā sarvaṃ prasādādvaḥ suśobhanam  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge pārvatīvivāhavarṇanaṃ nāma tryadhikaśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ

ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
kathaṃ vināyako jāto gajavaktro gaṇeśvaraḥ 
kathaṃ prabhāvastasyaivaṃ sūta vaktumihārhasi  LiP 
sūta uvāca
etasminnantare devāḥ sendropendrāḥ sametya te 
dharmavighnaṃ tadā kartuṃ daityānāmabhavandvijāḥ  LiP 
asurā yātudhānāś ca rākṣasāḥ krūrakarmiṇaḥ 
tāmasāś ca tathā cānye rājasāś ca tathā bhuvi  LiP 
avighnaṃ yajñadānādyaiḥ samabhyarcya maheśvaram 
brahmāṇaṃ ca hariṃ viprā labdhepsitavarā yataḥ  LiP 
tato 'smākaṃ suraśreṣṭhāḥ sadā vijayasaṃbhavaḥ 
teṣāṃ tatastu vighnārtham avighnāya divaukasām  LiP 
putrārthaṃ caiva nārīṇāṃ narāṇāṃ karmasiddhaye 
vighneśaṃ śaṅkaraṃ sraṣṭuṃ gaṇapaṃ stotumarhatha  LiP 
ityuktvānyonyamanaghaṃ tuṣṭuvuḥ śivamīśvaram 
namaḥ sarvātmane tubhyaṃ sarvajñāya pinākine  LiP 
anaghāya viriñcāya devyāḥ kāryārthadāyine 
akāyāyārthakāyāya hareḥ kāyāpahāriṇe  LiP 
kāyāntasthāmṛtādhāra maṇḍalāvasthitāya te 
kṛtādibhedakālāya kālavegāya te namaḥ  LiP 
kālāgnirudrarūpāya dharmādyaṣṭapadāya ca 
kālīviśuddhadehāya kālikākāraṇāya te  LiP 
kālakaṇṭhāya mukhyāya vāhanāya varāya te 
aṃbikāpataye tubhyaṃ hiraṇyapataye namaḥ  LiP 
hiraṇyaretase caiva namaḥ śarvāya śūline 
kapāladaṇḍapāśāsi carmāṅkuśadharāya ca  LiP 
pataye haimavatyāś ca hemaśuklāya te namaḥ 
pītaśuklāya rakṣārthaṃ surāṇāṃ kṛṣṇavartmane  LiP 
pañcamāya mahāpañca yajñināṃ phaladāya ca 
pañcāsyaphaṇihārāya pañcākṣaramayāya te  LiP 
pañcadhā pañcakaivalya devairarcitamūrtaye 
pañcākṣaradṛśe tubhyaṃ parātparatarāya te  LiP 
ṣoḍaśasvaravajrāṅga vaktrāyākṣayarūpiṇe 
kādipañcakahastāya cādihastāya te namaḥ  LiP 
ṭādipādāya rudrāya tādipādāya te namaḥ 
pādimeṇḍhrāya yadyaṅga dhātusaptakadhāriṇe  LiP 
śāntātmarūpiṇe sākṣāt kṣadantakrodhine namaḥ 
lavarephahalāṅgāya niraṅgāya ca te namaḥ  LiP 
sarveṣām eva bhūtānāṃ hṛdi niḥsvanakāriṇe 
bhruvor ante sadā sadbhir dṛṣṭāyātyantabhānave  LiP 
bhānusomāgninetrāya paramātmasvarūpiṇe 
guṇatrayoparisthāya tīrthapādāya te namaḥ  LiP 
tīrthatattvāya sārāya tasmādapi parāya te 
ṛgyajuḥsāmavedāya oṃkārāya namo namaḥ  LiP 
oṅkāre trividhaṃ rūpam āsthāyoparivāsine 
pītāya kṛṣṇavarṇāya raktāyātyantatejase  LiP 
sthānapañcakasaṃsthāya pañcadhāṇḍabahiḥ kramāt 
brahmaṇe viṣṇave tubhyaṃ kumārāya namonamaḥ  LiP 
aṃbāyāḥ parameśāya sarvoparicarāya te 
mūlasūkṣmasvarūpāya sthūlasūkṣmāya te namaḥ  LiP 
sarvasaṃkalpaśūnyāya sarvasmādrakṣitāya te 
ādimadhyāntaśūnyāya citsaṃsthāya namonamaḥ  LiP 
yamāgnivāyurudrāṃbu somaśakraniśācaraiḥ 
diṅmukhe diṅmukhe nityaṃ sagaṇaiḥ pūjitāya te  LiP 
sarveṣu sarvadā sarva mārge sampūjitāya te 
rudrāya rudranīlāya kadrudrāya pracetase 
maheśvarāya dhīrāya namaḥ sākṣācchivāya te  LiP 
atha śṛṇu bhagavan stavacchalena kathitamajendramukhaiḥ surāsureśaiḥ 
makhamadanayamāgnidakṣayajñakṣapaṇavicitraviceṣṭitaṃ kṣamasva  LiP 
sūta uvāca
yaḥ paṭhettu stavaṃ bhaktyā śakrāgnipramukhaiḥ suraiḥ 
kīrtitaṃ śrāvayedvidvān sa yāti paramāṃ gatim  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge devastutirnāma caturadhikaśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ

sūta uvāca
yadā sthitāḥ sureśvarāḥ praṇamya caivamīśvaram 
tadāṃbikāpatir bhavaḥ pinākadhṛṅ maheśvaraḥ  LiP 
dadau nirīkṣaṇaṃ kṣaṇād bhavaḥ sa tānsurottamān 
praṇemurādarāddharaṃ surā mudārdralocanāḥ  LiP 
bhavaḥ sudhāmṛtopamair nirīkṣaṇairnirīkṣaṇāt 
tadāha bhadramastu vaḥ sureśvarān maheśvaraḥ  LiP 
varārthamīśa vīkṣyate surā gṛhaṃ gatāstvime 
praṇamya cāha vākpatiḥ patiṃ nirīkṣya nirbhayaḥ  LiP 
suretarādibhiḥ sadā hy avighnamarthito bhavān 
samastakarmasiddhaye surāpakārakāribhiḥ  LiP 
tataḥ prasīdatād bhavān suvighnakarmakāraṇam 
surāpakārakāriṇām ihaiṣa eva no varaḥ  LiP 
tatastadā niśamya vai pinākadhṛk sureśvaraḥ 
gaṇeśvaraṃ sureśvaraṃ vapurdadhāra saḥ śivaḥ  LiP 
gaṇeśvarāś ca tuṣṭuvuḥ sureśvarā maheśvaram 
samastalokasaṃbhavaṃ bhavārttihāriṇaṃ śubham  LiP 
ibhānanāśritaṃ varaṃ triśūlapāśadhāriṇam 
samastalokasaṃbhavaṃ gajānanaṃ tadāṃbikā  LiP 
daduḥ puṣpavarṣaṃ hi siddhā munīndrās tathā khecarā devasaṃghāstadānīm 
tadā tuṣṭuvuścaikadantaṃ sureśāḥ praṇemurgaṇeśaṃ maheśaṃ vitandrāḥ  LiP 
tadā tayorvinirgataḥ subhairavaḥ sa mūrtimān 
sthito nanarta bālakaḥ samastamaṅgalālayaḥ  LiP 
vicitravastrabhūṣaṇair alaṃkṛto gajānanaḥ 
maheśvarasya putrako 'bhivandya tātam ambikām  LiP 
jātamātraṃ sutaṃ dṛṣṭvā cakāra bhagavānbhavaḥ 
gajānanāya kṛtyāṃstu sarvānsarveśvaraḥ svayam  LiP 
ādāya ca karābhyāṃ ca susukhābhyāṃ bhavaḥ svayam 
āliṅgyāghrāya mūrdhānaṃ mahādevo jagadguruḥ  LiP 
tavāvatāro daityānāṃ vināśāya mamātmaja 
devānāmupakārārthaṃ dvijānāṃ brahmavādinām  LiP 
yajñaś ca dakṣiṇāhīnaḥ kṛto yena mahītale 
tasya dharmasya vighnaṃ ca kuru svargapathe sthitaḥ  LiP 
adhyāpanaṃ cādhyayanaṃ vyākhyānaṃ karma eva ca 
yo 'nyāyataḥ karotyasmin tasya prāṇānsadā hara  LiP 
varṇāccyutānāṃ nārīṇāṃ narāṇāṃ narapuṅgava 
svadharmarahitānāṃ ca prāṇānapahara prabho  LiP 
yāḥ striyastvāṃ sadā kālaṃ puruṣāś ca vināyaka 
yajanti tāsāṃ teṣāṃ ca tvatsāmyaṃ dātumarhasi  LiP 
tvaṃ bhaktān sarvayatnena rakṣa bālagaṇeśvara 
yauvanasthāṃś ca vṛddhāṃś ca ihāmutra ca pūjitaḥ  LiP 
jagattraye 'tra sarvatra tvaṃ hi vighnagaṇeśvaraḥ 
saṃpūjyo vandanīyaś ca bhaviṣyasi na saṃśayaḥ  LiP 
māṃ ca nārāyaṇaṃ vāpi brahmāṇam api putraka 
yajanti yajñairvā viprair agre pūjyo bhaviṣyasi  LiP 
tvām anabhyarcya kalyāṇaṃ śrautaṃ smārtaṃ ca laukikam 
kurute tasya kalyāṇam akalyāṇaṃ bhaviṣyati  LiP 
brāhmaṇaiḥ kṣatriyairvaiśyaiḥ śūdraiścaiva gajānana 
sampūjya sarvasiddhyarthaṃ bhakṣyabhojyādibhiḥ śubhaiḥ  LiP 
tvāṃ gandhapuṣpadhūpādyair anabhyarcya jagattraye 
devairapi tathānyaiś ca labdhavyaṃ nāsti kutracit  LiP 
abhyarcayanti ye lokā mānavāstu vināyakam 
te cārcanīyāḥ śakrādyair bhaviṣyanti na saṃśayaḥ  LiP 
ajaṃ hariṃ ca māṃ vāpi śakramanyānsurānapi 
vighnair bādhayasi tvāṃ cen nārcayanti phalārthinaḥ  LiP 
sasarja ca tadā vighna gaṇaṃ gaṇapatiḥ prabhuḥ 
gaṇaiḥ sārdhaṃ namaskṛtvāpy atiṣṭhattasya cāgrataḥ  LiP 
tadā prabhṛti loke 'smin pūjayanti gaṇeśvaram 
daityānāṃ dharmavighnaṃ ca cakārāsau gaṇeśvaraḥ  LiP 
etadvaḥ kathitaṃ sarvaṃ skandāgrajasamudbhavam 
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi śrāvayedvā sukhībhavet  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge vināyakotpattirnāma pañcādhikaśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ

nṛtyārambhaḥ kathaṃ śaṃbhoḥ kimarthaṃ vā yathātatham 
vaktumarhasi cāsmākaṃ śrutaḥ skandāgrajodbhavaḥ  LiP 
sūta uvāca
dāruko 'surasambhūtas tapasā labdhavikramaḥ 
sūdayāmāsa kālāgnir iva devāndvijottamān  LiP 
dārukeṇa tadā devās tāḍitāḥ pīḍitā bhṛśam 
brahmāṇaṃ ca tatheśānaṃ kumāraṃ viṣṇumeva ca  LiP 
yamamindramanuprāpya strīvadhya iti cāsuraḥ 
strīrūpadhāribhiḥ stutyair brahmādyairyudhi saṃsthitaiḥ  LiP 
bādhitāstena te sarve brahmāṇaṃ prāpya vai dvijāḥ 
vijñāpya tasmai tatsarvaṃ tena sārdhamumāpatim  LiP 
samprāpya tuṣṭuvuḥ sarve pitāmahapurogamāḥ 
brahmā prāpya ca deveśaṃ praṇamya bahudhā nataḥ  LiP 
dāruṇo bhagavāndāruḥ pūrvaṃ tena vinirjitāḥ 
nihatya dārukaṃ daityaṃ strīvadhyaṃ trātumarhasi  LiP 
vijñaptiṃ brahmaṇaḥ śrutvā bhagavān bhaganetrahā 
devīmuvāca deveśo girijāṃ prahasanniva  LiP 
bhavatīṃ prārthayāmyadya hitāya jagatāṃ śubhe 
vadhārthaṃ dārukasyāsya strīvadhyasya varānane  LiP 
atha sā tasya vacanaṃ niśamya jagato 'raṇiḥ 
viveśa dehe devasya deveśī janmatatparā  LiP 
ekenāṃśena deveśaṃ praviṣṭā devasattamam 
na viveda tadā brahmā devāścendrapurogamāḥ  LiP 
girijāṃ pūrvavacchaṃbhor dṛṣṭvā pārśvasthitāṃ śubhām 
māyayā mohitastasyāḥ sarvajño 'pi caturmukhaḥ  LiP 
sā praviṣṭā tanuṃ tasya devadevasya pārvatī 
kaṇṭhasthena viṣeṇāsya tanuṃ cakre tadātmanaḥ  LiP 
tāṃ ca jñātvā tathābhūtāṃ tṛtīyenekṣaṇena vai 
sasarja kālīṃ kāmāriḥ kālakaṇṭhīṃ kapardinīm  LiP 
jātā yadā kālimakālakaṇṭhī jātā tadānīṃ vipulā jayaśrīḥ 
devetarāṇāmajayastvasiddhyā tuṣṭirbhavānyāḥ parameśvarasya  LiP 
jātāṃ tadānīṃ surasiddhasaṃghā dṛṣṭvā bhayād dudruvur agnikalpām 
kālīṃ garālaṃkṛtakālakaṇṭhīm upendrapadmodbhavaśakramukhyāḥ  LiP 
tathaiva jātaṃ nayanaṃ lalāṭe sitāṃśulekhā ca śirasyudagrā 
kaṇṭhe karālaṃ niśitaṃ triśūlaṃ kare karālaṃ ca vibhūṣaṇāni  LiP 
sārdhaṃ divyāṃbarā devyāḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitāḥ 
siddhendrasiddhāś ca tathā piśācā jajñire punaḥ  LiP 
ājñayā dārukaṃ tasyāḥ pārvatyāḥ parameśvarī 
dānavaṃ sūdayāmāsa sūdayantaṃ surādhipān  LiP 
saṃraṃbhātiprasaṃgād vai tasyāḥ sarvamidaṃ jagat 
krodhāgninā ca viprendrāḥ saṃbabhūva tadāturam  LiP 
bhavo 'pi bālarūpeṇa śmaśāne pretasaṃkule 
ruroda māyayā tasyāḥ krodhāgniṃ pātum īśvaraḥ  LiP 
taṃ dṛṣṭvā bālamīśānaṃ māyayā tasya mohitā 
utthāpyāghrāya vakṣojaṃ stanaṃ sā pradadau dvijāḥ  LiP 
stanajena tadā sārdhaṃ kopamasyāḥ papau punaḥ 
krodhenānena vai bālaḥ kṣetrāṇāṃ rakṣako 'bhavat  LiP 
mūrtayo 'ṣṭau ca tasyāpi kṣetrapālasya dhīmataḥ 
evaṃ vai tena bālena kṛtā sā krodhamūrchitā  LiP 
kṛtamasyāḥ prasādārthaṃ devadevena tāṇḍavam 
saṃdhyāyāṃ sarvabhūtendraiḥ pretaiḥ prītena śūlinā  LiP 
pītvā nṛtyāmṛtaṃ śaṃbhor ākaṇṭhaṃ parameśvarī 
nanarta sā ca yoginyaḥ pretasthāne yathāsukham  LiP 
tatra sabrahmakā devāḥ sendropendrāḥ samantataḥ 
praṇemustuṣṭuvuḥ kālīṃ punardevīṃ ca pārvatīm  LiP 
evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ proktaṃ tāṇḍavaṃ śūlinaḥ prabhoḥ 
yogānandena ca vibhos tāṇḍavaṃ ceti cāpare  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge śivatāṇḍavakathanaṃ nāma ṣaḍadhikaśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ

puropamanyunā sūta gāṇapatyaṃ maheśvarāt 
kṣīrārṇavaḥ kathaṃ labdho vaktumarhasi sāṃpratam  LiP 
sūta uvāca
evaṃ kālīm upālabhya gate deve triyaṃbake 
upamanyuḥ samabhyarcya tapasā labdhavānphalam  LiP 
upamanyuriti khyāto muniś ca dvijasattamāḥ 
kumāra iva tejasvī krīḍamāno yadṛcchayā  LiP 
kadācit kṣīram alpaṃ ca pītavān mātulāśrame 
īrṣyayā mātulasuto hy apibat kṣīram uttamam  LiP 
pītvā sthitaṃ yathākāmaṃ dṛṣṭvā provāca mātaram 
mātarmātarmahābhāge mama dehi tapasvini  LiP 
gavyaṃ kṣīram atisvādu nālpamuṣṇaṃ namāmyaham 
sūta uvāca
upalālitaivaṃ putreṇa putram āliṅgya sādaram  LiP 
duḥkhitā vilalāpārtā smṛtvā nairdhanyamātmanaḥ 
smṛtvā smṛtvā punaḥ kṣīram upamanyurapi dvijāḥ 
dehi dehīti tāmāha rodamāno mahādyutiḥ  LiP 
uñchavṛttyārjitān bījān svayaṃ piṣṭvā ca sā tadā 
bījapiṣṭaṃ tadāloḍya toyena kalabhāṣiṇī  LiP 
aihyehi mama putreti sāmapūrvaṃ tataḥ sutam 
āliṅgyādāya duḥkhārtā pradadau kṛtrimaṃ payaḥ  LiP 
pītvā ca kṛtrimaṃ kṣīraṃ mātrā dattaṃ dvijottamāḥ 
naitatkṣīramiti prāha mātaraṃ cātivihvalaḥ  LiP 
duḥkhitā sā tadā prāha samprekṣyāghrāya mūrdhani 
saṃmārjya netre putrasya karābhyāṃ kamalāyate  LiP 
taṭinī ratnapūrṇāste svargapātālagocarāḥ 
bhāgyahīnā na paśyanti bhaktihīnāś ca ye śive  LiP 
rājyaṃ svargaṃ ca mokṣaṃ ca bhojanaṃ kṣīrasaṃbhavam 
na labhante priyāṇyeṣāṃ no tuṣyati sadā bhavaḥ  LiP 
bhavaprasādajaṃ sarvaṃ nānyadevaprasādajam 
anyadeveṣu niratā duḥkhārtā vibhramanti ca  LiP 
kṣīraṃ tatra kuto 'smākaṃ mahādevo na pūjitaḥ 
pūrvajanmani yaddattaṃ śivamudyamya vai suta  LiP 
tadeva labhyaṃ nānyattu viṣṇumudyamya vā prabhum 
niśamya vacanaṃ mātur upamanyurmahādyutiḥ  LiP 
bālo 'pi mātaraṃ prāha praṇipatya tapasvinīm 
tyaja śokaṃ mahābhāge mahādevo 'sti cetkvacit  LiP 
cirādvā hyacirādvāpi kṣīrodaṃ sādhayāmyaham 
sūta uvāca
tāṃ praṇamyaivamuktvā sa tapaḥ kartuṃ pracakrame  LiP 
tamāha mātā suśubhaṃ kurviti sutarāṃ sutam 
anujñātastayā tatra tapastepe sudustaram  LiP 
himavatparvataṃ prāpya vāyubhakṣaḥ samāhitaḥ 
tapasā tasya viprasya vidhūpitamabhūjjagat  LiP 
praṇamyāhustu tatsarve haraye devasattamāḥ 
śrutvā teṣāṃ tadā vākyaṃ bhagavānpuruṣottamaḥ  LiP 
kimidaṃ tviti saṃcintya jñātvā tatkāraṇaṃ ca saḥ 
jagāma mandaraṃ tūrṇaṃ maheśvaradidṛkṣayā  LiP 
dṛṣṭvā devaṃ praṇamyaivaṃ provācedaṃ kṛtāñjaliḥ 
bhagavan brāhmaṇaḥ kaścid upamanyuritiśrutaḥ  LiP 
kṣīrārthamadahatsarvaṃ tapasā taṃ nivāraya 
etasminnantare devaḥ pinākī parameśvaraḥ 
śakrarūpaṃ samāsthāya gantuṃ cakre matiṃ tadā  LiP 
atha jagāma munestu tapovanaṃ gajavareṇa sitena sadāśivaḥ 
saha surāsurasiddhamahoragair amararājatanuṃ svayamāsthitaḥ  LiP 
sahaiva cāruhya tadā dvipaṃ taṃ pragṛhya vālavyajanaṃ vivasvān 
vāmena śacyā sahitaṃ surendraṃ kareṇa cānyena sitātapatram  LiP 
rarāja bhagavān somaḥ śakrarūpī sadāśivaḥ 
sitātapatreṇa yathā candrabiṃbena mandaraḥ  LiP 
āsthāyaivaṃ hi śakrasya svarūpaṃ parameśvaraḥ 
jagāmānugrahaṃ kartum upamanyos tadāśramam  LiP 
taṃ dṛṣṭvā parameśānaṃ śakrarūpadharaṃ śivam 
praṇamya śirasā prāha munirmunivarāḥ svayam  LiP 
pāvitaścāśramaścāyaṃ mama deveśvaraḥ svayam 
prāptaḥ śakro jagannātho bhagavānbhānunā prabhuḥ  LiP 
evamuktvā sthitaṃ vīkṣya kṛtāñjalipuṭaṃ dvijam 
prāha gaṃbhīrayā vācā śakrarūpadharo haraḥ  LiP 
tuṣṭo 'smi te varaṃ brūhi tapasānena suvrata 
dadāmi cepsitān sarvān dhaumyāgraja mahāmate  LiP 
evamuktastadā tena śakreṇa munisattamaḥ 
varayāmi śive bhaktim ityuvāca kṛtāñjaliḥ  LiP 
tato niśamya vacanaṃ muneḥ kupitavatprabhuḥ 
prāha savyagramīśānaḥ śakrarūpadharaḥ svayam  LiP 
māṃ na jānāsi devarṣe devarājānamīśvaram 
trailokyādhipatiṃ śakraṃ sarvadevanamaskṛtam  LiP 
madbhakto bhava viprarṣe māmevārcaya sarvadā 
dadāmi sarvaṃ bhadraṃ te tyaja rudraṃ ca nirguṇam  LiP 
tataḥ śakrasya vacanaṃ śrutvā śrotravidāraṇam 
upamanyuridaṃ prāha japan pañcākṣaraṃ śubham  LiP 
manye śakrasya rūpeṇa nūnam atrāgataḥ svayam 
kartuṃ daityādhamaḥ kaścid dharmavighnaṃ ca nānyathā  LiP 
tvayaiva kathitaṃ sarvaṃ bhavanindāratena vai 
prasaṃgāddevadevasya nirguṇatvaṃ mahātmanaḥ  LiP 
bahunātra kimuktena mayādyānumitaṃ mahat 
bhavāntarakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ śrutā nindā bhavasya tu  LiP 
śrutvā nindāṃ bhavasyātha tatkṣaṇādeva saṃtyajet 
svadehaṃ taṃ nihatyāśu śivalokaṃ sa gacchati  LiP 
yo vācotpāṭayejjihvāṃ śivanindāratasya tu 
triḥ saptakulamuddhṛtya śivalokaṃ sa gacchati  LiP 
āstāṃ tāvanmamecchāyāḥ kṣīraṃ prati surādhamam 
nihatya tvāṃ śivāstreṇa tyajāmyetatkalevaram  LiP 
purā mātrā tu kathitaṃ tathyameva na saṃśayaḥ 
pūrvajanmani cāsmābhir apūjita iti prabhuḥ  LiP 
evamuktvā tu taṃ devam upamanyurabhītavat 
śakraṃ cakre matiṃ hantum atharvāstreṇa mantravit  LiP 
bhasmādhārānmahātejā bhasmamuṣṭiṃ pragṛhya ca

dagdhuṃ svadeham āgneyīṃ dhyātvā vai dhāraṇāṃ tadā 
atiṣṭhacca mahātejāḥ śuṣkendhanamivāvyayaḥ  LiP 
evaṃ vyavasite vipre bhagavānbhaganetrahā

kṣīradhārāsahasraṃ ca kṣīrodārṇavameva ca 
dadhyāderarṇavaṃ caiva ghṛtodārṇavameva ca  LiP 
phalārṇavaṃ ca bālasya bhakṣyabhojyārṇavaṃ tathā 
apūpagirayaścaiva tathātiṣṭhan samantataḥ  LiP 
upamanyumuvāca sasmito bhagavānbandhujanaiḥ samāvṛtam 
girijām avalokya sasmitāṃ saghṛṇaṃ prekṣyatu taṃ tadā ghṛṇī  LiP 
bhuṅkṣva bhogānyathākāmaṃ bāndhavaiḥ paśya vatsa me 
upamanyo mahābhāga tavāṃbaiṣā hi pārvatī  LiP 
mayā putrīkṛto 'syadya dattaḥ kṣīrodadhis tathā 
madhunaścārṇavaścaiva dadhnaścārṇava eva ca  LiP 
ājyodanārṇavaścaiva phalalehyārṇavas tathā 
apūpagirayaścaiva bhakṣyabhojyārṇavaḥ punaḥ  LiP 
pitā tava mahādevaḥ pitā vai jagatāṃ mune 
mātā tava mahābhāgā jaganmātā na saṃśayaḥ  LiP 
amaratvaṃ mayā dattaṃ gāṇapatyaṃ ca śāśvatam 
varānvaraya dāsyāmi nātra kāryā vicāraṇā  LiP 
evamuktvā mahādevaḥ karābhyāmupagṛhya tam 
āghrāya mūrdhani vibhur dadau devyāstadā bhavaḥ  LiP 
devī tanayamālokya dadau tasmai girīndrajā 
yogaiśvaryaṃ tadā tuṣṭā brahmavidyāṃ dvijottamāḥ  LiP 
so 'pi labdhvā varaṃ tasyāḥ kumāratvaṃ ca sarvadā 
tuṣṭāva ca mahādevaṃ harṣagadgadayā girā  LiP 
varayāmāsa ca tadā vareṇyaṃ virajekṣaṇam 
kṛtāñjalipuṭo bhūtvā praṇipatya punaḥ punaḥ  LiP 
prasīda devadeveśa tvayi cāvyabhicāriṇī 
śraddhā caiva mahādeva sānnidhyaṃ caiva sarvadā  LiP 
evamuktastadā tena prahasanniva śaṅkaraḥ 
dattvepsitaṃ hi viprāya tatraivāntaradhīyata  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge upamanyucaritaṃ nāma saptādhikaśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ

dṛṣṭo 'sau vāsudevena kṛṣṇenākliṣṭakarmaṇā 
dhaumyāgrajastato labdhaṃ divyaṃ pāśupataṃ vratam  LiP 
kathaṃ labdhaṃ tadā jñānaṃ tasmātkṛṣṇena dhīmatā 
vaktumarhasi tāṃ sūta kathāṃ pātakanāśinīm  LiP 
sūta uvāca
svecchayā hyavatīrṇo 'pi vāsudevaḥ sanātanaḥ 
nindayanneva mānuṣyaṃ dehaśuddhiṃ cakāra saḥ  LiP 
putrārthaṃ bhagavāṃstatra tapastaptuṃ jagāma ca 
āśramaṃ copamanyorvai dṛṣṭavāṃstatra taṃ munim  LiP 
namaścakāra taṃ dṛṣṭvā dhaumyāgrajamaho dvijāḥ 
bahumānena vai kṛṣṇas triḥ kṛtvā vai pradakṣiṇam  LiP 
tasyāvalokanādeva muneḥ kṛṣṇasya dhīmataḥ 
naṣṭameva malaṃ sarvaṃ kāyajaṃ karmmajaṃ tathā  LiP 
bhasmanoddhūlanaṃ kṛtvā upamanyurmahādyutiḥ 
tamagniriti viprendrā vāyurityādibhiḥ kramāt  LiP 
divyaṃ pāśupataṃ jñānaṃ pradadau prītamānasaḥ 
muneḥ prasādānmānyo 'sau kṛṣṇaḥ pāśupate dvijāḥ  LiP 
tapasā tvekavarṣānte dṛṣṭvā devaṃ maheśvaram 
sāṃbaṃ sagaṇamavyagraṃ labdhavānputramātmanaḥ  LiP 
tadāprabhṛti taṃ kṛṣṇaṃ munayaḥ saṃśitavratāḥ 
divyāḥ pāśupatāḥ sarve tasthuḥ saṃvṛtya sarvadā  LiP 
anyaṃ ca kathayiṣyāmi muktyarthaṃ prāṇināṃ sadā 
sauvarṇīṃ mekhalāṃ kṛtvā ādhāraṃ daṇḍadhāraṇam  LiP 
sauvarṇaṃ piṇḍikaṃ cāpi vyajanaṃ daṇḍameva ca 
naraiḥ striyātha vā kāryaṃ maṣībhājanalekhanīm  LiP 
kṣurāḥ kartarikā cāpi atha pātramathāpi vā 
pāśupatāya dātavyaṃ bhasmoddhūlitavigrahaiḥ  LiP 
sauvarṇaṃ rājataṃ vāpi tāmraṃ vātha nivedayet 
ātmavittānusāreṇa yoginaṃ pūjayedbudhaḥ  LiP 
te sarve pāpanirmuktāḥ samastakulasaṃyutāḥ 
yānti rudrapadaṃ divyaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā  LiP 
tasmādanena dānena gṛhastho mucyate bhavāt 
yogināṃ saṃpradānena śivaḥ kṣipraṃ prasīdati  LiP 
rājyaṃ putraṃ dhanaṃ bhavyam aśvaṃ yānamathāpi vā 
sarvasvaṃ vāpi dātavyaṃ yadīcchenmokṣamuttamam  LiP 
adhruveṇa śarīreṇa dhruvaṃ sādhyaṃ prayatnataḥ 
bhavyaṃ pāśupataṃ nityaṃ saṃsārārṇavatārakam  LiP 
etadvaḥ kathitaṃ sarvaṃ saṃkṣepānna ca saṃśayaḥ 
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi viṣṇulokaṃ sa gacchati  LiP 
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge 'ṣṭottaraśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
